### [1] [Development and Performance Study of Vertical GaN $α$-Particle Detector with High Energy Resolution](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23923)
*Minjie Ye,Yuzi Yang,Jiangtao Wei,Weilong Qin,Hao Hong,Dong Han,Jianping Ni,Zhiyi Liu,Po-Chung Huang,Cheng-Chang Yu,Chao-Yi Fang,Entsai Lin,Zewen Liu,Shaomin Chen*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文提出一种集成20纳米超薄死层与保护环结构的垂直同质外延氮化镓（GaN）α粒子探测器，实现了2.195 nA（-200 V）的超低漏电流和2.69%的本征能量分辨率。研究首次通过Geant4模拟证明耗尽层宽度非均匀性是低能尾峰延伸的主导来源，并建立了耗尽层非均匀性模型。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能量分辨率的GaN α粒子探测器在空间辐射、核仪器和恶劣环境应用中潜力巨大，但现有器件仍面临死层厚度减薄、高反向偏压下漏电流抑制、能量分辨率提升以及低能尾峰物理机制阐明等关键挑战。

Method: 采用垂直同质外延结构，集成20纳米超薄死层和保护环（guard-ring）结构以抑制漏电流；利用Geant4模拟分析能谱低能尾峰的物理来源，并建立耗尽层宽度非均匀性（depletion-width nonuniformity）模型进行实验验证。

Result: 器件在-200 V下漏电流低至2.195 nA，在-260 V下电荷收集效率（CCE）达95.9%，本征能量分辨率达2.69%。Geant4模拟首次揭示耗尽层宽度非均匀性是部分能量泄漏并导致低能尾峰延伸的主导因素，模型与实验吻合良好。

Conclusion: 该工作阐明了低能尾峰现象的物理机制，为高性能GaN基辐射探测器的设计与优化提供了实践指导。

Abstract: High-energy-resolution GaN $α$-particle detectors have significant potential for space radiation, nuclear instrumentation, and harsh-environment applications. However, existing GaN $α$-particle detectors still face several key challenges, including reducing the dead-layer thickness, suppressing leakage current under high reverse bias, improving energy resolution, and clarifying the physical mechanism underlying the low-energy tail phenomenon. This study presents a vertical homoepitaxial GaN $α$-particle detector integrating a 20-nm ultrathin dead layer and a guard-ring structure. The detector exhibits an ultralow leakage current of 2.195 nA at -200 V and an intrinsic energy resolution of 2.69% with a charge collection efficiency (CCE) of 95.9% at -260 V. More importantly, this work demonstrates for the first time through Geant4 simulations that depletion-width nonuniformity is the dominant source of partial energy leakage, leading to an extended low-energy tail in the energy spectrum. We establish a depletion-width nonuniformity model and observe good agreement between simulation and experiment. This finding provides practical guidance for the design and optimization of high-performance GaN-based radiation detectors.

</details>


### [2] [Systematic Investigation of Acceptor Removal in HPK LGADs with Modified Gain Layers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23956)
*Yua Murayama,Mahiro Kobayashi,Tomoka Imamura,Koji Nakamura,Issei Horikoshi,Koji Sato,Masato Terada,Minoru Hirose,Tatsuya Masubuchi,Sayuka Kita*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文系统研究了低增益雪崩二极管（LGADs）中多种改良增益层设计（氧修饰、碳注入、硼-磷补偿结构）在质子与反应堆中子辐照后的辐射耐受性。结果表明，仅碳注入方案能显著提升辐射耐受性，而氧修饰、硼-磷补偿及碳注入补偿结构均未表现出明显优势；此外，受主移除系数依赖于辐照粒子的类型与能量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: LGADs 在高能强子对撞机中面临辐射环境中增益层受主移除（acceptor removal）导致的电场退化与性能衰减问题。提升增益层辐射耐受性（radiation tolerance）是未来四维（4D）径迹探测应用的关键需求。

Method: 本研究与滨松光子学株式会社（Hamamatsu Photonics K.K., HPK）合作，制备了具有氧修饰、碳注入及硼-磷补偿结构等不同增益层设计的LGAD原型。传感器先后接受质子与反应堆中子辐照，采用电流-电压（IV）测量提取受主移除系数（acceptor-removal coefficient），并通过辐照后恢复时间性能所需的工作电压来表征辐射耐受性。

Result: 碳注入是唯一能显著提升辐射耐受性的方案；氧修饰（包括部分活化硼（Partially Activated Boron, PAB）方案）及增益层补偿均未带来明显改善；碳注入与补偿结合的结构相较纯碳注入方案无明显优势。受主移除系数依赖于辐照粒子类型和能量。

Conclusion: 碳注入增益层设计在提升LGAD辐射耐受性方面最具前景，而氧修饰、补偿结构及两者组合的效果有限。辐照粒子种类与能量对受主移除系数的依赖性需在器件设计时加以考虑。

Abstract: Low-Gain Avalanche Diodes (LGADs) are fast silicon sensors with internal charge multiplication and are key candidates for precision timing layers in future high-energy hadron colliders. Their operation in harsh radiation environments, however, is limited by acceptor removal in the gain layer, which reduces the active acceptor concentration and degrades the internal electric field required for avalanche multiplication. Improving the radiation tolerance of the gain layer is therefore essential for future 4D tracking applications. In this work, we investigated several LGAD prototypes produced in collaboration with Hamamatsu Photonics K.K. (HPK), featuring modified gain-layer designs, including oxygen-modified, carbon-implanted, and boron--phosphorus compensated structures. The sensors were studied after proton and reactor-neutron irradiation. Radiation tolerance was characterized using the acceptor-removal coefficient extracted from IV measurements and the operation voltage required to recover the timing performance after irradiation. The results show that carbon implantation is the only approach among those studied here that provides a clear improvement in radiation tolerance. In contrast, neither oxygen-related modification, including the Partially Activated Boron (PAB) approach, nor gain-layer compensation alone yields a significant improvement, and the compensated carbon-implanted structure shows no clear advantage over the carbon-only case. In addition, the acceptor-removal coefficient is found to depend on the irradiation particle type and energy.

</details>

Wilking,A. Wilkinson,C. Wilkinson,R. J. Wilson,P. Winter,J. Wolcott,J. Wolfs,T. Wongjirad,A. Wood,K. Wood,E. Worcester,M. Worcester,K. Wresilo,M. Wright,M. Wrobel,S. Wu,Z. Wu,J. Wyenberg,B. M. Wynne,Y. Xiao,Z. Xie,D. Xing,B. Yaeggy,A. Yahaya,N. Yahlali,E. Yandel,G. Yang,J. Yang,T. Yang,A. Yankelevich,L. Yates,U. Yevarouskaya,K. Yonehara,T. Young,B. Yu,H. Yu,J. Yu,K. Yu,W. Yuan,R. Zaki,J. Zalesak,L. Zambelli,B. Zamorano,A. Zani,L. Zazueta,G. P. Zeller,J. Zennamo,J. Zettlemoyer,K. Zeug,C. Zhang,S. Zhang,Y. Zhang,L. Zhao,M. Zhao,K. Zhu,E. D. Zimmerman,S. Zucchelli,A. Zummo,V. Zutshi,R. Zwaska*

Main category: physics.ins-det

TL;DR: 本文描述了DUNE水平漂移（HD）远探测器的电荷读出电子学设计，并基于2024年运行的770吨ProtoDUNE-HD探测器原型数据展示了其性能结果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: DUNE（Deep Underground Neutrino Experiment）是一项长基线中微子振荡实验，其远探测器为有史以来最大的液氩时间投影室（liquid argon time projection chamber），需要定制的低温前端电子学（cryogenic front-end electronics）以满足所需探测器性能。

Method: 采用定制设计的电荷读出电子学（charge readout electronics）方案；利用ProtoDUNE-HD探测器（770吨液氩时间投影室）于2024年在CERN中微子平台（CERN Neutrino Platform）运行获取的数据进行性能评估。

Result: 展示了基于ProtoDUNE-HD探测器数据的电荷读出电子学性能结果，验证了该设计在DUNE HD远探测器中的应用可行性。

Conclusion: 该电荷读出电子学方案满足DUNE HD远探测器的性能要求，ProtoDUNE-HD的运行数据为最终探测器设计提供了实验验证。

Abstract: DUNE (Deep Underground Neutrino Experiment) is a long-baseline neutrino oscillation experiment currently under construction, whose far detectors will be the largest liquid argon time projection chambers ever built. This detector design calls for custom-built cryogenic front-end electronics to attain the required detector performance. This paper describes the charge readout electronics that will be used in the DUNE horizontal drift (HD) far detector and presents performance results using data from the ProtoDUNE-HD detector, a 770 ton liquid argon time projection chamber operated at the CERN Neutrino Platform in 2024 that served as the final prototype of the DUNE HD design.

# eess.SY [[Back]](#toc)

### [4] [Defining the Magnetization State of LCF Magnets: From Material Properties to Motor-Level Metrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23707)
*Taha El Hajji,Aleksandr Nadkin,Stefan Skoog,Lars Sjöberg,Kristoffer Nilsson,Anthony C. Morcos*

Main category: eess.SY

TL;DR: 本文针对采用低矫顽力（LCF）磁体的变磁通记忆电机，提出了一套统一的磁化状态（MS）定义框架，涵盖材料级（磁通密度B、磁极化J）和电机级（基波磁链、反电动势分量）共四种定义，并通过有限元分析在id-iq平面上评估了这些定义，揭示了材料特性与可测量电机量之间的关系，为不同应用目标下的MS指标选择提供了指导。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 变磁通记忆电机（variable flux memory motor）利用低矫顽力（Low Coercive Force, LCF）磁体实现可控磁化状态以拓宽高效运行范围，但目前缺乏统一的方法来在材料层面和电机层面定义和比较磁化状态（Magnetization State, MS），因此需要建立一套系统性的定义与评估框架。

Method: 本文提出了四种磁化状态定义：两种基于本征材料属性——磁通密度B（magnetic flux density）和磁极化J（magnetic polarization），以及两种基于电机级量——基波磁链（fundamental flux linkage）和反电动势分量（back-EMF components）。采用有限元分析（finite element analysis, FEA）在一台采用混合磁体构型（LCF和HCF，即High Coercive Force）的内置式永磁同步电机（interior PMSM）及特定电路设置下，在id-iq运行平面上对这些定义进行了评估。

Result: 研究结果厘清了材料级行为与可测量的电机级量之间的关联关系。所提出的框架能够根据应用目标（材料分析、控制实现或状态监测）为变磁通电机选择合适的MS指标提供指导。

Conclusion: 本文建立的统一MS定义与比较框架有助于桥接材料表征与电机应用之间的鸿沟，为变磁通记忆电机的设计、控制与监测提供了理论基础和实用指导。

Abstract: Variable flux memory motors, which employ Low Coercive Force (LCF) magnets, achieve extended high-efficiency operation through controllable magnetization states. To address the need for a unified approach to defining and comparing the magnetization state (MS) across material and motor levels, this paper proposes four MS definitions: two based on intrinsic material properties-magnetic flux density B and magnetic polarization J-and two based on motor-level quantities-fundamental flux linkage and back-EMF components. These definitions are evaluated across the id, iq operating plane using finite element analysis on an interior PMSM with a hybrid magnet configuration (LCF and HCF: High Coercive Force) and a defined circuit setup. The results clarify the relationship between material-level behavior and measurable motor quantities. The proposed framework provides guidance for selecting appropriate MS metrics depending on the application objective, whether for material analysis, control implementation, or condition monitoring in variable flux machines.

</details>

### [5] [Solving Einstein's Equation Numerically on Manifolds with Non-Orientable Spatial Slices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22954)
*Fan Zhang,Lee Lindblom*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了在具有紧致不可定向空间截流形上的爱因斯坦方程（Einstein's equation）解及其数值构造方法，涵盖正、负和零空间标量曲率（spatial scalar curvature）的多种流形，并利用这些解评估了数值方法的优劣与代码的可靠性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究动机在于探索紧致不可定向空间截流形上的简单宇宙学模型（cosmological model），这类流形在传统宇宙学研究中较少涉及；同时希望通过构建具体解来检验和评估所使用数值方法与代码的有效性及局限性。

Method: 采用数值方法求解爱因斯坦方程，在选取的具有不同空间标量曲率（正、负、零）的紧致不可定向流形上构造宇宙学模型解。其中部分解在局域上与均匀弗里德曼宇宙学模型（Friedman cosmological model）不可区分，另一些则包含显著的不均匀性（inhomogeneities）。

Result: 成功构建了多类解：一个例子在局域上等同于均匀弗里德曼模型，其余例子则表现出显著的不均匀性。这些解覆盖了正、负、零空间标量曲率的情形，并用于测试数值方法的适用范围。

Conclusion: 所构造的宇宙学模型解共同揭示了所用数值方法的优势与局限性，并验证了相关代码的正确性与鲁棒性。

Abstract: This paper presents solutions to Einstein's equation -- and the numerical methods used to construct them -- that describe simple cosmological models on manifolds with compact non-orientable spatial slices. These solutions have been constructed on a selection of manifolds having positive, negative, and vanishing spatial scalar curvatures. One example is shown to be indistinguishable locally from a homogeneous Friedman cosmological model, others are constructed with significant inhomogeneities. Together these examples are used to explore the strengths and the limitations of the numerical methods used in this study, and to test the code used to implement them.

</details>


### [6] [Assessing EMRI Detectability of the Rotating Quantum Oppenheimer-Snyder Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23163)
*Dan Zhang,Shulan Li,Guoyang Fu,Jian-Pin Wu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文评估了旋转量子奥本海默-斯奈德黑洞的量子引力效应在极端质量比旋近（EMRI）系统中产生的引力波信号，发现量子修正会导致可检测的去相（dephasing）效应，但黑洞自转会抑制这些量子特征，提示在利用EMRI观测探测量子引力时必须谨慎考虑旋转自由度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子引力效应在极端质量比旋近（EMRI）系统中的可观测印迹尚未被充分研究，特别是对于旋转量子黑洞模型，需要评估其引力波（GW）信号特征及其在LISA探测器中的可检测性。

Method: 采用绝热演化（adiabatic evolution）方法计算由量子修正参数α引起的引力波累积相位偏移（dephasing）；进一步生成增强分析克里奇（AAK）波形，对比含与不含量子参数α的波形在不同自转参数a下的忠实度（faithfulness）。

Result: 量子引力效应会在LISA探测器中产生可检测的印迹，但黑洞旋转会抑制这些量子特征信号。

Conclusion: 在利用EMRI观测探测量子引力时，必须仔细考虑旋转自由度的影响。

Abstract: This letter presents an assessment of quantum gravity effects on extreme-mass-ratio inspirals (EMRIs) for the rotating quantum Oppenheimer-Snyder (qOS) black hole. Employing the adiabatic evolution, we compute the gravitational wave (GW) dephasing, which quantifies the cumulative phase shift induced by the quantum correction α . We further generate the augmented analytic kludge (AAK) waveform and investigate the faithfulness between the waveforms with and without the quantum parameter α for different values of a. Our results reveal that the quantum gravity effect induces detectable imprints in LISA, while the presence of rotation suppresses these signatures. This suggests that rotational degrees of freedom must be carefully accounted for when probing quantum gravity with EMRI observations.

</details>


### [7] [Ground measurements of the gravitational redshift questioned:re-establishing the physical bases](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23250)
*Anna M. Nobili,Alberto Anselmi*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文反驳了Asenbaum等人（2024）关于Pound-Rebka实验的质疑，指出该质疑源于对参考系和非引力作用力的误解，从而维护了该实验作为引力红移首次实验测量的正统地位。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对Asenbaum等人声称Pound-Rebka实验（1960年）测得的并非爱因斯坦预言的重力红移（gravitational redshift）而是一种源于非引力反作用力的多普勒频移（Doppler shift）这一科学文献争议，作者旨在澄清相关基本概念并纠正误解。

Method: 本文通过重新审视Pound-Rebka实验所涉及的参考系（reference system）定义，分析非引力作用力（non-gravitational force）的物理解释，逐条指出Asenbaum等人论证中的概念混淆和非物理解读。

Result: 分析表明，Asenbaum等人的结论源于对参考系的错误理解以及非引力作用力的非物理解释；Pound-Rebka实验对引力红移测量的有效性得以恢复。

Conclusion: Pound-Rebka实验在物理学史上作为重力红移首次实验验证的地位应被重新确认，Asenbaum等人的质疑不成立。

Abstract: Motivated by alleged inconsistencies in the scientific and educational literature, Asenbaum, Overstreet and Kasevic \href{https://doi.org/10.1088/1402-4896/ad340c}{(2024)} aim to clarify some fundamental concepts in the physics of gravitation. To this end they reexamine the first experimental measurement of the gravitational redshift by Pound and Rebka in 1960, claiming that it did not in fact measure the gravitational redshift predicted by Einstein almost half a century earlier, but rather a Doppler shift originating from non-gravitational reaction forces. We show that their conclusion arises from a misunderstanding of the reference systems involved, along with an unphysical interpretation of non gravitational forces. Thus, our work restores the Pound and Rebka experiment to its rightful place in Physics.

</details>


### [8] [Spectral Butterfly Effect and Resilient Ringdown in Thick Braneworlds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23364)
*Hai-Long Jia,Wen-Di Guo,Yu-Peng Zhang,Yu-Xiao Liu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文发现厚膜世界（thick braneworlds）中的准正则模（quasinormal modes）谱表现出“频谱蝴蝶效应”：有效势的微小形变即可引发准正则模的剧烈迁移。尽管频谱本身高度脆弱，但在当前探测器灵敏度下，早期环降信号仍由原始基模主导，呈现出脆弱频谱与稳健环降的共存。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准正则模谱被视为连接引力波观测与额外维几何的唯一指纹，但其在厚膜世界中的稳定性尚未得到充分检验。

Method: 作者分别从频域和时域分析了厚膜世界中有效势微小扰动对准正则模谱的影响，考察了扰动位置和强度对不稳定性的敏感程度。

Result: 频域不稳定性对扰动的位置和强度高度敏感；时域中，近膜扰动主要改变早期环降（ringdown），远膜扰动则产生干净的晚期回波（late-time echoes）。引力子零模（graviton zero mode）保持局域化，四维引力得以保留。

Conclusion: 厚膜世界表现出脆弱频谱与稳健环降的非平凡共存：频谱虽高度敏感，但早期信号在当前探测器灵敏度下仍由原始基模主导，支持标准指纹在当代引力波天文学中的继续使用，同时揭示了其隐藏的敏感性。

Abstract: The quasinormal mode spectrum is a unique fingerprint linking gravitational-wave observations to extra-dimensional geometry. In this Letter, we show that thick braneworlds exhibit a spectral butterfly effect: infinitesimal deformations of the effective potential trigger dramatic migrations of quasinormal modes, challenging the presumed stability of this fingerprint. Frequency-domain instabilities depend sensitively on the perturbation's location and strength. In the time domain, near-brane perturbations primarily modify the early ringdown, while far-brane perturbations generate clean late-time echoes. Crucially, the graviton zero mode remains localized, preserving four-dimensional gravity. Despite this pronounced spectral fragility, the observable early-stage signal under current detector sensitivities is still dominated by the original fundamental mode. Hence, thick braneworlds display a nontrivial coexistence of a fragile spectrum and a resilient ringdown, supporting the continued use of the standard fingerprint in present-day gravitational-wave astronomy while revealing its hidden sensitivity.

</details>


### [9] [Forecasting graviton-mass constraints from the full covariance of PTA-astrometry ORF estimators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23384)

Method: 建立了一个全协方差（full-covariance）形式体系，推导了自动与交叉通道重叠约化函数（overlap reduction function）估计量的解析协方差表达式，涵盖信号-信号、噪声-噪声和信号-噪声贡献，并通过数值模拟进行验证。基于当前灵敏度（类似NANOGrav 15 yr和Gaia）和未来灵敏度（类似SKA和Theia/Gaia-NIR）分别进行预测性分析（forecast）。

Result: 在当前灵敏度预测中，引力子质量约束主要由PTA主导；在未来灵敏度预测中，联合PTA-天体测量推断可将引力子质量界限（graviton-mass bound）提升约一个数量级（one order of magnitude）。

Conclusion: PTA-天体测量多通道推断（PTA-astrometry multichannel inference）为获得更强的引力子质量约束提供了一条可行途径。

Abstract: We develop a full-covariance formalism for joint pulsar timing array (PTA) and astrometric analyses of a nanohertz stochastic gravitational-wave background and apply it to forecasts of graviton-mass constraints. Analytic covariance expressions are derived for auto- and cross-channel overlap reduction function estimators, including signal-signal, noise-noise, and signal-noise contributions, and are validated against numerical simulations. In a current-like forecast with sensitivities comparable to NANOGrav 15 yr and Gaia, the constraint remains PTA-dominated, while a future-like forecast with sensitivities comparable to the SKA and Theia/Gaia-NIR improves the joint graviton-mass bound by about one order of magnitude. These results demonstrate that PTA-astrometry multichannel inference provides a viable avenue for placing stronger constraints on the graviton mass.

### [10] [A Complete Invariant Analysis of the Kerr Spacetime and its Photon Region](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23389)
*Nicholas Layden,Dipanjan Dey,Alan Coley*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了Kerr时空的一个不变量（invariant）刻画，并利用该时空的不变量结构导出了一个函数，其零点识别出一族特殊的零测地线（null geodesics）。该族测地线与Kerr光子区域中的每个光子表面（photon surface）相切，从而提供了轴对称时空中光子表面的不变量表征方法，并给出了高效计算光子区域任意部分测地线方程的工具。识别所有球形光子轨道（spherical photon orbits）的不变量由一个洛伦兹参数（Lorentz parameter）参数化，该参数有效表示球形光子轨道穿过赤道平面的倾角。文章还展示了该不变量如何确定光子区域中所有球形轨道的运动常数，并简要推导了识别其他几何重要表面（如能层表面ergosurfaces和局域视界local horizons）的不变量。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为Kerr时空提供一种不变量（invariant）刻画方法，旨在通过几何不变量统一表征光子表面（photon surfaces）、球形光子轨道（spherical photon orbits）及其他重要几何结构（如能层表面ergosurfaces和局域视界local horizons），从而突破传统坐标依赖方法的局限性。

Method: 利用Kerr时空的不变量结构（invariant structure）导出一个函数，其零点对应一族特殊的零测地线（null geodesics），该族测地线与光子区域中所有光子表面相切，据此建立不变量表征方法。识别球形光子轨道的不变量由一个洛伦兹参数（Lorentz parameter）参数化，该参数等效于轨道穿过赤道平面的倾角。

Result: 得到了识别Kerr光子区域中一族特殊零测地线的不变量函数，并证明了该族测地线与所有光子表面相切；球形光子轨道的不变量由洛伦兹参数参数化，该参数等效于轨道倾角；进一步确定了光子区域中所有球形轨道的运动常数（constants of motion）；还推导了识别能层表面和局域视界的不变量。

Conclusion: 该工作为轴对称时空（axially symmetric spacetimes）中光子表面和光子区域（photon region）的不变量表征提供了系统性方法，并为高效计算光子区域中的测地线方程（geodesic equations）提供了实用工具。

Abstract: We present an invariant characterization of the Kerr spacetime, and utilize the invariant structure of the spacetime to derive a function whose zeros identify a special family of null geodesics. Each member of this family is tangent to every photon surface in the Kerr photon region, offering a method of invariantly characterizing photon surfaces in axially symmetric spacetimes and thereby a providing a computational tool for efficiently computing the geodesic equations for any part of the photon region. The invariant that identifies all of the spherical photon orbits is parameterized by a Lorentz parameter, where the parameter is effectively an inclination angle of the spherical photon orbits through the equatorial plane. We also show how the invariant determines the constants of motion for all spherical orbits in the photon region. Finally, we briefly derive invariants which identify the other geometrically important surfaces such as the ergosurfaces and local horizons.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用线性状态方程（EoS）$p_r=w_rρ$ 和 $p_θ=w_θρ$ 描述流体，通过调节Rastall参数使有效径向压强为零，从而获得一类精确非奇异解。

Result: 得到的解中物质壳经历收缩、反弹点（bounce point）后进入膨胀阶段；陷获面（trapped surface）的形成可以被避免，因此反弹事件不被表观视界（apparent horizon）覆盖；弱能量条件（WEC）得到满足。

Abstract: We study spherically symmetric gravitational collapse of an inhomogeneous fluid with anisotropic energy momentum tensor (EMT) in Rastall gravity. We therefore set the Rastall parameter in such a way that the effective radial pressure vanishes. This helps us to obtain a class of exact nonsingular solutions in which the matter shells undergo a {collapse} process in a contracting regime, reach a bounce point, and then enter an expanding phase. We further investigate formation of trapped surfaces during the dynamical evolution of the collapsing body. {It is found} that for the obtained solutions, {the} trapped surface formation can be avoided and consequently, the bounce event is not covered by the apparent horizon. Validity of weak energy condition (WEC) is also examined for the obtained solutions.

### [12] [Physics informed operator learning of parameter dependent spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23625)
*Haohao Gu,Sensen He,Hanlin Song,Bo Liang,Zhenwei Lyu,Xiaoguang Hu,Minghui Du,Peng Xu,Bo-Qiang Ma*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出DeepOPiraKAN，一种用于参数依赖型谱问题（spectral problem）的开源物理信息神经网络（PINN）架构。它通过算子学习（operator learning）一次性学习参数到谱的映射，避免了重复求解。在Kerr黑洞准正则模（quasinormal mode）计算中，单网络即可在完整自旋范围内高精度求解多个（ℓ,m）模式与高阶泛音，误差最低达10⁻⁶量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 微分算子谱问题广泛存在于物理系统中，但其谱对连续参数敏感，需在参数空间内反复求解，计算成本高昂。现有方法缺乏高效、可扩展的统一框架来解决此类参数依赖型谱问题。

Method: 提出名为DeepOPiraKAN的开源物理信息神经网络架构，核心思路是将算子学习与增强的优化稳定性相结合，训练单个模型捕捉从连续参数到谱的映射关系，从而避免在参数空间各孤立点重复进行谱求解。

Result: 在Kerr黑洞准正则模计算中，单网络对(ℓ,m)∈{(2,0),(2,1)}模式及其高达n=7的泛音，在完整自旋范围内实现精确分辨。基模相对误差达10⁻⁶量级，高阶泛音误差逐步上升至10⁻⁴量级（以Leaver方法为基准）。

Conclusion: 该精度对黑洞光谱学（black hole spectroscopy）及当前和未来观测台的环down（ringdown）建模已具有显著价值。更广泛地，结果展示了DeepOPiraKAN作为参数依赖型谱问题通用可扩展框架的潜力，适用于复杂物理系统。

Abstract: Spectral problems governed by differential operators underpin a wide range of physical systems, yet remain computationally challenging because their spectra depend sensitively on continuous parameters and often demand repeated evaluations across parameter space. Here we present $\texttt{DeepOPiraKAN}$, an open source physics informed neural network architecture for spectral analysis. By combining operator learning with enhanced optimization stability, it captures the underlying parameter-to-spectrum mapping in a single model, avoiding repeated spectral solutions at isolated points in parameter space. As a representative and stringent benchmark, we apply this framework to the computation of quasinormal modes of Kerr black holes. A single trained network accurately resolves modes with $(\ell,m)\in \{(2,0),(2,1)\}$ and overtones up to $n=7$ across the full spin range, achieving relative errors of $\mathcal{O}(10^{-6})$ for the fundamental mode and gradually increasing to $\mathcal{O}(10^{-4})$ for higher overtones, benchmarked against the Leaver's method. This level of accuracy is already significant for black hole spectroscopy and practical ringdown modelling for current and future observatories. More broadly, these results highlight the potential of $\texttt{DeepOPiraKAN}$ as a general and scalable framework for parameter dependent spectral problems across complex physical systems.

### [13] [Stationary solutions in the small-$c$ expansion of GR](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23677)
*Enes Bal,Ertuğrul Ekiz,Emre Onur Kahya,Utku Zorba*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在ADM变量下研究了广义相对论的小c展开至NNLO阶，在稳态扇区中构建了强引力和弱引力两支的精确真空解，包括Lense-Thirring型、C-metric型和Hartle-Thorne型解，并扩展了高阶多极矩修正。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用ADM变量对广义相对论进行小c展开至NLO和NNLO阶；在稳态扇区中区分强引力分支（strong-gravity branch）和弱引力分支（weak-gravity branch），分别求解精确真空解。

Result: 在强引力分支，NLO阶获得了Lense-Thirring和旋转C-metric精确真空解，NNLO阶构建了对应的Lense-Thirring型和C-metric型解，这些解来自Kerr和旋转C-metric几何的小c展开（NLO至O(J)，NNLO至O(J³)）。弱引力分支获得具有独立四极矩的Hartle-Thorne型解、自旋平方修正以及混合四极-旋转解，并将多极矩扩展至ℓ=4。

Abstract: We study the small-$c$ expansion of general relativity in ADM variables up to next-to-next-to-leading order (NNLO). We show that, in the stationary sector, this formulation renders the field equations more tractable for explicit solution building. The stationary sector exhibits both strong- and weak-gravity branches, whose structure becomes richer at NNLO. In the strong-gravity branch, we first obtain exact vacuum solutions of NLO Carroll gravity, including the Lense--Thirring and rotating C-metric backgrounds. At NNLO, we then construct the corresponding Lense--Thirring-type and C-metric-type exact vacuum geometries. These solutions also arise from the small-$c$ expansion of the Kerr and rotating C-metric geometries around the strong-gravity background, up to $\mathcal{O}(J)$ at NLO and up to $\mathcal{O}(J^3)$ at NNLO. In the weak-gravity branch, we find exact Hartle--Thorne-type solutions with an independent quadrupole moment, together with exact spin-squared corrections and a mixed quadrupolar-rotating solution. We further extend the $\ell=0,2$ sector by including higher multipoles up to $\ell=4$, where $\ell$ denotes the multipole index. These results show that the full NLO/NNLO theory admits a richer stationary vacuum sector than the magnetic Carroll truncation. More broadly, the ADM formulation provides a practical framework for constructing and analyzing stationary backgrounds in the small-$c$ expansion of general relativity, and may also offer a useful framework for organizing rotational and higher-multipole deformations relevant to compact astrophysical objects such as slowly rotating black holes and neutron stars.

### [14] [Photon regions, shadow observables and constraints from M87* of a Kerr-Newman-like black hole in Bumblebee gravity surrounded by plasma](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23721)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用非均匀幂律等离子体模型（non-homogeneous power-law plasma model）保证Hamilton-Jacobi方程的可分离性，导出零测地线（null geodesics）方程；引入两组阴影可观测量系统分析各物理参数（自旋a、电荷Q₀、Lorentz破缺参数ℓ、等离子体参数k）对阴影几何的影响；通过能量发射率（energy emission rate）评估参数变化对发射峰的影响；将M87*建模为该黑洞模型并利用EHT观测数据进行参数约束。

Result: 自旋参数a和Lorentz破缺参数ℓ主要增强阴影的扭曲（distortion），而电荷Q₀和等离子体参数k主要导致阴影径向收缩（radial shrinkage）。各参数增大普遍抑制能量发射率的发射峰。EHT观测的角直径θ_d=42±3 μas缩小了可行参数空间，圆度偏差ΔC≲0.1和轴比1<D_x≲4/3均在EHT限制范围内。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the photon regions, shadow, and observational constraints of a Kerr-Newman-like black hole in Bumblebee gravity within a plasma medium. By employing a specific non-homogeneous power-law plasma model to ensure the separability of the Hamilton-Jacobi equation, we derive the null geodesic equations, analyze the photon regions, and construct the black hole shadow. Furthermore, we introduce two sets of shadow observables to systematically analyze the distinct effects of each physical parameter (spin $a$, charge $Q_0$, Lorentz-violating parameter $\ell$, and plasma parameter $k$) on the shadow geometry. Specifically, we find that $a$ and $\ell$ mainly enhance the distortion of the shadow, whereas $Q_0$ and $k$ primarily lead to its radial shrinkage. Additionally, a brief evaluation of the energy emission rate shows that an increase in these parameters generally suppresses the emission peak. Finally, by modeling M87* as a charged rotating black hole in Bumblebee gravity surrounded by plasma, we can constrain the physical parameters using observations from the Event Horizon Telescope (EHT). While the angular diameter $θ_d = 42 \pm 3 \, μ\text{as}$ narrows the viable parameter space, the circularity deviation $ΔC \lesssim 0.1$ and axis ratio $1 < D_x \lesssim 4/3$ obey the EHT limits. This suggests that the charged rotating black hole in Bumblebee gravity surrounded by plasma might be a candidate for real astrophysical black holes.

### [15] [On gravitating dyonic configurations in nonlinear electrodynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23741)
*K. A. Bronnikov,S. V. Bolokhov,G. S. Nurbakova,B. Tynyshbay*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 该论文研究广义相对论及其他度规引力理论中非线性电磁场的静态球对称位形，重点关注电、磁荷相等（dyonic）系统，证明了在满足正确麦克斯韦极限的条件下，总能构造出电磁不变量f在全空间为零的场位形，进而使得这类解在多种引力理论中普遍存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管广义相对论（GR）中仅含单个电（electric charge, q_e）或磁荷（magnetic charge, q_m）的非线性电磁场精确解已广为人知，但兼具两者（dyonic）的非平庸解仅在少数拉格朗日量L(f)的特例中被发现。本文旨在系统研究电、磁荷相等这一特殊情形下dyonic系统的性质，并探索其在更广泛引力理论中的存在性。

Method: 假设拉格朗日量L(f)满足正确的麦克斯韦极限（Maxwell limit），对电、磁荷相等（q_e = q_m）的静态球对称非线性电磁场系统进行分析。通过理论推导证明，在这种对称条件下，总能找到使电磁不变量f = F_{μν} F^{μν}在全空间为零的场位形。

Result: 在电、磁荷相等的条件下，若L(f)具有正确的麦克斯韦极限，则必存在一种电磁场位形使得f在全空间恒为零。这一性质导致该解族广泛存在于广义相对论（含其他引力源如流体或标量场）及多种扩展引力理论（如标量-张量引力、F(R)引力）中，且此时非线性电磁场的行为表现出异常简单的形式。

Conclusion: 电、磁荷相等的dyonic非线性电磁系统在满足麦克斯韦极限时具有普适的退化行为（f=0），使得精确解不仅存在于GR中，还能推广至包含额外物质场或修正引力理论的框架。该结果为构建非线性电动力学与修正引力耦合的解析模型提供了通用途径。

Abstract: We consider static, spherically symmetric configurations of nonlinear electromagnetic fields with Lagrangians $L(f)$, where $f = F_{μν} F^{μν}$, in general relativity (GR) and other metric theories of gravity. The corresponding exact solutions are well known in the framework of GR in cases where only an electric charge ($q_e$) or a magnetic charge ($q_m$) are present, but only a few solutions in particular examples of $L(f)$ are known for dyonic systems with both nonzero $q_e$ and $q_m$. We study the properties of such systems in the special case of equal electric and magnetic charges and, assuming a correct Maxwell limit of $L(f)$, show that there always exists such a configuration of the electromagnetic field that the invariant $f$ is zero in the whole space. It leads to the existence of the corresponding families of solutions both in GR in the presence of other sources of gravity (like fluids or scalar fields) and in a wide range of extended theories of gravity (e.g., scalar-tensor and $F(R)$ gravity), in which the nonlinear electromagnetic field behaves in an especially simple manner.

</details>


### [16] [From Big Bang Nucleosynthesis to Late-Time Acceleration in $f(Q,L_m)$ Gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23793)
*Rajdeep Mazumdar,Kalyan Malakar,Kalyan Bhuyan*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在 $f(Q,L_m)$ 引力框架下系统研究了宇宙从早期到晚期的演化，该框架引入了非度量性（non-metricity）与物质之间的非最小耦合。通过结合 DESI DR2 BAO、先前的 BAO 测量、宇宙计时器（CC）以及引力波标准汽笛（gravitational-wave standard sirens）等多种观测数据，并利用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法进行参数约束，同时加入大爆炸核合成（BBN）冻结约束，模型参数被严格限制。结果表明模型与观测高度吻合，成功描述了从减速到加速膨胀的转变。有效状态方程参数、状态诊断因子（statefinder diagnostics）以及能量条件均显示出类 quintessence 行为，确认了模型的物理可行性。总体而言，$f(Q,L_m)$ 框架是 ΛCDM 模型的一个可行替代方案，在再现其预言的同时允许膨胀历史中的可控偏离。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有宇宙学标准模型 ΛCDM 虽取得巨大成功，但仍面临精细调节（fine-tuning）和巧合问题（coincidence problem）等理论困难。$f(Q,L_m)$ 引力通过引入非度量性与物质之间的非最小耦合，为解释宇宙加速膨胀提供了一种替代几何框架，有望缓解上述问题。

Method: 研究采用马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（MCMC）方法，结合 DESI DR2 BAO、先前 BAO 测量、宇宙计时器（CC）以及引力波标准汽笛（gravitational-wave standard sirens）等多源观测数据进行综合参数拟合。此外，还加入了大爆炸核合成（BBN）冻结约束，以确保模型在早期宇宙中的一致性。

Result: 模型参数受到严格约束，并与观测数据表现出强一致性。模型成功描述了从减速到加速膨胀的宇宙演化过渡。有效状态方程参数、状态诊断因子（statefinder diagnostics）以及能量条件的演化均展现出类 quintessence（quintessence-like）性质。

Conclusion: $f(Q,L_m)$ 引力框架被确认为 ΛCDM 模型的一个物理可行替代方案。它能够紧密复现 ΛCDM 的预测，同时又允许在膨胀历史上存在可控偏离，为研究超越标准模型的宇宙学提供了新的理论路径。

Abstract: We perform a comprehensive investigation of the early-to-late time cosmic evolution within the framework of $f(Q,L_m)$ gravity, characterized by a non-minimal coupling between non-metricity and matter. The model is further tested against a combined set of observational data, including DESI DR2 BAO, previous BAO measurements, cosmic chronometers (CC), and gravitational-wave (GW) standard sirens, using a Markov Chain Monte Carlo (MCMC) approach. Further by incorporating the Big Bang Nucleosynthesis (BBN) freeze-out constraint, we place stringent limits on the model parameters, ensuring consistency with early-Universe physics. The resulting constraints exhibit strong agreement with observations, with the model successfully describing the transition from decelerated to accelerated expansion. The evolution of the effective equation-of-state parameter, together with statefinder diagnostics and energy conditions, reveals a quintessence-like nature and confirms the physical viability of the model. Overall, the $f(Q,L_m)$ framework emerges as a viable alternative to $Λ$CDM, closely reproducing its predictions while allowing controlled deviations in the expansion history.

### [17] [Relative velocity in special relativity and quantum field theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23836)

### [18] [Primordial black hole production in scalar field inflation within $f(T)$ gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24011)
*Daniel Villalobos-Silva,Yerko Vásquez,Giovanni Otalora*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在标量-张量框架下研究了修正遥平行引力中的暴胀，通过弦理论启发的纤维暴胀势实现瞬态超慢滚阶段，数值求解背景方程和宇宙学扰动演化，发现修正引力在小尺度上放大原初曲率功率谱并保持与大尺度CMB约束一致，为原初黑洞形成提供了理论框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索修正遥平行引力（modified teleparallel gravity）在暴胀过程中的可行扩展，特别是超越广义相对论的遥平行等效理论（Teleparallel Equivalent of General Relativity, TEGR）的修正模型，并从原初黑洞（primordial black hole, PBH）形成的角度分析其观测可检验性。

Method: 采用幂律模型（power-law model）和指数模型（exponential model）两种遥平行引力修正方案，通过修正参数α控制偏离；使用弦理论启发的纤维暴胀势（fiber inflation potential）驱动暴胀并实现瞬态超慢滚（ultra slow-roll, USR）阶段；数值求解背景方程并计算修正遥平行框架下的宇宙学扰动演化。

Result: 两种模型均因USR阶段在小尺度上产生原初曲率功率谱的放大，同时在大尺度上与宇宙微波背景（cosmic microwave background, CMB）约束兼容；修正引力通过对扭率函数（torsion function）的导数引入慢滚参数、张量谱指数（tensor spectral index）和张标比（tensor-to-scalar ratio）的修正，产生不同于标准暴胀的可观测特征。

Conclusion: 修正遥平行引力为暴胀期间形成原初黑洞提供了理论上自洽且现象学丰富的框架，其修正效应可在未来的宇宙学观测中得到检验。

Abstract: We investigate inflation in modified teleparallel gravity within a scalar-tensor framework. We focus on two viable extensions of the Teleparallel Equivalent of General Relativity: a power-law model and an exponential model, which introduce controlled deviations from standard teleparallel gravity through a correction parameter $α$. Inflation is driven by a string-inspired fiber inflation potential that naturally realizes a transient ultra slow-roll (USR) phase. We solve the background equations numerically and compute the evolution of cosmological perturbations within the modified teleparallel framework. We show that both models generate an amplification of the primordial curvature power spectrum on small scales due to the USR phase, while remaining compatible with cosmic microwave background constraints at large scales. The modified gravity sector introduces corrections to the slow-roll parameters, tensor spectral index, and tensor-to-scalar ratio through derivatives of the torsion function, leading to potentially observable signatures distinct from canonical inflation. We further analyze the implications of enhanced scalar perturbations for primordial black hole (PBH) formation and demonstrate that modified teleparallel gravity provides a theoretically consistent and phenomenologically rich framework for producing PBHs during inflation.

### [19] [$g_{tt}g_{rr} =-1$ black hole thermodynamics in extended quasi-topological gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24101)
*Johanna Borissova*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个统一框架，用于讨论d维静态黑洞的热力学，这些黑洞具有球面、环面或紧致双曲视界拓扑，并满足Schwarzschild规范下的条件g_{tt}g_{rr}=-1。该框架将任何此类黑洞视为可积的二维有效胀子理论（dilaton theory）的解，进而视为扩展的d维准拓扑引力（quasi-topological gravity）的真空解。研究表明，决定运动方程中f(r)的生成函数在广义第一定律中提供了热力学质量，而熵则计算为Wald熵。该框架适用于具有平坦或反德西特（anti-de Sitter）渐近行为的奇异和规则黑洞。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有关于d维静态黑洞热力学的研究通常针对特定视界拓扑（球面、环面或双曲）或特定渐近行为分别处理，缺乏一个能够统一描述这些不同拓扑和渐近情形的理论框架。

Method: 将满足g_{tt}g_{rr}=-1条件的d维静态黑洞视为可积的二维有效胀子理论的解，进而将其等价于扩展的d维准拓扑引力的真空解。通过分析运动方程中决定f(r)的生成函数，推导广义第一定律中的热力学质量和Wald熵。

Result: 证明了决定f(r)的生成函数在广义第一定律中直接给出热力学质量（thermodynamic mass），而熵则采用Wald熵（Wald entropy）公式计算。该统一框架同时适用于奇异黑洞和规则黑洞，并可处理平坦（flat）或反德西特（anti-de Sitter）渐近边界条件。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一个统一处理不同视界拓扑（球面、环面、双曲）和不同渐近行为（平坦、反德西特）下d维静态黑洞热力学的理论框架，扩大了可应用黑洞解的范围，包括奇异和规则黑洞。

Abstract: We present a unified framework for the discussion of black hole thermodynamics of $d$-dimensional static black holes with spherical, toroidal or compact hyperbolic horizon topology satisfying $g_{tt}g_{rr}=-1$ in Schwarzschild gauge. To that end, we consider any such black hole as a solution to an integrable $2$-dimensional effective dilaton theory and thereby as a vacuum solution to an extended notion of $d$-dimensional quasi-topological gravity. We show that the generating function determining $f(r) = -g_{tt} $ in the integrated equation of motion provides the thermodynamic mass in a generalised first law with entropy computed as the Wald entropy. The framework presented here can be applied to singular and regular black holes with flat or anti-de Sitter asymptotics.

### [20] [Photon Surfaces in Higher-Curvature Gravity: Implications for Quasinormal Modes and Gravitational Lensing](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24115)
*Takamasa Kanai*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用有效场论（EFT）框架描述广义相对论的高阶曲率修正，通过分析静态球对称时空中的准正则模式（QNMs）与强/弱引力透镜效应，展示了强场可观测量（如光子球半径、临界碰撞参数）对EFT耦合系数的高度敏感性，为探测量子引力效应提供了新的观测窗口。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 有效场论（EFT）为描述广义相对论之外的可能偏离提供了一个系统性的框架，通过引力作用量中的高阶曲率修正来捕捉底层基础理论在低能下的效应。本文旨在利用强场可观测量来约束这些EFT修正。

Method: 本文研究了静态球对称时空中零测地线在光子球（photon sphere）附近的行为，采用Bozza发展的强偏转极限（strong deflection limit）形式体系，推导了偏转角（deflection angle）的对数发散结构，并将发散部分与正则部分显式分离。

Result: 在简化设定（$2M=1$）下，分析了EFT框架参数化的广义相对论偏离如何修改光子球半径、临界碰撞参数（critical impact parameter）以及控制强偏转展开的系数等关键可观测量。结果表明这些量直接编码了引力作用量中高阶曲率修正的信息。

Conclusion: 强场可观测量为探测EFT修正提供了灵敏的探针；对引力透镜和准正则模式（QNMs）谱的精密测量可对广义相对论之外的EFT耦合系数施加约束，从而为探测量子引力启发的效应开辟新的观测窗口。

Abstract: Effective field theory (EFT) provides a systematic framework to describe possible deviations from general relativity through higher-curvature corrections to the gravitational action, capturing low-energy effects of an underlying fundamental theory.
  In this work, we investigate quasinormal modes (QNMs) and both weak and strong gravitational lensing in static, spherically symmetric spacetimes, focusing on the behavior of null geodesics near the photon sphere. Adopting the strong deflection limit formalism developed by Bozza, we derive the logarithmic divergence structure of the deflection angle and explicitly separate the divergent and regular contributions.
  Within a simplified setup with $2M=1$, we analyze how deviations from general relativity, parametrized in an EFT framework, modify key observables such as the photon sphere radius, the critical impact parameter, and the coefficients governing the strong deflection expansion. We show that these quantities encode direct information about higher-curvature corrections to the gravitational action.
  Our results demonstrate that strong-field observables provide a sensitive probe of EFT corrections, and that precision measurements of gravitational lensing and QNM spectra could place constraints on EFT couplings beyond general relativity, offering a novel observational window into quantum gravity-inspired effects.

### [21] [BMS transformed Quantum String Dynamics near a Black Hole](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24145)
*Nihar Ranjan Ghosh,Malay K. Nandy*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究闭玻色弦在五维史瓦西黑洞近视界几何中受广义BMS超平移影响的动力学，发现弦的延伸性使其对角形变敏感：角形变破坏了背景SO(4)对称性，径向方程由修正贝塞尔模式支配且存在非零径向守恒流，径向挤压与角向展宽实现了弦在视界附近的动力学展宽，表明弦动力学可作为高维黑洞对称结构的探针。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 渐近对称性（asymptotic symmetries）预期会在引力量子探针上留下微妙但具有物理意义的印记，然而它们在近视界动力学（near-horizon dynamics）中的表现尚未被完全理解。本文旨在通过闭弦探针揭示BMS超平移对黑洞几何的形变效应。

Method: 研究闭玻色弦（closed bosonic string）在五维史瓦西黑洞（five-dimensional Schwarzschild black hole）近视界几何中传播的行为，并施加广义Bondi-van der Burg-Metzner-Sachs (BMS) 超平移（supertranslation）。在特定的规范与衰减条件下，分析弦世界面动力学（worldsheet dynamics）的各个扇区。

Result: 时间和径向扇区不受超平移影响；角扇区形变破坏了背景的SO(4)对称性。径向方程由修正贝塞尔模式（modified Bessel modes）支配，伴随非零径向守恒流（radial conserved current），表明存在输运式传播。引力导致的径向挤压与超平移引起的各向异性角向展宽在视界附近实现了弦展宽（string spreading）。

Conclusion: 弦探针动力学编码了BMS诱导形变的非平庸特征，为高维黑洞时空中对称结构（symmetry structures）的研究提供了动力学探针。

Abstract: Asymptotic symmetries are expected to leave subtle but physically meaningful imprints on quantum probes of gravity, yet their manifestation in near-horizon dynamics remains incompletely understood. We examine this question for a closed bosonic string propagating in the near-horizon geometry of a five-dimensional Schwarzschild black hole subjected to a generalized Bondi-van der Burg-Metzner-Sachs (BMS) supertranslation. The extended nature of the string makes it especially sensitive to the resulting anisotropic geometric distortions, and this sensitivity appears most clearly in the angular sector of the worldsheet dynamics. Under the gauge and falloff conditions adopted here, the temporal and radial sectors remain unaffected by the supertranslation, while the angular deformation breaks the original SO(4) symmetry of the background. The radial equation is governed by modified Bessel modes, with a nonvanishing radial conserved current, indicating transport-like propagation. Radial squeezing driven by gravity and anisotropic angular spreading induced by supertranslations provide a dynamical realization of string spreading near the horizon. Thus this analysis demonstrates that probe string dynamics encodes nontrivial signatures of BMS-induced deformations, providing a dynamical probe of symmetry structures in higher-dimensional black hole spacetimes.

### [22] [Cone hierarchy and the screening of matter by gravity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24213)
*Julio Arrechea,Carlos Barceló,Gil Jannes*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文在“谐和背景范式（Harmonic Background Paradigm, HBP）”框架下，将先前仅限于线性引力近似的思想扩展至完全非线性情形，提出引力体现为一种有效因果形变，并通过因果锥层级与负能量引力云的屏蔽机制相关联。论文以球对称物质分布为例进行说明，并讨论了超越广义相对论的未来方向。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作者此前在线性引力近似下提出了谐和背景范式（HBP），认为引力本质是一种相对于更基础因果性的有效因果形变。本文旨在将该思想推广至完整的非线性引力 regime，从而检验这一范式在更一般条件下的适用性。

Method: 通过建立因果锥层级（causal cone hierarchy）与负能量引力云屏蔽机制（screening mechanism of negative-energy gravitational clouds）之间的联系，将 HBP 扩展至非线性 regime；并以球对称物质分布（spherically symmetric matter distributions）作为具体算例来阐明该思想。

Result: 指出在完全非线性情形下，引力可被理解为一种围绕正能量种子（positive-energy seeds）的负能量引力云（negative-energy gravitational clouds）的屏蔽机制，且该屏蔽效应不会压倒正能量种子。

Conclusion: 论文以 HBP 在非线性框架下的扩展为核心贡献，总结了该范式的关键物理含义，并指出了超越广义相对论（General Relativity）的若干未来研究方向。

Abstract: In a previous paper by some of the authors (Gen. Rel. Grav. 56, 116, 2024), we introduced a novel paradigm with which to understand gravitational phenomena. We called it the Harmonic Background Paradigm (HBP). In this paradigm, gravity amounts to an effective causality deformation with respect to a more fundamental causality, which always encompasses the former through a causal cone hierarchy. In that paper, the fundamental idea was described in detail but fully elaborated only when restricted to the linear gravitational approximation. In this work, we discuss and conjecture how this idea could be extended to the full non-linear regime. We identify a connection between the cone hierarchy and a property of gravity that can be described as a screening mechanism of negative-energy gravitational clouds surrounding (but never overcoming) positive-energy seeds. We illustrate our ideas by applying them to spherically symmetric matter distributions. The paper concludes with a discussion of some key implications and directions for future research, including some remarks beyond General Relativity.

</details>


### [23] [Pre-localization of Massive Black Hole Binaries in the Millihertz Band](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24330)
*Xue-Ting Zhang,Jonathan Gair,Chris Messenger,Natalia Korsakova,Yi-Ming Hu,Hong-Yu Chen*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文开发了一种基于归一化流（normalising flow）的快速贝叶斯推理管道，用于天琴（TianQin）类空间引力波探测器对超大质量黑洞双星（MBHB）信号的早期预警分析，能够在约一分钟内提供参数后验样本，并实现约20平方度的预合并天区定位，为电磁波（EM）后随观测提供及时支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 空间引力波（GW）探测器可观测全宇宙的超大质量黑洞双星（massive black hole binaries, MBHBs），其中部分系统预期会产生电磁波（EM）对应体，为联合观测提供独特机会。然而，实现这一目标需要低延迟、高通量的数据分析管道，以快速提取可靠的源参数和天区定位，从而触发电磁后随观测。

Method: 该方法将探测器时间序列的学习嵌入（learned embedding）与神经样条流（neural spline flow, NSF）相结合，执行摊销贝叶斯推理（amortized Bayesian inference），每个事件约在一分钟内生成主要源参数的后验样本。

Result: 针对一个约15分钟后合并的代表性MBHB信号，该管道实现了约20平方度的预合并天区定位，恢复的天区模态数量与参考的并行回火马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（parallel-tempered Markov chain Monte Carlo, PTMCMC）方法一致，参数不确定性规模相当，且运行时间在实用的预警窗口内。

Conclusion: 基于神经样条流（NSF）的推理方法能够为空间MBHB引力波信号提供准确、近实时的参数估计，其产生的早期预警定位精度足以支持快速电磁后随观测。

Abstract: The space-borne gravitational-wave (GW) detectors will open a new mass and redshift regime, allowing us to observe massive black hole binaries (MBHBs) throughout the Universe. A subset of these systems is expected to produce electromagnetic (EM) counterparts, offering a unique opportunity to follow the continuous evolution of massive black holes through joint GW and EM observations. Realizing this potential, however, requires low-latency, high-throughput data-analysis pipelines that can extract reliable source parameters and sky localizations from space-borne data streams fast enough to trigger EM follow-up. In this work we develop a fast, normalising flow-based inference pipeline designed for early-warning analysis of MBHB signals in a TianQin-like configuration. Our method combines a learned embedding of the detector time series with a neural spline flow (NSF) to perform amortized Bayesian inference, producing posterior samples for the main source parameters in roughly one minute per event. For a representative MBHB whose merger occurs $\sim 15$ minutes after the end of the analyzed GW observation, the pipeline achieves pre-merger sky localizations of order $\sim 20~\mathrm{deg}^2$, recovers the same number of sky modes as a reference parallel-tempered Markov chain Monte Carlo (PTMCMC) analysis, and yields parameter uncertainties of comparable scale, while still operating within a practically useful pre-merger warning window. These results demonstrate that NSF-based inference can deliver accurate, near-real-time parameter estimation for space-borne MBHB GW signals, and that the resulting early-warning localizations are sufficiently precise to make rapid EM follow-up.

</details>


### [24] [Scalar, electromagnetic, and Dirac perturbations of a regular black hole supported by primordial dark matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24349)
*Bekir Can Lütfüoğlu*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了由幻影狄拉克-玻恩-英费尔德（Dirac--Born--Infeld）标量场支撑的精确渐近平坦规则黑洞上的无质量标量、电磁和狄拉克（Dirac）扰动。利用Padé改进的WKB方法（配以标量基模的时域Prony校验），计算了代表性的准正则频率（quasinormal frequencies），发现更大的规则性（regularity）偏移会使频谱向更小振荡频率和阻尼率方向移动，而品质因子变化微弱；这些谱偏移显著高于数值不确定度，表明DBI规则性尺度在环向下落（ringdown）中留下了稳健的自旋依赖印记。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索由幻影Dirac--Born--Infeld标量场所支撑的精确渐近平坦规则黑洞的微扰特性，检验规则性（regularity）尺度对准正则频率（quasinormal frequencies）的影响是否稳健且可观测。

Method: 采用Padé改进的WKB方法（Padé-improved WKB method）计算准正则频率，并对标量基模使用时域Prony（time-domain Prony）方法进行交叉校验；研究对象包括无质量标量、电磁和狄拉克（Dirac）三种扰动场。

Result: 规则性（regularity）增大使频谱向更低振荡频率和阻尼率方向移动，品质因子（quality factor）变化微弱；谱偏移量显著大于估计的数值不确定度，且效应具有自旋依赖性（spin-dependent）。

Conclusion: DBI规则性尺度在黑洞环向下落（ringdown）阶段留下了稳健的、自旋依赖的印记，表明该规则黑洞模型的微扰特征有可能作为引力波观测的区分标志。

Abstract: We study massless scalar, electromagnetic, and Dirac perturbations of the exact asymptotically flat regular black hole supported by a phantom Dirac--Born--Infeld scalar. Using the Padé-improved WKB method, with a time-domain Prony check for the scalar fundamental mode, we compute representative quasinormal frequencies and find that larger regularity shifts the spectrum toward smaller oscillation frequencies and damping rates, whereas the quality factor changes only weakly. The spectral shifts remain well above the estimated numerical uncertainty, demonstrating that the DBI regularity scale leaves a robust spin-dependent imprint on ringdown.

### [25] [Gravitational waves of extreme-mass-ratio inspirals in a rotating black hole with Dehnen dark matter halo](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24413)
*Kun Meng,Shao-Jun Zhang,Nan Yang*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过数值求解Teukolsky方程及Sasaki-Nakamura变换，计算了极端质量比旋进（EMRI）在Kerr黑洞和含Dehn型暗物质晕旋转黑洞（DMBH）背景下辐射的引力波波形，发现暗物质晕会导致波形振幅与相位发生显著变化，且与Kerr黑洞波形的失配度随暗物质晕质量参数和中心黑洞自旋增大而增加。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: EMRI是空间引力波探测器的关键信源，其波形对中心超大质量黑洞（SBH）的类型极为敏感，可作为探测背景时空的新型工具。本文旨在通过对比Kerr黑洞与含暗物质晕旋转黑洞的EMRI引力波，探究暗物质晕对引力波波形的具体影响。

Method: 采用Teukolsky形式，从Newman-Penrose（NP）方程推导曲率张量的微扰方程；对含暗物质晕的旋转黑洞（DMBH）通过变量分离得到径向和角向方程；运用Sasaki-Nakamura（SN）变换将Teukolsky型方程转换为SN方程，再通过数值方法求解。通过计算无穷远和视界处的能流与角动量流研究引力波辐射反作用，进而获得轨道演化；数值求解得到两种极化波形，并利用响应函数计算探测器应变和波形失配度。

Result: 暗物质晕的存在使EMRI引力波波形的振幅与相位均发生显著变化；DMBH与Kerr黑洞波形之间的失配度（mismatch）随暗物质晕质量参数和中心SBH自旋的增加而增大。

Conclusion: 含Dehn型暗物质晕的旋转黑洞背景会明显改变EMRI引力波波形，且这种效应随暗物质晕质量和黑洞自旋的增大而加强，表明EMRI波形有望成为探测暗物质晕和检验背景时空的有效探针。

Abstract: Extreme Mass Ratio Inspirals (EMRIs) are among the key targe sources for the space-based gravitational wave (GW) detectors. The waveforms of the EMRIs are highly sensitive to the types of the central supermassive black hole (SBH) and can serve as a novel sensitive tool to probe the background spacetime. In this work, we compute GWs radiated from EMRIs in the backgrounds of Kerr black hole and rotating black hole with Dehnen-type dark matter halo (DMBH). Following the Teukolsky prescription, we obtain the perturbed equations for curvature tensor from the Newman-Penrose (NP) equations, and for the DMBH we obtain the radial and angular equations through separation of variables. To solve the equations with numerical method we apply the Sasaki-Nakamura (SN) transformation to convert the Teykolsky-type equation into the SN equation. We study the radiation reaction of GWs by computing the energy flux and angular momentum flux at infinity and at the horizon. The orbital evolution is then derived from the total fluxes. We extract the two polarizations of GWs by solving the equation numerically. By comparing the waveforms of Kerr and DMBH, it is found that the DM halo induces noticeable changes in both the amplitude and phase of GWs. We compute the strain of GW detector with the response function and evaluate the mismatch between the waveforms of Kerr and DMBH. The results show that the mismatch increases with the mass parameter of DM halo and the spin of the SBH.

### [27] [Tests of scalar polarizations with multi-messenger events](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24526)
*Sk Md Adil Imam,Macarena Lagos*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文利用参数化后爱因斯坦（PPE）框架，首次结合来自伽马射线暴余辉的偏振角约束及其他电磁对应体信息，对GW170817进行广义相对论的参数化检验；通过引入标量呼吸模式和张量模式修正，对三个非GR参数进行贝叶斯推断，发现四极矩情形下对标量模式存在约2σ的微弱偏好，且电磁偏振角约束显著提高了非GR参数的估计精度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 引力波观测为检验强场下的爱因斯坦广义相对论（General Relativity, GR）提供了独特途径。GR仅预言两种张量极化模式，而一般度规理论允许多达六种独立模式，因此有必要通过实际数据对GR进行参数化检验。

Method: 采用参数化后爱因斯坦（parameterized post-Einsteinian, PPE）框架，首次将来自伽马射线暴余辉的偏振角约束与电磁对应体信息结合，在GR波形基础上添加标量呼吸（scalar breathing）模式及张量模式修正，引入三个非GR参数；对四极矩（ℓ=|m|=2）和偶极矩（ℓ=|m|=1）两种角谐波、两种频率演化模型进行贝叶斯推断。

Result: 对于ℓ=|m|=2的四极矩情形，发现对标量模式存在微弱偏好（标量振幅偏离零值约2σ）；对于ℓ=|m|=1的偶极矩情形，未发现对标量模式的偏好。电磁偏振角约束显著收紧非GR参数边界：在ℓ=|m|=2情形下，标量（张量）振幅修正参数的约束改进约60%（30%）。

Conclusion: 结果表明，电磁对应体的偏振角约束对引力波检验具有重要增强作用，特别是长期跟踪观测可大幅提升对非GR参数的约束能力。

Abstract: Gravitational wave (GW) observations provide a unique opportunity to test Einstein's General Relativity (GR) in the strong-field regime. While GR predicts only two tensor polarization modes, generic metric theories allow up to six independent modes. We perform a parameterized test of GR using the parameterized post-Einsteinian (PPE) framework applied to GW170817, incorporating for the first time the polarization angle constraints from the gamma-ray burst afterglow alongside other electromagnetic (EM) counterpart information. We extend the GR waveform by adding a scalar breathing mode and modifications to the tensor modes, introducing three non-GR parameters. We perform Bayesian inference for both quadrupole $\ell = |m|= 2$ and dipole $\ell = |m|= 1$ angular harmonics, with two frequency evolution models. For $\ell = |m|= 2$ , we find mild preference for a scalar mode (scalar amplitude deviates from zero at $\sim 2 σ$), while for the $\ell = |m|= 1$, we find no preference for a scalar mode. The EM constraint on the polarization angle places very tight bounds on non-GR parameters; for instance, in the case $\ell = |m| = 2$, the bound on the scalar (tensor) amplitude modification parameter improves by roughly $60\%$ $(30\%)$, highlighting the impact that long-term follow up of GW events can have on tests of gravity.

### [28] [Pair-Dependent Drift of Kerr Neighboring-Overtone Gap Minima](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24584)
*Yuye Wu,Hong-Bo Jin*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文通过追踪克尔（Kerr）黑洞准正则模（QNM）高泛音在自旋扫描中的行为，研究相邻泛音之间的复频率间隙，发现鲁棒的内禀极小值及其漂移规律，并通过将极小值设定重新表述为复分离的局部零点问题，给出了几何图像和诊断判据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 准正则模（quasinormal modes, QNMs）是黑洞振铃建模与光谱学的基础，其中高泛音（higher overtones）在早期有贡献，而相邻模在复频率平面上可能呈现局部组织结构。该研究旨在理解克尔黑洞泛音体系下相邻模之间的复频率间隙行为及其内在规律。

Method: 沿自旋扫描连续追踪克尔泛音，研究相邻泛音之间的复频率间隙（complex-frequency gap）。将极小值设定重新表述为两模式间复分离（complex separation）的局部零点问题。对平方间隙求导，得到无分母的实投影诊断量（real-projection diagnostic），即复分离与其共轭及自旋导数三者乘积的实部。

Result: 发现鲁棒的内部极小值，其自旋位置在不同泛音对之间漂移，即使在相同的\((s,\ell,m)\)扇区内也是如此。采样极小值由该诊断量的近似局部零点主导，因此极小值漂移对应其主导零点穿越（zero crossing）的漂移。经过扩展但审慎限制的代表性数据集（包括同族连续延拓、外部正转移和平滑无触发控制）支持了所考察情形下的局部图像，同时局部穿越环境本质上是依赖于泛音对的。

Conclusion: 极小值可被几何地理解为分离向量（separation vector）的局部径向转折事件，而角向运动在复平面上可能持续存在。研究揭示了克尔泛音间隙的局部结构特性，为黑洞光谱学中高阶泛音的组织行为提供了新视角。

Abstract: Quasinormal modes (QNMs) underpin black-hole ringdown modeling and spectroscopy, where higher overtones can contribute at early times and neighboring modes can become locally organized in the complex-frequency plane. Motivated by this, we continuously track Kerr overtones along a spin scan and study a raw neighboring-overtone quantity: the complex-frequency gap between adjacent overtones. We find robust interior minima whose spin locations drift from pair to pair, even within the same \((s,\ell,m)\) sector. We explain this by reformulating minimum setting as a local zero-setting problem for the complex separation between the two modes. Differentiating the squared gap yields a denominator-free real-projection diagnostic (the real part of the product between the complex separation, with conjugation, and its spin derivative). The sampled minimum is governed by an approximate local zero of this diagnostic, so minimum drift becomes the drift of its dominant zero crossing. This also yields a geometric picture: the minimum is a local radial turning event of the separation vector, while angular motion in the complex plane may persist. Finally, an expanded but deliberately restricted representative set (including same-family continuations, external positive transfers, and smooth no-trigger controls) supports this local picture for the triggered cases examined here. At the same time, the detailed local crossing environment remains intrinsically pair dependent.

</details>


### [29] [Hawking Temperature, Sparsity and Energy Emission Rate of Dark Matter Halo Regular Black Holes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24659)
*Faizuddin Ahmed,Edilberto O. Silva*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文研究了由埃纳斯托暗物质晕（Einasto dark matter halo）源起的正则黑洞的热力学与辐射性质，发现暗物质环境会抑制霍金温度（Hawking temperature）和能量发射率，并在有限视界半径范围内产生热力学稳定相及戴维斯型相变（Davies-type phase transition），同时使霍金通量（Hawking flux）更加稀疏。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 旨在理解暗物质晕（dark matter halo）背景对正则黑洞（regular black hole）热力学与辐射性质的影响，揭示暗物质分布参数如何改变黑洞的稳定性及霍金辐射行为。

Method: 采用埃纳斯托密度分布（Einasto density profile）描述暗物质晕，并将其作为源项构建正则黑洞解；推导霍金温度、比热容（specific heat capacity）、霍金通量稀疏参数（sparsity parameter）及光谱能量发射率（spectral energy emission rate）的闭合表达式，所有量均以暗物质特征尺度参数α的函数进行分析，并与标准史瓦西黑洞（Schwarzschild black hole）结果进行对比。

Result: 暗物质晕的存在会抑制霍金温度和能量发射率；比热容在有限视界半径范围内为正值，表明存在热力学稳定相，其边界对应戴维斯型相变；稀疏参数高于标准黑洞，表明霍金通量更为间歇性。

Conclusion: 暗物质环境显著改变正则黑洞的热力学和辐射特性，可能导致霍金辐射信号更微弱且更不连续，同时在一定条件下赋予黑洞热力学稳定性。

Abstract: In this paper, we investigate the thermodynamic and radiative properties of a regular black hole sourced by a dark matter halo described by the Einasto density profile. The closed-form expressions for the Hawking temperature, specific heat capacity, sparsity parameter of Hawking flux, and the spectral energy emission rate were obtained. All these are examined as a function of the characteristic scale parameter $α$ of the dark matter distribution and compared with the standard Schwarzschild results. We show that the presence of a dark matter halo suppresses both the Hawking temperature and energy emission rate relative to the standard black hole result. Crucially, the specific heat capacity can be positive for a finite range of horizon radii, signaling a thermodynamically stable phase; the boundary of this stable region defines a Davies-type phase transition. The sparsity parameter is higher than in the standard black hole, indicating that the dark matter environment makes the Hawking flux even more intermittent.

### [30] [Semiclassical phases of charged spin-$1/2$ matter-wave interferometers in gravitational wave backgrounds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24751)
*Nontapat Wanwieng,Apimook Watcharangkool*

Main category: gr-qc

TL;DR: 本文基于WKB展开协变狄拉克方程，建立了带电自旋-1/2物质波干涉仪在弯曲时空中的半经典框架，将相位分解为动力学、自旋和电磁Aharonov-Bohm三种贡献。在引力波背景下，三种通道受同一潮汐尺度调控但通过不同物理耦合进入，为曲率在量子干涉中的印记提供了统一描述。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究缺乏对带电自旋-1/2物质波在时变引力波（gravitational-wave）背景中干涉相位的统一理论框架，无法清晰区分并理解动力学、自旋和电磁通道的耦合机制。

Method: 对协变狄拉克方程（covariant Dirac equation）进行WKB展开，构建半经典（semiclassical）框架；利用自由下落探测器参考系分析局部潮汐场，并在弱引力波背景下通过麦克斯韦方程组导出曲率诱导的电磁场。

Result: 在Mach-Zehnder干涉仪（MZI）中，三种相位响应（动力学、自旋和AB）均由同一潮汐标度$ddot{h}_A sim Omega^2_{gw}h_0$决定，经共同几何核滤波，但通过不同物理耦合进入。AB贡献不仅取决于包围磁通，还依赖于诱导场的空间变化，并表现出由穿越时间（traversal time）设定的本征频率依赖性。

Conclusion: 该框架统一描述了时变引力波背景下的物质波干涉相位，并识别了时空曲率通过量子干涉对自身产生印记的三种互补路径：动力学、自旋和电磁途径。

Abstract: A matter wave propagating through curved spacetime accumulates phase that encodes both geometry and gauge structure. We develop a semiclassical framework for charged spin-$1/2$ matter-wave interferometers based on a WKB expansion of the covariant Dirac equation, in which the phase decomposes into dynamical, spin, and electromagnetic Aharonov-Bohm (AB) contributions. In a freely falling detector frame, all three channels are governed by local tidal fields. In a weak gravitational-wave (GW) background, the dynamical and spin phases probe the gravitoelectric and gravitomagnetic sectors of curvature, while the AB phase arises from curvature-induced electromagnetic fields obtained from Maxwell's equations in curved spacetime. For a Mach-Zehnder interferometer (MZI), all three responses are determined by the same tidal scale, $\ddot{h}_A \sim Ω^2_{gw}h_0$, and filtered by a common geometric kernel, while entering through distinct physical couplings. In particular, the AB contribution depends not only on the enclosed flux but also on spatial variations of the induced fields and exhibits an intrinsic frequency dependence set by the traversal time. These results provide a unified description of matter-wave interferometric phases in time-dependent GW backgrounds and identify complementary dynamical, spin, and electromagnetic pathways through which spacetime curvature imprints itself on quantum interference.

</details>

### [31] [Local regularity for anisotropic magnetic operators with general codimension singularities](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24314)
*Giovanni Siclari,Stefano Vita*

Main category: math.AP

TL;DR: 本文研究了由余维为 $2 \le n \le d$ 的奇异流形引起的稳态各向异性磁性薛定谔方程解的正则性，建立了局部 Hölder $C^{0,\alpha}$ 和 Schauder $C^{1,\alpha}$ 估计，并揭示了三维情形下螺线管几何形变对 Aharonov-Bohm 型模型的去理想化效应及其正则化机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究受收缩螺线管（shrinking solenoid）沿轴 $Σ_0$ 产生的磁势问题驱动，旨在理解各向异性与奇异磁势（magnetic potential）共同作用下解的局部正则性（local regularity）行为，以及螺线管几何形变对 Aharonov-Bohm 型（AB）模型的物理与正则性影响。

Method: 采用适应磁结构的爆破分析（blow-up analysis）方法，将问题归结为沿奇异集 $Σ_0$ 的极限球面 Laplace-Beltrami 算子（spherical Laplace-Beltrami operator）的谱分析，从而建立弱解的 $C^{0,\alpha}$ 与 $C^{1,\alpha}$ 估计。

Result: 建立了稳态各向异性磁性薛定谔方程弱解的局部 Hölder 与 Schauder 估计；在三维 $d=3, n=2$ 情形下，发现螺线管回路偏离正交截面的几何形变会破坏理想 AB 配置（使管外磁场非零），并通过谱正偏移（positive shift）产生意外正则化效应（regularizing mechanism）。

Conclusion: 各向异性和奇异磁势的耦合通过决定极限谱问题来调控正则性；三维形变螺线管效应打破了理想 AB 模型，同时提升了波动函数（wave function）的正则性，与 $C^{1,\alpha}$ 正则性结果一致。

Abstract: We study local regularity properties of solutions to stationary anisotropic magnetic Schrödinger equations in $\mathbb{R}^d$, $d \ge 2$, arising from singular magnetic potentials concentrated along manifolds of general codimension $2 \le n \le d$. The magnetic interaction is modeled through a covariant gradient of the form \[ \nabla_m u = (iM\nabla + A)u, \] where $M^T M$ is a uniformly elliptic matrix encoding anisotropy and $A$ is a magnetic potential with critical Hardy-type scaling along the $n$-codimensional singular set $Σ_0$; that is, $A\sim \mathrm{dist}(\cdot,Σ_0)^{-1}$. We establish local Hölder $C^{0,α}$ and Schauder $C^{1,α}$ estimates for weak solutions via a blow-up analysis adapted to the magnetic structure. The regularity is deeply influenced by the combined effect of anisotropy and the singular magnetic potential, which determines the spectrum of the limiting spherical Laplace-Beltrami operator arising in the blow-up at the singular set. Our model is motivated by the study of magnetic potentials generated by shrinking solenoids onto an axis $Σ_0$, in the three-dimensional setting $d=3$, $n=2$, leading to Aharonov-Bohm-type (AB) models. In this framework, we show that the geometry of the solenoidal loops plays a crucial role: in particular, any deviation from planar cross-sections orthogonal to $Σ_0$ induces a twofold effect. On the one hand, it breaks the ideal AB configuration, in the sense that the magnetic field outside the solenoid is no longer vanishing. On the other hand, it yields an unexpected regularizing mechanism on the wave functions, through a positive shift in the eigenvalues of the asymptotic spectral problem. This purely three-dimensional effect is consistent with our $C^{1,α}$ regularity.

</details>


<div id='math.PR'></div>

# math.PR [[Back]](#toc)

### [32] [The impact of disorder and non-convex interactions on delocalisation of height functions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24743)
*Paul Dario,Diederik van Engelenburg,Christophe Garban*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究四种自旋系统（XY模型、Villain模型、XY高度函数和整数值高斯自由场）在非椭圆淬火无序下的行为。第一部分将[DG25]中关于XY模型相变在超临界伯努利渗流无限团簇上保持的结果推广到Villain模型；第二部分分析二维情形下对偶整数值高度函数模型在淬火无序下的粗糙化相变保持性；最后应用方法于退火高斯相互作用的整数值高度函数，证明定量粗糙相的存在性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 淬火无序（quenched disorder）对统计力学系统相变行为的影响是凝聚态理论的核心问题之一。不同于椭圆无序情形，非椭圆（non-elliptic）无序下的相变保持性尚未充分理解。本文旨在填补这一空白，特别是将XY模型的相关结果推广到Villain模型，并系统分析对偶高度函数模型在淬火无序下的相变行为。

Method: 采用数学严格分析的方法，基于[DG25]的技术框架，将其拓展至Villain模型。对于二维情形，利用对偶性（duality）将自旋系统映射为整数值高度函数模型，并分析淬火无序（在相邻格点间以概率\bar{p}<1/2独立施加等式约束）下的粗糙化相变（roughening transition）。最后，将方法应用于退火高斯相互作用下的整数值高度函数，涵盖形式为|\nabla h|^p（p∈(0,2]）的所有势能。

Result: 成功将XY模型在超临界伯努利渗流（supercritical Bernoulli percolation）无限团簇上的相变保持性结果推广到Villain模型。证明在二维情形下，当淬火无序由相邻格点x,y间独立以概率\bar{p}<1/2施加\varphi(x)=\varphi(y)约束给出时，XY高度函数和整数值高斯自由场（integer-valued Gaussian free field）的粗糙化相变仍然保持。对于退火高斯相互作用的整数值高度函数，证明了定量粗糙相（quantified rough phase）的存在性，覆盖p∈(0,2]的所有势能，并恢复了[OS25]的最新结果。

Conclusion: 非椭圆淬火无序下多种自旋及高度函数系统的相变具有鲁棒性（robustness）：Villain模型在渗流无序下相变保持；二维对偶高度函数在特定淬火无序下粗糙化相变保持；退火高斯相互作用高度函数的粗糙相存在性可被定量证明。这些结果加深了对无序系统中相变普适性的理解。

Abstract: We study the behaviour of four spins systems (the XY model, the Villain model, the XY height function and the integer-valued Gaussian free field) in the presence of a non-elliptic quenched disorder. In the article [DG25], it was shown that the phase transitions of the XY model (the Berezinskii-Kosterlitz-Thouless phase transition in $d = 2$ and the order/disorder phase transition when $d \geq 3$) persist on the infinite cluster of a supercritical Bernoulli percolation. A first objective of this article is to extend these results to the Villain model.
  Our second objective is to analyse, for $d=2$, how the corresponding dual integer-valued height function models behave in the presence of a dual quenched disorder. These dual models are respectively the XY height function and the integer-valued Gaussian free field. Without disorder, these models are known to exhibit a phase transition in two dimensions called the roughening transition [FS81, Lam22b]. We show that this phase transition persists when the quenched disorder is given by enforcing $\varphi(x) = \varphi(y)$ independently with probability $\bar{p} < 1/2$ for neighboring sites $x, y$.
  Finally, we apply our methods to integer-valued height functions with annealed Gaussian interactions and prove the existence of a (quantified) rough phase. This includes all potentials of the form $|\nabla h|^p$ for $p \in (0, 2]$, recovering recent results of [OS25].

</details>


### [33] ["True" self-avoiding walks on general trees](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24389)
*Tuan-Minh Nguyen*

Main category: math.PR

TL;DR: 本文研究了无限局部有限树上的“真正”自避随机游走（true self-avoiding random walk）的渐近行为，发现该过程在常返（recurrence）与暂态（transience）之间存在尖锐的相变（phase transition），临界值由树的支岔-破产数（branching-ruin number）决定，当该值大于1/2时游走几乎必然暂态，小于1/2时几乎必然常返，从而解决了Kosygina提出的一个开放问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究无限局部有限树上的“真正”自避随机游走的渐近行为，解决Kosygina提出的关于该模型常返性与暂态性的开放问题。

Method: 定义游走在每一步以与当前边权重成正比的概率选择相邻边移动，边权重w(n)=exp(-βn)，n为已遍历次数；通过分析树的支岔-破产数（branching-ruin number）与边界豪斯多夫维数（Hausdorff dimension）的关系来刻画相变临界点。

Result: 该过程表现出尖锐的相变：当树的支岔-破产数大于1/2时，游走几乎必然暂态（transient）；当支岔-破产数小于1/2时，游走几乎必然常返（recurrent）。临界值恰好对应于树在合适度量下边界的豪斯多夫维数。

Conclusion: 成功刻画了“真正”自避随机游走在无限树上的常返-暂态相变，临界条件由支岔-破产数决定，并印证了该临界值与树边界豪斯多夫维数的一致性。

Abstract: We study the asymptotic behavior of ``true" self-avoiding random walks on general infinite locally finite trees. In this model, the walk starts at the root and, at each step, from its current vertex chooses a neighboring edge to traverse with probability proportional to the current weight of that edge, where the weight of each edge after being traversed $n$ times is given by $w(n)=\exp(-βn)$. We show that the process exhibits a sharp phase transition between recurrence and transience. The critical value is determined by the branching-ruin number of the tree, which coincides with the Hausdorff dimension of the boundary of the tree under a suitable metric. We prove that the walk is almost surely transient when the branching-ruin number is greater than $1/2$, and recurrent when it is less than $1/2$. This resolves an open question posed by Kosygina.

</details>

### [34] [Visons in Kitaev Spin Liquids with Majorana Fermi Surfaces](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23014)
*Caio V. S. Soares,Rodrigo G. Pereira*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文研究了Kitaev型量子自旋液体中visons的激发，发现当Majorana费米子形成费米面时，vison能隙随费米面增大而减小，表明量子自旋液体基态存在不稳定性，且大费米面会抑制Majorana-vison散射引起的局域自旋关联变化。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在Kitaev量子自旋液体中，激发谱由可无能隙或有能隙的Majorana费米子和始终有能隙的$\mathbb{Z}_2$规范场涡旋（visons）组成。本文旨在研究当Majorana费米子形成费米面时visons的行为，特别是费米面大小对vison能隙及系统稳定性的影响。

Method: 将visons对的产生类比于在金属中引入局域杂质势，结合数值计算有限格点上的vison能隙，并利用基于格林函数技术的解析方法进行对比，以处理无激发态模式带来的强有限尺寸效应。

Result: visons能隙随费米面增大而减小，暗示量子自旋液体基态存在不稳定性；较大的费米面倾向于抑制由Majorana-vison散射势引起的局域自旋关联变化。

Conclusion: 在Majorana费米子形成费米面的Kitaev型模型中，visons行为类似于金属中的杂质势问题，费米面的增大导致visons能隙减小，可能引发基态不稳定性，同时影响局域自旋关联的响应。

Abstract: The excitation spectrum of Kitaev quantum spin liquids consists of itinerant Majorana fermions, which can be gapless or gapped, and vortices of a $\mathbb{Z}_2$ gauge field, known as visons, which are always gapped. In this work, we investigate visons in Kitaev-type models where the Majorana fermions form a Fermi surface. In this case, the creation of a vison pair is analogous to introducing a local impurity potential in a metal. Since the gapless modes lead to strong finite-size effects, we compare the numerical calculation of the vison gap on finite lattices with the result from an analytical approach based on Green's function techniques. We find that the vison gap decreases as the size of the Fermi surface increases, signalling an instability of the quantum spin liquid ground state. We also show that larger Fermi surfaces tend to suppress the change in local spin correlations due to the Majorana-vison scattering potential.

</details>


### [35] [Exact momentum-space analysis of small spin-1/2 $J_1$-$J_2$ rings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23149)
*Zimeng Li,Ning Wu*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文通过精确少磁子布洛赫态（exact few-magnon Bloch states）对N=6和8的自旋-1/2 J1-J2环进行块对角化哈密顿量求解，解析得到了部分本征态，揭示了各向异性环中同时为总角动量算符本征态的子集，并在各向同性环中实现了多个重要基态（如Majumdar-Ghosh基态和Hamada-Kane-Nakagawa-Natsume基态）的动量空间呈现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究有限尺寸自旋-1/2 J1-J2环的精确本征态结构，特别是各向异性情况下的角动量守恒破缺与各向同性情况下重要基态（如MG态和HKNN态）的动量空间表征及其与实空间对应态的等价性。

Method: 利用一组精确的少磁子布洛赫态（exact few-magnon Bloch states）构建块对角化哈密顿量（block-diagonalized Hamiltonian），将问题简化为至多四维的块矩阵，并解析求解部分本征态。

Result: 对于六位点各向异性环，发现了一组同时为哈密顿量和总角动量算符本征态的子集，尽管后者并不守恒。对于六位点和八位点的各向同性环，在动量空间中实现了Majumdar-Ghosh（MG）基态和Hamada-Kane-Nakagawa-Natsume（HKNN）基态的显式表示，并在N=6时证明了其与实空间对应态的等价性。小环HKNN基态的结构暗示，对于任意偶数N，该态可能表现为N/2个连续下自旋束缚在一起的“束缚态”（bound state）。

Conclusion: 精确少磁子布洛赫态方法能有效解析有限尺寸J1-J2环的部分本征态结构；各向异性环中存在特殊的角动量本征态子集；HKNN基态在动量空间的结构揭示了其可能的束缚态性质，且这一性质可能推广至任意偶数N的系统。

Abstract: This paper considers an $N$-site spin-1/2 $J_1$-$J_2$ ring with $N=6$ and $8$. With the help of a set of exact few-magnon Bloch states, we obtain the block-diagonalized Hamiltonian consisting of block matrices of at most four dimensions. Partial of the eigenstates are analytically solved. For the six-site anisotropic ring, we reveal a subset of eigenstates that are simultaneous eigenstates of the Hamiltonian and the total angular momentum operator, even though the latter is not conserved. For both the six- and eight-site isotropic rings, we achieve momentum-space manifestations of several important states, including the famous Majumdar-Ghosh (MG) ground states and the Hamada-Kane-Nakagawa-Natsume (HKNN) ground state. The equivalence of these states with their real-space counterparts is explicitly shown for $N=6$. The structure of the HKNN ground state for small rings suggests that for any even number $N$ this state might behave like a ``bound state" with $N/2$ successive down spins binding together.

</details>


### [36] [Grassmann time-evolving matrix product operators for fermionic impurities coupled to a superconducting bath](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23301)
*Chu Guo,Wei Wu,Xiansong Xu,Ping-Xing Chen,Changming Yue,Tian Jiang,Ruofan Chen*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文扩展了Grassmann时间演化矩阵乘积算符（GTEMPO）方法，使其能够求解Nambu形式下的费米子杂质问题（即杂质与超导库耦合），并通过Bogoliubov变换将Feynman-Vernon影响泛函解析化为与正常库类似的形式，从而直接适配GTEMPO的核心算法。数值基准测试表明该方法在可解与非可解情形下均具准确性，可用于动力学平均场理论（DMFT）及其非平衡推广中的杂质求解器。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: GTEMPO方法已被证明是处理费米子量子杂质问题（fermionic quantum impurity problems）的一种灵活且可扩展的方案，但此前仅适用于正常库情形。本文旨在将GTEMPO扩展到Nambu形式（Nambu formalism），以处理杂质与超导库（superconducting bath）耦合的费米子杂质问题。

Method: 核心方法是利用Bogoliubov变换（Bogoliubov transformation）处理超导库，从而获得Feynman-Vernon影响泛函（Feynman-Vernon influence functional）的解析表达式，该表达式与正常库情形形式相似，使得GTEMPO（Grassmann time-evolving matrix product operator）的核心算法可以直接适配。算法将影响泛函表示为时间矩阵乘积态（temporal matrix product state），并基于此进行计算。

Result: 在多个精确可解情形下，通过与精确对角化（exact diagonalization）的基准对比验证了方法的准确性；在非可积情形下，通过与连续时间量子蒙特卡洛（continuous-time quantum Monte Carlo）方法在收敛的动力学平均场理论（DMFT）迭代结果进行对比，也验证了准确性。所有测试均同时进行了虚时（imaginary-time）和实时（real-time）计算，展示了方法的灵活性。

Conclusion: 该方法有潜力用作DMFT及其非平衡拓展中的杂质求解器（impurity solver），适用于Nambu形式下的费米子杂质问题。

Abstract: The Grassmann time-evolving matrix product operator (GTEMPO) method, which represents the Feynman-Vernon influence functional as a temporal matrix product state, has been shown to be a flexible and potentially scalable solution for fermionic quantum impurity problems. In this work, we extend GTEMPO to solve fermionic impurity problems in the Nambu formalism, in which the impurity is coupled to a superconducting bath. A key insight is that by employing the Bogoliubov transformation for the superconducting bath, one could obtain the analytic expression of the Feynman-Vernon influence functional in a similar form to the case of a normal bath, after which the core algorithms of GTEMPO can be straightforwardly adapted. We demonstrate the accuracy of our method by benchmarking it against exact diagonalization in several exactly solvable cases, and against the continuous-time quantum Monte Carlo method using converged dynamical mean field theory (DMFT) iterations on the imaginary contour in the non-integrable case. In all cases, we perform both imaginary- and real-time calculations to illustrate the flexibility of our method. These results illustrate that our method could be potentially useful as an impurity solver in DMFT as well as its non-equilibrium extension for fermionic impurity problems in the Nambu formalism.

</details>


### [37] [Non-Abelian Particle-Loop, Fracton, and Planon Condensation in Cage-Net Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24755)
*Yifei Wang,Yu Zhao,Yingcheng Li,Hao Song,Yidun Wan*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 本文提出了一个3+1维非阿贝尔p-loop、fracton和planon凝聚的框架，通过构建基于解耦HGW弦网模型层的扩展cage-net fracton模型，展示了非阿贝尔环凝聚如何驱动ICN模型到X-cube模型的相变，以及fracton和planon凝聚对拓扑序的不同影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有cage-net fracton模型基于Levin-Wen (LW)弦网模型，无法完全描述准粒子的内部空间。本文旨在利用Hu-Geer-Wu (HGW)弦网模型的tail自由度，构建扩展cage-net模型，从而建立非阿贝尔p-loop、fracton和planon凝聚的统一框架。

Method: 采用解耦的二维HGW弦网模型层构建三维扩展cage-net fracton模型；通过投影父二维层的准粒子谱导出cage-net模型的准粒子谱；构造扩展Ising Cage-Net (ICN)模型中$(σ\barσ, 1)$-环的凝聚投影算符。

Result: 非阿贝尔环凝聚驱动ICN模型到截断立方晶格上X-cube (XC)模型的相变，显式揭示非阿贝尔planon分裂为不同子维度激发。fracton凝聚导致三维fracton序退耦回孤立的二维拓扑有序层；planon凝聚使系统完全坍缩为平庸相。

Conclusion: 建立了不同fracton序之间相变的显式哈密顿量机制，提供了一种分析子维度激发演化的可推广方法。

Abstract: We present a framework for non-Abelian p-loop, fracton, and planon condensation in 3+1 dimensions by constructing extended cage-net fracton models using decoupled layers of the Hu-Geer-Wu (HGW) string-net model. These cage-net models extend the conventional cage-net models based on the Levin-Wen (LW) string-net model in the sense that they inherit the tail degrees of freedom of the HGW models, which are essential for completely describing the internal spaces of quasiparticles. This approach allows us to explicitly derive the quasiparticle spectra of the cage-net models by projecting those of the parent 2D HGW layers. Utilizing this framework, we can condense the p-loops formed by non-Abelian anyons within a fracton phase. Specifically, we construct the condensation projector for $(σ\barσ, 1)$-loops within the extended Ising Cage-Net (ICN) model. We demonstrate that condensing these non-Abelian loops drives a phase transition that maps the ICN model to the X-cube (XC) model defined on a truncated cubic lattice, a process that explicitly reveals the splitting of non-Abelian planons into distinct sub-dimensional excitations. Furthermore, our framework extends to the condensation of fractons and planons: we demonstrate that in the ICN model fracton condensation drives the decoupling of the 3D fracton order back into isolated 2D topological order layers, while planon condensation collapses the system entirely into a trivial phase. Our results establish a concrete Hamiltonian mechanism for phase transitions between distinct fracton orders and provide a generalizable method for analyzing the evolution of sub-dimensional excitations.

</details>


### [38] [Coherent spin waves in a maximal entropy phase](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23597)
*Arnau Romaguera,Eugenio Paris,Elizabeth Skoropata,Stefano Agrestini,Mirian Garcia-Fernandez,Marisa Medarde,Noah Schnitzer,Lopa Bhatt,Berit H. Goodge,Yun Yen,Matthias Krack,Michael Schüler,Romain Sibille,Tom Fennell,Daniel G. Mazzone,Jakob Lass,Ellen Fogh,Anirudha Ghosh,Marco Caputo,Carlos William Galdino,Zhijia Zhang,Thorsten Schmitt,Milan Radovic,Luc Patthey,Hiroki Ueda,Monica Ciomaga Hatnean,Elia Razzoli*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该研究通过实验和理论结合，发现反铁磁材料YBaCuFeO5中由熵驱动的混合相（mixed phase）使得无序（disorder）反而增强而非削弱自旋波（spin wave）的相干性，挑战了传统上认为无序会破坏集体激发的观点。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固体中无序通常被认为会破坏相干性，例如安德森局域化（Anderson localization）或磁激发展宽。高熵材料虽利用无序稳定均相混合相，但仍被认为会阻止相干磁激发的形成。本文旨在检验这一传统认知的极限。

Method: 选取反铁磁体系（antiferromagnetic system）YBaCuFeO5，因其含两种磁矩差异显著的过渡金属原子，自旋动力学（spin dynamics）对局域原子序（local atomic ordering）极为敏感。结合共振非弹性X射线散射（resonant inelastic x-ray scattering, RIXS）与线性自旋波理论（linear spin wave theory）进行分析。

Result: 在该熵驱动的混合相中，自旋波保持色散性（dispersive），与有序基态预期显著不同，且呈现分明的声学和光学分支（acoustic and optical branches），两者间由大光学带隙（large optical gap）分隔。无序并未降低集体激发的寿命，反而有利于相干性。

Conclusion: 在熵稳定磁体（entropy-stabilized magnets）中，无序可以促进相干集体模式（coherent collective modes）的形成，而这些模式先前被认为仅限于低熵体系。

Abstract: In solids, disorder is conventionally regarded as detrimental to coherence. It typically localizes and dampens collective excitations, as exemplified by Anderson localization or the broadening of magnetic modes in systems lacking long-range order. While high-entropy materials are specifically designed to harness disorder and stabilize homogeneous mixed-phase structures that can display unique properties, this same disorder is nonetheless expected to preclude the formation of coherent magnetic excitations. To test the limits of this picture, we selected the antiferromagnetic system YBaCuFeO5, as it features two distinct transition metal atoms with significantly different magnetic moments, rendering its spin dynamics exceptionally sensitive to local atomic ordering. Combining resonant inelastic x-ray scattering and linear spin wave theory, we reveal a surprising paradox: YBaCuFeO5 exhibits an unexpected, entropy-driven mixed phase, in which disorder, rather than reducing the lifetime of the collective excitations, favors coherence. In this mixed phase, the spin waves remain dispersive, markedly distinct from those expected for an ordered ground state, and exhibit well-defined acoustic and optical branches separated by a large optical gap. These results demonstrate that in entropy-stabilized magnets, disorder can favor coherent collective modes previously thought to be exclusive to low-entropy systems.

</details>

Generally, our results show that a reliable extraction of topological content through modular methods requires the usage of large systems

Abstract: The identification and manipulation of charge-neutral fractionalized quasi-particles, in particular chiral edge modes (CEM), is a long-standing quest in physics. Remarkably, the microscopically mediated interaction between light and charge-neutral excitations in Mott-Hubbard insulators can take an identical form to the Raman coupling between light and particles with electric charge. However, since CEMs are Raman-inactive due to conservation of lattice momentum, Raman probes have been deemed unsuitable for their identification. Here, using the Kitaev quantum spin liquid (KSL) as an illustrative example, we demonstrate that the long-range correlated disorder inherent to a closed edge can lead to a Raman circular dichroism (RCD) signal that avoids suppression by linear and angular momentum selection rules, and exhibits a dependence on experimentally tunable length and energy scales that are characteristic of CEM. ### [41] [Umklapp corrections to Landau damping and conditions for non-trivial modifications to quantum critical transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24274)
*Vibhu Mishra*

Main category: cond-mat.str-el

TL;DR: 该论文计算了二维d=2时，伊辛向列金属（Ising-nematic metal）中临界费米面接近布里渊区边界时粒子-空穴气泡（particle-hole bubble）的贡献，发现除了标准的对映体（antipodal）贡献外，还存在来自区边界电子（umklapp）的额外贡献，其标度行为依赖于温度，并讨论了该贡献对电阻率线性温度行为起始温度的潜在影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用解析计算方法，对二维d=2和三维d=3伊辛向列金属中的粒子-空穴气泡进行微扰计算，区分了来自费米面对映点的标准贡献（antipodal piece）和来自布里渊区边界附近的倒逆散射贡献（umklapp piece），并分析了不同温度T下后者的标度行为。

Result: 在d=2时，标准对映体贡献给出Π_ATP∝Ω/q；而倒逆（umklapp）贡献在最小倒逆动量q≈Δ_q处给出Π_U∝Ω^α，其中α=2/3或1/2取决于温度T。当α=1/2时，线性/准线性电阻率的最小激活温度T_U可能从z=3临界性预期的T_U∝Δ_q^3降低为T_U∝Δ_q^4。在d=3时，倒逆贡献始终给出Π_U~Ω，因此T_U不受修改。

Conclusion: 二维伊辛向列金属中，临界费米面接近布里渊区边界会引入新的倒逆散射量子临界贡献，其在特定条件下可能改变线性电阻率行为的标度，但该方案仅在一种高度特化的场景下可能实现；三维情况下则无此修正。

Abstract: We compute the particle--hole bubble for an Ising-nematic metal when the critical Fermi surface approaches the Brillouin zone boundary for $d=2$ dimensions. We find two qualitatively distinct contributions: i)~the standard antipodal piece, which gives $Π_{\rm{ATP}}(\mathbf{q}, iΩ)\proptoΩ/q$ and ii)~an additional umklapp piece from electrons near the zone boundary, which gives $Π_{\rm{U}}(\mathbf{q}, iΩ)\propto Ω^α$ at the minimum umklapp momentum $q\approx Δ_q$ with $α= 2/3 $ or $1/2$ depending on the temperature $T$. At high $T$ when $α= 1/2$, the minimum $T$ for the activation of linear/quasi-linear in $T$ resistivity, which is expected to be $T_U \propto Δ_q^3$ from $z=3$ criticality, could potentially get reduced to $T_U \propto Δ_q^4$ due to the $\sqrtΩ$ term and discuss why we find only one hyper-specific scenario where this possibility might be realized. For $d=3$ the umklapp contribution gives $Π_{\rm{U}}\sim Ω$ irrespective of $T$ therefore $T_U$ is not modified in this case.
