### [42] [Field-induced jammed polyhex spin liquid in the honeycomb Ising antiferromagnet](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24687)

Method: 采用基态简并与多六边形铺砌问题的映射分析，结合蒙特卡洛（Monte Carlo）模拟研究自旋扩散行为，并引入量子涨落（quantum fluctuations）中的横向耦合（transverse coupling）考察简并解除机制。

Result: 有限磁场下基态简并映射为多六边形铺砌问题，该态为无局域零模的堵塞自旋液体；磁场强度可控制自旋扩散；横向耦合部分解除简并，保留12-六边形非周期铺砌的广延子空间。

Conclusion: 堵塞多六边形自旋液相存在于实验可行的参数区域，可能在FePX₃类化合物中被观测到。

Abstract: We analyze the ground state properties of the honeycomb Ising antiferromagnet in an external magnetic field. We demonstrate the existence of extensive ground state degeneracy at finite field that maps to a polyhex tiling problem. This state is shown to be a jammed spin liquid, with no local zero modes connecting ground states. Through Monte Carlo simulations, we explore the properties of these states and show that the spin diffusion can be controlled by the magnetic field strength. By considering quantum fluctuations, we demonstrate that transverse coupling partially lifts the ground state degeneracy, selecting an extensive subspace of non-periodic tilings of 12-hexes. We suggest that the jammed polyhex spin liquid phase exists in an experimentally realizable region of parameter space and may be present in the FePX$_3$ compounds.

Result: 研究揭示了晶格结构与阈值翻转场之间的对应关系：通过对比方形晶格（square lattice）、简单立方晶格（simple cubic lattice）和蜂窝晶格（honeycomb lattice），发现配位数（coordination number）的变化会系统性地影响阈值翻转场的大小。

Conclusion: 该工作证明时间相关施温格玻色子平均场理论是描述反铁磁翻转过程的合理框架，为未来超快自旋电子学（spintronics）或磁振子学（magnonics）器件的理论计算与计算模拟奠定了基础。

Abstract: The switching of antiferromagnetic order and its efficient control promise to enable ultrafast manipulation of data and large storage capacity. Recently, the time-dependent Schwinger boson mean-field theory has been successfully developed to study the Néel vector switching in hypercubic antiferromagnetic lattices. In the present article, we aim at demonstrating that the approach is a well-justified framework to capture the essentials of the switching process, even in low-symmetry quantum antiferromagnets. To this end, we show the possibility of the sublattice magnetization reorientation in the quantum antiferromagnetic honeycomb lattice. First, equilibrium properties of the honeycomb lattice are analyzed using the Schwinger boson mean-field theory and compared to the continuous similarity transformation method to justify the applicability of the approach. Then, the Schwinger boson mean-field theory is employed for switching process. We provide a comprehensive answer to the question what the threshold switching fields are when the coordination number of the lattice is varied. Indeed, the results of the study reveal a correspondence between lattice structures and the threshold fields by comparing them for the square and the simple cubic lattices and the honeycomb lattice. The findings of the present article extend the foundation for future theoretical and computational advancements in the field of antiferromagnetic switching. These advancements are of particular relevance for the development of ultrafast spintronic or magnonic devices.

### [44] [Delay Modeling with Conformable and Caputo Derivatives: Analytical and Computational Insights](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23008)
*Yhon Flores,Michel Molina del Sol,Genly Leon,Byron Droguett,Guillermo Fernández-Anaya,Yoelsy Leyva*

Main category: math.NA

TL;DR: 本文对基于相容导数（conformable derivative）和Caputo导数的分数阶延迟微分方程进行了解析与数值对比研究，发现相容导数框架在数值稳定性、解析-数值一致性及物理可解释性方面均优于Caputo导数框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 分数阶延迟微分方程在建模具有记忆和延迟效应的动态现象时具有重要应用，但不同分数阶导数定义（如相容导数与Caputo导数）在解析可解性和数值稳定性上存在显著差异，亟需系统比较。

Method: 针对相容导数情形，发展了相应的积分、指数函数和拉普拉斯变换（Laplace transform）体系，利用级数展开和变换方法处理延迟项；针对Caputo导数情形，分析了卷积记忆核（convolutional memory kernel）带来的挑战。数值上采用网格对齐算法：对相容动力学使用Euler和Runge-Kutta格式，对Caputo动力学使用Euler、L2-σ及序列锚定预测-校正格式。

Result: 对比实验表明，相容导数能实现解析解与数值解的稳定一致吻合；Caputo动力学则需要高阶或序列锚定格式来抑制离散化噪声并维持长期精度。

Conclusion: 相容导数形式在建模具有延迟和记忆的动态现象方面具有显著优势，为基于积分的分数阶模型提供了一种可处理且物理可解释的替代方案。

Abstract: This work presents an analytical and computational study of fractional-order delay differential equations formulated using both the conformable and Caputo derivatives. For the conformable case, we develop the associated integral, exponential function, and Laplace transform, showing how the conformable Laplace framework preserves algebraic structure and facilitates explicit solutions. Delay terms are treated through series expansions and transform-based methods, ensuring causal and finite representations. In parallel, Caputo-based formulations are examined, highlighting the challenges posed by convolutional memory kernels and the potential for long-term numerical instability. Numerical implementations are carried out using mesh-aligned algorithms: Euler and Runge--Kutta schemes for conformable dynamics, and Euler, L2--$σ$, and a series--anchored predictor--corrector method for Caputo dynamics. Comparative experiments demonstrate that conformable derivatives yield stable, consistent agreement between analytic and numerical solutions, whereas Caputo dynamics require higher-order or series-anchored schemes to suppress discretization noise and maintain long-term accuracy. These results underscore the advantages of the conformable formalism in modeling dynamic phenomena with delay and memory, offering a tractable and physically interpretable alternative to integral-based fractional models.

### [45] [Dissipative Vortex Binaries in Compact Fluid Domains with Geometric Corrections](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23857)
*Aswathy K. R.,Rickmoy Samanta*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 本文研究双周期流体域中涡旋二元运动的耗散扩展，通过在保守系统中引入最小旋转速度（相互摩擦）项，将哈密顿演化转化为混合辛-梯度流。论文揭示了局部耗散二元系统的解析可解性，并展示了环面几何对涡旋对动力学（包括偶极子的有限时间坍缩、非对称对的非线性啁啾行为）产生的系统性修正。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解有限温度超流体动力学中由相互摩擦（mutual friction）引起的耗散对涡旋对运动的影响，特别是环面几何如何改变保守系统原有的可积结构和动力学行为。

Method: 从保守涡旋对系统的可积简化（单一复相对坐标）出发，引入最小旋转速度（mutual-friction）耗散项，将哈密顿演化转化为混合辛-梯度流（mixed symplectic–gradient flow）。在局部（planar limit）和环面（toroidal geometry）两种几何条件下分别进行解析求解和系统性修正分析。

Result: 同号等强度涡旋对表现出向外螺旋运动；等强度异号对（偶极子，dipole）在平面极限下发生有限时间坍缩。在环面上，偶极子取向不再守恒，几何诱导出缓慢的角漂移。对于不等强度异号对，耗散导致耦合的收缩与旋转，产生有限时间的非线性啁啾（chirp），其标度律为$\dotω\proptoω^2$，区别于电磁和引力旋近（inspiral）的$\dotω\propto ω^{3}$和$\dotω\propto ω^{11/3}$。

Conclusion: 这些结果突出了哈密顿结构（Hamiltonian structure）、耗散（dissipation）和几何（geometry）在周期流体系统中的相互耦合作用，揭示了环面几何对涡旋对动力学行为的关键修正效应。

Abstract: We study a dissipative extension of vortex-binary motion in a doubly periodic fluid domain. The underlying conservative system admits an exact integrable reduction to a single complex relative coordinate. Dissipation is introduced via a minimal rotated-velocity (mutual-friction) term, as motivated by finite-temperature superfluid dynamics, converting the Hamiltonian evolution into a mixed symplectic--gradient flow with monotonic energy decay for quantized vortices. In the local regime, the dissipative binary remains analytically solvable and admits closed-form solutions, with systematic corrections arising from the toroidal geometry. Equal same-sign vortices execute outward spiraling motion, while equal opposite-sign pairs (dipoles) undergo finite-time collapse in the planar limit. On the torus, however, the dipole orientation is no longer invariant: the geometry induces a slow angular drift, even in regimes where planar dynamics would preserve alignment. For unequal opposite-sign pairs, dissipation induces coupled contraction and rotation, leading to a finite-time nonlinear chirp characterized by $\dotω\proptoω^2$, in contrast with electromagnetic and gravitational inspirals where $\dotω\propto ω^{3}$ and $\dotω\propto ω^{11/3}$. These results highlight the interplay between Hamiltonian structure, dissipation, and geometry in periodic fluid systems.

### [46] [Synchronized molecular dynamics method for thin-layer flows of complex fluids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24138)
*Shugo Yasuda,Kotaro Oda,Fumito Muragaki,Yuta Taketa,Masashi Iwayama,Tomohide Ina*

Main category: physics.flu-dyn

TL;DR: 提出了一种用于复杂流体薄层流动的多尺度计算方法——同步分子动力学（SMD）方法，通过将局部分子动力学（MD）模拟与宏观润滑描述直接耦合，在无需预设本构关系或边界条件的情况下，高效获取横截面速度剖面和流向压力分布，并在Lennard-Jones流体和聚合物润滑流动中得到了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 复杂流体在薄层流动中涉及跨尺度的物理过程，传统方法需要预设本构关系或边界条件，难以准确捕捉界面效应与微观动力学耦合行为。因此，亟需一种既能高效处理宏观流动又能解析微观结构演变的多尺度模拟方法。

Method: SMD方法利用薄层流动中横截面动力学（受界面效应强烈影响）与流向传输之间的尺度分离，沿流向稀疏分布局部MD单元，并通过宏观守恒律（continuity equation）将其同步。通过迭代更新施加在每个MD单元上的外力来强制执行宏观连续性方程，从而在不预设本构关系或边界条件的情况下获得横截面速度剖面和流向压力分布。

Result: 在楔形通道中Lennard-Jones流体的压力驱动和壁面驱动流动中，SMD方法的结果与考虑了边界滑移的修正Reynolds方程高度吻合。在Kremer-Grest链模型模拟的聚合物润滑流动中，该方法在大压差下自然地捕捉到了显著的剪切稀化行为及与之耦合的微观聚合物构象动力学。

Conclusion: SMD方法为复杂流体薄层流动的多尺度模拟提供了一种高效且物理自洽的计算框架，能够在宏观流动与微观结构演变之间建立直接而一致的耦合。

Abstract: We propose a multiscale computational method for thin-layer flows of complex fluids, termed the synchronized molecular dynamics (SMD) method, which directly couples local molecular dynamics (MD) simulations with a macroscopic lubrication description. In thin layers, the flow can be decomposed into cross-sectional dynamics that are strongly influenced by interfacial effects, and streamwise transport along the channel. The SMD method exploits this separation of scales by sparsely distributing local MD cells along the channel and synchronizing them through macroscopic conservation laws.
  In this framework, the macroscopic continuity equation is enforced by iteratively updating the external forces applied to each MD cell, thereby allowing the cross-sectional velocity profiles and the streamwise pressure distribution to be obtained without prescribing constitutive relations or boundary conditions. The method is validated for pressure-driven and wall-driven flows of Lennard--Jones fluids in a wedge-shaped channel, demonstrating excellent agreement with a modified Reynolds equation that accounts for boundary slip.
  The SMD method is further applied to polymeric lubrication flows modeled by the Kremer--Grest chain model. At large pressure differences, the present approach naturally captures pronounced shear-thinning behavior coupled with microscopic polymer conformation dynamics. The results demonstrate that the SMD method provides an efficient and physically consistent framework for the multiscale simulation of complex fluid thin-layer flows.

</details>

### [47] [Efficient Generation of Neutrons Based on Ultrashort Laser-driven Direct Acceleration in Microwire-Array Targets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23913)
*Kaiyuan Feng,Debin Zou,Bo Cui,Shukai He,Yingzi Dai,Wei Qi,Jinlong Luo,Jie Feng,Xinyan Li,Zehao Chen,Lixiang Hu,Chengyu Qin,Guobo Zhang,Hui Zhang,Zhigang Deng,Xiaohu Yang,Fuqiu Shao,Liangliang Ji,Weiming Zhou,Tongpu Yu*

Main category: physics.plasm-ph

TL;DR: 该研究基于飞秒激光驱动微线阵列靶的直接激光加速，实验演示了高效中子产生，在约10²⁰ W/cm²中等强度下实现了高达8.33×10⁶ n/sr/J的中子产额，并通过模拟预测使用Be转换器可获得创纪录的3.67×10⁷ n/sr/J脉冲中子源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索基于直接激光加速（direct laser acceleration）的高效中子产生方案，寻找最优微线阵列周期以最大化质子能量与高能质子数目，并实现可在紧凑经济型激光系统上高重频运行的中子源。

Method: 采用超短飞秒激光脉冲（~25 fs）轰击微线阵列靶（microwire-array target），通过直接激光加速机制驱动质子，再经LiD转换器（converter）触发⁷Li(p,n)和D(p,n)³He核反应产生中子。实验与自洽集成模拟（self-consistent integrated simulations）相结合，并模拟Be转换器性能。

Result: 在1 PW、~25 fs激光及~10²⁰ W/cm²强度下，从LiD转换器测得高达(8.33±0.84)×10⁶ n/sr/J的中子产额；模拟预测相同激光条件下采用Be转换器可获得3.67×10⁷ n/sr/J的脉冲中子源产额。

Conclusion: 该脉冲中子源在单位焦耳下的产额优于现有方案，有利于在紧凑经济的激光系统中实现高重复率运行，适用于相关应用场景。

Abstract: We report on an experimental demonstration of efficient neutron generation based on direct laser acceleration in microwire-array targets irradiated by ultrashort (tens of femtoseconds) laser pulses. The optimal array period was identified, at which the maximum proton energy and the number of protons with energies exceeding $1~\mathrm{MeV}$ were significantly increased. Using a $1~\mathrm{PW}$, $\sim25~\mathrm{fs}$ laser at a moderate intensity of $\sim10^{20}~\mathrm{W/cm^2}$, a high neutron yield of up to $(8.33\pm0.84)\times10^{6}~\mathrm{n/sr/J}$ was detected from the LiD converter via $^7\mathrm{Li}(p,n)$ and $\mathrm{D}(p,n)^3\mathrm{He}$ nuclear reactions. Self-consistent integrated simulations reproduced the experimental results and predicted that with a Be converter, a forward pulsed neutron source with an unprecedented yield per joule of $3.67\times10^{7}~\mathrm{n/sr/J}$ can be obtained under identical laser conditions. This type of neutron source is favorable for applications that require a high repetition rate utilizing compact and economical laser systems.

### [48] [Constraints on the Primordial Black Hole Abundance using Pulsar Parameter Drifts](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22634)
*Yan-Chen Bi,Yu-Mei Wu,Qing-Guo Huang*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 该论文首次利用脉冲星参数漂移搜索原初黑洞（PBH）伴生的标量诱导引力波（SIGW），在95%置信水平上给出PBH丰度上限f_PBH < 10^{-10}（质量范围[0.3, 40000] M⊙），强烈排除LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA（LVK）观测到的双黑洞（BBH）起源于原初黑洞（PBH）的可能性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原初黑洞（primordial black holes, PBHs）为解释地面引力波（gravitational-wave, GW）探测器观测到的双黑洞（binary black holes, BBHs）提供了一个有说服力的解释，尤其是那些处于理论质量间隙（mass gap）中的双黑洞。然而，产生PBH所需的标量扰动（scalar perturbations）会不可避免地产生标量诱导引力波（scalar-induced GWs, SIGWs），后者可通过脉冲星参数漂移被观测到。

Method: 利用脉冲星自转周期的二阶导数（jerk-like drifts）来搜索SIGW信号，首次将该方法应用于PBH丰度的约束。

Result: 在95%置信水平上，给出PBH丰度上限f_PBH < 10^{-10}，质量范围覆盖[3 × 10^{-1}, 4 × 10^{4}] M⊙。

Conclusion: 该结果强烈不支持目前LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA（LVK）合作组探测到的双黑洞（BBHs）起源于原初黑洞（PBH）的假说。

Abstract: Primordial black holes (PBHs) provide a compelling interpretation for the binary black holes (BBHs) observed by ground-based gravitational-wave (GW) detectors, especially for those BBHs in the theoretical mass gap. In the early Universe, the scalar perturbations required to produce such PBHs inevitably generate scalar-induced GWs (SIGWs). These SIGWs peak in the sub-nanohertz band, and manifest secularly as measurable jerk-like drifts in the second derivative of pulsar spin periods. In this Letter, we perform the first search for SIGWs using pulsar parameter drifts, and place a 95\% confidence-level upper limit on the PBH abundance of $f_{\mathrm{PBH}} < 10^{-10}$ over the mass range $[3 \times 10^{-1}, 4 \times 10^{4}] M_{\odot}$. Our results strongly disfavor a PBH origin for the BBHs currently detected by the LIGO-Virgo-KAGRA (LVK) Collaborations.

### [49] [Cosmological evolution of interacting dark energy with a CPL equation of state](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22970)
*Gerald Neumann,Nelson Videla,Dorian Araya*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文在 Chevalier-Polarski-Linder (CPL) 参数化框架下研究相互作用暗能量模型，推导了包含不完全伽马函数的精确解析解，并通过贝叶斯分析和多种天文观测数据（OHD、SNIa、BAO、CMB）进行检验。结果表明，与暗能量密度成正比的相互作用项虽能适度改善拟合，但贝叶斯信息准则仍偏好 ΛCDM 模型；而与暗物质密度成正比的相互作用未获观测支持。该模型展现出暗能量状态方程从高红移的有效幻影（phantom）态向低红移的类精质（quintessence）态演化，并暗示未来可能存在暂态宇宙加速膨胀阶段。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准 ΛCDM 模型面临巧合问题（coincidence problem）等理论困境，而相互作用暗能量模型为缓解这些问题提供了可能路径。本文旨在 CPL 参数化框架下系统检验两种常见相互作用项的观测可行性，并揭示其解析结构中被数值分析忽略的数学特征。

Method: 采用两种相互作用项 Q = βHρ_de 和 Q = βHρ_c，在 CPL 参数化下推导暗区演化的精确解析解（涉及不完全伽马函数）。利用哈勃参数观测数据（OHD）、Ia 型超新星（SNIa）、重子声学振荡（BAO）和宇宙微波背景（CMB）数据，进行贝叶斯分析（Bayesian analysis），并采用赤池信息准则（AIC）和贝叶斯信息准则（BIC）进行模型比较。

Result: 与暗能量密度成正比的相互作用项（Q = βHρ_de）能适度改善观测拟合（AIC 指标），但 BIC 仍因模型复杂度惩罚而偏好 ΛCDM；与暗物质密度成正比的相互作用项（Q = βHρ_c）未获得观测支持。暗能量状态方程呈动态演化：高红移时为有效幻影（phantom）态，晚期转为类精质（quintessence）行为。模型暗示宇宙未来可能出现暂态加速阶段。

Conclusion: CPL 框架下的相互作用暗能量模型能在保持与当前观测一致的前提下，引入更丰富的现象学特征，拓展了标准宇宙学模型。不过，ΛCDM 仍是当前数据下更简约的首选模型。

Abstract: This paper examines interacting dark energy models within the Chevallier-Polarski-Linder (CPL) parametrization, emphasizing both theoretical structure and observational viability. Two commonly adopted interaction terms are considered: $Q = βH ρ_{de}$ and $Q = βH ρ_c$. We derive exact analytic solutions that describe how the dark sector evolves. These solutions involve incomplete gamma functions and reveal a non-trivial mathematical structure that is often missed in numerical analyses. We perform a Bayesian analysis using current cosmological observations, including the Hubble parameter (OHD), Type Ia supernovae (SNIa), baryon acoustic oscillations (BAO), and cosmic microwave background (CMB) data. Relative to the non-interacting CPL scenario, the interacting model with $Q = βH ρ_{de}$ yields a modestly improved fit, as indicated by the Akaike Information Criterion (AIC). However, the Bayesian Information Criterion (BIC) penalizes increased model complexity, leading to a continued preference for $Λ$CDM. In contrast, the interaction model that depends on dark matter density does not provide observational support. The preferred interacting scenario indicates that the dark energy equation of state evolves dynamically, transitioning from an effective phantom regime at high redshift to quintessence-like behavior at late times. Further analysis indicates the potential for a transient phase of cosmic acceleration in the future. These findings suggest that interacting dark energy models within the CPL framework enrich the standard cosmological model by introducing more diverse phenomenology while maintaining consistency with current observations.

</details>


### [50] [\texttt{SWIM}: Stochastic Warm Inflation Module to generate and analyse Warm Inflationary power spectrum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24654)
*Umang Kumar,Suratna Das*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文介绍SWIM（随机暖暴胀模块），一个用C++和Python编写的开源数值平台，可生成暖暴胀（Warm Inflation）标量功率谱（scalar power spectrum），集成Cobaya进行参数估计，利用机器学习加速MCMC分析，并提供完整的暖暴胀模型数值分析能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在暖暴胀范式中，标量功率谱的确定需要通过数值分析实现，且现有公开的MCMC代码（如COSMOMC或Cobaya）需要与暖暴胀模型结合。此外，半解析方法在某些情况下无法准确确定标量功率谱，因此需要全数值方案进行参数估计。

Method: SWIM通过数值求解暖暴胀的标准随机扰动方程（stochastic perturbation equations）而不作任何近似，采用机器学习技术加速MCMC分析中全数值功率谱的计算，从而显著降低计算成本。该模块支持任意形式的暴胀势（inflationary potential）和耗散系数（dissipative coefficient），并可半解析或全数值生成功率谱。

Result: 在多数情况下，SWIM在运行时（runtime）上优于其他仅提供半解析功率谱的暖暴胀数值代码。SWIM是目前唯一能处理需要全数值功率谱进行参数估计情况的代码。

Conclusion: SWIM为暖暴胀模型与当前宇宙学数据（如CMB数据）的对比分析提供了一个完整的数值平台，可系统地对任意暖暴胀模型进行检验。该模块已在GitHub上公开。

Abstract: Numerical analysis to determine the form of the scalar power spectrum in Warm Inflationary paradigm is inevitable. One further needs numerical techniques to analyse any Warm Inflation model with the current observational data through the MCMC codes that are available publicly, like COSMOMC or Cobaya. We present \texttt{SWIM} (Stochastic Warm Inflation Module) written in C++ and Python, that not only helps generate the Warm Inflationary scalar power spectrum, either semi-analytically or fully numerically, but also is integrated with Cobaya enabling the user to constrain the model parameters with current CMB data and thus to put any Warm Inflation model to test. \texttt{SWIM} numerically solves the standard stochastic perturbation equations of Warm Inflation without any approximations, uses machine learning techniques to speed up the MCMC analysis while analysing the fully numerical power spectrum that significantly reduces the computational cost, and is able to accommodate any Warm Inflation model with any form of inflationary potential and dissipative coefficient for numerical analysis. We show that \texttt{SWIM}, in most of the cases, outperforms other numerical codes on Warm Inflation that are designed to yield only the semi-analytical power spectrum as far as the runtimes are concerned. We further point out that there can be situations where the semi-analytical way of determining the scalar power spectrum in Warm Inflation can fall short, and one needs the full numerical power spectrum for parameter estimation given the observational data. In such cases, \texttt{SWIM} is the only code available so far that is designed to perform the task. Hence, \texttt{SWIM} offers a complete numerical platform for thorough analysis of Warm Inflation models against the current cosmological data. \texttt{SWIM} has been made publicly available at https://github.com/umg-kmr/SWIM.

</details>


### [51] [Parametric Resonance in $φ^4$ Preheating: An Exact Numerical Study](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23224)
*Hrisikesh Thakur,Malay K. Nandy*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过完全数值分析研究φ⁴混沌暴胀模型中再加热（preheating）阶段的参数共振（parametric resonance）结构，揭示了弱耦合、中等耦合和强耦合三种情形下短波模与长波模截然不同的共振行为，强调精确数值方法对捕捉再加热动力学的重要性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 再加热阶段通过参数共振机制实现高效粒子产生，但早期研究多采用近似解析处理，未能完整捕捉共振动力学细节。本文旨在通过全数值方法精确刻画φ⁴暴胀模型中参数共振的结构，避免近似方法的局限性。

Method: 对暴胀场（inflaton field）和产生粒子的模函数（mode function）所满足的耦合动力学方程组进行全数值求解（fully numerical analysis），不采用先前研究中常见的近似处理。

Result: 弱耦合下短波模快速稳定振荡、占据数（occupation number）趋于饱和，长波模振幅渐进增长并进入非线性振荡；耦合增强后动力学趋于非线性并出现随机行为（stochastic behavior）；强耦合下短波模占据数呈阶梯状（step-like/staircase）演化，长波模则呈现单调增长叠加小幅度涨落。

Conclusion: φ⁴暴胀模型的参数共振结构表现出丰富的耦合依赖性，不同波段的模函数演化特征差异显著，精确数值处理对于准确捕捉再加热动力学必不可少。

Abstract: Preheating after inflation proceeds through parametric resonance, leading to efficient particle production in scalar field models. In this work, we investigate the structure of parametric resonance in the $φ^4$ chaotic inflationary model during the preheating phase by performing a fully numerical analysis of the coupled dynamical equations governing the inflaton field and the mode function of the produced particles, thereby avoiding the approximations commonly employed in earlier studies. Our results reveal resonance patterns that differ significantly from those obtained with approximate analytical treatments. In the weak coupling regime, short-wavelength modes rapidly settle into oscillations with nearly constant amplitude, while the corresponding occupation numbers approach saturation. However, the long-wavelength modes exhibit gradual amplitude growth, with occupation numbers transitioning into a non-linear oscillatory regime. As the coupling strength increases, the dynamics becomes increasingly nonlinear, leading to the emergence of stochastic behavior. In the strong coupling regime, short-wavelength modes display a step-like (staircase) evolution in the occupation number, indicative of intermittent bursts of particle production. However, the long-wavelength modes exhibit a more gradual, monotonic growth with small superimposed fluctuations. These findings highlight the rich, coupling-dependent, structure of parametric resonance in the quartic inflationary model and underscore the importance of exact numerical treatment in accurately capturing preheating dynamics.

</details>


### [52] [Testing Scalar Field Dark Matter models in M31 galaxy through the Rotation Curve analysis](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23353)
*Gulnara Suliyeva,Kuantay Boshkayev,Talgar Konysbayev,Yergali Kurmanov,Guldana Rabigulova*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文通过分析仙女座星系（M31）的旋转曲线，检验了标量场暗物质晕模型的可行性。研究发现双核球重子结构能更好描述M31旋转曲线，且在标量场暗物质模型中，具有平滑核的暗物质晕（如模糊暗物质FDM）对M31运动学描述最为一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验标量场暗物质晕（scalar field dark matter halo）模型在真实星系中的可行性，通过M31的旋转曲线分析，并纳入实际的重子物质结构描述，以评估不同暗物质模型与观测数据的符合程度。

Method: 重子质量模型包括由一个Freeman轮廓描述的恒星盘（stellar disk）和两种核球（bulge）结构：经典的单de Vaucouleurs核球以及由指数球轮廓（exponential sphere profiles）建模的内核球与主核球的两分量结构。暗物质晕采用三种标量场驱动模型：模糊暗物质（FDM）、玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚态（Bose-Einstein condensate）和多态标量场暗物质（multistate scalar-field dark matter）。模型参数通过Levenberg-Marquardt非线性最小二乘法拟合确定，并使用贝叶斯信息准则（Bayesian Information Criterion）评估模型相对表现。

Result: 双核球重子结构配置无论采用何种暗物质晕模型，均能对M31旋转曲线提供更优的统计描述。在标量场暗物质模型中，具有平滑核（smooth cored）的暗物质晕（如FDM）对M31运动学描述最为一致。

Conclusion: 研究支持双核球重子结构在描述M31旋转曲线中的优越性，并指出在标量场暗物质框架下，平滑核类模型（如FDM）是当前最符合M31运动学数据的选择。

Abstract: We explore the viability of scalar field dark matter halo models through the rotation curve analysis of the Andromeda galaxy (M31), taking into account a realistic description of its baryonic structure. The mass model includes a stellar disk described by the Freeman profile and two alternative bulge configurations: a classical single de Vaucouleurs bulge and a two-component structure consisting of inner and main bulges modeled by exponential sphere profiles. The dark matter halo is modeled using three scalar field motivated models: fuzzy dark matter (FDM), Bose-Einstein condensate and multistate scalar-field dark matter. The model parameters are determined through the Levenberg-Marquardt nonlinear least-squares fitting, and the relative performance of the models is evaluated using the Bayesian Information Criterion which allows a direct comparison with previous phenomenological halo studies performed for the same galaxy. We find that the two-bulge baryonic configuration ensures a better statistical description of the M31 rotation curve, independently of the adopted halo model. The results also suggest that, within scalar field dark matter scenarios, smooth cored halos, such as FDM, provide the most consistent description of the M31 kinematics.

</details>


### [53] [STVG-MOG Cluster Dynamics and the Cosmological $1/r^2$ Force Law from Pairwise kSZ Data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23440)
*John W. Moffat*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文检验了标量-张量-矢量引力（STVG-MOG）的弱场修正引力形式能否解释从运动学Sunyaev-Zeldovich（kSZ）效应测量中推断出的星系团尺度反平方力定律。研究表明，基于X-COP星系团拟合的参数外推至30–230 Mpc尺度后，STVG-MOG的加速度律简化为有效反平方形式，预测的成对速度曲线与观测数据一致，证明该理论在星系团和宇宙学尺度上具有自洽性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 检验标量-张量-矢量引力（Scalar-Tensor-Vector Gravity, STVG-MOG）在弱场修正引力形式下，能否复现近期运动学Sunyaev-Zeldovich（kSZ）测量所推断的星系团尺度反平方力定律，从而评估该理论在无需暗物质（dark matter）情况下的跨尺度自洽性。

Method: 以X-COP星系团对STVG-MOG的拟合结果为起点（代表性重子星系团质量 M∼10¹⁵M⊙，参数 α∼9.11 和 μ∼0.196 Mpc⁻¹），将拟合外推至成对kSZ分析相关的分离尺度范围30至230 Mpc。由于汤川（Yukawa）过渡长度 μ⁻¹≃5.1 Mpc远小于该分离尺度，STVG-MOG加速度律简化为有效反平方形式；在此基础上推导对应的成对速度曲线，并拟合单个整体kSZ振幅。

Result: 外推后的STVG-MOG预测能够复现成对kSZ数据的测量趋势，表明X-COP星系团拟合与宇宙学尺度上的kSZ力律结果在STVG-MOG框架内具有相互自洽性（mutual consistency）。

Conclusion: STVG-MOG理论能够在星系团尺度上成功描述动力学而不需要粒子暗物质，同时其弱场形式在更大尺度上自动退化为符合观测的牛顿反平方律，不同于MOND（Modified Newtonian Dynamics）类理论的长程修正行为，展现出跨尺度的自洽解释能力。

Abstract: We investigate whether Scalar-Tensor-Vector Gravity in its weak-field modified gravity form can account for the cluster-scale inverse-square force law inferred from recent kinematic Sunyaev-Zeldovich measurements of cluster pairwise motions. The starting point is the X-COP cluster fit of STVG-MOG, for which a representative baryonic cluster mass $M\sim 10^{15}M_\odot$ together with parameters $α\sim 9.11$ and $μ\sim 0.196~{\rm Mpc}^{-1}$ provides a successful description of cluster dynamics without particle dark matter. We extrapolate this fit to the separation range $30$ to $230~{\rm Mpc}$, relevant for the pairwise kSZ analysis. Since the Yukawa transition length $μ^{-1}\simeq 5.1~{\rm Mpc}$ is much smaller than these separations, the STVG-MOG acceleration law reduces to an effective inverse-square form. This explains why the theory can satisfy the observed Newtonian behavior while remaining distinct from MOND-like long-distance modifications. We derive the corresponding pairwise velocity curve and show that, after fitting a single overall kSZ amplitude, the extrapolated STVG-MOG prediction reproduces the measured trend of the pairwise kSZ data. The analysis shows that the X-COP cluster fit and the cosmological-scale kSZ force-law result are mutually consistent within STVG-MOG.

</details>


### [54] [Reconstructing the cosmic expansion with a generalized q(z) parameterization: A decelerating Universe from late-time constraints](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23992)
*Tomás Verdugo,Alberto Hernández-Almada,Miguel A. García-Aspeitia,Juan Magaña,Verónica Motta*

Main category: astro-ph.CO

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种推广的减速参数 $q(z)$ 唯象参数化方案，通过引入有效辐射成分（ERC）来调控高红移行为，并利用宇宙计时仪、Pantheon+ Ia型超新星、HII星系和中等光度类星体等低-中红移观测数据对参数进行约束，发现当前宇宙在 $z_T \simeq 0.80$ 发生减速-加速转变，且晚时加速可能弱于 $\Lambda$CDM 模型预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有两参数 $q(z)$ 重建方案在高红移区域的行为缺乏明确调控，因此需要一种能够同时保持晚时转变动力学（transition dynamics）并规范高红移行为的推广参数化框架。

Method: 提出一种包含有效辐射成分（effective radiative component, ERC）和局域晚时贡献的广义唯象参数化方案，对减速参数 $q(z)$ 进行建模；利用宇宙计时仪（cosmic chronometers, CC）、Pantheon+ Ia型超新星（Type Ia supernovae, SNIa）、HII星系（HIIG）和中等光度类星体（QSO）四种晚时观测数据对自由参数 $(h, q_0, z_c, z_e)$ 进行约束。

Result: 基于完整数据组合（CC+SNIa+HIIG+QSO）得到 $q_0 = -0.25^{+0.04}_{-0.04}$，转变红移 $z_T \simeq 0.80$，表明当前宇宙处于加速膨胀且转变早于 $\Lambda$CDM 模型；哈勃参数 $h = 0.729 \pm 0.006$；ERC 受晚时数据约束较弱；重建的 $q(z)$ 在数据探测红移范围内偏离 $\Lambda$CDM 趋势，暗示晚时加速可能减弱。

Conclusion: 在观测红移区间内，新参数化方案有效复现了以往方案中的晚时行为，同时提供了向早期红移的可控扩展；当前低-中红移数据与晚时加速减弱的图像相容。

Abstract: We present a generalized phenomenological parameterization of the deceleration parameter $q(z)$ that incorporates an effective radiative component (ERC) in addition to a localized late-time contribution. The proposed framework extends previous two-parameter $q(z)$ reconstructions by explicitly regulating the high-redshift behavior while preserving the late-time transition dynamics. We constrain the free parameters $(h, q_0, z_c, z_e)$ using late-time observational data from cosmic chronometers (CC), Pantheon+ Type Ia supernovae (SNIa), H\,\textsc{ii} galaxies (HIIG), and intermediate-luminosity quasars (QSO). For the full data combination (CC+SNIa+HIIG+QSO), we obtain $q_0 = -0.25^{+0.04}_{-0.04}$ and a transition redshift $z_T \simeq 0.80$, indicating a currently accelerating Universe with a transition occurring earlier than in the $Λ$CDM model. Within the redshift range probed by the data, the reconstructed $q(z)$ deviates from the $Λ$CDM trend, suggesting a possible reduction of the late-time acceleration. Furthermore, the reconstruction favors a relatively high value of the Hubble parameter, $h = 0.729 \pm 0.006$. The ERC remains weakly constrained by late-time data but ensures a smooth and monotonic evolution of $q(z)$, $j(z)$, and $w_{\rm eff}(z)$ across a wide redshift range. Within the observed interval, the model effectively reproduces the late-time behavior of the previous parametrization, while providing a controlled extension toward early epochs. Our results show that current low- and intermediate-redshift data are compatible with a reduced late-time acceleration.

</details>

### [55] [Delocalization transition for light in two dimensions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22919)
*Sébastien Lucas,Christian Miniatura,Sergey E. Skipetrov*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文预测，在二维平行板波导中，由双能级原子（two-level atoms）随机散射的光波会发生局域化-退局域化相变（localization-delocalization transition），突破了传统认为二维体系中任意弱无序必然导致所有本征模空间局域化的认知。该相变由原子间的近场偶极-偶极相互作用（near-field dipole-dipole interactions）驱动，当面数密度（areal number density）超过某一临界值时发生，有限尺寸标度分析给出临界指数 ν = 1.4 ± 0.2。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有实验和普遍认知认为，在二维（2D）波动传播中，任意弱的无序都会导致标量波方程本征模的空间局域化。本文旨在挑战这一传统信念，探索在特定光子系统中是否存在局域化-退局域化相变的可能性。

Method: 研究采用有限尺寸标度分析（finite-size scaling analysis）方法，对随机分布在二维平行板波导中平面内的双能级原子所构成的光散射系统进行理论分析，评估随原子面数密度增加时系统行为的标度律，并提取相变的临界指数。

Result: 结果表明，局域化-退局域化相变确实存在，转变发生在原子面数密度超过某一临界值时。有限尺寸标度分析给出了该相变的临界指数（critical exponent）ν = 1.4 ± 0.2。

Conclusion: 该发现推翻了二维体系中任意弱无序必然导致空间局域化的传统观点，揭示了近场偶极-偶极相互作用在驱动局域化-退局域化相变中的关键作用，为二维无序光子系统的理论理解提供了新的视角。

Abstract: Common belief, confirmed by existing experiments, is that arbitrarily weak disorder should lead to spatial localization of eigenmodes of scalar wave equations when wave propagation is two-dimensional (2D). We predict that contrary to this belief, a localization-delocalization transition can take place for light scattered by two-level atoms placed at random positions in the middle plane of a parallel-plate 2D waveguide fed by its fundamental transverse-magnetic (TM) mode (electric field polarized perpendicular to the waveguide and atomic planes). This transition, driven by near-field dipole-dipole interactions between atoms, occurs upon increasing the areal number density of atoms beyond some critical value. A finite-size scaling analysis of the transition yields an estimate of its critical exponent $ν$ = 1.4 $\pm$ 0.2.

### [56] [Motifs Enrichment as a Driver of an Emergent Preferential Attachment in rewired random regular graphs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23152)
*Pawat Akara-pipattana,Sergei Nechaev*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文在正则系综（canonical ensemble）框架下研究重连随机正则图（rewired random regular graphs）的统计性质，其中三角形平均数量由逸度（fugacity）λ控制。通过平均场（mean-field）论证，估计了相变点λ⁻的位置，并重点分析了λ⁻以上的富三角形相（triangle-enriched phase），发现该相中图结构呈现松散连接的簇网络，具有无标度（scale-free）特性和幂律度分布P(d) ∼ d⁻^γ（γ ≈ 2），将此归因于“涌现优先连接（emergent preferential attachment）”机制，并推测簇间三角形的典型拓扑与共形不变势中的Efimov态之间存在可能的联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究重连随机正则图在正则系综下的统计行为，特别是当三角形密度受逸度λ控制时，图结构如何从随机相（random phase）向富三角形相（triangle-enriched phase）转变。

Method: 采用正则系综框架，引入逸度λ来控制图中三角形的平均数量；运用平均场（mean-field）论证来估计相变点λ⁻的位置，并分析富三角形相中的图统计性质。

Result: 在λ⁻以上的富三角形相中，图呈现松散连接的簇网络结构（loosely connected web of clusters），该簇间网络具有无标度（scale-free）特性，顶点度分布服从幂律（power-law）P(d) ∼ d⁻^γ，且指数γ ≈ 2不依赖于图的大小和度。

Conclusion: 该无标度行为源于三角形模体（triangle motifs）的“涌现优先连接”（emergent preferential attachment）机制，并通过平均场方法推导出指数γ；此外，推测簇间三角形的典型拓扑与共形不变势（conformally invariant potential）中的Efimov态（Efimov states）可能存在联系。

Abstract: We study the statistics of rewired random regular graphs within the canonical ensemble, in which the average number of triangles is controlled by the fugacity $λ$. Using mean-field arguments, we estimate the location of the transition point $λ^{-}$. We focus primarily on the triangle-enriched phase above $λ^{-}$, where the graph becomes a loosely connected web of clusters. This inter-cluster network is scale-free and exhibits a power-law vertex degree distribution $P(d) \sim d^{-γ}$, with $γ\approx 2$ independent of degree and size of the graph. We attribute this behavior to an "emergent preferential attachment" for triangle motifs, derive the exponent $γ$ with a mean-field approach, and speculate on a possible connection between the typical topology of inter-cluster triangles and Efimov states in a conformally invariant potential.

Method: 通过测量不同厚度Co70Zr30层的磁矩和序化温度，分析有限尺寸效应；结合界面区域磁相互作用减弱的假设进行数据解释，并利用Griffiths相的概念解释临界区附近的磁行为。

Result: 发现磁性薄膜的磁矩和序化温度均表现出显著的有限尺寸效应；界面上存在约1 nm厚的磁相互作用和磁矩减弱的区域。

Conclusion: Co70Zr30薄膜中的有限尺寸效应可归因于界面区域的磁性减弱，且Griffiths相为理解临界点附近的磁性质提供了理论框架。

Abstract: Profound finite size effects are observed in both the moment and ordering temperature in thin Co$_{70}$Zr$_{30}$ layers. The results are consistent with the presence of interface regions with reduced magnetic interactions and moment. The extension of this region is determined to be around 1 nm thick at each interface. Above and near the apparent critical temperature, the magnetic properties can be understood in terms of Griffith phases.

### [58] [Physics-Informed Deep Image Prior Reconstruction of In-Plane Magnetization from Scanning NV Magnetometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23431)
*Zander Scholl,Justin Woods,Charudatta Phatak,Hanu Arava*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于物理信息的深度图像先验（physics-informed deep image prior, DIP）框架，仅利用简单的卷积自编码器，从扫描氮-空位（NV）磁力测量数据中实现纳米尺度薄膜复杂面内磁化模式的重建，无需预训练数据集且计算成本低于监督学习方法。研究发现用户自定义掩模的取向对收敛性有显著影响，最优取向可将重建信噪比提升至多3分贝（decibel, dB）。该方法结合实验引导的空间约束，分析了光刻图案化坡莫合金（Permalloy）纳米结构中的朗道（Landau）和偶极（dipole）畴结构，并通过磁力显微镜（magnetic force microscopy）测量进行了验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 纳米尺度磁性薄膜的磁化重建对下一代存储器、传感器及自旋电子学技术至关重要，但由于杂散场逆问题（stray field inverse problem）的不适定性（ill-posed nature），即给定杂散场分布对应无穷多个磁化解，导致重建极其困难。

Method: 采用物理信息深度图像先验（physics-informed DIP）框架，以简单卷积自编码器（convolutional autoencoder）为核心；通过用户定义掩模（user-defined mask）限制重建解空间，并结合实验引导的空间约束（experimentally-guided spatial constraints）分析朗道（Landau）和偶极（dipole）畴结构；无需预训练数据集，计算强度低于监督学习方法。

Result: 该方法可以从扫描NV磁力测量数据中实现复杂面内磁化模式的定性与定量重建；掩模取向显著影响收敛性，最佳对齐可将重建信噪比（signal-to-noise ratio）提升至多3分贝（dB）；成功分析了光刻图案化坡莫合金（Permalloy）纳米结构中的Landau和dipole畴结构。

Conclusion: 物理信息DIP框架为纳米尺度磁化重建提供了一种无需预训练数据且计算高效的替代方案；掩模取向优化可作为诊断工具；互补磁力显微镜（magnetic force microscopy）测量支持了扫描NV测量结果的可靠性。

Abstract: Reconstructing magnetization in nanoscale magnetic thin films is essential for developing next-generation memory, sensors, and various spintronic technologies. However, this remains challenging due to the ill-posed nature of the stray field inverse problem, i.e., there are infinitely many magnetization solutions to a given stray field distribution. Here, we demonstrate that a physics-informed deep image prior (DIP) framework, using a simple convolutional autoencoder conditionally achieves a reasonable qualitative and quantitative reconstruction of complex in-plane magnetization patterns from scanning NV magnetometry. We find that the orientation of user-defined masks implemented to restrict the reconstruction solution space dramatically affects convergence. The optimal alignment of the mask improves the reconstruction signal-to-noise ratio by up to $\SI{3}{\decibel}$, thereby also serving as a diagnostic tool. The DIP approach requires no pre-trained datasets and is considered computationally less intensive as compared to supervised learning approaches. We analyze both Landau and dipole domain structures in lithographically patterned Permalloy nanostructures by incorporating experimentally-guided spatial constraints. Complementary magnetic force microscopy measurements were carried out to support the Scanning NV measurements.

</details>


### [59] [Linear equivalence of nonlinear recurrent neural networks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23489)
*David G. Clark*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文利用双站点空穴法（two-site cavity method）推导了随机耦合大非线性循环神经网络（recurrent neural networks）中协方差矩阵（covariance matrix）的解析形式，证明了其等价于相同耦合的线性网络在独立噪声驱动下的协方差结构，并通过数值验证了该结论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 大非线性循环神经网络中随机耦合产生的高维混沌活动结构对神经科学、机器学习、生态学等领域具有重要意义，而协方差矩阵是编码群体活动结构的基本对象。此前对该协方差矩阵的分析仅停留在低维汇总统计量，未能刻画特定耦合实现下的全高维结构，因此需要发展新的理论方法。

Method: 采用双站点空穴法（two-site cavity method）给出两种推导：第一种将每个单元的活动分解为线性分量和非线性残差（residual），证明不同位点残差间的互协方差被强烈抑制，残差在等效线性网络中表现为独立噪声；第二种写出协方差矩阵的自洽矩阵方程，朴素高斯闭合（Gaussian closure）给出错误结果，而空穴法通过分离高斯贡献与非高斯贡献得到正确方程。

Result: 推导证明了对此前提出的ansatz——典型淬火（quenched）实现下的大N协方差矩阵与相同耦合的线性网络在独立噪声驱动下的协方差形式一致，其中均值场序参量（mean-field order parameters）决定了有效传递函数和噪声谱——并通过一系列网络规模的数值模拟验证了理论预测。

Conclusion: 该结果将线性等价性（linear equivalence）从前馈高维非线性系统（权重与输入独立）扩展到了循环网络（活动依赖于产生它们的同一组耦合），为理解循环网络中的高维集体动力学提供了理论基础。

Abstract: Large nonlinear recurrent neural networks with random couplings generate high-dimensional, potentially chaotic activity whose structure is of interest in neuroscience, machine learning, ecology, and other fields. A fundamental object encoding the collective structure of this activity is the $N \times N$ covariance matrix. Prior analytical work on the covariance matrix has been limited to low-dimensional summary statistics, not the full high-dimensional object for a specific realization of the couplings. Recent work proposed an ansatz in which, at large $N$, the covariance matrix for a typical quenched realization takes the same form as that of a linear network with the same couplings, driven by independent noise, with mean-field order parameters setting the effective transfer function and the noise spectrum. Here, we derive this ansatz using the two-site cavity method, providing two distinct derivations that offer complementary perspectives. The first decomposes each unit's activity into a linear component and a nonlinear residual, and shows that cross-covariances between residuals at distinct sites are strongly suppressed, so that residuals act as independent noise within a linear network. The second writes a self-consistent matrix equation for the covariance matrix. A naive Gaussian closure for the joint statistics of activity at distinct sites gives the wrong equation; the cavity method separates Gaussian and non-Gaussian contributions, which enter at the same order, and produces the correct one. We verify the predictions numerically across a range of network sizes. These results extend linear equivalence from feedforward high-dimensional nonlinear systems, where the weights being analyzed are independent of their inputs, to recurrent networks, where the activities depend on the same couplings that generate them.

</details>


### [60] [Solution of a large nonlinear recurrent neural network at fixed connectivity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24141)
*Albert J. Wakhloo*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本文在大N极限下计算了非线性随机循环神经网络（nonlinear random recurrent neural network）的矩（moments）与响应函数（response functions），无需对突触权重进行平均，并推导出一般强度级关联函数（intensive-order correlation functions）的1/√N展开的首个非平凡项，从而作为特例证明了Shen和Hu近期提出的一个猜想。研究结果建立了突触连接、自发活动中的相关性以及网络对小扰动的响应之间的解析联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有方法通常需要对突触权重进行平均处理，且缺乏对自发活动相关性（correlations in spontaneous activity）与网络响应之间关系的解析理解。本文旨在绕过权重平均，直接在大N极限下分析非线性随机循环神经网络的关联函数，以提供更精确的理论工具。

Method: 采用大N极限下的分析方法，不依赖突触权重的平均化处理；通过对一般强度级关联函数进行1/√N展开（1/√N expansion），计算其首个非平凡项，从而导出网络的矩和响应函数。

Result: 首次给出了强度级关联函数在1/√N展开中的非平凡项，并作为特例证实了Shen和Hu的猜想；建立了突触连接、自发活动相关性及网络响应之间的解析关系。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一种无需权重平均即可分析非线性随机循环网络关联结构的理论框架，为理解神经网络中突触连接、自发活动与扰动响应之间的相互作用奠定了解析基础。

Abstract: We calculate the moments and response functions of a nonlinear random recurrent neural network in the large $N$ limit. Our approach does not require averaging over synaptic weights and gives the first nontrivial term in a $1/\sqrt{N}$ expansion of general intensive-order correlation functions, proving a recent conjecture by Shen and Hu as a special case. Our results provide an analytical link between synaptic connectivity, correlations in spontaneous activity, and the response of a network to small perturbations.

</details>


### [61] [Electrical conductivity of crack-template-based transparent conducting films: mean-field approximation, effective medium theory, and simulation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24211)
*Yuri Yu. Tarasevich,Andrei V. Esrkepov,Irina V. Vodolazskaya*

Main category: cond-mat.dis-nn

TL;DR: 本研究以泊松-沃罗诺伊图（Poisson–Voronoi diagram）的边缘网络模拟裂纹模板透明导电膜，对比原始网络（电导与边长成反比）与有效网络（基于有效介质理论（effective medium theory）赋予均匀电导），发现平均场近似（mean field approximation）会高估电导率，且对层级裂纹等非均匀体系可能导致显著误差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 针对裂纹模板透明导电膜（crack-template-based transparent conducting films）这一特殊导电网络结构，传统平均场近似（mean field approximation）和有效介质理论（effective medium theory）在其电导率预测中的适用性尚不明确，尤其当裂纹宽度不均（hierarchical cracks with variable width）时可能存在系统性偏差。

Method: 将裂纹模板导电膜建模为二维泊松-沃罗诺伊图（Poisson–Voronoi diagram）的边缘网络。设定原始网络（original network）中每条边的电导与其长度成反比；有效网络（effective network）中所有边具有基于有效介质理论（effective medium theory）得到的相同电导。采用平均场近似（mean field approximation）解析评估电导率，并辅以泊松-沃罗诺伊图上的直接数值计算进行验证。此外，研究了具有对应电导分布的六边形网络（hexagonal network）。

Result: 直接数值计算表明，平均场近似（mean field approximation）高估了原始网络（original network）电导率约13%，高估了有效网络（effective network）电导率约79%。对于六边形网络（hexagonal network），有效介质理论（effective medium theory）的预测比泊松-沃罗诺伊图（Poisson–Voronoi diagram）更准确，该差异归因于六边形周期晶格（periodic hexagonal lattice）更高的结构均匀性。

Conclusion: 在模拟裂纹模板透明导电膜（crack-template-based transparent conducting films）时，特别是当存在层级裂纹（hierarchical cracks）且裂纹宽度可变（电阻不再与长度成正比）的情况下，直接应用平均场近似（mean field approximation）可能导致显著误差。

Abstract: In our work, crack-template-based transparent conducting films were modeled as networks corresponding to the edges of a two-dimensional Poisson--Voronoi diagram. Two types of networks were considered: the original one, in which the conductivity of each edge was inversely proportional to its length, and the effective one, where all edges had the same conductivity obtained from the effective medium theory. The mean field approximation was used for analytical evaluation of the electrical conductivity. Direct numerical calculations for the Poisson--Voronoi diagram showed that the mean field approximation overestimated the conductivity of the original network by approximately 13\%, and of the effective network by 79\%. In addition, a hexagonal network with an edge conductivity distribution corresponding to the Poisson--Voronoi diagram was studied: for it, the predictions of the effective medium theory turned out to be more accurate than for the Poisson--Voronoi diagram, which was explained by the greater structural homogeneity of the periodic hexagonal lattice. Our results showed that when modeling crack-template-based transparent conducting films, especially in the case of hierarchical cracks with variable width (where the resistance was not simply proportional to the length), the application of the mean field approximation could potentially lead to significant errors.

### [62] [Generalized Aubry-André formula and continuity of the intersection spectrum of the Almost Mathieu operator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23852)
*Anton Gorodetski,Victor Kleptsyn*

Main category: math.SP

TL;DR: 本文研究了几乎马蒂厄算子（Almost Mathieu Operator, AMO）的交集谱上勒贝格测度（Lebesgue measure）的矩，证明其是耦合常数λ的多项式，系数为频率α的三角多项式；进而证明该测度在弱星拓扑下连续依赖参数，且在λ上解析、在α上无穷可微。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 推广Aubry-André关于AMO谱测度的经典公式，并系统研究谱测度对频率α和耦合λ的依赖性质（连续性、解析性与光滑性）。

Method: 通过分析交集谱上勒贝格测度的矩，将矩表示为λ的多项式，其系数为α的三角多项式；进而利用矩的解析性推导测度在弱星拓扑下的参数依赖性质。

Result: 交集谱的勒贝格测度μ⁻_{α,λ}在弱星拓扑下连续依赖于α和λ；且对解析测试函数的积分在λ上解析、在α上C^∞光滑；作为推论，两个能隙之间谱的勒贝格测度在λ上解析、在α上C^∞光滑（在能隙不分叉的开区域内，远离临界耦合λ=1）。

Conclusion: 证明了AMO谱测度具有比已知结果更精细的解析与光滑参数依赖结构，为理解准周期算子的谱性质提供了新的分析工具。

Abstract: We consider the spectrum of the Almost Mathieu operator (AMO) and show that the moments of the restriction of the Lebesgue measure to the intersection spectrum $\text{Leb}|_{Σ_{α,λ}}$ are polynomials in coupling $λ$ with coefficients that are trigonometric polynomials in frequency $α$. The statement can be considered as a generalization of the Aubry-André formula for the measure of the spectrum of AMO. As a corollary, we obtain that the restriction of the Lebesgue measure to the intersection spectrum that we denote by $μ^{-}_{α, λ}$ depends continuously on the parameters (frequency $α$ and coupling $λ$) in weak-* topology.
  Moreover, we prove that the dependence is not just continuous but analytic in $λ$ and $C^{\infty}$ in $α$ in a sense that an integral of an analytic test function $\varphi(x)$ with respect to $μ^{-}_{α, λ}$ has the same kind of dependence. In particular, this implies that the Lebesgue measure of the part of the spectrum $Σ_{α,λ}$ that lies between two gaps depends analytically on the coupling constant $λ$ and $C^{\infty}$ on the frequency $α$ in an open domain (away from the critical coupling $λ=1$) where these gaps do not bifurcate.

</details>

### [63] [Enabling users to work sustainably on shared institute computing resources](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22799)
*Niclas Eich,Johannes Erdmann,Martin Erdmann,Benjamin Fischer,Paul Gilles,Tim Hauptreif,Jan Kelleter*

Main category: cs.HC

TL;DR: VISPA项目通过用户中心措施（user-centric measures）——包括作业级能耗监测、绿色窗口调度、个人碳足迹报告和自愿参与机制——在一栋1970年代建筑中的中型计算集群上实现可持续性，旨在通过提升资源意识来中长期减少温室气体排放。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: VISPA计算集群位于一栋1970年代的研究所建筑内，翻新改造空间有限，传统能效升级仅能带来微小的节能效果。因此，项目旨在通过技术与行为相结合的用户中心方法，在不依赖硬件改造的前提下实现可持续性目标。

Method: 方法包括：(1) 部署监控系统，记录每个作业（per-job）的能耗；(2) 利用德国电网可再生能源占比的实时数据，实现“绿色窗口调度（green-window scheduling）”；(3) 向用户提供个人能耗与碳足迹查询、每周报告，以及按项目标记作业（tag jobs）进行汇总核算；(4) 利用历史运行的内存记录避免资源过度申请（oversubscription）。所有选项均为自愿参与，不强制执行。

Result: 建立了模拟框架（simulation framework）以评估上述措施的潜在影响。系统已实现作业级能耗记录、用户能耗与碳足迹报告，以及基于绿色电力的调度提示等功能。

Conclusion: 通过技术监测与自愿行为改变相结合，VISPA项目旨在中长期减少温室气体排放（greenhouse-gas emissions），推动科学社区内的资源意识文化转变。

Abstract: The VISPA project is a self-managed, mid-scale computing cluster that supports physics data analysis in research and teaching. Because the cluster is housed in a 1970s institute building with limited retrofit options, conventional efficiency upgrades would yield only minor energy savings. We therefore target sustainability primarily through user-centric measures. A monitoring system now records per-job energy consumption, while real-time data on the renewable share of the German power grid enable `green-window' scheduling. Users can query their individual energy consumption and carbon footprints, receive weekly reports, and tag jobs by project for aggregate accounting; memory records from previous runs help avoid oversubscription. All options are voluntary, fostering a cultural shift rather than imposing hard constraints. A simulation framework evaluates the potential impact of these measures. Together, the technological and behavioral interventions aim at medium- to long-term reductions in greenhouse-gas emissions by increasing resource awareness within the scientific community.

### [64] [Dynamical stability and multifunctional properties of Ni2+/Pr3+ co-doped CsPbCl3 perovskite: insights from first-principles lattice dynamics and carrier transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22874)
*Sikander Azam,Asif Zaman,Qaiser Rafiq,Amin Ur Rahman,Saleem Ayaz Khan*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文采用基于FP-LAPW方法的第一性原理密度泛函理论（DFT），系统研究了Ni²⁺/Pr³⁺共掺杂对CsPbCl₃钙钛矿的稳定性、电子结构、光学性质及输运性能的影响。结果表明，共掺杂能稳定晶格、抑制缺陷形成、降低有效质量、红移光吸收并提高载流子迁移率，整体上改善了材料的光电性能。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 全无机卤化物钙钛矿（all inorganic halide perovskites）具有低成本的光电性能优势，但其结构软性和热不稳定性限制了实际应用，亟需寻找有效的掺杂策略来提升其稳定性与光电性能。

Method: 采用基于全势线性缀加平面波（FP-LAPW）方法的密度泛函理论（Density Functional Theory, DFT），借助WIEN2k软件包对Ni²⁺/Pr³⁺共掺杂CsPbCl₃体系进行第一性原理计算。

Result: Ni²⁺占据B位替代Pb²⁺，Pr³⁺占据A位替代Cs⁺，保持电荷平衡；共掺杂稳定了晶格，提高了卤素和金属空位的形成能，降低了带隙中的深能级缺陷态；声子色散证实体系保持动力学稳定，共掺杂抑制低能振动并导致3–5 THz范围出现模分裂，增强了声子散射并降低了晶格热导率；弹性常数和体模量升高，延展性不变；电子结构显示Ni-3d和Pr-4f态出现在带边，降低了有效载流子质量并钝化了空位态；光学吸收发生红移，高频介电常数ε=2.4，低频介电常数ε=7.4；较轻的有效质量带来更高的载流子迁移率。

Conclusion: Ni²⁺/Pr³⁺共掺杂能有效降低CsPbCl₃中的缺陷浓度，并全面改善其光电性能，为该类钙钛矿材料的稳定性优化提供了可行的掺杂策略。

Abstract: All inorganic halide perovskites offer promising optoelectronic properties at low cost, but their structural softness and thermal instability limit applications. Density functional theory using the FP-LAPW method (WIEN2k) was used to study Ni2+/Pr3+ co-doping in CsPbCl3. Results show Ni2+ substitutes for Pb2+ at the B-site and Pr3+ for Cs at the A-site, keeping charge balance. Co-doping stabilizes the lattice, raises formation energies of halogen and metal vacancies, and reduces deep defect levels in the band gap. Phonon dispersion confirms that both pristine and co-doped CsPbCl3 are dynamically stable. Ni2+/Pr3+ co-doping suppresses low-energy vibrations and causes mode splitting in the 3 to 5 THz range, increasing phonon scattering and lowering lattice thermal conductivity. Mechanical analysis reveals higher elastic constants and bulk modulus, while ductility remains unchanged. Electronic structure calculations reveal Ni-3d and Pr-4f states at the band edges, reducing effective carrier mass and passivating vacancy states. Optical absorption is red-shifted, and the high-frequency (ε = 2.4) and low-frequency (ε = 7.4) dielectric constants are distinct. Transport analysis finds higher carrier mobility due to lighter effective masses. Altogether, Ni2+/Pr3+ co-doping reduces defect concentrations and improves the optoelectronic properties of CsPbCl3.

### [65] [Thermodynamic Modeling of Pure Elements from 0 K with Uncertainty Quantification using PyCalphad and ESPEI](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22910)
*Alexander Richter,Abdulmonem Obaied,Irina Roslyakova,Boris Wilthan,Allison Beese,Zi-Kui Liu*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过将多种基于物理的纯元素热力学模型（thermodynamic models）集成到开源软件 PyCalphad 和 ESPEI 中，实现了对模型参数与拟合优度的系统评估与定量比较；通过 41 种纯元素的重建模，展示了不同模型之间的量化对比，为多组分材料的高通量 CALPHAD 建模提供了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当前 CALPHAD 建模中纯元素吉布斯自由能（Gibbs energy）的基准温度范围始于 298.15 K，但近年来已有多种物理模型将其延伸至 0 K。为使这些模型能够被系统性地、定量地比较与采纳，需要统一的实现框架与评估工具。

Method: 将不同的纯元素热力学模型实现到开源软件包 PyCalphad 和 ESPEI 中；利用 ESPEI 中的马尔可夫链蒙特卡洛（Markov Chain Monte Carlo, MCMC）方法进行模型参数的不确定性量化（uncertainty quantification）；对 41 种纯元素进行重建模以评估模型拟合优度。

Result: 通过对 41 种纯元素的重建模，展示了不同纯元素热力学模型之间的定量比较；验证了 PyCalphad 和 ESPEI 作为实施上述模型并进行高通量多组分 CALPHAD 建模的适用工具。

Conclusion: 该工作使纯元素 CALPHAD 描述的持续改进成为可能，并为多组分系统的有效开发提供了支持。

Abstract: Thermodynamic modeling of pure elements is the foundation of the CALPHAD modeling of engineering materials. Recently, multiple physics-based models have been proposed to describe Gibbs energy of pure elements down to 0 K, extending from 298.15 K in the current CALPHAD modeling. To enable their systematic and quantitative comparison and adoption, those thermodynamic models of pure elements are implemented into the open-source software packages PyCalphad and ESPEI in the present work for evaluation of model parameters and model fitness. PyCalphad and ESPEI are suitable tools for implementation of these models for high throughput CALPHAD modeling of multicomponent materials. Particularly, Markov Chain Monte Carlo used in ESPEI allows for uncertainty quantification of model parameters and model predictions. Through the remodeling of 41 pure elements, the present work demonstrates the quantitative comparison of modeling of pure elements with different models and enables the efficient development of multicomponent systems with continuously improved CALPHAD description of pure elements.

### [66] [Large language model-enabled automated data extraction for concrete materials informatics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22938)
*Zhanzhao Li,Kengran Yang,Qiyao He,Kai Gong*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种基于大语言模型（LLM）的自动化管道，用于从非结构化科学文献中提取和结构化材料数据。以混凝土为代表性案例，该管道在一小时内从超过27,000篇出版物中提取近9,000条高质量记录（涵盖100多个属性），构建了最大的开放式混凝土实验数据库。机器学习分析表明，大规模、多样化和信息丰富的数据集对提高模型在分布内准确性和分布外泛化能力至关重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 数据驱动的材料发现受限于大规模、高质量且可获取的实验数据集的稀缺性，尤其是从非结构化科学文献中系统提取材料数据仍缺乏通用且高效的解决方案。

Method: 提出一种基于大语言模型（large language model, LLM）的通用自动化管道，用于从非结构化科学文献中提取和组织材料数据；以混凝土为具体且具有挑战性的示例进行验证，并评估其在多种LLM上的鲁棒性。

Result: 该管道在多种LLM上表现稳健，对成分-工艺-性能（composition–process–property）属性的F1分数最高达0.97；一小时内从超过27,000篇出版物中提取近9,000条高质量记录（含100多个属性），构建了最大的开放式混凝土实验数据库。

Conclusion: 机器学习分析强调大规模、多样化和信息丰富的数据集对提升分布内准确性和分布外泛化能力（out-of-distribution generalization）的重要性。该管道可便捷地迁移至其他材料领域，加速材料信息学（materials informatics）中可扩展数据基础设施的构建。

Abstract: The promise of data-driven materials discovery remains constrained by the scarcity of large, high-quality, and accessible experimental datasets. Here, we introduce a generalizable large language model (LLM)-powered pipeline for automated extraction and structuring of materials data from unstructured scientific literature, using concrete materials as a representative and particularly challenging example. The pipeline exhibits robust performance across a broad range of LLMs and achieves an $F_1$ score of up to 0.97 for diverse composition--process--property attributes. Within one hour, it extracts nearly 9,000 high-quality records with over 100 attributes screened from more than 27,000 publications, enabling the construction of the largest open laboratory database for blended cement concrete. Machine learning analyses underscore the importance of large, diverse, and information-rich datasets for enhancing both in-distribution accuracy and out-of-distribution generalization to unseen materials. The proposed pipeline is readily adaptable to other materials domains and accelerates the development of scalable data infrastructures for materials informatics.

### [67] [Chirality Transfer to the Centrosymmetric Magnetic Sublattice in the Hybrid Perovskite (R)-/(S)-3-Fluoropyrrolidinium Copper(II) Chloride](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22952)
*Zheng Zhang,Mingyu Xu,Jose L. Gonzalez Jimenez,Stephen Zhang,Weiwei Xie,Xianghan Xu,Daniel B. Straus*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文报道了一种新型二维手性金属卤化物材料 (R)-/(S)-C₄H₉FN₂CuCl₄，通过引入手性有机阳离子，使原本中心对称的无机亚晶格诱导出手性磁有序（chiral magnetic order），而外消旋体则无此现象。该材料在尼尔温度（Néel temperature）2.23 K 处发生反铁磁相变，且手性变体中存在场致磁手性（field-induced magnetic chirality）及其二阶磁电效应（second-order magnetoelectric effect）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索将手性有机阳离子（chiral organic cation）引入有机-无机杂化材料中，能否诱导无机亚晶格产生手性磁有序（chiral magnetic order），从而将手性磁性与其他光学、电子性质相结合。

Method: 合成两种手性变体 (R)-和 (S)-C₄H₉FN₂CuCl₄ 以及外消旋变体（racemic variant）；通过磁化率测量和比热容测量确认反铁磁相变，并通过测量二阶磁电效应检测场致磁手性。

Result: 手性变体中存在手性磁有序，而外消旋变体中没有；两种变体均在垂直于无机 Cu-Cl 层传播方向测得的磁化率中显示尼尔温度 TN = 2.23 K 的反铁磁相变，比热容测量也支持该相变；手性变体中观察到二阶磁电效应，表明存在场致磁手性，而外消旋体中无磁电信号。

Conclusion: 通过在手性有机-无机杂化磁性材料中引入手性阳离子，可以创造出具有手性磁有序的材料，这为设计兼具手性磁性与其他光学和电子性质的定制材料提供了可能。

Abstract: Incorporating chiral organic cations into organic-inorganic hybrid materials has been shown to enable the inorganic sublattice to display chiroptical properties. We report a new two-dimensional magnetic (S=1/2) chiral metal halide material, (R)- and (S)-$(C_4H_9FN)_2CuCl_4$ (where $(C_4H_9FN)^+$ is 3-fluoropyrrolidinium), which consists of Cu-Cl inorganic layers separated by $(C_4H_9FN)^+$ organic cations. The presence of the chiral $(C_4H_9FN)^+$ organic cation induces formation of chiral magnetic order, even though the inorganic sublattice itself is structurally centrosymmetric. We also report the racemic variant, containing an equal amount of (R)- and (S)- cations, which shows no evidence of chiral magnetic order. When the magnetic susceptibility is measured perpendicular to inorganic Cu-Cl layer propagation direction, an antiferromagnetic phase transition at Néel temperature $T_N = 2.23~K$ is observed in both the chiral and racemic materials, and the existence of the magnetic phase transition is supported by specific heat capacity measurements. Field-induced magnetic chirality is observed through the existence of a second-order magnetoelectric effect in the chiral variant, while no magnetoelectric signal is observed for the racemic material, indicating the absence of magnetic chirality. Our findings demonstrate that materials exhibiting chiral magnetic order can be created through the incorporation of a chiral cation into an organic-inorganic hybrid magnetic material, potentially allowing for the design of tailored materials that combine chiral magnetism with other desirable optical and electronic properties that come from structural chirality.

### [68] [Sustainability-informed materials design](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22987)
*Rachel Woods-Robinson,Amalie Trewartha*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文主张将生命周期思维（life cycle thinking）引入材料开发的早期阶段——在不确定性最高但设计自由度最大的时候——并提出了一个面向决策的适应性框架，旨在将可持续性嵌入无机固体材料的设计全过程，推动从“事后修正”向“前瞻性、负责任的材料设计”转变。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 新兴材料（emerging materials）的环境与社会影响通常在设计选择被“锁定”之后才进行评估，导致干预空间极其有限。作者认为应当将这一时序颠倒过来。

Method: 识别了材料科学与可持续性分析之间的脱节（disconnects），提出了一个可适应、面向决策的框架（adaptable, decision-oriented framework），将可持续性嵌入不同技术演进阶段的材料设计，并强调预测合成（predictive synthesis）等近期进展可以帮助实现这一整合。

Result: 发现并系统梳理了无机固体材料领域在设计早期缺乏可持续性评估的结构性问题，指出了关键脱节环节。

Conclusion: 提出了一份跨利益相关方议程（cross-stakeholder agenda），呼吁从“回顾性修正”转向“前瞻性、负责任的材料设计”，在设计之初就纳入可持续性考量。

Abstract: While material innovation can enable sustainable development, environmental and social impacts of emerging materials are often assessed only after design choices are "locked in." Here, we argue for a shift in perspective: life cycle thinking should enter at the earliest stages of materials development, where uncertainty is highest but design freedom is greatest. Rather than treating incomplete knowledge as a barrier, we reframe it as an inherent feature that can illuminate trajectories, tradeoffs, and consequences -- and enable intervention while change remains possible. Focusing on inorganic solid materials, we identify disconnects between materials science and sustainability analysis, propose an adaptable, decision-oriented framework to embed sustainability into material design across evolving technology stages, and highlight how recent advances such as predictive synthesis can help operationalize this integration. Guided by the framework's governing principles, we outline a cross-stakeholder agenda to shift from retrospective correction to anticipatory, responsible material design from the outset.

### [69] [RKKY interaction in altermagnets with adiabatic electron-phonon coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23082)
*Bui D. Hoi*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文理论上研究了二维Rashba d波交变磁体（altermagnets）中慢声子重整化的RKKY相互作用，发现静态晶格畸变可通过电子-声子耦合（EPC）有效调控RKKY耦合的强度、各向异性、相位和手性，为基于交变磁体的自旋电子学器件提供了一种低能调控手段。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用连续模型哈密顿量（continuum model Hamiltonian）描述交变磁各向异性、Rashba自旋-轨道耦合（RSOC）和绝热晶格畸变；通过二阶微扰论（second-order perturbation theory）和数值动量空间积分计算非共线RKKY交换张量（noncollinear RKKY exchange tensor）。

Abstract: Altermagnets, characterized by time-reversal symmetry breaking without net magnetization and momentum-dependent spin-split bands, offer a promising platform for spintronics due to their anisotropic spin textures and potential for tunable magnetic interactions. Here, we theoretically investigate the slow phonon-renormalized Ruderman-Kittel-Kasuya-Yosida (RKKY) interaction in two-dimensional Rashba $d$-wave altermagnets, incorporating arbitrary Rashba spin-orbit coupling (RSOC) strength and spin-dependent static-Holstein electron-phonon coupling (EPC). Using a continuum model Hamiltonian that captures altermagnetic anisotropy, RSOC, and adiabatic lattice distortions, we compute the noncollinear RKKY exchange tensor via second-order perturbation theory and numerical momentum-space integration. Our results reveal that static lattice distortions provide a versatile tuning knob for engineering the magnitude, anisotropy, and chirality of RKKY couplings: moderate EPC suppresses long-range coherence while inducing component-specific phase shifts and sign reversals, particularly in Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya and compass-like terms, enabling control over ferromagnetic/antiferromagnetic alignments and clockwise/counterclockwise chiralities. Systematic parameter scans demonstrate enhanced oscillatory complexity with altermagnetic order, RSOC, and doping. These findings establish slow phonons as a low-energy tuning knob that systematically controls the magnitude, anisotropy, phase, and chirality of noncollinear RKKY couplings - even at arbitrary Rashba strength - thereby providing a practical route to engineer ferromagnetic/antiferromagnetic alignments and clockwise/counterclockwise DM chiralities in altermagnet-based heterostructures.

### [70] [Effective phonon models based on symmetry-adapted multipole basis -- Hidden chiral phonon angular momentum splitting in ferroaxial systems](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23109)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有声子模型通常缺乏对微观对称性与声子角动量、手性等现象之间关系的系统理解，因此需要一种基于对称性的统一框架来揭示隐藏和涌现的声子现象，并探索通过电子有序化或外场对声子性质进行调控的可能性。

Method: 提出一种对称适配多极基方法，将力常数矩阵（force-constant matrix）分解为以键为中心的电多极子，并以此识别导致声子角动量分裂的微观要素；随后将该框架应用于最小锯齿链模型（zigzag-chain model），分析铁轴向序和极性贡献对手性声子的影响。

Result: 铁轴向序可在锯齿链模型中产生隐藏的子晶格分辨手性声子（hidden sublattice-resolved chiral phonons）；当引入额外的极性贡献时，可获得有限全局手性（finite global chirality）。

Conclusion: 该框架提供了隐藏与涌现声子现象的统一对称性描述，并建议通过电子有序化及外场调控声子性质的可能路径。

Abstract: We propose a symmetry-based framework for constructing effective harmonic phonon models using a symmetry-adapted multipole basis. By decomposing the force-constant matrix into bond-centered electric multipoles, we identify the minimal microscopic ingredients responsible for phonon angular-momentum splitting. Applying this framework to a minimal zigzag-chain model, we show that ferroaxial order gives rise to a hidden sublattice-resolved chiral phonons, while an additional polar contribution leads to finite global chirality. Our results provide a unified symmetry-based description of hidden and emergent phonon phenomena and suggest a route to control phonon properties via electronic orderings and external fields.

In this work, we investigate the high strain rate response of the CrCoNi-based ODS-MPEA alloy GRX-810 and its non-ODS variant. The ODS variant contains a high density of hexagonal yttria nanoparticles that serve as the strengthening oxide phase. At high strain rates and ambient temperature, GRX-810 ODS exhibits higher dynamic strength, approximately 2.79 times its quasi-static strength, than both conventional alloys and its non-ODS variant because of the additional athermal strengthening provided by the nanoscale oxide dispersion. At high strain rates and elevated temperatures, however, GRX-810 ODS undergoes thermal softening. This response is consistent with dislocation confinement associated with the small interparticle spacing of the oxide dispersion, which limits the phonon-drag contribution, together with the temperature-dependent reduction of elastic constants that lowers the athermal strengthening terms, including the oxide-related contribution. Additional weakening of the solute-pinning mechanism at elevated temperature further reduces the dynamic yield strength.

Conclusion: 全杂化分子束外延（hMBE）方法是一种可扩展、确定性强且性能优异的材料制备平台，在晶圆级集成铁电光子学（wafer-scale integrated ferroelectric photonics）领域具有显著优势。

By utilizing titanium tetraisopropoxide as a titanium precursor, we achieve a self-regulating, adsorption-controlled layer-by-layer growth at rates exceeding 75 nm/h, while maintaining an atomically sharp and structurally coherent BTO/STO interface. We systematically compare the structural, ferroelectric, and electro-optic (EO) properties of fully hMBE-grown BTO with those deposited via pulsed laser deposition (PLD) on identical STO/Si templates. While both techniques yield high-quality c-domain dominated films, the optimized hMBE-grown BTO exhibits superior crystallinity and a larger effective EO coefficient of 248 pm/V, surpassing that of the PLD-grown films (220 pm/V). ### [73] [Weak Polar Optical Phonon Scattering Decouples Electron and Phonon Transport in Layered Thermoelectric Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23328)
*Zhonghao Xia,Michele Reticcioli,Yateng Wang,Yali Yang,Alessandro Stroppa,Jiangang He*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过高通量密度泛函理论计算筛选236种层状半导体，识别出23种具有高跨平面迁移率的候选材料，其中GaGe₂Te凭借低有效质量、弱极性光学声子散射和超低晶格热导率（0.57 W/m·K），实现了电热输运解耦，为高性能热电材料设计提供了新策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 热电（thermoelectric, TE）材料性能受电导率、塞贝克系数（Seebeck coefficient）和晶格热导率（lattice thermal conductivity, κL）之间的强烈相互制约所限制。层状化合物虽能有效抑制跨平面方向的热导率，但常因能带色散有限和强烈极性光学声子（polar optical phonon, POP）散射而导致载流子迁移率（carrier mobility, μ）低下。为此，亟需寻找可同时实现高迁移率和低热导率的层状热电材料。

Method: 采用高通量密度泛函理论（high-throughput density functional theory, DFT）计算，对236种层状半导体进行系统筛选。以低有效质量（effective mass, m*）和弱POP散射为判据，识别具有高跨平面迁移率的候选材料，并进一步评估其功率因子（power factor, S²σ）和晶格热导率。

Result: 筛选出23种具有高跨平面迁移率的化合物，其中14种展现出较大的功率因子。GaGe₂Te尤为突出，其跨平面电导率和功率因子极高，源于小有效质量与小离子介电常数的有利组合；同时其跨平面晶格热导率在300 K时仅为0.57 W/m·K，归因于弱层间键合和显著的声子非简谐性（phonon anharmonicity）。

Conclusion: 研究表明，通过抑制极性光学声子散射，可有效解耦层状材料中的电子与声子输运，从而为开发高性能热电材料提供了一条有前景的途径。

Abstract: High-performance thermoelectric (TE) materials are crucial for efficient waste-heat recovery and solid-state cooling technologies. A persistent challenge in TE materials design arises from the strong interdependence among the electrical conductivity ($σ$), Seebeck coefficient ($S$), and lattice thermal conductivity ($κ_{\mathrm{L}}$). Layered compounds can effectively suppress $κ_{\mathrm{L}}$ along the cross-plane direction owing to weak interlayer interactions; however, they often suffer from low carrier mobility ($μ$) caused by limited band dispersion and strong polar optical phonon (POP) scattering. Here, we perform high-throughput density functional theory calculations to screen 236 layered semiconductors and identify candidates with low effective mass ($m^{*}$) and weak POP scattering. We identify 23 compounds with high cross-plane $μ$, among which 14 exhibit large power factors ($S^{2}σ$). Notably, GaGe$_{2}$Te stands out with exceptionally high cross-plane $σ$ and power factor, enabled by a favorable combination of small $m^{*}$ and a small ionic dielectric constant. Simultaneously, GaGe$_{2}$Te exhibits an ultralow cross-plane $κ_{\mathrm{L}}$ of 0.57~W~m$^{-1}$~K$^{-1}$ at 300~K, originating from weak interlayer bonding and pronounced phonon anharmonicity. These results demonstrate an effective strategy to decouple electron and phonon transport in layered materials by mitigating POP scattering, thereby providing a promising pathway toward high-performance thermoelectric materials.

### [74] [From Data-Driven Models to Physical Insight: Vibrational Entropy Governed by Atomic Volume](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23369)
*Shivam Tripathi,Jatin Kawatra,Varun Malviya,Krishna Mehta*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本研究结合数据驱动建模与物理分析，构建了一个高效且可解释的框架，用于预测材料的振动熵（vibrational entropy）。通过前馈神经网络（feedforward neural network）和SHAP分析，发现原子体积（atomic volume）是控制振动熵的主导因素，并据此建立了一个对数线性模型（logarithmic linear model），该模型在不同温度下均能准确描述振动熵的结构与热贡献，为替代全声子计算（full phonon calculations）提供了一种计算高效的途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 振动熵在决定材料相稳定性（phase stability）和温度依赖行为中起核心作用，但基于第一性原理（first-principles）的声子（phonon）计算方法计算成本高昂，亟需一种高效且可解释的替代方案。

Method: 利用PhononDB数据集，训练基于Materials Project和成分描述符（composition based descriptors）的前馈神经网络进行预测；采用SHAP分析（SHAP analysis）识别关键物理因素；基于分析结果构建简化解析模型（simplified analytical models），包括对数线性模型和考虑温度依赖的扩展模型（引入低温T³标度与高温对数依赖）。

Result: 神经网络达到了高预测精度；SHAP分析表明原子体积是振动熵的主导因素；对数线性模型准确且物理可解释地描述了全材料范围内的振动熵；温度依赖模型统一捕获了振动熵的结构贡献与热贡献，与德拜（Debye）和爱因斯坦（Einstein）型行为一致。

Conclusion: 研究表明，振动熵可以通过简单、物理有意义的函数关系进行预测，为全声子计算提供了一种计算高效的替代方案，并可用于熵驱动的材料筛选（entropy informed materials screening）。

Abstract: Vibrational entropy plays a central role in determining phase stability and temperature dependent behavior in materials, yet its calculation from first-principles phonon methods remains computationally demanding. In this work, we combine data-driven modeling with physically motivated analysis to develop an efficient and interpretable framework for predicting vibrational entropy. Using a dataset derived from PhononDB, a feedforward neural network trained on Materials Project and composition based descriptors achieves high predictive accuracy, while SHAP analysis identifies atomic volume as the dominant factor governing vibrational entropy. Guided by this insight, simplified analytical models are constructed, revealing a logarithmic dependence of vibrational entropy on atomic volume consistent with lattice dynamical considerations. A logarithmic linear model is shown to provide an accurate and physically interpretable description across the full range of materials.
  To extend the analysis to finite temperatures, a temperature dependent formulation is introduced that incorporates T3 scaling at low temperatures and logarithmic dependence at higher temperatures, consistent with Debye and Einstein type behavior. This unified model captures both structural and thermal contributions to vibrational entropy with good accuracy. Overall, the proposed framework demonstrates that vibrational entropy can be predicted using simple, physically meaningful relationships, offering a computationally efficient alternative to full phonon calculations and enabling entropy informed materials screening.

Here, we present results of electronic spectroscopy experiments performed on individual defects in the prototypical TMD molybdenum disulfide (MoS2) under ambient conditions, by way of conductive atomic force microscopy (C-AFM). Data acquired in the form of consecutive, high-resolution current maps at various bias voltages allow the assessment of local conductivity and differential conductance as a function of bias voltage for individual defects, the effects of which range from single atomic sites to several nanometers in lateral size. Characteristic behavior in spectroscopy data allows the categorization of observed defects into distinct groups, and their chemical identification as n-type and p-type transition metal substitutions of molybdenum atoms, as well as oxygen substitutions of sulfur atoms.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 提出两种变体：配对sfTA（paired sfTA）和结合sfTA（binding sfTA）。二者通过改变sfTA协议中使用的扭角（twist angles）集合以及基于结合结构因子（binding structure factor）选取特殊扭角的方式，将结合相互作用纳入sfTA的扭角选取算法中。在多种双层系统上对两种变体进行测试，并将所得结合相关能（binding correlation energies）与原始sfTA结果进行对比。

Conclusion: 针对低维材料提出的sfTA变体方法能够以较低成本获得接近TA精度的结合相关能，结合sfTA表现最优，且误差抵消机制是提升精度的主要原因。

Abstract: Structure factor twist averaging (sfTA) is a newer method that has been shown to reproduce twist-averaged (TA) CCSD energies for bulk systems at a low computational cost. In this work, we extend this method for the treatment of low-dimensional materials in the form of two variants: paired sfTA and binding sfTA. These variants affect which twist angles are used in the sfTA protocol, as well as how the special twist angle is selected, namely by using the binding structure factor. These changes are meant to incorporate the binding interaction into the twist-angle selection algorithm within sfTA. Both variants are tested on a variety of bilayer systems, and the resulting binding correlation energies are compared to original sfTA results. We show that the variants are able to produce results approaching TA, with binding sfTA producing the most accurate energies. We also use contour plots of the test systems to show that these improvements are most likely caused by a cancellation of errors.

Abstract: We calculate the theoretical non-degenerate two photon absorption and three color injected current response tensors for bulk GaAs and Ge$_{1-x}$Sn$_x$ for a range of alloy compositions. ### [78] [Amorphous High Density Plutonium](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23491)

Conclusion: 低温下的体积变化可能由一种密度介于 α 和 δ 之间的非晶相（amorphous phase）的向内生长（ingrowth）解释；该非晶相在约 100 K 以上温度下可快速退火至对应晶相。室温下 δ-钚晶格参数与长度增长的不一致也可由不断形成并退火的更致密非晶相来解释。

Abstract: Metastable aluminum-alloyed $δ$-plutonium shrinks rapidly and pure $α$-plutonium swells rapidly at 4 K. At ambient temperature alloyed $δ$-plutonium swells about $10^{-3}$ as fast as it shrinks at 4 K, but its bulk density decreases more slowly than would be inferred from the increase in its lattice parameter determined by X-ray diffraction. These results might be explained as the result of ingrowth of the opposite phases, but they have not been found in X-ray diffraction. The cryogenic results may be explained by ingrowth of an amorphous phase with density intermediate between those of $α$ and $δ$. This phase, when formed from alloyed $δ$-plutonium, rapidly but not instantaneously anneals to $δ$-plutonium at temperatures $\gtrapprox 100\,$K; when formed from pure $α$-plutonium it anneals to $α$ at similar temperatures. The room temperature discrepancy between growth of lattice parameter and length of $δ$-plutonium is also explained by ingrowth of a denser amorphous phase that is continuously formed and annealed out.

Abstract: We employ density functional theory within a non-collinear framework to investigate the magnetic properties of the octanuclear molecular rings Cr$_8$ and V$_8$. Our aim is to generalize the evaluation of the effective magnetic interactions by explicitly including non-collinear spin configurations, thereby refining our understanding of their dependence upon the underlying electronic structure and molecular geometry. By analyzing the energetics of a variety of magnetic configurations, particularly non-collinear arrangements with neighboring spins oriented along different directions, we move beyond the exchange-only Heisenberg Hamiltonian describing the low-energy sector of the excitation spectrum. This approach enables us to distinguish between in-plane and out-of-plane exchange interactions, and to incorporate biquadratic coupling terms into the effective spin Hamiltonian. We reveal significant antisymmetric exchange interactions of the Dzyaloshinskii-Moriya (DM) type whose dependence on the curvature of the annular structure is clarified by a comparison with the results obtained from linear chains of equal composition. Our work demonstrates that interactions beyond conventional exchange, particularly biquadratic anisotropic terms, in the spin Hamiltonian are essential for accurately capturing the low-energy excitations of these systems. The closest quantitative agreement with experimental results (particularly for the case of Cr$_8$) is achieved when extended Hubbard functionals are used for the evaluation of the effective magnetic couplings.

Abstract: Among the group-IV vacancy color centers in diamond, the SnV holds promise for photonics based quantum applications. In this work, the Tin-Vacancy (SnV) zero-phonon line (ZPL) and its pressure coefficient are calculated using first principles approaches. The predicted absolute ZPL position is shown to be strongly influenced by the method and supercell size used. The results are therefore extrapolated to the dilute limit allowing for direct comparison with experiments. The importance of identifying the color-center related Kohn--Sham states is highlighted, as well as the shifting of these states due to electron excitations as well as supercell size and k-point position. ### [81] [Attention Is Not All You Need for Diffraction](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23811)
*Elizabeth J. Baggett,Edward G. Friedman,Abhishek Shetty,Derrick Chan-Sew,Vanellsa Acha,Harshita Dwarcherla,Paul Kienzle,William Ratcliff*

Method: 提出一种物理信息Transformer（physics-informed transformer），包含：(1) 显式的sin²θ坐标通道；(2) 物理感知位置编码（physics-aware positional encoding）；(3) 结构化多任务解码器（structured multi-task decoder），将几何规则学习与整体模式识别分离。训练采用三阶段课程：平衡合成预训练、带显式择优取向（preferred-orientation）建模的真实微调、贝叶斯先验注入（Bayesian prior injection）。后处理使用温度缩放（post-hoc temperature scaling）提升鲁棒性。

Result: 模型将粉末衍射图谱分类到99个消光群（extinction groups），这是仅凭衍射数据所能达到的最具体对称性分类。误差在最大平移子群（maximal translationengleiche subgroups）的有向无环图（directed acyclic graph）上保持局部性，且主要流向低对称性后代，与真实噪声擦除系统消光线索（systematic-absence cues）的物理过程一致。

Conclusion: 研究成果表明，对于衍射数据的科学机器学习，物理信息引导的目标设计（physics-informed target design）、课程学习（curriculum）和校准推理（calibrated inference）与模型容量同等重要。

Abstract: Determining crystal symmetry from powder X-ray diffraction is a central problem in materials characterization, yet multiple space groups can produce indistinguishable patterns, making automated classification difficult. We show that attention-based architectures, while superior to convolutional networks for this task, are insufficient on their own: reliable symmetry extraction requires encoding crystallographic knowledge into both the network architecture and the training curriculum. We introduce a physics-informed transformer that classifies powder patterns into 99 extinction groups, the most specific symmetry classification accessible from diffraction data alone, using an explicit sin^2(theta) coordinate channel, physics-aware positional encoding, and a structured multi-task decoder that separates geometric rule learning from holistic pattern recognition. A three-stage curriculum of balanced synthetic pretraining, realistic fine-tuning with explicit preferred-orientation modeling, and Bayesian prior injection proves essential for bridging the synthetic-to-real domain gap, while post-hoc temperature scaling rather than additional training is the key remaining ingredient for robust real-data transfer. By mapping predictions onto the directed acyclic graph of maximal translationengleiche subgroups, we show that the calibrated model's errors are not random but physically structured: they remain local on the subgroup hierarchy and flow predominantly toward lower-symmetry descendants, consistent with the physical erasure of systematic-absence cues by real-world noise. These results establish that physics-informed target design, curriculum, and calibrated inference matter as much as model capacity for scientific machine learning on diffraction data.

### [82] [Accelerating Quantum Materials Characterization: Hybrid Active Learning for Autonomous Spin Wave Spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23821)
*William Ratcliff*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文提出TAS-AI，一种将无模型（model-agnostic）发现与物理信息（physics-informed）推理分离的混合框架，用于自主中子自旋波谱的三轴光谱学。在盲重建中，无模型方法优于物理信息规划；在物理信息阶段，系统可在10次测量内实现哈密顿量判别与参数精修，并识别出后验加权设计的算法短视（algorithmic myopia）失败模式，通过约束证伪通道加以缓解。
