Abstract: Autonomous neutron spectroscopy must solve three distinct tasks: detection (where is the signal?), inference (which Hamiltonian governs it?), and refinement (what are the parameters?). No single controller solves all three equally well. We present TAS-AI, a hybrid agnostic-to-physics-informed framework for autonomous triple-axis spin-wave spectroscopy that separates these tasks explicitly. In blind reconstruction benchmarks, model-agnostic methods such as random sampling, coarse grids, and Gaussian-process mappers reach a global error threshold more reliably and with fewer measurements than physics-informed planning, supporting the claim that discovery and inference are distinct tasks requiring distinct controllers. Once signal structure is localized, the physics-informed stage performs in-loop Hamiltonian discrimination and parameter refinement: in a controlled square-lattice test between nearest-neighbor-only and J1-J2 Hamiltonians, TAS-AI reaches a decisive AIC-derived evidence ratio (>100) in fewer than 10 measurements, while motion-aware scheduling cuts wall-clock time by 32% at a fixed measurement budget. We also identify a failure mode of posterior-weighted design, algorithmic myopia, in which the planner over-refines the current leading model while under-sampling low-intensity falsification probes. A constrained falsification channel sharply reduces time spent committed to the wrong model and accelerates correct model selection without modifying the Bayesian inference engine. In controlled two-model ablations, both a deterministic top-two max-disagreement rule and an LLM-based audit committee achieve this gain under identical constraints. ### [83] [Optical Properties of Indium-Gallium-Oxide Microcrystalline Alloy Films: From the Visible to the Deep-UV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23884)
*HM Borhanul Alam,Dipak Oli,You Qiang,Bisheswor Acharya,Jesse Huso,Matthew D. McCluskey,Leah Bergman*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过透射光谱、Urbach能量分析和自陷空穴（STH）发光的空间光致发光（PL）映射，系统研究了(In_xGa_{1-x})_2O_3微晶薄膜的光学性质随组分x的变化。结果表明，光学带隙和STH发光均随In含量增加发生红移；当x ≥ 0.3时出现早期相分离，而x = 0.63时发生明显相分离；Urbach能量分析揭示了与Mg_xZn_{1-x}O类似的组分依赖趋势，但(In_xGa_{1-x})_2O_3的Urbach能量显著更大，归因于其更强的空穴-声子耦合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究目的旨在解决该合金体系特有的材料特性问题，通过多种光谱手段系统表征(In_xGa_{1-x})_2O_3微晶薄膜的光学性质随组分x的变化规律。

Method: 采用透射光谱测量提取光学带隙，利用Urbach能量分析表征无序度，并结合自陷空穴（STH）发射的空间光致发光（PL）映射来研究光学性质随组分x的变化。还将(In_xGa_{1-x})_2O_3的Urbach分析结果与Mg_xZn_{1-x}O进行了对比。

Result: 当x ≤ 0.46时，光学带隙从深紫外到近紫外范围红移约1 eV，STH发光在可见光范围红移约0.5 eV。当x = 0.63时，透射光谱显示两个光学带隙共存，表明样品发生相分离。光学带隙和STH发光的饱和行为表明，相分离在更低组分（x ~ 0.3）时已开始发生，与Urbach能量的组分趋势一致。与Mg_xZn_{1-x}O相比，两体系Urbach能量对组分的依赖趋势相似，但(In_xGa_{1-x})_2O_3的Urbach能量显著更大。

Conclusion: (In_xGa_{1-x})_2O_3合金在x ≥ 0.3时即出现早期相分离，相分离是甚至在其早期阶段就已存在的主要缺陷。该体系较大的Urbach能量源于其强烈的空穴-声子耦合，这种耦合提供了除缺陷类型之外的一种动态跃迁机制。

Abstract: The tailored optical properties of $(In_xGa_{1-x})_2O_3$ microcrystalline films were studied as a function of composition x via transmission, Urbach energy analysis, and spatial photoluminescence (PL) mapping of the self-trapped hole (STH) emission, with the objective of addressing material characteristics specific to this alloy system. Up to x = 0.46, the optical gap exhibited a redshift of 1 eV from the deep to the near-UV range, while the STH PL was redshifted by 0.5 eV in the visible range. For higher composition, x = 0.63, the transmission spectra indicated the co-existence of two optical gaps attributed to Ga-rich and to In-rich domains, implying that this sample is phase-separated. However, the saturation behavior of the optical gap and that of the STH PL showed that incipient phase separation occurs at a lower composition: x ~ 0.3. This is consistent with the compositional trend found for Urbach energy, implying that phase segregation in the alloys is a major defect even at its incipient stages. Additionally, Urbach analysis of $(In_xGa_{1-x})_2O_3$ was compared to that of $Mg_xZn_{1-x}O$. Both systems were found to have similar compositional dependence: at lower range, Urbach energies exhibited a negligible increase, while at the higher range a significant dependence on the composition was found. The main difference between the two alloy systems is in their Urbach energy: those for $(In_xGa_{1-x})_2O_3$ were significantly larger than those of $Mg_xZn_{1-x}O$. This stems from the strong hole coupling to phonons of $(In_xGa_{1-x})_2O_3$, which provides a dynamic transition additionally to that of defect-type.

</details>


### [84] [Nearly Isotropic Magnon Transport in Epitaxial Lithium Aluminum Ferrite Thin Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23943)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 低损耗磁性绝缘薄膜在通过磁振子进行信息传输方面具有潜力，而这需要各向同性的面内磁振子传播特性。该研究旨在探索具有面内磁各向异性的材料中磁振子扩散的各向同性程度。

Method: 采用非局域测量方法，分别通过电学和热学方式激发磁振子，在外延(001)锂铝铁氧体（Li0.5Al0.7Fe1.8O4）薄膜中测量逆自旋霍尔效应（inverse spin Hall effect）信号随磁振子扩散距离的变化，从而推导磁振子扩散长度。

Result: 沿[100]和[110]两个方向测得的磁振子扩散长度在250 K下近乎相同，这一各向同性结果与近乎各向同性的交换刚度（exchange stiffness）相一致。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，尖晶石铁氧体（spinel ferrites）是实现各向同性磁振子输运的可行平台。

Abstract: Low-loss magnetic insulating thin films are promising for information transport via magnons, where isotropic in-plane magnon propagation is desirable. We report nonlocal measurements of electrically and thermally generated magnons in epitaxial (001) lithium aluminum ferrite Li$_{0.5}$Al$_{0.7}$Fe$_{1.8}$O$_4$ thin films with pronounced fourfold in-plane magnetic anisotropy. By measuring the inverse spin Hall signal as a function of the magnon diffusion distance, we deduce magnon diffusion lengths that are nearly identical along the [100] and [110] directions at 250~K. This isotropy is consistent with a nearly isotropic exchange stiffness. These results highlight spinel ferrites as viable platforms for isotropic magnon transport.

### [85] [Three-dimensional topological ferroelectrics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23969)
*Haohao Sheng,Sheng Zhang,Zhong Fang,Hongming Weng,Zhijun Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文通过第一性原理计算预测了γ相Bi4Br4和Bi4I4是一种理想的三维拓扑铁电绝缘体（topological ferroelectric insulator），其非平庸拓扑性由自旋陈数（spin Chern number）C_{s_z}=2表征，且可通过层间滑动实现极化翻转，并设计了电控自旋滤波器器件以实现可切换的自旋极化电流。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 寻找拓扑序（topological order）与铁电序（ferroelectric order）自然共存的三维材料，以实现场控自旋电子器件（field-controlled spintronic devices）。

Method: 采用第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）预测γ相Bi4Br4和Bi4I4的结构稳定性与可合成性；利用自旋陈数（spin Chern number）和自旋分辨Wilson环（spin-resolved Wilson loops）表征拓扑性质。

Result: γ相Bi4X4（X=Br, I）在空间群Cmc2_1中结晶，虽无对称性分类指标，但自旋陈数C_{s_z}=2表明其具有三维量子自旋霍尔绝缘体（3D quantum spin Hall insulator）的自旋分辨拓扑态；z方向极化可通过层间滑动（interlayer sliding）翻转，能垒较低；基于双层薄膜设计了电控自旋滤波器（electrically controlled spin-filter device）。

Conclusion: 单相晶体、可观带隙（sizable band gap）及对铁电翻转鲁棒的带拓扑性（robust band topology）使Bi4Br4和Bi4I4成为本征三维拓扑铁电绝缘体的原型材料，为自旋电子器件中新型非易失性功能（nonvolatile functionalities）的实现提供了理想平台。

Abstract: Three-dimensional (3D) topological ferroelectric (FE) insulators, in which topological and FE orders naturally coexist, enable field-controlled spintronic devices. In this work, we predict a new structure of bismuth monohalides Bi4Br4 and Bi4I4, denoted $γ$ phase, and demonstrate that it is an ideal 3D topological FE insulator. Systematic first-principles calculations confirm the stability and synthesizability of $γ$-Bi4X4 (X=Br, I). Although the noncentrosymmetric $γ$ phase crystallizes in the space group $Cmc2_1$ with no symmetry-based classifications/indicators, the nontrivial topology can be characterized by the spin Chern number (SCN). Spin-resolved Wilson loops show the $s_z$ SCN $C_{s_z}=2$, indicating the spin-resolved topology of a 3D quantum spin Hall insulator state. The $z$-direction polarization can be switched by interlayer sliding, requiring only crossing a small energy barrier. Finally, we design an electrically controlled spin-filter device on bilayer films that can generate a switchable spin-polarized current. Combining a single-phase crystal, a sizable band gap, and robust band topology against FE switching, these bismuth monohalides serve as a prototype of intrinsic 3D topological FE insulators, providing an ideal platform for realizing new nonvolatile functionalities in spintronic devices.

### [86] [Room-temperature shape-memory effect in Sr(Ni$_{1-x}$Cu$_x$)$_2$P$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24019)

Method: 使用Cu替代的Sr(Ni₁₋ₓCuₓ)₂P₂单晶样品，开展温度依赖的电阻测量和单晶X射线衍射（single-crystal x-ray diffraction）实验，系统研究Cu含量和温度对晶体结构转变的影响，并构建T-x相图。

Conclusion: Sr(Ni₀.₉₆₃Cu₀.₀₃₇)₂P₂在室温附近展现出可调的tcO-to-cT转变热滞特性，使其具备成为室温形状记忆材料（shape memory material）的潜力。

The system can be tuned into its different states by changing temperature, mechanical stress, or chemical composition. Changes in bonding may manifest in changes of macroscopic properties of the material, such as its shape, electrical conductivity, or magnetism. In this work, we show that SrNi$_2$P$_2$ can be tuned among the three states by changing Cu substitution and temperature. We present temperature-dependent resistance and single-crystal x-ray diffraction results in Sr(Ni$_{1-x}$Cu$_x$)$_2$P$_2$ single-crystals that show that Cu substitution favors the P-P bonding, stabilizing the cT state at ambient pressure. We construct a $T-x$ phase diagram that shows how all of these transition temperatures increase with increasing Cu fraction, $x$. The transition between the tcO state and the cT state exhibits a very large thermal hysteresis, which can be tuned to temperatures close to room temperature. In particular, the properties of Sr(Ni$_{0.963}$Cu$_{0.037}$)$_2$P$_2$ may make it suitable for applications as a shape memory material at room temperature.

### [87] [Spin excitation of the Heisenberg antiferromagnet with frustration: from the bounce-lattice antiferromagnet through the maple-leaf-lattice antiferromagnet to the exact-dimer system](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24055)
*Hiroki Nakano,Toru Sakai*

Method: 采用高并行化数值对角化（highly parallelized numerical diagonalization）方法，对由孤立二聚体相互作用（J_d）和弹跳晶格相互作用（J_b）构成的系统进行基态自旋激发能隙的精确计算。分别计算了S=1/2时42位点团簇和S=1时24位点团簇。

Abstract: The spin-S Heisenberg antiferromagnet on the two-dimensional lattice is investigated for S=1/2 and S=1. We consider interaction at isolated dimers ($J_{\rm d}$) and interaction bonds that form the bounce lattice ($J_{\rm b}$). For $J_{\rm d}=J_{\rm b}$, the system is reduced to the maple-leaf-lattice antiferromagnet. We primarily conduct highly parallelized numerical diagonalization to examine the spin excitation gap above the ground state for various $J_{\rm b}/J_{\rm d}$ cases. For S=1/2, we report calculations for a 42-site cluster that has not been previously treated. The S=1 case is examined for the first time for clusters up to 24 sites. Regardless of whether S=1/2 or 1, we find that the system has a gapped nature for small $J_{\rm d}/J_{\rm b}$ and becomes gapless at $J_{\rm d}/J_{\rm b}\sim 1.4$. For S=1, we also find that another gapped region appears between the gapless case at $J_{\rm d}/J_{\rm b}\sim 1.4$ and the boundary of the exact-dimer phase.

### [88] [Interfacial breathing as a dynamic failure law in all-solid-state batteries: amplitude, phase lag and dual-timescale memory as design principles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24075)
*Changdeuck Bae*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 全固态电池（all-solid-state batteries）的失效既受体相传输限制，也受循环过程中演化的反应界面控制。降解由两个耦合过程主导：界面呼吸（interfacial breathing）——锂接触的循环尺度振荡，以及反应记忆（reactive memory）——电解质分解的缓慢累积。四个描述符刻画呼吸行为，结合基于分解界面层厚度的记忆指标。实验表明，离子电导率对平均放电电压影响微弱，而阴极电解质界面（cathode electrolyte interphase, CEI）电阻造成显著的电压和能量损失。硫化物基电池的相场模型（phase-field model）显示，更高堆叠压力强烈抑制呼吸相关波动，但几乎不改变反应记忆；因此压力控制呼吸而非记忆。由此构建的机制图（regime map）识别出空隙生长主导区、愈合主导区和界面层记忆主导区。该理论还预测了能量密度随C倍率（C rate）的排序翻转——初始性能更优的构型在高倍率下因呼吸加剧和界面层记忆锁定而失去优势。因此设计目标不仅是更高电导率或更低电阻，而是通过界面化学同时抑制呼吸并独立控制反应记忆。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究多关注全固态电池的体相传输限制，但对循环过程中反应界面的动态演化及其与力学和电化学过程的耦合机制认识不足，亟需建立统一的理论框架来揭示降解的主导因素。

Method: 通过四个描述符（descriptors）量化界面呼吸，并基于分解界面层厚度定义反应记忆指标；采用简化的电化学基准实验评估离子电导率和CEI电阻的影响；构建硫化物基全固态电池的相场模型（phase-field model），分析堆叠压力对呼吸和记忆的差异化作用。

Result: 离子电导率对平均放电电压影响很小，而CEI电阻导致显著的电压和能量损失。高堆叠压力有效抑制呼吸相关波动，但对反应记忆几乎无影响。建立了包含空隙生长主导区、愈合主导区和界面层记忆主导区的机制图，并预测了能量密度随C倍率的排序翻转现象。

Conclusion: 全固态电池的设计目标不应仅追求更高的离子电导率或更低的电阻，而应同时抑制界面呼吸并独立控制反应记忆，后者需要通过界面化学（interphase chemistry）手段实现。

Abstract: All-solid-state batteries fail not only by bulk transport limits, but by a reactive interface that evolves during cycling. We show that degradation is governed by two coupled processes: interfacial breathing, the cycle-scale oscillation of lithium contact, and reactive memory, the slow accumulation of electrolyte decomposition. Four descriptors capture breathing, together with a memory metric based on decomposed interphase thickness. A reduced electrochemical benchmark shows that ionic conductivity has little effect on mean discharge voltage, whereas cathode electrolyte interphase resistance causes major voltage and energy losses. A phase-field model of a sulfide-based cell shows that higher stack pressure strongly suppresses breathing-related fluctuations, but leaves reactive memory nearly unchanged. Thus, pressure controls breathing, not memory. The resulting regime map identifies void-growth-dominant, healing-dominant, and interphase-memory-dominant regions. The theory also predicts energy-density rank inversion with C rate, where an initially superior architecture loses advantage at higher rate as breathing intensifies and interphase memory locks in. The design target is therefore not merely higher conductivity or lower resistance, but simultaneous suppression of breathing and independent control of reactive memory through interphase chemistry.

</details>


### [89] [Understanding Damping Mechanisms via Spin Diffusion Length in Low-damping Li$_{0.5}$Al$_{1.0}$Fe$_{1.5}$O$_4$ Spinel Ferrite Thin Films](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24094)
*Katya Mikhailova,Lerato Takana,Guanxiong Qu,Juan A. Hofer,Hervé M. Carruzzo,Ivan K. Schuller,Clare C. Yu,Yuri Suzuki*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 该研究发现低阻尼铁磁绝缘体薄膜Li₀.₅Al₁.₀Fe₁.₅O₄（LAFO）中电生与热生磁振子（magnon）的自旋扩散长度（spin diffusion length, SDL）随温度呈现截然不同的变化趋势，并归因于不同的磁振子布居与散射机制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 磁振子阻尼（magnon damping）的机制在低阻尼材料的物理基础和应用研究中具有重要的科学与技术意义，但相关机理尚待阐明。

Method: 选取低阻尼铁磁绝缘体（ferrimagnetic insulator）薄膜Li₀.₅Al₁.₀Fe₁.₅O₄（LAFO）作为模型体系，通过对比电生和热生磁振子的自旋扩散长度（SDL）随温度的变化趋势来探测阻尼机制。

Result: 随着温度升高，电生磁振子的SDL几乎不变，而热生磁振子的SDL则下降；两种趋势表现出显著差异。

Conclusion: 热生成的高波矢（high k）磁振子主要受磁振子-声子散射（magnon-phonon scattering）限制，而电生成的低波矢（low k）磁振子则受来自磁杂质的弛豫散射（relaxational scattering）限制；上述差异可解释不同温度依赖行为。

Abstract: The mechanisms underlying magnon damping are of fundamental and technological interest in low-damping materials. We find low-damping ferrimagnetic insulator Li$_{0.5}$Al$_{1.0}$Fe$_{1.5}$O$_4$ (LAFO) thin films to be a promising model system for probing these mechanisms because of its distinct temperature dependent spin diffusion length (SDL) trends for electrically and thermally generated magnons. With increasing temperature, the electrical SDL shows minimal change, while the thermal SDL decreases. We attribute these trends to distinct magnon populations and scattering mechanisms: thermally generated high $k$ magnons are limited by magnon-phonon scattering, whereas electrically generated low $k$ magnons are limited by relaxational scattering from magnetic impurities.

</details>


### [90] [Characterizing Fill Factor Limitations in Perovskite-Silicon Tandem Solar Cells](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24098)

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 钙钛矿-硅叠层太阳电池（perovskite-silicon tandem solar cell）虽然已超过单结理论效率极限，但距离热力学极限仍有差距，主要受限于填充因子（fill factor, FF）。目前对FF损失机制的理解尚不充分，需要系统性地分析其内在机理。

Method: 本文提出了一种方法论，用于阐明钙钛矿-硅单片叠层太阳电池中FF损失的机制。该方法通过电致发光（electroluminescence）表征串联电阻（series resistance）相关的损失，同时引入光分流（photoshunt）概念——即钙钛矿太阳电池在光照下因电荷传输层迁移率（charge transport layer mobility）不足而导致并联电阻（parallel resistance）明显降低的现象。此外，还考虑了硅电池的双二极管特性（two-diode property）对叠层器件FF的影响。

Result: 除串联电阻损失外，光分流和硅电池的双二极管特性是影响叠层电池FF的两个重要因素。当底电池（bottom cell）处于过光照（over illuminated）状态时，光分流现象会被隐藏，这解释了高效叠层太阳电池通常受限于底电池的现象。

Conclusion: 克服光分流问题可以使钙钛矿顶电池（top cell）在叠层太阳电池中更接近低FF损失状态，从而推动器件效率向热力学极限接近。

Abstract: Perovskite-silicon tandem technology has exceeded the single junction theoretical efficiency limit. However, there is still distance to the thermodynamic limit mainly caused by the fill factor. This work presents a methodology to illustrate the mechanisms of FF loss in perovskite-Si monolithic tandem solar cells. Apart from the series resistance related loss characterized by electroluminescence, another loss factor is from the photoshunt, a phenomenon in which the parallel resistance apparently reduces under illumination in perovskite solar cells due to the moderate charge transport layer mobility. In addoition, the two-diode property of the Si cell can also influence the FF of tandem devices. The photoshunt can be hidden when the bottom cell is over illuminated, which explains highly efficient tandem solar cells are usually bottom cell limited. This work outlines strategies that overcoming the photoshunt issue can move the perovskite top cell closer to low FF losses in tandem solar cells.

</details>


### [91] [Electron-phonon coupling across the TMD/hBN van der Waals interface](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24139)
*G. Gatti,C. Berthod,J. Issing,M. Straub,S. Mandloi,Y. Alexanian,J. Avila,P. Dudin,T. K. Kim,M. D. Watson,C. Cacho,K. Watanabe,T. Taniguchi,W. Wang,N. Clark,R. Gorbachev,N. Ubrig,I. Gutierrez-Lezama,A. F. Morpurgo,A. Tamai,F. Baumberger*

Method: 采用角分辨光电子能谱（angle resolved photoemission, ARPES）实验技术，观测单层TMD（过渡金属二硫族化物）中准粒子的能带结构；同时发展了一个修正的Fröhlich模型（modified Fröhlich model），用于与实验谱函数（spectral functions）进行半定量对比分析。

Result: 在单层TMD中观测到了复制带（replica bands），这是长程电子-声子相互作用（long-range electron-phonon interaction）的明确标志。修正的Fröhlich模型与实验谱函数取得了半定量一致，表明远程电子-声子耦合是hBN界面的普适性质。

Conclusion: 远程电子-声子耦合是hBN界面的普适属性，该发现对二维材料中的电子迁移率（electron mobilities）、超导（superconductivity）以及moiré关联相（moiré correlated phases）等物理现象具有重要启示。

Abstract: Many-body interactions can couple electronic states in one layer with collective excitations in the adjacent layer, providing a route to tailor properties of heterostructures. However, detecting and quantifying interlayer many-body interactions proved a major challenge. Here, we demonstrate that quasiparticles in monolayer transition metal dichalcogenides (TMDs) are dressed by a remote cloud of phonons in the adjacent hexagonal boron nitride slab. Using angle resolved photoemission, we identify replica bands in the TMDs which are a clear fingerprint of long-range electron-phonon interaction. We develop a modified Fröhlich model that shows semi-quantitative agreement with the experimental spectral functions. Our analysis shows that remote electron-phonon coupling is a generic property of interfaces with hBN. This has implications for electron mobilities in 2D materials, for superconductivity and possibly for moiré correlated phases.

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 单层MoS₂中亚稳T'相在强热力学驱动下仍表现出显著的持久性（persistence），但其背后动力学阻滞（kinetic arrest）的微观机制尚不清楚。

Method: 采用机器学习加速分子动力学（machine learning-accelerated molecular dynamics）与第一性原理计算（first-principles calculations）相结合的方法进行模拟分析。

Result: 发现动力学阻滞源于硫-硫（S-S）排斥作用在成核（nucleation）和晶界传播（grain boundary propagation）过程中施加的高能垒；硫空位（sulfur vacancies）在部分界面可降低能垒，但在最稳定的ZZ-Mo|-界面因热力学不稳定而无法加速转变；空位反而迁移进入T'相，使推进前沿保持无缺陷；纳米结构模拟证实H相成核始于角或边缘，所有生长前沿均呈现ZZ-Mo|-构型。

Conclusion: 二维材料中的相变由缺陷与移动界面的局部兼容性（local compatibility）控制，而非全局缺陷浓度（global defect concentration），为通过界面特异性设计（interface-specific design）调控结构转变提供了新范式。

Abstract: The metastable T' phase in monolayer MoS2 exhibits remarkable persistence despite a strong thermodynamic driving force toward the stable H phase. Using machine learning-accelerated molecular dynamics and first-principles calculations, we reveal that this kinetic arrest originates from repulsive S-S interactions, which impose high energy barriers during both nucleation and grain boundary propagation. While sulfur vacancies can alleviate these barriers in certain interfaces, they fail to accelerate transformation at the most stable interface, ZZ-Mo|-, due to their thermodynamic instability there. Instead, vacancies migrate into the T' phase, leaving the advancing front defect-free. Direct simulations of nanostructures confirm that H-phase nucleation initiates at corners or edges, and all observed growth fronts adopt the ZZ-Mo|- configuration, consistent with its low interfacial energy but slow kinetics. Our work establishes that phase transformation in 2D materials is governed not by global defect concentration, but by the local compatibility between defects and moving interfaces, offering a new paradigm for controlling structural transitions through interface-specific design.

Abstract: Metal-insulator transitions (MITs) in correlated oxides offer immense potential for next-generation Mottronic devices. However, their integration into practical applications is often hindered by the coupling of MITs with symmetry-lowering structural phase transitions, which limits switching speed and endurance. In this study, we engineered an iso-symmetric MIT on average in epitaxial rutile VO2 thin films via an in-situ nitrogen doping strategy. Nitrogen incorporation effectively suppresses V-V dimerization, enabling an iso-symmetric MIT, while preserving the original crystal symmetry. Furthermore, in-operando time-resolved optical reflectivity measurements revealed a shortened switching time in nitrogen-doped films, highlighting their enhanced performance. Our findings provide critical insights into the underlying mechanisms of MITs and introduce anion doping as a powerful tool for tailoring phase transitions in strongly correlated electron systems. This approach opens new avenues for the development of high-performance electronic and photonic devices.

### [94] [Atomistic Mechanisms of Temperature-Dependent Ion Track Formation in Gallium Nitride under Swift Heavy Ion Irradiation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24288)
*Jiayu Liang,Shaowei He,Wenlong Liao,Tan Shi,Hang Zang,Yonghong Li,Xiaojun Fu,Chuanjian Yao,Chaohui He,Jianan Wei,Huan He*

TL;DR: 本文通过双温模型与分子动力学模拟的耦合方法，系统研究了宽温域下快速重离子辐照氮化镓（gallium nitride, GaN）产生离子径迹（ion track）的微观机制，揭示了温度驱动的径迹形态转变、原子尺度分解行为以及闪锌矿（zincblende）纳米畴与位错网络的关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用双温模型（two-temperature model）与分子动力学（molecular dynamics）模拟的耦合方法，解析了宽温域下快速重离子辐照诱发离子径迹生成的完整过程。

Result: 观测到温度驱动的离子径迹形态转变：从不连续片段演变为由孤立纳米气泡（nanobubble）构成的连续径迹，最终形成完全连续的通道。低电子阻止损失条件下，升温增强径迹可视性、增大径迹半径并促进纳米气泡形成；高电子阻止损失条件下，300 K时即出现由不连续纳米气泡组成的连续径迹，随后热激活转变为连续通道并进一步径向膨胀。原子尺度上，辐照导致纤锌矿（wurtzite）GaN分解为Ga团簇和N2分子，富Ga区与再结晶纤锌矿相在气泡界面附近累积，N2优先偏析于气泡核心。闪锌矿纳米畴在离子径迹周围成核，与辐照诱导的位错网络（尤其是螺位错）呈现强空间关联。

Conclusion: 温度是调控GaN中离子径迹形态的关键因素；闪锌矿纳米畴与螺位错（screw dislocation）网络的关联可能为漏电流提供通路并增加单事件烧毁（single-event burnout）的敏感性。

Abstract: The radiation tolerance of gallium nitride under extreme conditions is critical for its deployment in next-generation electronic and optoelectronic devices, yet the microscopic mechanisms governing swift heavy ion induced damage at elevated temperatures remain poorly understood. Therefore, this study employs a coupled approach including the two-temperature model and molecular dynamics simulations to resolve the entire processes of ion track generation induced by swift heavy ions irradiation across a wide temperature range. A temperature-driven morphological transition of ion tracks, evolving from discontinuous segments to continuous tracks composed of isolated nanobubbles, and ultimately to fully continuous channels is observed. Under lower electronic stopping loss of 430 MeV Kr irradiation, increasing temperature significantly enhances track visibility, enlarges track radii and promotes nanobubble formation. For higher electronic stopping conditions of 1171 MeV Ta irradiation, continuous ion tracks consisting of discontinuous nanobubbles (~1.5 nm radius) emerge already at 300 K, followed by a thermally activated transition into continuous channels with further radial expansion. At the atomic scale, SHI irradiation induces decomposition of wurtzite GaN into Ga clusters and N2 molecules along the ion trajectory, with Ga-rich regions and recrystallized wurtzite phases accumulating near bubble interfaces, while N2 preferentially segregates within bubble cores. Additionally, zincblende nanodomains nucleate around ion tracks and exhibit strong spatial correlation with radiation-induced dislocation networks, particularly screw dislocations, providing potential pathways for leakage current and increased susceptibility to single-event burnout.

Here, first-order reversal curve (FORC) measurements are used to map how these interactions govern magnetization reversal in square arrays as the element shape and spacing are varied. The FORC diagrams show that some geometries reverse more uniformly, whereas others exhibit broader, more asymmetric responses, indicating stronger interaction effects and more complex reversal pathways. Abstract: Group-V monolayer materials exhibit intriguing electronic and optical properties, influenced by their unique crystal symmetries and structural phases. ### [97] [Step- and terrace-resolved crystal truncation rod scattering from vicinal surfaces under coherent heteroepitaxy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24604)
*Junlin Wu,Erqi Xu,Qihui Lin,Jiaqing Yue,Jiale Wang,Zihao Xu,Guangxu Ju*

Main category: cond-mat.mtrl-sci

TL;DR: 本文发展了一个适用于相干应变异质外延薄膜邻晶面的晶体截断杆（CTR）散射的通用理论，将薄膜干涉条纹、弹性晶格畸变、台阶有序、表面重构及实时生长演化纳入统一描述，并通过InGaN/GaN实例展示了其对静态与实时CTR测量的定量解释能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有模型（如Nagai模型）对邻晶面CTR散射的描述不够完整，缺乏对相干应变薄膜中弹性畸变、台阶有序、表面重构等复杂因素的统一处理。

Method: 构建了一个包含薄膜诱导干涉条纹、全弹性晶格畸变（elastic lattice distortion）、台阶有序（terrace ordering）、表面重构（surface reconstruction）及实时生长演化（real-time growth evolution）的统一理论框架。将Nagai模型与基于弹性力学（elasticity-based）的模型进行对比，分析晶格倾斜与三斜形变的差异。

Result: 两种模型预测的晶格倾斜（lattice tilt）几乎相同，但弹性力学模型额外预测了由剪切应变（shear strain）引起的三斜形变（triclinic deformation）。该形变对镜面CTR影响极小，却显著改变非镜面杆（non-specular rods），使其成为探测相干外延薄膜全弹性状态的高灵敏度探针。此外，邻晶面CTR对台阶有序、表面重构及台阶分辨成分修饰的敏感性在相干薄膜存在下仍然保持稳健。

Conclusion: 该框架能够定量解释静态与实时CTR测量数据，为异质外延生长过程中台阶分辨和台阶分辨的结构与动力学信息提供获取途径。

Abstract: We develop a general theory of crystal truncation rod (CTR) scattering from vicinal surfaces with a coherently strained heteroepitaxial film. The formalism incorporates film-induced interference fringes, full elastic lattice distortion, terrace ordering, surface reconstruction, and real-time growth evolution within a unified description. Comparison between Nagai model and elasticity-based model shows that the lattice tilt is nearly identical in the two approaches, whereas the elasticitybased model predicts an additional triclinic deformation arising from shear strain. This deformation has little effect on specular CTRs but strongly modifies non-specular rods, making them a sensitive probe of the full elastic state of coherent epitaxial films. We further show that the characteristic sensitivity of vicinal CTRs to terrace ordering, surface reconstruction, and terrace-resolved compositional modification remains robust in the presence of a coherent film. Representative calculations for InGaN/GaN demonstrate that the framework enables quantitative interpretation of both static and real-time CTR measurements and provides access to step- and terrace-resolved structural and kinetic information during heteroepitaxial growth.

</details>

Method: 开发了一种两步骤工作流：第一步进行方位角样品旋转（azimuthal sample rotation），第二步结合样品翻转（sample flipping），从而系统性地抑制各向异性引起的伪影。为此自制了样品台，配合Python脚本进行数据采集与处理。

Result: 在两种来自不同研究领域的样品上验证了该工作流的可靠性：一是附着在金属表面的手性分子（chiral molecules attached to metallic surfaces），二是掺入手性间隔分子（chiral spacer molecules）的金属卤化物钙钛矿（metal halide perovskites）。

Conclusion: 该教程提供了完整的样品台设计方案和开源Python脚本，使商用CD光谱仪能够可靠地测量各向异性手性薄膜的真实CD信号，有望推动CD光谱在薄膜手性表征中的广泛应用。

Abstract: Circular Dichroism (CD) spectroscopy has evolved from a purely solution based method towards a powerful tool in the analysis of chiral thin films. Although a straightforward technique, the genuine CD signal is often accompanied by artifacts arising from optical anisotropy and instrumental imperfections. This tutorial presents a two-step workflow that reliably isolates the orientation invariant CD response for anisotropic thin films by combining azimuthal sample rotation with sample flipping. For this purpose, a home-built sample stage was developed, which enables systematic suppression of many anisotropy-induced artifacts in commercial CD spectrophotometers. Both a detailed description of the setup itself as well as the needed python script are provided. The reliability of the workflow is demonstrated on two selected samples from different research fields: chiral molecules attached to metallic surfaces as well as metal halide perovskites incorporating chiral spacer molecules

The high quality of the synthesized heterostructure, together with its type-II band alignment, establishes pentacene/WS2 as a model system for orbital-resolved studies of charge transfer, energy-level renormalization, and non-equilibrium interfacial processes in hybrid organic-inorganic-2D heterostructures.

### [101] [Improved Electrochemical Performance and Diffusion kinetics by Boron-doping in Na$_{0.66}$Mn$_{0.8}$Fe$_{0.2}$O$_{2}$ Layered Cathodes for Sodium-Ion Batteries](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24683)

Method: 采用硼掺杂的Na₀.₆₆Mn₀.₈Fe₀.₂O₂（B-NMFO）作为正极材料；利用恒电流间歇滴定技术（galvanostatic intermittent titration technique, GITT）和循环伏安法（cyclic voltammetry, CV）评估扩散系数；使用温度依赖的弛豫时间分布（distribution of relaxation time, DRT）分析电化学过程中的物理过程；通过密度泛函理论（density functional theory, DFT）计算掺杂能量学与电子性质；采用经典分子动力学（molecular dynamics, MD）模拟研究Na离子输运特性。

Abstract: We report the electrochemical investigation and study the diffusion kinetics of boron doped Na$_{0.66}$Mn$_{0.8}$Fe$_{0.2}$O$_{2}$ (B-NMFO) cathode materials for sodium-ion batteries. Notably, the B-NMFO cathode exhibits improved specific capacity of 163 mAh g$^{-1}$ as compared to 133 mAhg$^{-1}$ at 0.1~C for the NMFO cathode. Further, we observe better capacity retention of 70\% for B-NMFO as compared to the NMFO (60\%) at 1 C after 200 cycles, indicating high structural stability due to the presence of strong B-O bonds. The diffusion coefficient evaluation through galvanostatic intermittent titration technique and cyclic voltammetry, which is found to be in the range of 10$^{-8}$--10$^{-10}$ cm$^{2}$s$^{-1}$. Interestingly, the temperature dependent distribution of relaxation time (DRT) analysis provides a clear understanding about the individual physical processes occurring at different time domains during the electro-chemical testing. Moreover, density functional theory is employed to determine the energetics and the electronic properties of B-NMFO, which suggests that the interstitial tetrahedral sites, especially those next to vacancies, are the dominant incorporation path ways for B in the host structure. Additionally, classical molecular dynamics (MD) simulations are applied to gain insights into the Na-ion transport properties in the bulk structures cathode materials.

### [102] [Remotely programming the weights of a spintronic neural network by a radiofrequency broadcast signal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24561)
*M. Menshawy,D. Sanz-Hernández,L. Mazza,V. Puliafito,G. Finocchio,A. Jenkins,R. Ferreira,L. Benetti,J. Grollier,F. A. Mizrahi*

Main category: cs.ET

TL;DR: 本文提出一种利用广播射频（RF）信号远程编程基于涡旋磁隧道结（vortex-based magnetic tunnel junctions）链中突触权重的方法，无需独立访问线或选择器件，并通过22突触网络在两种任务（手写数字分类与无人机射频信号识别）上展示了硬件可重构性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在内存计算（in-memory computing）中，如何在保持可扩展性的前提下选择性地编程大量非易失性突触权重是一个关键挑战。

Method: 通过共享带状线（strip line）施加广播射频信号，基于涡旋核心极性（vortex-core polarity）的频率选择性翻转，对11个串联的涡旋磁隧道结链进行远程编程，从而在频率复用（frequency-multiplexed）的射频输入上重塑加权求和结果。

Result: 在22突触网络中，数字优化配置在手写数字分类上达到94.91±0.26%的准确率，但在无人机射频签名识别上仅为13.17±0.47%；无人机优化配置在无人机任务上达到97.33±0.62%，但在数字任务上仅为47.59±1.5%。

Conclusion: 广播射频编程提供了一种紧凑且可扩展的途径，用于实现快速可重构的自旋神经形态硬件（spintronic neuromorphic hardware）。

Abstract: Selectively programming large number of non-volatile synaptic weights without compromising scalability is a key challenge for in-memory computing. Here, we demonstrate remote programming of synaptic weights in series-connected chains of 11 vortex-based magnetic tunnel junctions using broadcast radiofrequency signals applied through a shared strip line. The programming relies on frequency-selective reversal of the vortex-core polarity and therefore does not require individual access lines or selector devices. By reconfiguring the binary states of these chains, we reshape the weighted sums they perform on frequency-multiplexed RF inputs. Using a 22-synapse network composed of two such chains, we remotely reconfigure the same hardware to perform two distinct tasks: handwritten-digit classification and drone RF-signature identification. The digit-optimized configuration reaches 94.91 +/- 0.26% accuracy on handwritten digits but only 13.17 +/- 0.47% on drone RF signatures, whereas the drone-optimized configuration reaches 97.33 +/- 0.62% on drones but only 47.59 +/- 1.5% on digits. Broadcast RF programming thus provides a compact and scalable route to rapidly reconfigurable spintronic neuromorphic hardware.

### [103] [Passage of particles through matter and the effective straggling-function: High-fidelity accelerated simulation via Physics-Informed Machine Learning](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22993)
*Oleksandr Borysov,Rotem Dover,Eilam Gross,Nilotpal Kakati,Noam Tal Hod*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文提出PHIN-GAN，一种基于物理信息的生成对抗网络（physics-informed generative adversarial network），通过推导Landau分布的解析概率密度函数并引入参数化分布级学习目标，实现了对粒子-物质相互作用的高保真、无损生成建模，其计算成本仅为传统蒙特卡洛模拟工具GEANT4的一小部分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高保真粒子-物质相互作用模拟是多个物理学科的核心理论参考，但为当前及未来实验规模生成合成数据集的计算开销已变得难以承受。因此需要一种兼具高保真度和计算效率的生成式方法。

Method: 方法核心包括：(1) 推导一组与Landau“离散函数（straggling function）”对应的解析概率密度函数（probability density functions），首次实现其在全相空间（phase-space）上的连续评估；(2) 利用这些解析形式强制施加一个参数化分布级学习目标（parametric distribution-level learning objective）；(3) 构建物理信息生成对抗网络（PHIN-GAN）架构，将上述物理先验嵌入生成过程。

Result: PHIN-GAN在保持与GEANT4同等高保真度的前提下，实现了无损生成建模，同时计算成本仅为后者的极小部分。该方法具有可泛化性（generalizable）、可解释性（interpretable）和可扩展性（scalable）。

Conclusion: PHIN-GAN作为一种基于第一性原理（first principles）的概念验证方法，为高保真、低成本的粒子-物质相互作用模拟提供了可行的生成式替代方案，有望缓解大规模实验中的数据生成瓶颈。

Abstract: High-fidelity simulation of particle-matter interactions provides the essential theoretical reference for diverse physics disciplines, yet generating synthetic datasets at the scale of current and future experiments has become prohibitive. Here, we introduce PHIN-GAN, a novel physics-informed generative adversarial network designed to address this challenge. We derive a set of analytical probability density functions, that effectively describe the ``straggling function'' identified with Landau. For the first time, this enables their continuous evaluation across the entire phase-space. These analytical forms are leveraged to enforce a parametric distribution-level learning objective. Rooted in first principles, PHIN-GAN offers a generalizable, interpretable and scalable proof-of-concept approach for a lossless generative model that maintains the high fidelity of the standard-bearer for simulating such interactions, namely GEANT4, at a fraction of the computational cost.

</details>


### [104] [Incorporating Inelasticity Reconstruction into Neutrino Mass Ordering Studies with IceCube](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23055)
*J. H. Peterson,M. Jacquart*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本研究开发了两种新的非弹性度（inelasticity）重建算法——基于图神经网络（graph neural network, GNN）和二维卷积神经网络集成（ensemble of 2D convolutional neural networks），用于分离大气中微子与反中微子，并利用物质效应（matter effect）探测中微子质量顺序（neutrino mass ordering, NMO）。研究评估了将非弹性度作为第四观测量（与能量、方向和味共同使用）对IceCube DeepCore及即将升级的IceCube Upgrade探测器在NMO测量灵敏度上的提升效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 地球物质对大气中微子与反中微子的振荡影响取决于中微子质量顺序（NMO），而IceCube探测器预期探测到的中微子数量多于反中微子，因此物质效应可用于探测NMO。此外，中微子与反中微子因手性（chirality）相反，其相互作用中的非弹性度（inelasticity）分布存在差异，理论上可用于统计分离二者，但此前尚未在IceCube DeepCore分析中被利用。

Method: 开发了两种新的非弹性度重建算法：一种基于图神经网络（GNN），另一种基于二维卷积神经网络集成（ensemble of 2D convolutional neural networks）。将重建的非弹性度作为第四观测量，与粒子能量、方向和味（flavor）共同用于计算NMO灵敏度。

Result: 展示了两种重建算法（GNN与二维CNN集成）的开发过程及其性能表现。通过引入非弹性度作为额外观测量，计算了在IceCube DeepCore及未来IceCube Upgrade探测器上中微子质量顺序（NMO）测量的新灵敏度，并评估了非弹性度对测量效果的提升程度。

Conclusion: 非弹性度可作为有效观测量提升IceCube DeepCore及IceCube Upgrade探测器对中微子质量顺序（NMO）的测量灵敏度，两种基于神经网络的算法能够在统计上分离中微子与反中微子，从而增强物质效应对NMO的探测能力。

Abstract: Earth's matter affects the oscillation of atmospheric neutrinos and antineutrinos differently depending on the neutrino mass ordering (NMO). As more neutrinos than antineutrinos are expected to be detected in the IceCube detector, this matter effect can be used to probe the NMO. The fraction of energy transferred to the nucleon during a neutrino interaction, known as the inelasticity, has a different distribution for neutrinos and antineutrinos because of their opposite chirality. This can in theory be used to statistically separate neutrinos from antineutrinos, but hasn't been exploited in IceCube DeepCore analyses yet. To this end, two new inelasticity reconstructions were developed using a graph neural network and an ensemble of two-dimensional convolutional neural networks. This presentation discusses the development and performances of these reconstruction algorithms. The inelasticity is then used as a fourth observable, along with the particle energy, direction and flavor, to calculate new NMO sensitivities and determine the impact of adding the inelasticity in the measurement of the NMO with the IceCube DeepCore and upcoming IceCube Upgrade detectors.

</details>


### [105] [Search for heavy resonances decaying into two Higgs bosons in the $\mathrm{b}\bar{\mathrm{b}}\,τ^{+}τ^{-}$ final state in proton-proton collisions at $\sqrt{s}=13~\text{TeV}$ with the CMS detector](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23502)
*Ganesh Parida*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本文基于CMS探测器在LHC上收集的13 TeV质子-质子对撞数据（积分亮度138 fb⁻¹），搜索质量范围为1–4.5 TeV的窄宽度共振态衰变至双希格斯玻色子（HH）的过程，具体通道为X→HH→bb̅ τ⁺τ⁻。观测数据与标准模型本底预期一致，在95%置信水平上对共振HH产生截面设定了上限，并在1.4–4.5 TeV质量区间内给出了当前LHC最灵敏的限制。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 对TeV能级重共振态（massive resonances）衰变至希格斯玻色子对（HH）的搜索，是检验超出标准模型（Beyond Standard Model, BSM）新物理的重要途径，例如某些扩展的希格斯模型或复合希格斯模型预言的额外重标量粒子。

Method: 利用CMS探测器在2016–2018年采集的质子-质子（proton-proton）对撞数据，质心能量为13 TeV，总积分亮度（integrated luminosity）为138 fb⁻¹。分析选取的末态通道为X→HH→bb̅ τ⁺τ⁻，即一个希格斯玻色子衰变为一对底夸克（bottom quarks），另一个衰变为一对τ轻子。

Result: 观测数据与标准模型（Standard Model, SM）本底预期在统计上一致。在95%置信水平（confidence level, CL）上，对质量介于1–4.5 TeV之间的共振HH产生过程设定了产生截面的上限。在1.4–4.5 TeV质量范围内，该分析给出了LHC上对X→HH→bb̅ τ⁺τ⁻衰变通道目前最灵敏的限制结果。

Conclusion: 在搜索质量范围内未发现窄宽度共振态存在的显著证据，所设上限对约束相关超出标准模型的新物理模型具有重要参考价值。

Abstract: A search is presented for massive narrow-width resonances in the mass range of $1\text{-}4.5\,\text{TeV}$ decaying into pairs of Higgs bosons (HH), using proton-proton collision data at a center-of-mass energy of $13\,\text{TeV}$ collected with the CMS detector at the LHC during the $2016\text{-}2018$ data-taking. The data correspond to an integrated luminosity of $138~\mathrm{fb}^{-1}$. The analysis targets final states where one Higgs boson decays into a pair of bottom quarks and the other into a pair of tau leptons, $\mathrm{X}\rightarrow\mathrm{HH}\rightarrow \mathrm{b}\bar{\mathrm{b}}\,τ^{+}τ^{-}$. The observed data are found to be consistent with standard model background expectations. Upper limits at $95\%$ confidence level (CL) are set on the production cross section for resonant HH production for masses between $1$ and $4.5\,\text{TeV}$. This analysis sets the most sensitive LHC limits to date on $\mathrm{X}\rightarrow\mathrm{HH}\rightarrow \mathrm{b}\bar{\mathrm{b}}\,τ^{+}τ^{-}$ decays in the mass range of $1.4$ to $4.5\,\text{TeV}$.

</details>

### [107] [Initial Performance of the E320 Tracker](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23805)
*Oleksandr Borysov,Sébastien Corde,Gal Evenzur,Alexander Knetsch,Alon Levi,Sebastian Meuren,Nathaly Nofech-Mozes,Ivan Rajkovic,Sheldon Rego,David A. Reis,Arka Santra,Tania Smorodnikova,Doug W. Storey,Noam Tal Hod,Roman Urmanov*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 本研究在SLAC实验320中，利用缩小的ALPIDE芯片追踪探测器原型，在极高背景噪声（约1.7/mm²）条件下成功测量了电子-激光碰撞产生的非线性Breit-Wheeler深隧穿过程的正电子信号，信号率为每发(1.20±0.06统计±0.56系统)×10⁻¹个正电子，达到主实验预期水平，且与模拟结果吻合。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 测量电子-激光碰撞中通过非线性Breit-Wheeler深隧穿过程（nonlinear Breit-Wheeler deep-tunneling process）产生的单个正电子，验证在SLAC实验320（FACET-II RF LINAC）中实现该测量的可行性。

Method: 使用由五层单个ALPIDE芯片构成的缩小型追踪探测器原型（2024年8月安装）；以束流电子在薄铍箔中转换轫致辐射光子产生的正电子作为非线性Breit-Wheeler过程的代理信号；采用基于Hough变换（Hough-Transform）种子算法结合探测器体积内的直线拟合进行追踪。

Result: 测得信号率为(1.20±0.06统计±0.56系统)×10⁻¹个正电子/发，与主实验预期非线性Breit-Wheeler信号率相当；在约1.7/mm²的极端背景命中密度下实现测量（主实验预期密度至少低一倍）；箔片收回时假阳性信号率比信号率低四个数量级；空间追踪分辨率约5微米，可表征正电子能谱。

Conclusion: 该追踪探测器能够在极高背景噪声环境下有效测量正电子信号，实验数据与模拟结果兼容，验证了在SLAC实验320中利用此探测器测量非线性Breit-Wheeler过程正电子的可行性。

Abstract: Our recent study discussed the prospects for measuring single positrons produced in electron-laser collisions via the nonlinear Breit-Wheeler deep-tunneling process in the SLAC Experiment 320 at the FACET-II RF LINAC. In this work, we demonstrate how a tracking detector, that is a scaled-down version of the one discussed in the prospective simulation study, enables the measurement. This prototype detector, installed in Aug 2024, is built out of five layers of single ALPIDE chips. The data are taken from several standalone runs completed in Nov 2024 and Feb 2025. We use positrons generated through conversion of Bremsstrahlung photons as a proxy to the nonlinear Breit-Wheeler process. These positrons are produced by the beam electrons in a thin Beryllium foil close to the experiment's interaction point. The tracking approach used in this initial work is based on a Hough-Transform seeding algorithm followed by a straight line fit confined to the detector volume. Even with this relatively simple approach, we are able to measure a signal rate of $(1.20\pm0.06_{stat.}\pm0.56_{syst.})\times10^{-1}$ positrons per shot. This signal rate is comparable to the nonlinear Breit-Wheeler rate expected in the main experiment. Notably, the measurement is achieved under an extreme, unprecedented background hit density of ~1.7/mm$^2$, unlike the main experiment, where at least a twice lower density is expected. This large background is mostly due to secondary particles produced when the large flux of Bremsstrahlung photons interacts with the material of the beamline elements. When the foil is retracted, the false-positive signal rate is shown to be four orders of magnitude smaller than the signal rate. We further show that the high spatial tracking resolution of ~5 micron allows to characterize the positrons' spectra. The results are compared to simulations, which are found to be compatible with the data.

</details>


### [108] [Search for associated production of a Higgs boson and two vector bosons via vector boson scattering at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24531)
*CMS Collaboration*

Main category: hep-ex

TL;DR: 该论文利用CMS实验在质心能量13 TeV、积分亮度138 fb⁻¹的质子-质子对撞数据，搜索通过矢量玻色子散射（VBS）产生的希格斯玻色子（H）与两个矢量玻色子（V=W, Z）的联合产生过程。在95%置信水平下，排除VVHH耦合修正因子κ_VV的标准模型外区间（观测值：0.40 < κ_VV < 1.60），并进一步对κ_2W和κ_2Z单独耦合修正因子及二者参数平面施加约束。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 直接测量希格斯玻色子与两个矢量玻色子之间的四顶点耦合（VVHH interaction）是检验电弱对称性破缺机制和超出标准模型新物理的重要途径。本研究旨在利用矢量玻色子散射过程首次独立约束该耦合强度。

Method: 基于CMS探测器在√s=13 TeV、积分亮度138 fb⁻¹的质子-质子对撞数据，选取包含两个符合VBS特征的前向喷注、来自 boosted H → b夸克对衰变的大半径喷注以及来自V衰变的0、1或2个带电轻子的事件。

Result: 在95%置信水平下，假设其他耦合取标准模型值，观测（预期）排除VVHH耦合修正因子κ_VV的区间为0.40 < κ_VV < 1.60（0.34 < κ_VV < 1.66）。同时给出了对κ_2W和κ_2Z单独耦合修正因子的约束，以及κ_2W-κ_2Z参数平面的允许区域。

Conclusion: 该分析首次通过矢量玻色子散射过程对VVHH相互作用建立了一种新的探针（novel probe），为检验标准模型电弱规范耦合结构提供了独立的实验约束。

Abstract: A search for Higgs boson (H) production in association with two vector bosons (V = W, Z) via vector boson scattering (VBS) is presented using proton-proton collision data collected at $\sqrt{s}$ = 13 TeV by the CMS experiment, corresponding to an integrated luminosity of 138 fb$^{-1}$. Events containing two forward jets consistent with VBS, a large-radius jet from the decay of a boosted H to a pair of b quarks, and 0, 1, or 2 charged leptons coming from V decays are selected. The process is excluded at 95% CL for observed (expected) values of the VVHH coupling modifier $κ_\mathrm{VV}$ outside the interval 0.40 $\lt$ $κ_\mathrm{VV}$ $\lt$ 1.60 (0.34 $\lt$ $κ_\mathrm{VV}$ $\lt$ 1.66), assuming standard model values for all other couplings, thus establishing a novel probe of the VVHH interaction. Constraints are also set on the individual $κ_\mathrm{2W}$ and $κ_\mathrm{2Z}$ coupling modifiers, and on the allowed region in the $κ_\mathrm{2W}$-$κ_\mathrm{2Z}$ plane.

### [109] [High-Precision Ground Characterization of Test-Mass Magnetic Properties for the Taiji Gravitational Wave Mission via a Physics-Informed Neural Framework](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23510)
*Chang Liu,Qiong Deng,Huadong Li,Liwei Yang,Xiaodong Peng,Ziren Luo,Yuzhu Zhang,Chen Gao,Xiaotong Wei,Minghui Du,Zihao Xiao,Peng Xu,Bo Liang,Zhi Wang,Li-e Qiang*

Main category: astro-ph.IM

TL;DR: 针对太极（Taiji）空间引力波探测任务中测试质量（test mass）的剩余磁矩和体积磁化率的地面高精度表征问题，提出了一种AI增强的可微分加权最小二乘（AI-WLS）框架。该方法融合膨胀一维残差网络与可微分析物理求解器，在保留磁参数到扭矩响应精确线性映射的同时，自主识别并抑制受污染的数据段。在长春光机所扭摆实验装置实测噪声上验证，估计误差满足太极地面测试要求。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 太极（Taiji）空间引力波探测任务的最终灵敏度部分受限于引力参考传感器（gravitational reference sensor, GRS）的残余加速度噪声，其中测试质量与波动环境磁场之间的耦合是关键杂散力来源之一。因此，在发射前对测试质量的剩余磁矩（$\vec{m}_r$）和体积磁化率（$χ$）进行高精度地面表征是核心步骤。然而，扭摆（torsion-pendulum）设施的固有非平稳有色背景噪声（non-stationary, colored background noise）会系统性地偏差经典估计方法（如普通最小二乘OLS和卡尔曼滤波KF）的结果，这一问题亟待解决。

Method: 提出一种AI增强的可微分加权最小二乘（AI-Enhanced Differentiable Weighted Least Squares, AI-WLS）框架：该架构将膨胀一维残差网络（dilated one-dimensional residual network）作为动态噪声评估器，与一个完全可微的分析物理求解器（fully differentiable analytical physical solver）相融合。该方法在保留从磁参数到扭矩响应的精确线性映射的同时，能够自主识别并抑制受污染的数据片段。

Result: 在长春光学精密机械与物理研究所（Changchun Institute of Optics, Fine Mechanics and Physics）为太极任务开发的扭摆设施实测噪声（扭矩灵敏度达$10^{-13}\,\mathrm{N\cdot m\,Hz^{-1/2}}$量级）上验证，AI-WLS框架将$\vec{m}_r$的最大绝对估计误差限制在$4.46\times 10^{-10}\,\mathrm{A\cdot m^2}$，$χ$的最大绝对估计误差限制在$7.8\times 10^{-8}$，同时满足太极地面测试要求。

Conclusion: AI-WLS框架能够有效克服扭摆设施非平稳有色噪声对经典估计方法的系统性偏差，在太极任务测试质量的磁参数地面表征中实现了满足任务需求的估计精度。该方法为空间引力波探测任务中关键传感器组件的发射前标定提供了一条可行的技术路径。

Abstract: Taiji is a gravitational wave detection mission in space initiated by the Chinese Academy of Sciences, which will open the millihertz window through a heliocentric triangular constellation of three drag-free spacecraft. Its ultimate sensitivity is determined partly by the residual acceleration noise of the gravitational reference sensors (GRS), within which the coupling between the test-mass and the fluctuating environmental magnetic field constitutes one of the key stray-force contributions. Following the path established by the LISA and TianQin teams, high-precision ground characterization of remanent magnetic moment $\vec{m}_r$ and volume susceptibility $χ$ of the test masses is a central step in the Taiji pre-launch test program. A persistent challenge for this characterization is the non-stationary, colored background noise inherent to torsion-pendulum facilities, which systematically biases classical Ordinary Least Squares (OLS) and Kalman filter (KF) estimators. We propose an AI-enhanced Differentiable Weighted Least Squares (AI-WLS) framework that fuses a dilated one-dimensional residual network, acting as a dynamic noise evaluator, with a fully differentiable analytical physical solver. This architecture preserves the exact linear mapping from the magnetic parameters to the torque response while autonomously identifying and suppressing contaminated data segments. Validated on real measured noise from the Changchun Institute of Optics, Fine Mechanics and Physics torsion-pendulum facility developed for Taiji, which achieves a torque sensitivity of order $10^{-13}\,\mathrm{N\cdot m\,Hz^{-1/2}}$, the AI-WLS framework bounds the maximum absolute estimation errors at $4.46\times 10^{-10}\,\mathrm{A\cdot m^2}$ for $\vec{m}_r$ and $7.8\times 10^{-8}$ for $χ$, satisfying Taiji's ground-test requirements on all these parameters simultaneously.

### [110] [Diagnostic Disagreement as an Information-Projection Divergence: An Information-Theoretic Reading of the Quiet-Sun Temperature Ratio](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23752)
*V. Edmonds*

Main category: astro-ph.SR

TL;DR: 该论文将宁静日冕电子温度比 R ≈ 2.4 解读为日冕电子分布函数向 Maxwellian 族投影的两个诊断之间的相对熵测量，并建立了投影差异与 Kullback-Leibler 散度及 Itakura-Saito 距离之间的解析关系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 宁静日冕的电子温度比 R（EUV 电离温度与射电亮温度之比）在八年的太阳周期中保持稳定（≈ 2.4），这一现象缺乏理论解释。作者试图从信息论和统计力学（statistical mechanics）的角度，将 R 解读为两个诊断投影之间的相对熵（relative entropy）测量。

Method: 采用 kappa 分布（kappa distribution）作为日冕电子非平衡分布模型，在平均能量（mean-energy）约定下，利用 Fleishman & Kuznetsov (2014) 给出的射电端闭式解和 Dudík et al. (2014) 强度比包络中的 EUV 端有效温度表达式，计算真实分布与其两个 Maxwellian 投影之间的 Kullback-Leibler 散度（Kullback-Leibler divergence），并推导其差值的解析形式。

Result: 在 κ = 2.5 时，两个 Kullback-Leibler 散度分别为 0.32 和 1.20 nats；其差值满足 ΔD_KL = (3/2)[R_0 - ln R_0 - 1] = (3/2) d_IS(T_eff, T_core)，其中 R_0 ≡ κ/(κ - 3/2) 为理想闭式比，d_IS 为 Itakura-Saito 距离（Itakura-Saito distance）。

Conclusion: 该恒等式可用于描述两个诊断投影同一非平衡分布不同矩的观测系统；R 持续八年的稳定性反映了投影结构本身的稳定性。

Abstract: The quiet-Sun coronal electron-temperature ratio $R \equiv T_\mathrm{EUV}/T_B \approx 2.4$, stable across an eight-year solar cycle, is read here as a measurement of relative entropy between two diagnostic projections of the coronal electron distribution onto the one-parameter Maxwellian family. The EUV ionization temperature is a moment-matching projection against a Bethe-type ionization kernel; the radio brightness temperature is the Rayleigh-Jeans source function of thermal bremsstrahlung. For a kappa distribution in the mean-energy convention, Fleishman & Kuznetsov (2014) give the radio-side projection in closed form as $T_B = T_\mathrm{core}$; the EUV side returns $T_\mathrm{eff}$ up to a shape-dependent correction within the Dudík et al. (2014) intensity-ratio envelope. At $κ= 2.5$ the Kullback-Leibler divergences between the true distribution and its two Maxwellian projections evaluate to $0.32$ and $1.20$ nats, and their difference satisfies $ΔD_\mathrm{KL} = (3/2)[R_0 - \ln R_0 - 1] = (3/2) d_\mathrm{IS}(T_\mathrm{eff}, T_\mathrm{core})$, where $R_0 \equiv κ/(κ- 3/2)$ is the ideal closed-form ratio and $d_\mathrm{IS}$ is the Itakura-Saito distance. The identity is offered as an analytical reference for observational systems in which two diagnostics project different moments of a common non-equilibrium distribution; the eight-year stability of $R$ expresses a stability of that projection structure.

</details>

### [111] [Fraunhofer Patterns in Atomic Josephson Junctions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22923)
*Kevin T. Geier,Giampiero Marchegiani,Vijay Pal Singh,Juan Polo,Luigi Amico*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文展示了在驱动型原子约瑟夫森结（driven atomic Josephson junctions）中，合成磁场（synthetic magnetic fields）能够诱导临界电流的夫琅禾费型调制（Fraunhofer-like modulations），并通过数值模拟揭示了约瑟夫森涡旋（Josephson vortices）在空间调制电流分布中的作用。尽管该现象与超导器件中的夫琅禾费图案（Fraunhofer patterns）有相似之处，但超流体的中性本质使其展现出独特特征。研究结果为物质波电路（matter-wave circuits）理解约瑟夫森结中的空间相干性（spatial coherence）开辟了新途径，对新型量子技术发展具有基础意义。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管冷原子体系中的约瑟夫森效应（Josephson effect）已在多种情境下被广泛研究，但合成电磁场（synthetic electromagnetic fields）中的原子约瑟夫森结仍基本未被探索。本研究旨在填补这一空白，考察合成磁场对原子约瑟夫森结临界电流的调制效应。

Method: 作者通过数值模拟方法，研究了合成磁场作用下原子约瑟夫森结中的空间干涉机制，并分析了约瑟夫森涡旋对空间调制电流分布形成的贡献。

Result: 研究发现合成磁场可以诱导临界电流出现夫琅禾费型调制，与超导器件中的夫琅禾费图案具有类比性，但由于超流体的电中性本质，该效应展现出独特的特征。

Conclusion: 该工作为物质波电路深入理解约瑟夫森结中的空间相干性提供了新途径，对于开发新型量子技术具有基础性意义。

Abstract: Driven atomic Josephson junctions allow one to monitor phase-coherent dynamics with unprecedented control and flexibility of the system's physical conditions. While cold-atom manifestations of the Josephson effect have been extensively studied in a wide variety of settings, atomic Josephson junctions in synthetic electromagnetic fields remain largely unexplored. Here, we show that synthetic magnetic fields can induce Fraunhofer-like modulations of the critical current in atomic Josephson junctions. Although this effect presents analogies to the Fraunhofer patterns found in superconducting devices, distinctive features emerge due to the neutral nature of the superfluid. We investigate the underlying spatial interference mechanisms and elucidate the role of Josephson vortices in the formation of spatially modulated current distributions based on numerical simulations. Our results open up new avenues for matter-wave circuits to deepen our understanding of spatial coherence in Josephson junctions, which are fundamental to the development of novel quantum technologies.

</details>


### [112] [Realizing multi-orbital Emery models with ultracold atoms](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22955)
*Conall McCabe,Jamie Boyd,Kaizhao Wang,Martin Lebrat,Cindy Regal,Adam Kaufman,Ana Maria Rey,Lukas Homeier*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于光超晶格（optical superlattice）的量子模拟器架构，利用超冷费米子（ultracold fermions）实现三带Emery模型（three-band Emery model），从而模拟铜氧化物高温超导（high-temperature superconductivity）中的多轨道哈伯德物理（multi-orbital Hubbard physics），并通过量子蒙特卡罗模拟、量子行走和哈密顿学习等方法验证其可行性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过渡金属氧化物中强关联电子（strongly-correlated electrons）会产生高温超导等涌现现象，而仅用单带Hubbard模型不足以完整描述铜氧化物（cuprates）中铜与氧轨道的相互作用。因此，需要实现更为真实的、包含多轨道描述的Emery模型，但现有的超冷原子量子模拟器尚难以实现此类多轨道Hubbard模型。

Method: 提出一种光学超晶格（optical superlattice）架构，通过晶格光束的可控干涉来工程化轨道自由度，再现铜氧化物能带结构的关键特征，并实现对轨道依赖相互作用（orbital-dependent interactions）和电荷转移能（charge-transfer energy）的独立控制。利用量子行走（quantum walks）对标定出的紧束缚模型（tight-binding model）进行基准验证，采用行列式量子蒙特卡罗（determinant quantum Monte Carlo）研究未掺杂（undoped）体系的有限温度热力学性质，并应用哈密顿学习（Hamiltonian learning）协议从实验实现的Emery模型中推断出有效的单带Hubbard模型。

Result: 单粒子量子行走可有效基准测试所得到的紧束缚模型。行列式量子蒙特卡罗模拟显示，在未掺杂区域存在有限温度下的金属-绝缘体转变（metal-insulator crossover），并伴随反铁磁关联（antiferromagnetic correlations）的出现，这些现象在当前实验条件下可观测。哈密顿学习协议可从Emery模型实验中提取有效的单带Hubbard模型。

Conclusion: 该光超晶格架构为实现多轨道Hubbard物理的量子气体显微镜（quantum gas microscope）模拟提供了一条实用路径，有望推动铜氧化物高温超导机制等强关联电子系统的基础研究。

Abstract: Strongly-correlated electrons in transition-metal oxides give rise to intriguing emergent phenomena, including high-temperature superconductivity in cuprates. While simplified one-band Hubbard models capture some aspects, explicitly describing the interplay of copper and oxygen orbitals -- as in the three-band Emery model -- is essential to capture the full phenomenology of cuprates. Quantum simulators based on ultracold atoms offer a promising route to study such systems in a controlled setting, but realizing realistic multi-orbital Hubbard models remains challenging. Here we propose an optical superlattice architecture that implements the three-band Emery model with ultracold fermions. By combining lattice beams with controllable interference, we engineer orbital degrees of freedom that reproduce key features of the cuprate band structure, while enabling independent control of orbital-dependent interactions and charge-transfer energy. We show that single-particle quantum walks can benchmark the resulting tight-binding model. Using determinant quantum Monte Carlo, we further investigate thermodynamic properties in the undoped regime and find a finite-temperature metal-insulator crossover accompanied by the onset of antiferromagnetic correlations accessible in current experiments. Finally, we apply a Hamiltonian learning protocol enabling to infer effective single-band Hubbard models from experimental realizations of Emery models. Our results provide a practical pathway to simulate multi-orbital Hubbard physics with quantum gas microscopes.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 通过解析推导建立一般性表达式；对实验相关的李-黄-杨（Lee-Huang-Yang, LHY）系统进行数值模拟验证。

Result: 在托马斯-费米区域内，剪刀模式的频率与非线性形式无关；该模式是一种不探测系统压缩性的剪切模式；数值模拟展示了从非相互作用区域到强相互作用（托马斯-费米）区域的频率演化；即使在强淬火下，剪刀模式频率仍可清晰识别。

Conclusion: 剪刀模式频率在托马斯-费米区域具有普适性，不依赖于非线性项的具体形式，且其作为剪切模式的特性有利于实验观测，尤其是在强淬火条件下。

Abstract: We investigate scissors modes in nonlinear systems with arbitrary power-law dependence of the nonlinear term. Through analytical derivation, we establish a general expression demonstrating that, in the Thomas-Fermi regime, the frequency of the scissors mode is independent of the specific form of the nonlinearity. We conclude that the scissors mode is a shear mode that does not probe the compressibility of the system, which depends on nonlinearity. To validate our findings, we perform numerical simulations of experimentally relevant Lee-Huang-Yang (LHY) systems. Our results illustrate the transition of the scissors mode frequency from the non-interacting to the strongly interacting (Thomas-Fermi) regime. Finally, we demonstrate that the scissors mode frequency remains clearly identifiable even under strong quenches, which should facilitate the experimental observation of our findings.

### [114] [Core-Hole Excitation Dynamics of One-Dimensional Ultracold Trapped Fermions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23785)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索一维自旋极化费米海（Fermi sea）耦合单个重可移动杂质构成的少体系统中，核穴激发（core-hole excitations）的非平衡动力学行为，并理解其作为可观测多体特征的有效性。

Method: 采用两种互补的从头算（ab initio）方法：混合物的多层多组态含时哈特里方法（Multi-Layer Multi-Configuration Time-Dependent Hartree method）与多通道玻恩-奥本海默框架（multi-channel Born-Oppenheimer framework），通过突然打开杂质-浴相互作用触发淬火动力学（quench dynamics）。

Result: 发现深核空穴（deep core holes）在占据数动力学上远比体态空穴（bulk vacancies）或边缘空穴（edge vacancies）更具鲁棒性；密度演化和杂质质心运动表现出杂质与浴之间混合与去混合（mixing and demixing）的竞争；冯·诺依曼熵（von Neumann entropy）揭示了显著多体关联的建立。

Conclusion: 研究结果建立了核穴激发作为囚禁超冷费米子中稳健的动力学多体特征，并为实时探测正交性响应（orthogonality response）、关联建立和空穴填充提供了可控途径。

The bath is initially prepared in a particle-hole configuration by emptying a selected bath single-particle orbital, while the impurity is displaced with respect to the center of the bath confinement potential. The quench dynamics are initialized by suddenly switching on the impurity-bath interaction. To resolve the resulting dynamics, we combine two complementary \textit{ab initio} approaches, namely the Multi-Layer Multi-Configuration Time-Dependent Hartree method for mixtures and a multi-channel Born-Oppenheimer framework. We show that the postquench response is governed by the interaction strength, impurity confinement, mass imbalance, and the location of the initially prepared hole within the Fermi sea. The density evolution and impurity center-of-mass motion reveal a competition between mixing and demixing of impurity and bath, while the von Neumann entropy demonstrates the buildup of pronounced many-body correlations. Most importantly, the occupation dynamics of the initially emptied orbital identifies deep core holes as substantially more robust against refilling than bulk or edge vacancies. Our results establish core-hole excitations as robust dynamical many-body features in trapped ultracold fermions and provide a controlled route towards probing orthogonality response, correlation buildup, and hole refilling in real time.

### [115] [Ground state of the Hubbard model with spin-dependent linear potential](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24068)
*Jacek Dobrzyniecki,Thomas Busch*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解自旋依赖外势（spin-dependent external potential）如何与相互作用竞争，从而实现对束缚费米子对数量的精确控制。

Method: 采用密度矩阵重整化群（density-matrix renormalization group, DMRG）方法模拟一维费米-哈伯德模型（Fermi-Hubbard model）基态；辅以唯象模型（phenomenological model）和局域密度近似（local-density approximation）分析，推导临界阈值的解析估计。

Result: 识别出三个相区：小β区配对稳健，中间β区双占据数呈阶梯状下降（对应成对逐个断裂），大β区两自旋组分完全分离；阶梯结构在附加谐振囚禁下依然存在。

Conclusion: 自旋依赖线性势（spin-dependent linear potential）可在整数层面精确控制束缚费米子对的数量；结果可直接在冷原子实验中得到检验。

Abstract: We investigate the competition between attractive spin-spin interactions and spin-separating external forces in the ground state of a one-dimensional Fermi-Hubbard model. We consider a lattice with open boundary conditions, subject to a linear external potential whose gradient is opposite for the two spin components, so that each spin species sees a potential minimum at a different end of the lattice. Using density-matrix renormalization group (DMRG) simulations, we map the ground-state density distributions and the number of doubly occupied sites as a function of the potential gradient $β$ and interaction strength. We identify three distinct regimes separated by critical threshold gradients: (i) a small-$β$ regime where fermion pairing remains robust against the external potential; (ii) an intermediate-$β$ phase-separated regime characterized by a staircase-like decrease in the doublon number, corresponding to the successive, one-by-one breaking of bound pairs; and (iii) a large-$β$ regime where the two spin components are completely spatially separated. We complement the numerical results with a phenomenological model and a local-density approximation analysis, from which we derive closed-form analytical estimates for these critical threshold values. We also verify that the staircase structure persists under additional harmonic confinement. Our results are directly testable in cold-atom experiments, and demonstrate that a spin-dependent linear potential enables precise, integer-level control of the number of bound fermion pairs.

### [116] [Fragmentation Temperature of 1D and 3D Quantum Droplets in a BEC Mixture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24375)
*Jeroen Van Loock,Denise Ahmed-Braun,Jacques Tempere*

TL;DR: 本文研究双组分玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensates）中量子液滴（quantum droplets）在有限温度下的碎裂行为，发现液滴通过分裂成多个小液滴和/或气体来降低自由能，碎裂条件取决于相互作用强度、原子数、密度和温度等参数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究虽考察了三维和一维构型下量子液滴的基态，但尚未考虑其可能发生的碎裂（fragmentation）现象。

Method: 通过理论分析，研究双组分玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体混合体系中量子液滴在不同维度（三维和一维）下的自由能最小化过程，考察液滴分裂或碎裂的条件。

Result: 三维液滴在种间相互作用（interspecies interaction）远强于种内相互作用（intraspecies interaction）、且原子数与形成液滴所需的最小原子数相当时发生分裂；一维液滴在种内与种间相互作用强度相差不大且密度相对于散射长度（scattering length）不太大时发生碎裂；温度升高时，一维液滴通过排出原子形成以自由原子和原子对为主的气体来实现分裂，这些原子对在远高于转变温度（transition temperature）的温度下仍存在。

Conclusion: 研究结果揭示了量子液滴稳定性的重要机制，为理解其碎裂行为提供了关键见解。

Abstract: In a mixture of two Bose-Einstein condensates, the interactions can be tuned such that self-bound objects called quantum droplets appear. Whereas the ground states of such quantum droplets at finite temperature have been studied for three- and one-dimensional configurations, the possible fragmentation of these droplets has so far not been considered in these studies. In this paper, we show that droplets can lower their free energy by splitting or fragmenting in a combination of multiple smaller droplets and/or a gas. Three-dimensional droplets will split when the interspecies interaction strength is considerably stronger than the intraspecies interaction strength, and the number of atoms is of the same order as the minimum number of atoms necessary to form a droplet. One-dimensional droplets will fragment as long as the intraspecies and interspecies interactions strength do not vary too much in strength and the density is not to big compared with the scattering length. If the temperature rises, 1D droplets will split by expelling atoms, forming a gas of predominantly free atoms and pairs of atoms. These pairs remain present in the system up to considerably high temperatures compared to the transition temperature. Our results provide important insights on the stability of these droplets.

### [117] [Deterministic Nucleation and Dynamics of Infilled Multiply-Charged Vortices in an Immiscible $^{87}\mathrm{Rb}$-$^{41}\mathrm{K}$ Mixture](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24511)
*R. Doran,K. E. Wilson*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文提出一种在不可混溶玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（immiscible Bose-Einstein condensates）中可控产生多电荷涡旋（multiply-charged vortices）的方法，通过激光搅拌技术（laser stirring）在$^{87}\mathrm{Rb}$-$^{41}\mathrm{K}$混合物中生成并由次级组分填充的涡旋。数值模拟表明涡旋电荷（charge）可通过搅拌参数可重复调节，从而实现稳定高拓扑荷（topological charge）涡旋的确定性生成。进一步研究发现，在圆形陷阱中，多电荷涡旋呈现电荷依赖的长期进动（precession）以及填充组分的集体呼吸模式（collective breathing modes），且在足够大的缠绕数（winding numbers）下观察到导致涡旋位错（vortex dislocation）的动态不稳定性（dynamical instabilities）。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文采用激光搅拌技术（laser stirring technique）作用于$^{87}\mathrm{Rb}$-$^{41}\mathrm{K}$不可混溶混合物，通过调节搅拌参数（stirring parameters）可重复调控所生成涡旋的电荷（vortex charge）。数值模拟（numerical simulation）被用于验证该方法的可靠性并分析涡旋动力学行为。

Result: 数值结果表明，涡旋电荷可通过搅拌参数可重复调节，实现稳定填充的高拓扑荷（topological charge）涡旋的确定性生成。在圆形陷阱中，多电荷涡旋表现出长寿命的电荷依赖进动（precession）频率以及填充组分的集体呼吸模式（collective breathing modes）。当缠绕数足够大时，观察到动态不稳定性（dynamical instabilities）并导致涡旋位错（vortex dislocation）。

Conclusion: 该工作证明，在不可混溶双组分BEC体系中，通过激光搅拌技术和次级组分填充，可以实现多电荷涡旋的稳定生成与电荷可控调节。这一发现与单组分凝聚体中多电荷涡旋不稳定的传统认识形成显著对比，并揭示了其独特的动力学行为（进动、呼吸模式及不稳定性），为涡旋物理和量子流体的研究提供了新的可控平台。

Abstract: We propose a method for controllably generating multiply-charged vortices in immiscible Bose-Einstein condensates. We achieve this by applying a laser stirring technique to a $^{87}\mathrm{Rb}$-$^{41}\mathrm{K}$ mixture, where the vortices generated are infilled by the secondary component. We numerically demonstrate that the charge of the vortex can be tuned reproducibly by varying the stirring parameters, allowing the deterministic generation of stable infilled vortices with high topological charge. We then consider the dynamics of these multiply-charged vortices in a circular trap; in contrast to single-component condensates, we observe long-lived precession of the multiply-charged vortices with a charge dependent frequency and collective breathing modes of the infilling component. For sufficiently large winding numbers, we observe distinct dynamical instabilities leading to vortex dislocation.

### [118] [Entropy Signatures of Collective Modes and Vortex Dynamics in Rotating Two--Dimensional Bose--Einstein Condensates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24557)
*L. A. Machado,N. D. Chavda,B. Chatterjee,M. A. Caracanhas,B. Chakrabarti,A. Gammal,R. P. Sagar*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We investigate the nonequilibrium dynamics of a two-dimensional rotating Bose gas confined in a symmetric anharmonic trap, employing the multiconfigurational time-dependent Hartree method for bosons (MCTDHB). We study states ranging from vortex-free configurations to multicharged (giant) vortices, prepared by tuning the rotation frequency, and analyze their response to sudden interaction and trap quenches. In vortex-free states, interaction quenches induce regular breathing--like dynamics, whereas in the presence of giant vortices they lead to symmetry-breaking surface excitations. In contrast, trap deformations that excite quadrupole-like modes produce stable oscillations in vortex-free condensates but trigger rapid, irregular, and effectively chaotic splitting dynamics in multicharged vortices. To characterize these processes beyond conventional density and phase observables, we employ information-theoretic measures, including marginal and joint entropies, mutual information, and Kullback-Leibler (KL) divergence, supplemented by an angular-resolved KL measure that captures symmetry breaking and azimuthal localization. We find that chaotic splitting is accompanied by a pronounced growth of information-theoretic indicators, signaling the buildup of many-body correlations and increasing complexity in the system dynamics. Our results demonstrate the extreme sensitivity of giant vortices to excitation protocols and establish information-theoretic measures as a powerful framework to quantify correlations and complexity in rotating quantum gases.

### [119] [Floquet engineering of tight-binding Hamiltonians in momentum space lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24722)
*D. Ronco,F. Arrouas,N. Ombredane,E. Flament,Q. Levoy,B. Peaudecerf,D. Guéry-Odelin*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 在Floquet框架下利用周期驱动转子的量子共振，基于一阶时间相关微扰论（first-order time-dependent perturbation theory）导出晶格调制与有效紧束缚参数间的解析关系，并识别多个共振态的显式解。进一步运用最优控制技术（optimal-control techniques）提升多周期Floquet保真度（multi-period Floquet fidelity），扩展可达参数范围。

Result: 实验上采用铷-87（rubidium-87）原子的玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚体（Bose-Einstein condensate）在动态调制光学晶格（dynamically modulated optical lattice）中实现该方案，成功模拟了Rice-Mele模型，测量了能带结构（band structure）并观测到拓扑边缘态、动量布洛赫振荡以及具有可控周期性的超晶格构型（superlattice configurations）。

Conclusion: 研究结果表明，量子共振可作为Floquet工程在动量空间中构建紧束缚模型的有力工具，为可编程量子模拟与拓扑物态研究提供了新途径。

Abstract: Quantum simulation with ultracold atoms provides a versatile platform to emulate condensed-matter models. In particular, momentum-space lattices enable the realization of programmable tight-binding Hamiltonians. Here, we generalize this approach by exploiting quantum resonances of a periodically driven (shaken) rotor within the Floquet framework. Using first-order time-dependent perturbation theory, we derive analytical relations between the lattice modulation and the effective tight-binding parameters, and identify explicit solutions for several resonances. We further apply optimal-control techniques to enhance the multi-period Floquet fidelity and extend the accessible parameter regimes. Experimentally, we implement this scheme with a Bose-Einstein condensate of rubidium-87 atoms in a dynamically modulated optical lattice. We demonstrate the simulation of the Rice-Mele model, including band-structure measurements and topological edge states, as well as momentum Bloch oscillations, and superlattice configurations with controlled periodicity. Our results establish quantum resonances as a powerful resource for Floquet engineering of tight-binding models in momentum space.

</details>


### [120] [Dynamical preparation of U(1) quantum spin liquids in an analogue quantum simulator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24744)
*Simon Karch,Melissa Will,Irene Prieto Rodriguez,Nikolas Liebster,SeungJung Huh,Michael Knap,Frank Pollmann,Clemens Kuhlenkamp,Immanuel Bloch,Monika Aidelsburger*

Main category: cond-mat.quant-gas

TL;DR: 本文利用超冷原子在方形光学超晶格中实现了一个超过3000个格点的大尺度二维U(1)晶格规范理论（lattice gauge theory），并通过非平衡量子模拟展示了U(1)量子自旋液体（quantum spin liquid）区域的制备与相干性观测。实验验证了高斯定律（Gauss's law），观测到实空间关联与动量空间针尖点（pinch points），并通过往返干涉测量直接观测到约100个格点尺度上的多体相干性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 局域约束规范理论（locally constrained gauge theories）在粒子物理和量子材料中至关重要，但量子自旋液体这类强关联系统的奇异态在实验上极难实现和探测，尤其是在固态和合成量子系统中难以检测多体态之间的脆弱相干性。

Method: 该研究采用超冷原子在方形光学超晶格（square optical superlattice）中构建二维U(1)晶格规范理论，通过非平衡淬火实验（quench experiment）制备量子自旋液体；利用新发展的双占据位点探测显微技术验证高斯定律；采用往返干涉测量协议（round-trip interferometric protocols）直接观测多体构型之间的大尺度相干性。

Result: 实验实现了超过3000个格点的大尺度系统，产生了延伸约100个格点的U(1)量子自旋液体区域；验证了高斯定律的有效性；观测到特征性的实空间关联和动量空间针尖点，这些是涌现U(1)规范结构（emergent U(1) gauge structure）的标志。

Conclusion: 该工作确立了非平衡量子模拟协议（non-equilibrium quantum simulation protocols）作为一条强有力的途径，用于访问和探测超出热平衡下哈密顿量所支持的奇特高纠缠态。

Abstract: Locally constrained gauge theories underpin our understanding of fundamental interactions in particle physics and the emergent behaviour of quantum materials. In strongly correlated systems, they can give rise to quantum spin liquids that lack conventional order and are defined by coherent superpositions of an extensive number of many-body configurations. Realising and probing such exotic states experimentally is an outstanding challenge both in solid-state and synthetic quantum systems, not least due to the difficulty of detecting the fragile coherences between many-body states. Here, we report a large-scale (>3,000 sites) realisation of a two-dimensional U(1) lattice gauge theory with ultracold atoms in a square optical superlattice and demonstrate non-equilibrium preparation of extended regions of U(1) quantum spin liquids. We demonstrate Gauss's law validity in a quench experiment, enabled by a new microscopy technique for detecting doubly occupied sites. We observe characteristic real-space correlations and momentum-space pinch points, hallmarks of the emergent U(1) gauge structure. Using round-trip interferometric protocols, we directly observe large-scale coherence between many-body configurations, providing strong evidence for quantum spin liquid regions extending over ~100 lattice sites. Our results establish non-equilibrium quantum simulation protocols as a powerful route for accessing and probing exotic, highly-entangled states beyond those hosted by the engineered Hamiltonian in thermal equilibrium.

*Nikos Theodorakopoulos*

Main category: physics.bio-ph

TL;DR: 针对Peyrard-Bishop-Dauxois（PBD）DNA解链模型在预测熔化熵、解链力和动力学性质（如发夹动力学）上的不足，本文提出了一个基于平面矢量（planar vector）序参量的原子级“玩具模型”（toy model），能够准确估算熔化熵、解链力、发夹打开速率以及亚氨基质子交换过程中的开/闭碱基对平衡常数。

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 本文提出了一个基于原子级“玩具模型”的描述碱基对内部运动的方法，其核心创新在于将传统的标量序参量（scalar order parameter）替换为平面矢量序参量（planar vector order parameter）来描述DNA解链的热力学行为。

Conclusion: 采用平面矢量序参量替代标量序参量，能够显著改善DNA解链热力学和动力学的预测能力，弥补了PBD模型的不足。

Abstract: The Peyrard-Bishop-Dauxois (PBD) model of DNA denaturation, although successful in the description of melting profiles, fails to predict melting entropies, unzipping forces and dynamical properties, e.g. hairpin dynamics. The paper presents an atomistic "toy model" of the intra base-pair motion which suggests that the thermodynamics may be better described by a planar vector - rather than a scalar - order parameter. ### [122] [Coupled-channel study of the three-body $DDK$ and $D^{*}D^{*}K$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23298)
*Hai-Peng Xie,Si-Yi Chen,Ning Li,Wei Chen*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文在三体DDK系统中，通过耦合道框架和格点QCD约束的手征有效理论，发现DDK系统支持深度束缚态和可能的浅层晕态，而D*D*K耦合道效应可忽略，且未发现共振态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索粲介子与Kaon构成的三体系统DDK的束缚态与共振态性质，理解少体动力学在含粲粒子体系中的表现。

Method: 采用耦合道框架（coupled-channel framework），包含DDK和D*D*K两种组态；D(*)D(*)相互作用由单玻色子交换模型（one-boson-exchange model）描述并经重夸克对称性（heavy-quark symmetry）约束，拟合X(3872)、T_cc^+、Z_c(3900)的极点位置；D(*)K相互作用来自手征有效理论（chiral effective theory），并受格点QCD（lattice-QCD）结果的DK散射长度约束。三体问题用高斯展开法（Gaussian expansion method）求解，复缩放法（complex scaling method）用于寻找共振态。

Result: D*D*K耦合道效应可忽略；DDK系统在广泛参数范围内支持一个深度束缚态（deeply bound state）；依赖于DK相互作用的长程行为，可能在粒子-二聚体（D-DK）阈值附近出现一个额外的浅层态（shallow state）；深度束缚态呈现紧凑三体结构，浅层态展现三体晕态（three-body halo）特征；在所探索参数区域内未发现明显的共振极点；D*D*K系统也得到类似结果。

Conclusion: 研究结果为含粲介子与Kaon系统的少体动力学提供了新见解，尤其是三体束缚态与晕态结构的存在及其性质。

Abstract: We investigate the three-body $DDK$ system with quantum numbers $I(J^P) = \frac{1}{2}(0^-)$ within a coupled-channel framework that incorporates both $DDK$ and $D^{*}D^{*}K$ configurations. The $D^{(*)}D^{(*)}$ interactions are described using the one-boson-exchange model constrained by the heavy-quark symmetry and fitted to the pole positions of $X(3872)$, $T_{cc}^+$, and $Z_c(3900)$. The $D^{(*)}K$ interaction is from the chiral effective theory, motivated by the molecular interpretation of $D_{s0}^*(2317)$, and is further constrained by lattice-QCD results for the $DK$ scattering lengths. The resulting three-body problem is solved using the Gaussian expansion method, while the complex scaling method is employed to search for possible resonant states. We find that coupled-channel effects from $D^{*}D^{*}K$ are negligible, and the $DDK$ system supports a deeply bound state across a wide range of parameters. Depending on the long-range behavior of the $DK$ interaction, an additional shallow state may emerge near the particle-dimer ($D$-$DK$) threshold. The deeply bound state exhibits a compact three-body structure, whereas the shallow state displays characteristic features of a three-body halo configuration. No clear resonance poles are identified within the explored parameter region. Similar results are obtained for the $D^{*}D^{*}K$ system. These findings may provide new insight into few-body dynamics in systems involving charmed mesons and kaons.

*L. Ya. Glozman*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文综述了量子色动力学（Quantum Chromodynamics，QCD）相图在小子化学势（chemical potential）和递增温度下的最新进展，指出在三条转变线之间存在三个相区：手征恢复温度（chiral restoration temperature, T_ch）以下的强子气体（hadron gas）、T_ch与退禁闭温度（deconfinement temperature, T_d）之间的弦性流体（stringy fluid），以及T_d以上的夸克-胶子等离子体（quark-gluon plasma）。这些相区在对称性、自由度及大N_c标度行为（N_c scaling）上存在本质差异。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解QCD相图的结构对揭示强相互作用物质在极端条件下的行为至关重要，尤其是极小化学势与高温区域中不同相区间的过渡与共存机制。

Method: 本文采用综述（review）方法，系统梳理并比较了各相区在对称性、自由度及大N_c标度行为三个维度上的理论特征与近期进展。

Result: 识别出QCD在低温、小子化学势区域的三个相区：强子气体（T < T_ch）、弦性流体（T_ch < T < T_d）以及夸克-胶子等离子体（T > T_d）。三者分别对应不同的对称性和自由度，其大N_c标度行为亦不同。

Conclusion: QCD相图在小子化学势和递增温度下呈现三重结构，各相区由手征恢复温度与退禁闭温度分隔，并为未来理论及格点QCD（lattice QCD）研究提供了清晰的参考框架。

Abstract: We review recent developments on the QCD phase diagram at small chemical potentials and increasing temperature. There are three regimes/phases in QCD which differ by symmetries, degrees of freedom and N_c scaling: the hadron gas below the chiral restoration temperature T_ch, the stringy fluid between T_ch and the deconfinement temperature T_d and the quark-gluon plasma above T_d.
