### [124] [Probing the electron Yukawa coupling via resonant Higgs boson production at FCC-ee via $e^+e^- \to H \to WW^*$ in lepton-plus-jets final states](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24152)
*Apranik Fatehi,Reza Jafari Seyedabad,Amir Amiri,Kazem Azizi,David d'Enterria,Louis Portales,Michele Selvaggi*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过模拟在CERN未来正负电子对撞机（FCC-ee）上质心能量√s=125 GeV的s道希格斯玻色子产生过程，研究了对电子汤川耦合（electron Yukawa coupling）ye的约束能力。利用多类梯度提升决策树（multiclass gradient boosted decision tree）区分信号与背景事件，在10 ab⁻¹积分亮度下达到2.0标准差的统计显著性，给出了耦合修饰因子κe ≤ 1.35（95%置信水平）的模拟最严上限。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 电子汤川耦合（ye）是标准模型中尚缺乏精确实验约束的基本参数之一，直接测量该耦合对检验希格斯机制与味物理具有重要意义。

Method: 研究聚焦于s道希格斯玻色子产生过程e⁺e⁻→H→WW*→ℓ±ν+jj，考虑四种WW*末态（包含离壳与在壳W玻色子衰变为双轻子或双喷注）；采用多类梯度提升决策树（multiclass gradient boosted decision tree）基于全面的运动学与拓扑变量对信号和背景事件进行分类。

Result: 在单色化质心能散度4.1 MeV、共振截面280 ab、积分亮度10 ab⁻¹条件下，组合统计显著性为2.0个标准差，对应耦合修饰因子κe = ye/ye^SM ≤ 1.35（95%置信水平），为模拟研究迄今对电子汤川耦合的最强约束。

Conclusion: FCC-ee在低能段（√s=125 GeV）的s道希格斯产生过程能够有效约束电子汤川耦合（ye），所得上限优于现有模拟研究结果，为未来高能对撞机实验提供了重要参考。

Abstract: We report a detailed simulation study of the search for $s$-channel Higgs boson production in $e^+e^-$ collisions at a center-of-mass (c.m.) energy of $\sqrt{s}=125\,\mathrm{GeV}$ at the CERN Future Circular Collider (FCC-ee), as a means to constrain the electron Yukawa coupling, $y_e$. The process of interest is $e^+e^-\to H\to WW^*\to \ell^\pmν+ jj$ with four different $WW^*$ final states considered, involving both on- and off-shell $W$ bosons decaying either into dileptons ($\ell^\pm = e^\pm$ and $μ^\pm$, including those from $τ^\pm$ decays) or into dijets ($jj$). Signal and background events are discriminated through a multiclass gradient boosted decision tree exploiting a comprehensive set of kinematic and topological variables across the four final-state categories. Assuming a monochromatized c.m. energy spread of 4.1 MeV, yielding a $σ_{e^+e^-\to H} = 280\,\mathrm{ab}$ resonant cross section, and an integrated luminosity of $10\,\mathrm{ab}^{-1}$, the analysis achieves a combined statistical significance of 2.0 standard deviations. This corresponds to an upper limit on the coupling modifier $κ_e = y_e/y_e^{\rm SM} \lesssim 1.35$ at 95\% confidence level, and provides the most stringent constraint on the electron Yukawa coupling achieved in simulation-based studies to date.

</details>


### [125] [How to understand $ρ$ Resonance from the Quark Model and $ππ$ $P$-wave phase shift](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24270)
*Wen-Ze Zhao,Ru-Hui Ni,Jia-Jun Wu*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文为研究ρ介子（rho meson）结构建立了一个统一的框架，该框架结合了夸克-胶子（quark-gluon）与强子（hadronic）两种自由度。首先通过手征夸克模型（chiral quark model）拟合窄介子数据得到裸质量（bare mass），随后基于逆散射理论（inverse scattering theory）引入裸态与ππ连续态的耦合，利用P波ππ散射相移数据提取相互作用并计算宽度及裸态成分。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 作为最轻的同位旋矢量（isovector）矢量介子，ρ介子对研究强相互作用中共振态（resonant states）的结构具有重要意义。传统的组分夸克模型（constituent quark model）将ρ介子简单视为纯q\bar q束缚态（bound state），忽略了强子道耦合（hadronic-channel coupling）效应，难以充分描述其物理性质，因此需要建立更完整的理论框架。

Method: 在夸克-胶子层面，通过重新拟合一组不存在开放OZI允许强衰变道的窄介子（narrow mesons），确定手征夸克模型（chiral quark model）参数，进而获得ρ介子的裸质量（bare mass）。在强子层面，基于逆散射理论（inverse scattering theory）构造包含裸态与ππ连续态耦合的模型，利用P波ππ散射相移（phase-shift）数据提取ρ₀-ππ相互作用，并计算ρ介子的衰变宽度以及物理态中裸态成分。

Result: 通过上述两阶段分析，得到ρ介子的裸质量并计算了其衰变宽度，同时量化了物理态中裸态成分的比例。论文还建立了一个可推广的分析框架（generalizable analytical framework），适用于其他具有显著道耦合效应（channel-coupling effects）的强子共振态研究。

Conclusion: 本文提出的统一框架有效克服了传统组分夸克模型在处理ρ介子等宽共振态（broad resonances）时的局限性，为后续研究其他具有显著强子道耦合效应的共振态提供了可推广的分析方法。

Abstract: As the lightest isovector vector meson, the $ρ$ meson is an important object for investigating the structure of resonant states in strong interactions. Owing to its strong coupling to the $ππ$ channel and its large decay width, the conventional constituent quark model treatment, in which it is simply regarded as a pure $q\bar q$ bound state while the hadronic-channel coupling effects are neglected, is insufficient to fully characterize its physical properties. To this end, in the present work we establish a unified framework for studying the structure and resonant properties of the $ρ$ meson by combining the quark-gluon and hadronic degrees of freedom. At the quark-gluon level, we first determine the parameters of the chiral quark model by refitting a set of narrow mesons for which open OZI-allowed strong-decay channels are absent or strongly suppressed. With these parameters fixed, the bare mass of the $ρ$ meson is obtained and used as the input for the subsequent hadronic-level analysis. At the hadronic level, based on inverse scattering theory, we construct a model including the coupling between the bare state and the $ππ$ continuum, extract the $ρ_0-ππ$ interaction using the $P$-wave $ππ$ scattering phase-shift data, and further calculate the width of the $ρ$ meson as well as the bare-state component in the physical state. The present work also provides a generalizable analytical framework for further studies of other hadronic resonances with significant channel-coupling effects.

</details>


### [126] [Same-Sign Tetralepton Signature at $μ$TRISTAN](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24383)
*Lin-Kun Yan,Zhi-Long Han,Feng-Lan Shao,Fa-Xin Yang*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出在μTRISTAN对撞机的同号缪子模式（μ⁺μ⁺，2 TeV）下，通过带电希格斯粒子的产生与衰变链，探测由低能标跷跷板机制（low scale seesaw）中Yukawa相互作用$y \overline{L}\tildeΦ_νN$导致的同号四轻子（same-sign tetralepton）新物理信号。模拟显示该信号存在有希望的探测区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 中微子质量的微小性可以通过低能标跷跷板机制自然解释，其中重中性轻子（heavy neutral lepton）$N$与中微子亲和希格斯二重态（neutrinophilic Higgs doublet）$Φ_ν$耦合，后者获得远小于标准模型希格斯二重态$Φ$的真空期望值。本文旨在探索这一模型在μTRISTAN对撞机上的可探测特征。

Method: 基于低能标跷跷板模型中Yukawa相互作用$y \overline{L}\tildeΦ_νN$，提出μTRISTAN对撞机2 TeV同号缪子模式下的两种带电希格斯产生通道：对产生（pair production）$μ^+μ^+\to H^+ H^+\to μ^+N +μ^+ N\to μ^+ μ^+ jj + μ^+ μ^+ jj\to 4μ^+ + 4j$，以及单产生（single production）$μ^+μ^+ \to μ^+ N H^+ \to μ^+N +μ^+ N\to μ^+ μ^+ jj + μ^+ μ^+ jj\to 4μ^+ + 4j$。对同号四轻子信号进行了详细的蒙特卡洛模拟。

Result: 通过模拟得到了同号四轻子信号在μTRISTAN对撞机上的有希望探测区域（promising region），表明该信号在2 TeV能量下具有可观的事例率。

Conclusion: 低能标跷跷板模型中的Yukawa相互作用可以在μTRISTAN上产生可观测的同号四缪子（4μ⁺）加四喷注（4j）新物理信号，为探测重中性轻子和中微子质量起源提供了独特的对撞机探针。

Abstract: Naturally tiny neutrino masses can be explained by the low scale seesaw with heavy neutral lepton $N$ coupling to the neutrinophilic Higgs doublet $Φ_ν$, which obtains a much smaller vacuum expectation value than the standard Higgs doublet $Φ$. Within this model, the neutrino masses originate from the new Yukawa interaction $y \overline{L}\tildeΦ_νN$. In this paper, we propose the novel same-sign tetralepton signature at the 2 TeV same-sign muon mode $μ^+μ^+$ of $μ$TRISTAN. We investigate two distinct channels of this signature, which are both generated by the Yukawa interaction $y \overline{L}\tildeΦ_νN$. One is from the pair production of charged Higgs $μ^+μ^+\to H^+ H^+\to μ^+N +μ^+ N\to μ^+ μ^+ jj + μ^+ μ^+ jj\to 4μ^+ + 4j$, and the other one is from the single production of charged Higgs $μ^+μ^+ \to μ^+ N H^+ \to μ^+N +μ^+ N\to μ^+ μ^+ jj + μ^+ μ^+ jj\to 4μ^+ + 4j$. We then perform a detailed simulation of this same-sign tetralepton signature, and obtain the promising region at $μ$TRISTAN.

</details>

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 基于晶格QCD启发的参数化方案构建Minkowski空间夸克传播子，利用广义谱表示分离瞬时贡献，推导出光前离解预解式，并通过投影到组分夸克螺旋度基上得到有效穿衣服饰质量平方算符。

Abstract: We construct an effective light-front mass-squared operator for quark-antiquark systems that incorporates quark dressing effects through a running quark mass. We introduce an effective light-front quark self-energy and analyze its momentum dependence. As an application, we study pion structure using representative light-front wave-function models and compute unpolarized transverse-momentum-dependent distributions, unpolarized parton distribution functions and distribution amplitudes. Our results show that quark dressing induces sizable infrared modifications while preserving controlled ultraviolet behavior, providing a framework to incorporate nonperturbative QCD dynamics into light-front descriptions of hadrons.

### [128] [Some approximate renormalization group invariants for supersymmetric extensions of the Standard Model and the Yukawa unification](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23329)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在超对称标准模型扩展中，寻找量子修正较小、近似为重整化群不变量（renormalization group invariants）的耦合表达式，以探讨汤川耦合在统一标度下的可能关系，并试图解释基本粒子质量的实验观测值。

Method: 构造包含第三代和第二代汤川耦合且量子修正较小的表达式；利用这些近似重整化群不变量分析统一标度$M_X$下的耦合关系及$\mbox{tg}\,β$和$α(M_X)$的预言值；向MSSM场内容中引入构成$SU(5)$群$5+\bar{5}$表示的奇异超场，检验汤川耦合统一与实验值的兼容性。

Result: 证明了在MSSM基础上添加构成$SU(5)$群$3$个$5+\bar{5}$表示的奇异超场后，可以实现与实验基本粒子质量一致的第三代和第二代汤川耦合统一（Yukawa unification）。

Conclusion: 所提出的汤川耦合关系与实验数据吻合，且支持一种可能的潜在$E_6$规范对称性作为理论框架。

Abstract: For supersymmetric extensions of the Standard Model we construct some expressions that include Yukawa couplings for the third and second generations and receive relatively small quantum corrections. This implies that they slightly depend on scale and are therefore approximate renormalization group invariants. Using these invariants we try to analyse possible relations between the Yukawa couplings at the unification scale $M_X$ as well as the predictions for values of $\mbox{tg}\,β$ and $α(M_X)$. In particular, we suggest two variants of such relations and investigate whether they agree with the experimental values of elementary particle masses. It is demonstrated that the Yukawa unification for the third and second generations consistent with them can be achieved by adding exotic superfields forming 3 representations $5+\bar{5}$ of the group $SU(5)$ to the MSSM field content. We argue that this may indicate the possible underlying $E_6$ gauge symmetry.

### [129] [Possible Evidence for Neutral Color-Singlet $q\bar q$ Quark Matter from High-Energy Pb-Emulsion Collisions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23473)
*Cheuk-Yin Wong*

Main category: hep-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出，CERN SPS上160 A GeV铅-乳胶碰撞产生的e⁺e⁻对不变质量谱中的宽增强结构和多个共振峰（包括19 MeV处支持X17粒子的共振）可以用QED(U(1))退紧闭和紧闭相中的中性色单态夸克物质（neutral color-singlet q\bar{q} quark matter）统一解释。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高能铅-乳胶碰撞中观察到的e⁺e⁻对不变质量谱呈现复杂的共振结构叠加在低于50 MeV的宽增强背景之上，其中19 MeV共振为假设的X17粒子提供了独立支持。现有解释尚未能统一描述这一复杂结构，因此需要提出一个连贯的理论框架。

Method: 该研究通过理论分析，将e⁺e⁻对谱分解为两个来源：低于50 MeV的宽增强来自QED(U(1))退紧闭相中夸克与反夸克在相变温度T_c(QED)≈4.75±1.2 MeV下的热湮灭；而3±1 MeV、7±1 MeV和19±1 MeV的共振分别对应于QED(U(1))退紧闭的d\bar{d}和u\bar{u}库仑束缚态以及QED(U(1))紧闭的同位旋标量QED介子。

Result: 理论预测的谱与实验观测的e⁺e⁻对不变质量谱在近似层面吻合，表明高能铅-乳胶碰撞中可能同时产生了QED(U(1))紧闭相和QED(U(1))退紧闭相的中性色单态夸克物质。

Conclusion: 该研究为X17粒子相关的实验现象提供了夸克物质相变的理论解释，并建议开展后续实验以证实或反驳这些发现。

Abstract: The invariant mass spectrum of $e^+e^-$ pairs produced in high-energy Pb-emulsion collisions at 160 A GeV at CERN SPS exhibits a complex structure of many resonances resting on top of a broad enhancement at invariant masses below 50 MeV, with the prominent resonance at 19 $\pm$1 MeV providing independent support for the hypothetical X17 particle. We show that this complex structure may be coherently described as signatures for the neutral color-singlet $q\bar q$ quark matter in both its deconfined and confined phases. That is, the broad enhancement may arise from thermal annihilation of QED(U(1))-deconfined quarks and antiquarks into $e^+e^-$ pairs at the phase transition temperature $T_c$(QED), theoretically estimated to be 4.75 $\pm$ 1.2 MeV from the transitional equilibrium condition. The observed 3$\pm$1 and 7$\pm$1 MeV resonances may correspond to the QED(U(1))-deconfined $d\bar d$ and $u\bar u$ Coulomb bound states near their quark rest masses, respectively, whereas the observed 19 $\pm$ 1 MeV resonance may correspond to the QED(U(1))-confined isoscalar QED meson. The approximate agreement between the theoretical and the experimental spectrum suggests that both QED(U(1))-confined and QED(U(1))-deconfined neutral color-singlet $q\bar q$ quark matter may have been produced in these high-energy Pb-emulsion collisions. We propose future experiments to confirm or refute these findings.

### [130] [A Diamagnetic, Light-Driven Tesla Engine Based on a Mechanically Displaced, Magnetically Levitated Graphene Disk](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22803)
*Tian Tong,Feng Lin,Wei Zhang,Runjia Li,Xinxin Xing,Zhuochen Duan,Chunhui Xu,Bing Tu,Zhaoping Liu,Xufeng Zhou,Zhiming Wang,Dong Liu,Jonathan Hu,Jiming Bao*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文首次演示了基于石墨烯（graphene）强抗磁性的抗磁特斯拉发动机（diamagnetic Tesla engine），通过横向偏移悬浮圆盘产生恢复力，在光照驱动下实现最高2000 rpm（激光）和1000 rpm（阳光）的稳定旋转，并展示了齿轮传动能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铁磁材料在特斯拉热磁发动机中已被广泛应用，但抗磁材料在此类系统中的应用尚未被探索。本研究旨在填补这一空白，利用石墨烯的强抗磁性实现首个抗磁特斯拉发动机。

Method: 通过堆叠石墨烯片制备石墨烯圆盘作为发动机轮盘。首先验证了传统特斯拉发动机设计——在圆盘边缘附近放置永磁体以在非对称局部加热下产生不平衡热磁力——无法实现旋转。随后采用横向偏移悬浮圆盘使其偏离平衡位置的方法，从而产生强恢复力，在光激发下驱动旋转。

Result: 计算与测量建立了位移依赖的驱动力关系，最优偏移量为0.8 mm。在激光加热下转速可达2000 rpm，在直射阳光下可达1000 rpm。添加叶片后圆盘可作为齿轮使用，驱动石墨烯车辆并将能量传递至另一个圆盘。

Conclusion: 该设计利用了石墨烯的强各向异性抗磁性（strong and anisotropic diamagnetism），为光驱动传感器、执行器和微型车辆等应用开辟了新途径。

Abstract: Ferromagnetic materials are widely used in Tesla thermomagnetic engines, whereas diamagnetic counterparts have remained unexplored. Here, we demonstrate the first diamagnetic Tesla engine by exploiting the strong diamagnetism of graphene. A graphene disk, fabricated by stacking graphene sheets, serves as the engine wheel. We first show that the conventional Tesla engine design using a permanent magnet placed near the disk edge to create unbalanced thermomagnetic forces under asymmetric local heating fails to generate rotation. We achieve stable operation by laterally displacing the levitated disk from equilibrium, creating a strong restoring force that drives rotation under light excitation. Calculations and measurements establish the displacement-dependent force, with an optimal offset of 0.8 mm yielding speeds up to 2000 rpm under laser heating and 1000 rpm under direct sunlight. Adding vanes allows the disk to function as a gear, powering a graphene vehicle and transferring energy to another disk. This design utilizes the strong and anisotropic diamagnetism of graphene and paves the way for light-powered sensors, actuators, and micro-vehicles.

</details>


### [131] [Evidence of Micron-Scale Ion Damage in (010), (110), and (011) $β-Ga_2O_3$ Epitaxial Layers](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24190)
*Carl Peterson,Chinmoy Nath Saha,Yizheng Liu,James S. Speck,Sriram Krishnamoorthy*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本研究实验观察到，在β-Ga₂O₃外延层中，溅射和ICP刻蚀造成的离子损伤导致(010)、(110)、(011)取向出现深达11.5 μm的电荷耗尽，而(001)取向的耗尽极小。取向依赖的电荷密度降低首先在NiOₓ反应溅射异质结p-n二极管中被发现，且损伤机制与开放沟道中的高能离子注入及补偿点缺陷的形成扩散有关。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究β-Ga₂O₃不同晶向（crystallographic orientation）外延层在溅射（sputtering）和电感耦合等离子体（ICP）刻蚀工艺中因离子损伤（ion damage）导致的电荷耗尽行为差异，以明确该材料在器件制造中的取向敏感性。

Method: 通过比较NiOₓ反应溅射异质结p-n二极管（HJDs）与低损伤肖特基势垒二极管（SBDs）的电学特性，以及ICP刻蚀前后不同取向（010, 110, 011, 001）β-Ga₂O₃ SBDs的电容-电压（CV）测量数据，分析净施主浓度（N_D - N_A）和比导通电阻（R_on,sp）的变化。

Result: 在(010)取向的溅射损伤HJDs中，零偏下比导通电阻（R_on,sp）增大9.4倍，净施主浓度（N_D - N_A）降低85%；(010)材料的溅射SiO₂导致N_D - N_A在11.5 μm深处减少。ICP刻蚀后的(010) SBDs中R_on,sp增大7.7倍，N_D - N_A降低91%；(110)和(011)取向也观察到约82%的N_D - N_A降低，而(001)取向变化极小。

Conclusion: β-Ga₂O₃的(010)、(110)、(011)取向对溅射和ICP刻蚀引起的离子损伤高度敏感，损伤深度可达11.5 μm，而(001)取向具有显著的抗损伤能力。损伤机制归因于高能离子沿[010]方向的开放沟道（open channel）注入，产生补偿点缺陷（compensating point defects）并可能进一步扩散。

Abstract: We report on the experimental observation of up to 11.5 $μm$ deep charge depletion in (010), (110), and (011) $β-Ga_2O_3$ epitaxial layers due to ion damage from sputtering and inductively coupled plasma (ICP) etching processes whereas charge depletion in (001) $β-Ga_2O_3$ epitaxial layers was minimal. The orientation-dependent reduction in CV-measured charge density was first observed in $NiO_x$ reactively sputtered heterojunction p-n diodes (HJDs). When compared to reference low-damage Schottky barrier diodes (SBDs), the sputtered HJDs showed a $9.4{\times}$ increase in the specific on resistance $(R_{on,sp})$ and 85% reduction in net donor concentration $(N_D - N_A)$ at zero bias for sputter-damaged HJDs on (010) epitaxial layers whereas HJDs on (001) remained unchanged. Similarly, sputtered SiO2 caused a reduction of $N_D - N_A$ 11.5 $μm$ deep into the (010) material. Next, SBDs were fabricated on $β-Ga_2O_3$ surfaces previously etched via a BCl3 based ICP process and compared to SBDs on un-etched surfaces. The (010) SBDs on etched surfaces exhibited a $7.7{\times}$ increase in $R_{on,sp}$ and a 91% reduction in $N_D - N_A$ at zero bias where the (001) etched diodes exhibited little change. Additionally, (110) and (011) diodes fabricated on ICP damaged surfaces also saw a ~82% reduction in $N_D - N_A$ at zero bias, indicating (110) and (011) are also susceptible to ion damage. Damage in the (010), (110), and (011) diodes is potentially caused by energetic ions that travel into the open channels present along the [010] direction and create compensating point defects which could potentially diffuse further.

### [132] [Complementary-polarity double-layer LiTaO3 resonators for symmetry-selective SH2 excitation with ultrahigh electromechanical coupling (kt^2 = 25.7%)](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24309)
*Hao Yan,Zhen-hui Qin,Zhi-Wen Wang,Shu-Mao Wu,Chen-Bei Hao,Hua-Yang Chen,Sheng-Nan Liang,Ke Chen,Si-Yuan Yu,Yan-Feng Chen*

Main category: physics.app-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种结构简单的双层钽酸锂（LiTaO3）体声波谐振器，通过互补极性键合和纵向电场驱动，实现了对二阶厚度剪切（SH2）模式的对称选择性激发，获得了高达25.7%的有效机电耦合系数（kt²），这是目前LiTaO3谐振器架构中的最高报道值。该结构具有良好的频率可调性、工艺容差性，并可通过减薄膜层实现5 GHz以上频率缩放，同时引入SiO2补偿层可改善温度稳定性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高耦合、低寄生模式的声波谐振器（acoustic resonator）是宽带宽滤波器（wideband filter）和超声换能器（ultrasonic transducer）的核心需求。现有LiTaO3谐振器在机电耦合系数（electromechanical coupling coefficient）方面仍有提升空间，且高阶厚度剪切模式的激发效率有限，亟需一种结构简单、耦合高效、寄生抑制良好的谐振器设计。

Method: 采用两片31°Y切单晶LiTaO3薄膜，以互补极化方向（+X/-X）旋转键合（rotation-bonded），构成双层结构，并通过纵向电场（longitudinal electric field）驱动。利用有效压电对称性（effective piezoelectric symmetry）与二阶厚度剪切（SH2）模式之间的匹配，实现对称选择性激发。

Result: 在5.24 MHz频率下获得kt² = 25.7%的有效机电耦合系数，为LiTaO3谐振器中的最高报道值。实测响应以目标SH2模式为主，工作频带内寄生特征（parasitic features）微弱。可通过几何参数（geometric parameters）调节谐振频率和耦合，保持稳定的模态行为。有限元分析（finite-element analysis）表明，减薄膜层和电极厚度可将频率缩放至5 GHz以上，同时维持约25%的kt²。引入SiO2补偿层后，预测温度系数（temperature coefficient of frequency）可改善至约-25 ppm/°C。

Conclusion: 互补极性双层LiTaO3结构提供了一种高耦合、低寄生模式、工艺容差良好的声波谐振器平台，为宽带超声谐振器、滤波器及相关换能器（transducer）的实现提供了可规模化扩展的路径。

Abstract: We report a structurally simple double-layer lithium tantalate (LiTaO3) bulk acoustic resonator that enables symmetry-selective excitation of the second-order thickness-shear (SH2) mode with ultrahigh electromechanical coupling. Two 31 deg Y-oriented single-crystal LiTaO3 films are rotation-bonded with complementary polarization (+X/-X) and driven by a longitudinal electric field. Matching between the effective piezoelectric symmetry and the SH2 mode yields an effective electromechanical coupling coefficient of kt^2 = 25.7% at 5.24 MHz. To our knowledge, this is the highest kt^2 reported for a LiTaO3 resonator architecture to date. The measured response is dominated by the target SH2 mode, with only weak parasitic features in the operating band. The structure is also tunable: the resonance frequency and coupling can be adjusted through geometric parameters while maintaining stable modal behavior, indicating good process tolerance. Finite-element analysis further suggests straightforward frequency scaling beyond 5 GHz by reducing the film and electrode thickness while preserving approximately 25% kt^2. In addition, introducing a SiO2 compensation layer is predicted to improve the temperature coefficient of frequency to approximately -25 ppm/deg C. These results establish complementary-polarity double-layer LiTaO3 as a practical platform for high-coupling, spurious-suppressed acoustic resonators and provide a scalable route toward wideband ultrasonic resonators, filters, and related transducers.

### [133] [Heterotic Ouroboros](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22915)

TL;DR: 本文基于M理论在${\mathbf{S}}^1\vee{\mathbf{S}}^1$上的构造，通过商操作得到十维非超对称弦理论，并聚焦于杂化弦理论（heterotic theories）。作者重新审视了相关构造，发现了一套一致的规则，能够复现轻粒子谱（light spectra）和规范群（gauge groups），并暗示了其全局结构。方法上利用I'型弦理论（type I' string theory）的规范增强机制（gauge enhancement mechanism），应用于I'型区间自我卷曲且两个边界由分支切割（branch cut）分隔的设置，从而复现十维杂化弦理论并提供它们之间结（junctions）的证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 该研究旨在系统性地理解M理论在${\mathbf{S}}^1\vee{\mathbf{S}}^1$上通过商操作导出的非超对称弦理论，特别是杂化弦理论的构造规则与全局结构。

Method: 采用I'型弦理论的规范增强机制，将其应用于一个I'型区间自我卷曲、两边界由分支切割分隔的几何设置中，以此复现杂化弦理论。

Result: 提出了一套一致的构造规则，成功复现了十维杂化弦理论的轻粒子谱和规范群，并提供了不同杂化弦理论之间存在结（junctions）的证据，暗示了它们之间的非平凡连接关系。

Conclusion: 该工作为M理论在${\mathbf{S}}^1\vee{\mathbf{S}}^1$上构造非超对称弦理论提供了更系统的理解，特别揭示了杂化弦理论的一致规则与全局结构联系。

Abstract: M-theory on ${\mathbf{S}}^1\vee{\mathbf{S}}^1$ has recently been proposed to yield, via quotients, ten-dimensional non-supersymmetric string theories. We revisit the construction that leads to the heterotic theories, finding a consistent set of rules that reproduces the light spectra and gauge groups, including indications of their global structure. Our approach uses the gauge enhancement mechanism of type I' string theory, applied to a setting in which the type I' interval is curled onto itself, with its two boundaries separated by a branch cut. Using these tools, we reproduce the ten-dimensional heterotic theories and provide some evidence for junctions among them.

### [134] [String theory in the infrared](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22916)
*Ivano Basile*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文系统总结了近期一项研究计划，旨在从全局视角探索弦论低能相图景。通过借用沼泽地计划的概念框架，论证低能弦论产生的有效引力理论远非任意；其红外数据受普适标度关系约束，这些关系在种类极限中变得非平凡。具体而言，世界面分析揭示高阶导数Wilson系数与真空能之间存在有效场论无法察觉的紫外/红外关联，从而导出了全息界形式的参数不等式。这为沼泽地动机的现象学场景以及从宇宙学观测中提取弦论间接可检验信号提供了更坚实的理论支持。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解决弦论低能有效理论空间并非任意、而是受普适结构约束这一核心问题，旨在为沼泽地计划提供更坚实的理论支撑，并探索从宇宙学观测中提取弦论可检验信号的可能性。

Method: 借用沼泽地计划（swampland program）的概念框架，从全局视角分析弦论低能相空间；通过世界面（worldsheet）分析研究高阶导数Wilson系数与真空能之间的紫外/红外关联（UV/IR relations），推导出全息界形式的参数不等式。

Result: 低能弦论产生的有效引力理论受到普适标度关系约束；世界面分析揭示了有效场论无法察觉的UV/IR关联，导出了全息界形式的参数不等式。

Conclusion: 该研究为沼泽地动机的现象学场景提供了更坚实的理论支持，并增强了从宇宙学观测中提取弦论间接可检验信号的可行性。

Abstract: I briefly summarize a recent research program aiming to probe the landscape of low-energy phases of string theory from a global perspective. Borrowing conceptual lessons from the swampland program, I will discuss how the effective theories of gravity produced by low-energy string theory are far from generic; rather, their infrared data is connected by universal scaling relations which become non-trivial in species limits. In particular, a worldsheet analysis reveals that higher-derivative Wilson coefficients and the vacuum energy exhibit UV/IR relations which are invisible from the viewpoint of effective field theory, leading to parametric inequalities which take the form of holographic bounds. This lends a more solid theoretical support to swampland-motivated phenomenological scenarios, and to the broader hopes of extracting less direct, but empirically accessible, signatures of string theory from cosmological observations.

### [135] [Kinematic Flow for Banana Loops and Unparticles](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22918)
*Tom Westerdijk,Chen Yang*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过非粒子（unparticle）交换的双重描述，将运动学流（kinematic flow）拓展到动量积分的圈级宇宙学关联函数（loop-level cosmological correlators），发现这些关联函数可由一组满足一阶微分方程组的有限主积分（master integrals）描述，并基于标记图的管道结构（tubings of marked graphs）构建了对应基，由四条组合规则推导出连接矩阵（connection matrices）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 将运动学流方法从树图级拓展至动量积分的圈级宇宙学关联函数，特别是香蕉圈图（banana loops）和任意混合的无质量与共形耦合标量场，以系统描述更复杂的圈图结构。

Method: 利用非粒子交换的双重描述，将圈级关联函数映射为树图级非粒子交换；基于标记图的管道结构构建主积分基，其中包含嵌套管道和树序顶点排序；提出四条组合规则——激活（activation）、合并（merger）、交换（swap）和复制（copy）——来推导连接矩阵。

Result: 发现关联函数由一组满足一阶微分方程组的有限主积分描述；交换和复制规则是唯一针对非粒子交换的，它们诱导了基函数之间更丰富的混合并引入了新的运动学字母（kinematic letters）。该框架可系统推广到任意复杂配置，包括项链图（necklace diagrams）。

Conclusion: 非粒子交换被确立为运动学流的一个独立类别，该框架为系统处理更复杂的圈级宇宙学关联函数提供了统一方法。

Abstract: We extend kinematic flow to momentum-integrated loop-level cosmological correlators, focusing on banana loops of conformally coupled scalars in power-law cosmologies and, in de Sitter, on arbitrary mixtures of massless and conformally coupled scalars. Exploiting their dual description as tree-level exchanges of unparticles, we show that the associated correlators are described by a finite set of master integrals obeying a first-order system of differential equations. The corresponding basis is constructed from tubings of marked graphs and is distinguished by the appearance of nested tubes and an arborescence ordering of the vertices. We derive the connection matrices from four combinatorial rules -- activation, merger, swap, and copy. The last two are unique to unparticle exchanges: they induce richer mixing among basis functions and introduce new kinematic letters. Our framework extends systematically to arbitrarily complicated configurations, including necklace diagrams, and establishes unparticle exchange as a distinct class of kinematic flow.

### [136] [Particle and Superparticle Confinement in Higher Codimension Braneworlds](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22929)
*F. E. A. de Souza,M. O. Tahim,R. I. de Oliveira Júnior,I. M. Macêdo*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文分析了相对论性和超对称性自旋粒子在高余维膜世界中的经典约束现象。通过弦状标量缺陷（n=2）和全局标量缺陷（n≥3）生成的翘曲背景，从Polyakov型作用量导出有效径向动力学。无自旋粒子因有效势单调递减而无法被约束；而对于N=1,2的自旋粒子，自旋-曲率耦合修正势能，产生稳定平衡点，粒子可被约束在膜上或附近区域，呈现束缚或卫星式运动。这些结果强调了自旋在局域化机制中的关键作用。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索高余维膜世界（braneworlds）中相对论性和超对称性自旋粒子的经典约束（confinement）问题，特别关注自旋自由度对粒子局域化行为的影响。

Method: 基于Polyakov型作用量（Polyakov-type action）推导有效径向动力学；考虑两种翘曲背景（warped backgrounds）：弦状n=2标量缺陷和全局标量缺陷（global scalar defects）n≥3；分别分析无自旋粒子和N=1,2自旋粒子的有效势行为。

Result: 无自旋粒子的有效势单调递减，呈现排斥行为，无法实现约束。N=1,2自旋粒子因自旋-曲率耦合（spin-curvature coupling）修正势能，可产生稳定平衡点（stable equilibrium points）。根据耦合参数的不同，粒子可被约束在膜上或附近区域，展示束缚或卫星式（satellite-like）运动。

Conclusion: 自旋-曲率耦合在膜世界局域化机制中发挥关键作用，自旋自由度能够改变有效势的形状，使得原本无法约束的无自旋粒子系统在引入自旋后获得稳定约束的可能性。

Abstract: In this work we analyze the classical confinement of relativistic and supersymmetric spinning particles in higher-codimension braneworlds. Considering warped backgrounds generated by string-like $ n=2$ and global scalar defects $ n \geq 3$, we derive the effective radial dynamics from a Polyakov-type action. For spinless particles, the effective potential is monotonically decreasing, leading to repulsive behavior and the absence of confinement. In contrast, for $N=1,2 $ spinning particles, spin-curvature coupling modifies the potential, allowing the emergence of stable equilibrium points. Depending on the coupling parameter, particles may be confined on the membrane or in nearby regions, exhibiting bounded or satellite-like motion. These results emphasize the role of spin in localization mechanisms.

### [137] [Fractions and Fakeons in Quantum Field Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23215)
*Damiano Anselmi*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究具有分数阶或连续阶 d'Alembert 算符的量子场论表述，重点解决微扰幺正性和经典极限问题，提出了“假粒子（fakeon）”方案和高斯分解方法，并证明了 Ward 恒等式与 Cutkosky 恒等式在所有表述中成立。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索含有分数阶或连续阶 d'Alembert 算符（d'Alembert operator）的量子场论（quantum field theory）表述形式，核心要求是满足微扰幺正性（perturbative unitarity）并具有良好定义的经典极限（classical limit）与有限个初始条件。

Method: 直接方法：利用“假粒子（fakeon）”方案处理幂指数中的分数部分，将关联函数从欧几里得空间（Euclidean space）延拓至闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime）。替代方法：通过分解（decomposition）将分数部分表示为连续分布的普通假粒子（fakeons）。在树图（tree level）和气泡图（bubble diagrams）层面验证这些特征。

Result: 两种方法均产生无限种不等价的闵可夫斯基理论（Minkowskian theories），但它们共享相同的欧几里得对应（Euclidean counterpart）。在规范理论（gauge theory）与引力理论（gravity）中，连续阶协变 d'Alembert 算符可被合理处理。Ward 恒等式（Ward identities）与 Cutkosky 恒等式（Cutkosky identities）在所有表述中均成立。

Conclusion: 分数阶和连续阶 d'Alembert 算符的量子场论可以通过假粒子方案与分解方法构建，尽管存在无限多种不等价表述，但 Ward 与 Cutkosky 恒等式保证了这些理论在幺正性和对称性方面的自洽性。

Abstract: We investigate formulations of quantum field theories whose kinetic terms involve fractional or continuous powers of the d'Alembert operator. The primary requirements are perturbative unitarity and a well-defined classical limit with a finite number of initial conditions. A direct approach consists of continuing the correlation functions from Euclidean space to Minkowski spacetime using the fakeon prescription for the fractional part of the power. Alternative formulations arise through decomposition, in which the fractional part is represented as a continuum of ordinary fakeons. These options are infinite in number and yield inequivalent Minkowskian theories with the same Euclidean counterpart. We demonstrate these features at tree level and for bubble diagrams. We also point out potential pitfalls in the calculations. Finally, we show how to treat continuous powers of covariant d'Alembertians in fractional gauge and gravity theories. The Ward and Cutkosky identities hold in all formulations.

</details>


### [138] [Chaos of Berry curvature for BPS microstates](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23287)
*Yiming Chen,Sean Colin-Ellerin,Ohad Mamroud,Kyriakos Papadodimas*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出利用非阿贝尔Berry曲率（non-Abelian Berry curvature）作为超对称系统中混沌的内在探针，发现黑洞微观态对应的Berry曲率具有随机矩阵行为，而无视界几何对应的态则呈现非随机甚至严格为零的Berry曲率，从而提供了一种区分黑洞微观态与光滑无视界态的新诊断方法。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 超对称黑洞微观态与其他几何对应的态在混沌性质上应存在差异，但传统能级统计（level statistics）因超对称系统的能级精确简并而无法区分这一差异，因此亟需一种新的混沌诊断工具。

Method: 利用在理论耦合变化下微观态混合所决定的非阿贝尔Berry曲率（non-Abelian Berry curvature）作为混沌的内在探针；在D1/D5 CFT中的1/2-BPS态和𝒩=4 SYM中的1/4-BPS态上计算Berry曲率，并通过𝒩=2 super-JT引力和𝒩=2 SYK模型进行数值计算与解析分析。

Result: 对于无视界几何对应的态，边际形变下的Berry曲率是非随机的，且在一般耦合下常严格为零；而对于超对称黑洞微观态，Berry曲率呈现随机矩阵（random matrix）行为；此外，在𝒩=2 SYK模空间中还发现了由陈数（Chern numbers）表征的拓扑特征。

Conclusion: Berry曲率能够清晰地区分黑洞微观态与光滑无视界态，为超对称扇区中的混沌性质提供了一种鲁棒的诊断手段。

Abstract: We expect black hole microstates to differ in their chaotic properties from states associated with other geometries. For supersymmetric black holes, ordinary level statistics cannot diagnose this distinction, since their energy levels are exactly degenerate. We propose that there is an intrinsic probe of chaos, encoded in the mixing of the microstates under changes in the couplings of the theory, as determined by the non-Abelian Berry curvature of the BPS states under certain deformations. For states dual to horizonless geometries in holographic systems, such as 1/2-BPS states in the D1/D5 CFT and 1/4-BPS states in $\mathcal{N}=4$ SYM, we find that the Berry curvature for marginal deformations is non-random and often exactly zero at generic couplings. By contrast, for states dual to supersymmetric black holes, we show through computations in $\mathcal{N}=2$ super-JT gravity and explicit numerics in the $\mathcal{N}=2$ SYK model that the Berry curvature resembles a random matrix. We also uncover interesting topological features of the $\mathcal{N}=2$ SYK moduli space, as probed by Chern numbers. These results suggest that the Berry curvature sharply distinguishes black hole microstates from smooth horizonless states and provides a robust diagnostic of chaos in supersymmetric sectors.

</details>


### [139] [Smooth Threshold Effects from Dimensional Regularization](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23526)
*Yannick Kluth*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 提出一种基于维度正规化（dimensional regularization）的非最小重整化方案，该方案自然包含重粒子阈值效应，在高能极限下退化为最小消减方案（minimal subtraction），同时实现Appelquist-Carazzone定理，并在QCD单圈计算中验证其性质。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 标准的最小消减方案（minimal subtraction）等与质量无关的重整化方案（mass-independent scheme）无法自然处理重粒子阈值效应，且不满足Appelquist-Carazzone退化定理；需要一种与质量相关（mass-dependent）的方案来弥补这一缺陷。

Method: 基于维度正规化提出非最小重整化方案，通过在d≥4的维度中消去所有极点（poles）来重整化耦合常数和质量，从而引入质量依赖性；该方案在保留最小消减方案的规范无关性（gauge independence）等优势的同时，自然实现了阈值效应。

Result: 在QCD中进行显式单圈计算表明，该方案在高能极限下退化为最小消减方案，同时在粒子阈值处提供平滑过渡，并且实现了Appelquist-Carazzone定理，即重粒子在低能时自然退耦（decouple）。

Conclusion: 该非最小重整化方案兼具与质量无关方案和与质量相关方案的优点，为处理阈值效应提供了统一框架；论文还讨论了未来的潜在应用与扩展方向。

Abstract: We suggest a non-minimal renormalization scheme based on dimensional regularization that naturally incorporates threshold effects of heavy particles. By renormalizing couplings and masses to subtract all poles in $d \geq 4$, the resulting scheme is mass-dependent and circumvents shortcomings of mass-independent schemes like minimal subtraction. At the same time, many advantages of minimal subtraction such as gauge independence are retained. Through explicit one-loop computations in QCD, we demonstrate that this scheme reduces to minimal subtraction at high energies while providing smooth transitions at particle thresholds and implementing the Appelquist-Carazzone theorem. Potential future applications and extensions are discussed.

</details>


### [140] [Universal Interpretation of Hidden Zero and $2$-Split of Tree-Level Amplitudes Using Feynman Diagrams, Part $\mathbf{I}$: ${\rm Tr}(φ^3)$, NLSM and YM](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23680)
*Kang Zhou*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种通用的图论解释（universal diagrammatic interpretation），将原本为Tr(φ³)理论树图振幅开发的隐零点（hidden zeros）与2-分裂（2-splits）机制扩展至非线性西格玛模型（NLSM）和杨-米尔斯理论（YM），其核心是基于沿特定线的洗牌分解（SFASL）的费曼图因子化行为。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 方法的核心是沿特定线的洗牌分解（shuffle factorization along a specific line, SFASL），即在特定运动学约束下，费曼图通过洗牌置换（shuffle permutations）求和后沿特定线分离的因子化行为。将该机制从Tr(φ³)情形适配扩展至NLSM和YM振幅，实现统一处理。

Result: 通过SFASL，Tr(φ³)、NLSM和YM三种理论中树图振幅的隐零点与2-分裂获得了统一解释：隐零点归因于无质量粒子的在壳条件（on-shell condition）k_j²=0；2-分裂则对应于每个费曼图沿两条线分离的过程，类似于拉开两条拉链（unzipping two zippers）。

Conclusion: 本文建立了一个跨理论的统一图论框架，将此前仅适用于标量场理论的隐零点和2-分裂现象推广至涉及自发对称性破缺（NLSM）和规范相互作用（YM）的重要理论，表明该图论机制在树图振幅层面具有普适性。

Abstract: In this paper, we propose a universal diagrammatic interpretation of hidden zeros and $2$-splits of tree-level amplitudes. Originally developed for ${\rm Tr}(φ^3)$ amplitudes in our previous work, this interpretation is now extended to tree-level amplitudes in Nonlinear sigma model (NLSM) and Yang-Mills (YM) theories. The interpretation is based on a certain factorization behavior of Feynman diagrams under specific kinematic constraints, which we term shuffle factorization along a specific line (SFASL). This mechanism allows us to separate Feynman diagrams along specific lines after summing over shuffle permutations. When applied to NLSM and YM amplitudes, we perform proper extensions of the SFASL used in the ${\rm Tr}(φ^3)$ case. Through the SFASL, the interpretation for the hidden zeros and $2$-splits of tree amplitudes of ${\rm Tr}(φ^3)$, NLSM, and YM can be unified as: the hidden zeros are ascribed to the on-shell condition $k_j^2=0$ of a massless particle, while the $2$-splits are caused by separating each Feynman diagram along two lines, akin to unzipping two zippers.

</details>


### [141] [Rotating End of the World](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23845)

Result: 成功推导出包含边界自由度的BCFT热力学第一定律；确认阴影熵（shadow entropy）与边界熵（boundary entropy）通过HRT曲面等价；发现单关节与双关节EoW膜在视界外具有相同的外部构型，但视界内能量比较表明可能存在相变。

Abstract: We study the thermodynamics and interior structures of dynamical end of the world (EoW) branes in the rotating BTZ black hole. In addition, we verify that the shadow entropy is equivalent to the boundary entropy via Hubeny-Ryu-Takayanagi (HRT) surfaces. Furthermore, we explore the possible interior configurations of the EoW brane inside the horizon. Two representative configurations, namely single and double-joint EoW branes, are considered. These disparate configurations share the same exterior brane configuration outside the horizon. By comparing their energies, we show that a transition could occur within the horizon.

*Shi-Zheng Yang,Jian-Hua Gao,Zuo-Tang Liang,Georgy Yu. Prokhorov,Shi Pu,Oleg V. Teryaev,Valentin I. Zakharov*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明外尔（Weyl）迹反常（trace anomaly）在加速相对论流体中会诱导出一个新的非耗散矢量流。该反常唯一地确定了控制电磁场与流体加速度耦合的二阶输运系数。研究通过将流体动力学反常匹配（anomaly matching）扩展至包含迹反常，并在边界量子场论中利用加速观测者的林德勒视界（Rindler horizon）作为有效边界独立复现了这一结果。从边界视角看，电场和磁场扇区分别对应边界附近的屏蔽效应和真空磁化效应。在局部静止系中，电场贡献诱导额外电荷密度，磁场贡献产生具有能斯特（Nernst）型、更一般地具有热磁霍尔（thermomagnetic Hall）型张量结构的横向电流。该结果揭示了一类由迹反常控制的新型反常诱导输运现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索相对论流体中由量子反常（quantum anomaly）引发的非耗散输运现象，特别是超越传统的轴反常（axial anomaly）或手征反常（chiral anomaly），首次研究外尔迹反常（Weyl trace anomaly）在加速流体中对输运过程的独特作用。

Method: 采用两种互补方法：一是将流体动力学反常匹配（anomaly matching）框架扩展至包含迹反常（trace anomaly）；二是在边界量子场论中，将加速观测者的林德勒视界（Rindler horizon）视为有效边界，独立推导输运系数。

Result: 证明了迹反常唯一地确定了控制电磁场与流体加速度耦合的二阶输运系数；在边界图像中，电场扇区产生屏蔽效应并诱导额外电荷密度，磁场扇区产生真空磁化效应并生成具有能斯特-霍尔（Nernst-Hall）型张量结构的横向电流。

Conclusion: 发现了一类由外尔迹反常（Weyl trace anomaly）驱动的新型反常诱导输运机制，为理解反常流体动力学（anomalous hydrodynamics）提供了新的理论维度。

Abstract: We show that the Weyl (trace) anomaly gives rise to a new non-dissipative vector current in accelerated relativistic fluids. The anomaly uniquely fixes the second-order transport coefficient governing the coupling between the electromagnetic field and the fluid acceleration. We derive this result by extending hydrodynamic anomaly matching to include the trace anomaly, and independently reproduce it in boundary quantum field theory by treating the Rindler horizon of an accelerated observer as an effective boundary. From the boundary perspective, the electric- and magnetic-field sectors correspond to screening and vacuum magnetization effects near the boundary. In the local rest frame, the electric-field contribution induces an additional charge density, while the magnetic-field contribution generates a transverse current with a Nernst-like, more generally thermomagnetic Hall-like, tensor structure. Our results reveal a new class of anomaly-induced transport governed by the trace anomaly.

</details>


### [143] [Low-energy hadronic physics in holographic $\mathrm{QCD_{3}}$ with anisotropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24046)
*Si-wen Li*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文基于规范-引力对偶（gauge-gravity duality）构建各向异性D3/D7模型作为三维类QCD理论，系统研究了各向异性对强子质量谱、拖拽项（dragging terms）以及最低阶强子相互作用的影响。结果表明，拖拽项对各向异性理论的输运性质至关重要，且各向异性过大会导致强子系统失稳，这与此前模型结论一致。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在规范场论（gauge field theory）中理解各向异性（anisotropy）对强子物理性质的影响，是本研究的主要动机。通过全息方法（holography）构建各向异性类QCD模型，旨在系统阐明各向异性如何调制强子质量谱、拖拽项及最低阶强子相互作用。

Method: 采用规范-引力对偶（gauge-gravity duality）构建各向异性D3/D7模型，将其作为三维类QCD理论（three-dimensional QCD-like theory），在全息框架下系统研究各向异性对强子质量谱、拖拽项及最低阶强子相互作用的影响。

Result: 推导表明，拖拽项（dragging terms）在各向异性理论的有效作用量（effective action）中不可或缺，是影响对偶理论输运性质（transport properties）的关键因素。数值结果进一步揭示，当各向异性远大于禁闭能标（confinement energy scale）时，强子系统（hadronic system）将变得不稳定。

Conclusion: 各向异性足够大时，该模型的禁闭相（confining phase）会失稳，这与前期工作结论一致。因此，本研究有助于理解规范场论中的各向异性行为。

Abstract: Using the gauge-gravity duality, we construct the anisotropic D3/D7 approach as a three-dimensional QCD-like theory, then investigate systematically the hadronic mass spectra, the dragging terms and the lowest hadronic interactions in the presence of the anisotropy in holography. Our derivation illustrates the dragging terms in the effective action are very necessary for an anisotropic theory since they are the key roles to affect the transport properties of the dual theory. And the numerical results in addition imply the hadronic system will become unstable if the anisotropy is much larger than its confinement energy scale. It agrees with that the confining phase in this approach becomes unstable if the anisotropy is sufficiently large in our previous works with this model. Therefore, this work is constructive to understand the anisotropy in the gauge field theory.

</details>


### [144] [On a Deformed Holomorphic Chern-Simons Theory](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.12055)
*Eirik Høgmoe Kjelsnes,Eirik Eik Svanes,Vegard Undheim*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过在Calabi-Yau三流形上对经典全纯陈-西蒙斯理论进行复结构形变，发现了新的瞬子解（instanton solutions），并围绕这些背景对形变理论进行量子化，计算了大形变极限下的配分函数，同时研究了反常（anomalies）以及配分函数对形变参数$h$的依赖关系；特别地，耦合额外引力自由度后，在形变空间的特定方向得到了无反常的理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索在Calabi-Yau三流形（Calabi-Yau three-fold）上对全纯陈-西蒙斯理论（holomorphic Chern-Simons theory）进行复结构形变（complex structure deformation）后，能否产生新型瞬子解，并研究这些解在量子化及反常结构方面的物理后果。

Method: 利用形变参数$h \in \mathscr{H}^{0,1}(T^{1,0}X)$对复结构进行形变，导出运动方程并寻找对$h$重标不变的新瞬子解；通过Morse理论（Morse theory）对形变空间中使实规范理论（real gauge theory）具有厄米联络的方向进行分类；围绕瞬子背景对形变理论进行量子化，并在大形变极限下得到配分函数的显式表达式。

Result: 得到了与$G_2$流形上$G_2$-瞬子类似的新瞬子解，且当$h$的Yukawa耦合${\rm Yuk}(h,h,h)\neq 0$时可用于定义${\rm End}(T^{1,0}X)$上的联络来满足瞬子约束；该联络仅在形变空间的特定方向给出实丛${\rm End}(TX)$上的厄米（自伴）联络；大形变极限下得到了配分函数的显式形式，并揭示了反常及$h$依赖性；引入额外引力自由度后，形变空间的特殊方向产生了无反常的新理论。

Conclusion: 全纯陈-西蒙斯理论的复结构形变能够产生具有$G_2$-瞬子特征的新解，且通过特定形变方向可构造出无反常的实规范理论，为高维规范场论与几何结构之间的关联提供了新的理解。

Abstract: We deform classical holomorphic Chern--Simons theory on a Calabi--Yau three-fold $X$ by deforming the complex structure by a deformation parameter $h \in\mathscr{H}^{0,1}(T^{1,0}X)$. The corresponding equations of motion admit new "instanton solutions" which which are invariant under re-scalings of $h$, and are perhaps more reminiscent of $G_2$-instantons for $G_2$ manifolds. We give examples of such instantons. In particular, when $h$ has non-vanishing Yukawa coupling ${\rm Yuk}(h,h,h)\neq 0$, it may be used to define a connection on ${\rm End}(T^{1,0}X)$ solving the instanton constraint. Interestingly, this connection gives rise to a hermitian (self-adjoint) connection for a real gauge theory on the real bundle ${\rm End}(TX)$ for only specific directions in deformation space, which may be classified using Morse theory. We quantize the deformed theory around these instanton backgrounds, and derive explicit expressions for the partition function in the limit where the complex structure deformation is large. We study anomalies, and the $h$-dependece of the partition function. In particular, coupling the theory to additional gravitational degrees of freedom, we find that the special directions in deformation space give rise to novel anomaly free theories on ${\rm End}(T^{1,0}X)$.

</details>


### [145] [Super Landau Model and Howe Duality: From Supermonopole Harmonics to Quantum Matrix Geometry](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24112)
*Kazuki Hasebe*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文证明霍韦对偶（Howe duality）是超朗道模型（super Landau model）的核心结构，揭示了其与模糊超球面几何（fuzzy supersphere geometry）的联系，并通过能级投影方法构造了任意朗道能级下的非对易矩阵坐标，指出霍韦对偶可能构成矩阵模型几何（Matrix model geometries）的基本基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 朗道模型（Landau model）可作为量子矩阵几何的生成系统，而超朗道模型的深层代数结构和几何意义尚待揭示。本文旨在阐明霍韦对偶作为该模型底层结构的作用，并建立其与模糊几何（fuzzy geometry）及矩阵模型几何之间的系统性联系。

Method: 采用超旋量导数算子（super-spinor derivative operators）显式构造整数与半整数朗道能级（Landau level）下的超单极子谐函数（supermonopole harmonics）；通过能级投影方法（level projection method）导出任意朗道能级下的模糊超球面矩阵坐标，并精确确定非对易尺度因子（non-commutative scale factor）。

Result: 建立了超霍韦对偶与不同朗道能级之间的关联，揭示了其对偶模糊几何的涌现机制；构造了完整的超希尔伯特空间（super-Hilbert space）代数结构；提出了超流形上波函数的自洽概率诠释；证明了霍韦对偶的θ对应（theta correspondence）诱发了模糊对象之间的几何变换。

Conclusion: 霍韦对偶实现了内-外空间对偶（internal-external space duality），是量子矩阵几何（quantum matrix geometry）的底层结构，可能在理解矩阵模型几何中发挥基础性作用。

Abstract: Landau models serve as quantum mechanical systems for generating quantum matrix geometries. In this paper, we demonstrate that Howe duality provides the underlying structure of the super Landau model, reflecting a general feature of coset-type Landau models. The (super) Howe duality relates different Landau levels and accounts for the emergence of a dual fuzzy geometry. By employing super-spinor derivative operators, the supermonopole harmonics in both integer and half-integer Landau levels are explicitly constructed and the algebraic structure of the super-Hilbert space is revealed. We propose a consistent probabilistic interpretation for these wavefunctions defined on a supermanifold. Through a level projection method, we derive the matrix coordinates of fuzzy supersphere geometries for arbitrary Landau levels, along with a precise determination of the non-commutative scale factor. It is shown that the theta correspondence of Howe duality induces a geometric transformation between fuzzy objects. Finally, we point out that Howe duality realizes an internal-external space duality and underlies quantum matrix geometries, suggesting that it may play a fundamental role in understanding Matrix model geometries.

</details>


### [146] [Bounds on nonlinear effective field theories via resurgent relative entropy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24286)
*Pietro Conzinu,Daiki Ueda*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文研究具有阶乘增长微扰展开的非线性有效场论（effective field theory, EFT），利用重求和相对熵（resummed relative entropy）推导出EFT系数的符号约束，并通过费米子QED中的施温格效应（Schwinger effect）提供非微扰不稳定性的具体示例。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非线性有效场论的微扰展开常呈现阶乘增长，导致微扰级数不收敛，因此需要非微扰方法加以约束。此外，相对熵作为量子信息理论中的核心量，其与EFT算子结构的联系尚待深入探索。

Method: 研究了一类特定非线性EFT，其中相对熵编码了无穷高维算子（higher-dimensional operators）的塔式结构。通过对相对熵进行重求和，利用其非负性约束EFT系数的渐近增长符号。

Result: 重求和相对熵的非负性固定了EFT系数渐近增长的符号；相对熵的违反标志着理论存在不稳定性。在费米子QED中，通过从欧几里得时空（Euclidean spacetime）解析延拓到闵可夫斯基时空（Minkowski spacetime），具体展示了施温格效应这一非微扰不稳定性可由重求和相对熵捕捉。

Conclusion: 重求和相对熵为约束非线性EFT系数的渐近行为以及诊断非微扰不稳定性提供了有效工具，并可通过具体的量子场论实例（如施温格效应）加以验证。

Abstract: We study nonlinear effective field theories (EFTs) with factorially growing perturbative expansions, focusing on a class in which the relative entropy encodes an infinite tower of higher-dimensional operators. Using the resummed relative entropy, we derive bounds on EFT coefficients: the non-negativity of the resummed relative entropy fixes the sign of their asymptotic growth, while its violation signals instabilities. In fermionic QED, analytic continuation from Euclidean to Minkowski spacetime yields a concrete example: the Schwinger effect, a nonperturbative instability captured by the resummed relative entropy.

### [147] [Asymptotic regularization method. A constructive approach](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24292)
*Christian Durán Romero,Luis J. Garay,Mercedes Martín-Benito,Rita B. Neves*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于被积函数渐近展开结构分解的新型正则化方案（asymptotic regularization），通过区分并扣除驱动紫外奇点的贡献来系统处理量子场论中的发散积分，同时保持协变性与规范对称性。该方法在单尺度理论中可导出与重整化群无关的对数项，并自然适用于非标准紫外标度理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有正则化方案（如维数正规化、截断正规化）依赖相对论性幂次计数（relativistic power counting）或重整化群（renormalization group）流动，在处理具有修正色散关系（modified dispersion relations）和非标准紫外标度（non-standard UV scaling）的理论时面临限制。因此需要一种仅依赖于被积函数渐近结构而非具体幂次计数的系统性发散处理框架。

Method: 该方法对被积函数的渐近展开（asymptotic expansion）进行结构分解，区分驱动紫外奇点（UV singularities）的贡献与保持有限的贡献。通过隔离真正奇异的部分，在保持协变性（covariance）和规范对称性（gauge symmetry）的前提下实现发散的系统扣除。

Result: 在单尺度理论（single-scale theories）中，重整化量（renormalized quantities）表现出非局域的对数依赖性（non-local logarithmic dependence），该依赖由紫外渐近行为唯一决定。这一对数项的推导独立于标准重整化群流动。

Conclusion: 该渐近正则化方法（asymptotic regularization）不依赖标准相对论性幂次计数，因此可自然应用于具有修正色散关系和非标准紫外标度的理论。虽然本文针对紫外发散（ultraviolet divergences）进行阐述，但基本策略可直接推广至红外奇点（infrared singularities）。

Abstract: We introduce a new regularization scheme for divergent integrals in quantum field theory. The framework is based on the structural decomposition of the integrand asymptotic expansion, which distinguishes between contributions that drive UV singularities and those that remain finite. This asymptotic regularization method isolates the genuinely singular sector and enables a consistent subtraction of divergences while maintaining covariance and gauge symmetry. In single-scale theories, we show that the renormalized quantities exhibit a non-local logarithmic dependence uniquely determined by the UV asymptotics, offering a derivation of logarithmic terms that is independent of standard renormalization-group flows. Because it relies only on asymptotic structure rather than on standard relativistic power counting, the method is naturally applicable to theories with modified dispersion relations and non-standard UV scaling. Although formulated here for ultraviolet divergences, the underlying strategy extends straightforwardly to infrared singularities.

</details>


### [148] [Chiral Magnetic effect as the anomaly in the transverse axial vector Ward Identity](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24410)
*Fei Gao,Yi Lu,Minghui Ding,Xinyang Wang,Yuxin Liu*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文通过分析磁场下的夸克传播子，建立了轴反常（axial anomaly）源自磁场诱导的额外狄拉克结构这一结论，并证明手征磁效应（chiral magnetic effect, CME）与轴反常来自同一项，进而确认其电导率 $C_{\rm CME}=1/(2\pi^2)$ 在温度、化学势、磁场及相互作用下均保持稳健。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究磁场下夸克传播子中轴反常在狄拉克结构层面的起源，并厘清手征磁效应（chiral magnetic effect, CME）与轴反常之间的内在关联。

Method: 通过分析磁场下夸克传播子中出现的额外狄拉克结构，结合轴矢量Ward恒等式（axial vector Ward identity）将轴反常与系统的拓扑性质相联系；对树图传播子再现了Dirac Hamiltonian方法和动理学理论中反常轴流的结果，并利用泛函QCD方法下的完整夸克传播子进行数值验证。

Result: 手征磁效应（CME）来自与轴反常相同的项，具体而言是横向轴矢量Ward恒等式的反常；CME电导率 $C_{\rm CME}=1/(2\pi^2)$ 为常数，且对温度、化学势、磁场和相互作用均具有鲁棒性（robustness）。

Conclusion: 磁场下夸克传播子中的额外狄拉克结构是轴反常的根源；CME电导率的常数性质由横向轴矢量Ward恒等式的反常严格保证，并在泛函QCD计算中得到数值确认。

Abstract: Through analyzing the quark propagator under the magnetic field, we establish that the axial anomaly originates from an additional Dirac structure in quark propagator induced by the magnetic field. This Dirac structure also allows one to connect the axial anomaly with the topological properties of the system by checking the axial vector Ward identity. For the tree level propagator, we reproduce the result of the anomalous axial current as in the Dirac Hamiltonian approach and kinetic theory. Particularly, we confirm that the chiral magnetic effect (CME) comes from the same term that is in charge of the axial anomaly, specifically, as the anomaly of the transversal axial vector Ward Identity. The identity guarantees that the CME conductivity $C_{\rm CME}$ is a constant as $C_{\rm CME}=\frac{1}{2π^2}$, and is robust against the temperature, chemical potential, magnetic field and also interaction. Finally, we verify this numerically by applying the full quark propagator under magnetic field calculated from the functional QCD methods.

### [149] [Non-Relativistic Chern-Simons Supergravity with Torsion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24615)
*Francisco Barriga,Patrick Concha,Nelson Merino,Evelyn Rodríguez*

Main category: hep-th

TL;DR: 本文在Mielke-Baekler框架下构造了一个同时包含曲率(torsion)和挠率(curvature)的三维非相对论Chern-Simons超引力理论，通过从N=2超对称扩展的Mielke-Baekler代数出发并采用半群展开方法(semigroup expansion method)而非简单收缩，克服了非相对论超引力构造中的常见困难，得到了由两个参数(p,q)表征的统一框架，可插值于扩展Bargmann、Newton-Hooke及挠率模型等多种非相对论超引力理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非相对论超引力(non-relativistic supergravity)的构造通常面临超代数闭合性(superalgebra closure)和非退化不变双线性形式(non-degenerate invariant bilinear form)存在性等困难，已有方法难以同时包含曲率和挠率。本文旨在发展一种系统性的构造方法，在Mielke-Baekler框架下统一处理这些难题。

Method: 采用Mielke-Baekler框架，从N=2超对称扩展的Mielke-Baekler代数出发，利用半群展开方法(semigroup expansion method)而非传统的收缩(contraction)方法，进行非相对论展开，从而保证超代数的闭合性和非退化不变双线性形式的存在性。

Result: 成功构造了一个三维非相对论Chern-Simons超引力理论，该理论同时包含曲率(curvature)和挠率(torsion)。所得模型由两个自由参数(p,q)刻画，能够插值于扩展Bargmann、Newton-Hooke以及挠率模型等不同的非相对论超引力理论。

Conclusion: 该工作为非相对论超引力理论提供了一个包含挠率的统一框架(unified framework)，并为探索伽利略(Galilean)和卡罗尔(Carrollian)引力理论的超对称扩展(supersymmetric extension)开辟了新途径。

Abstract: In this work, we construct a three-dimensional non-relativistic Chern--Simons supergravity theory with both curvature and torsion within the Mielke--Baekler framework. We show that a consistent non-relativistic supergravity formulation requires starting from a $\mathcal{N}=2$ supersymmetric extension of the Mielke--Baekler algebra and implementing a non-relativistic expansion via the semigroup expansion method, rather than a naive contraction. This procedure allows one to overcome the usual difficulties of non-relativistic supergravity constructions, ensuring closure of the superalgebra and the existence of a non-degenerate invariant bilinear form. The resulting model is characterized by two parameters $(p,q)$, which interpolate between different non-relativistic supergravity theories, including the extended Bargmann, Newton--Hooke, and torsional models. Our results provide a unified framework for non-relativistic supergravity with torsion and open new avenues for exploring supersymmetric extensions of Galilean and Carrollian gravity theories.

</details>

### [150] [Spin-current model of electric polarization with the tensor gyromagnetic ratio](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22968)
*Mariya Iv. Trukhanova,Pavel A. Andreev*

Main category: cond-mat.other

TL;DR: 本文发展了考虑各向异性张量回磁比（g因子）的自旋电流模型，用于描述自旋起源的电极化。提出了三种磁电效应机制，分别由海森堡交换相互作用、Dzyaloshinsky-Moriya相互作用以及通过非磁性离子的对称交换相互作用奇次各向异性相关的自旋-自旋相互作用引起。推导了广义自旋电流模型中电极化对自旋密度和张量g因子的依赖关系，预测了摆线型和螺旋型自旋序中由回磁比非对角分量导致的新宏观电极化解。该扩展模型对含有重离子的磁性铁电体尤为重要。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有自旋电流模型通常假设各向同性的回磁比（g因子），难以描述具有各向异性g因子的磁性结构中由自旋起源产生的电极化（electric polarization）行为。

Method: 采用理论推导方法，针对具有各向异性张量回磁比的磁性结构，发展广义的自旋电流模型（spin-current model），分别引入对称海森堡交换相互作用、Dzyaloshinsky-Moriya相互作用以及与非磁性离子相关的奇次各向异性对称交换相互作用这三种磁电效应机制。

Result: 导出了广义自旋电流模型中电极化对自旋密度和张量g因子的依赖关系。预测了在摆线型（cycloidal）和螺旋型（helicoidal）自旋序中，由回磁比非对角分量引起的宏观电极化新解。

Conclusion: 将自旋电流模型扩展到包含张量g因子，对于研究含有重离子且参与形成磁电效应（magnetoelectric effect）的磁性铁电体具有重要意义。

Abstract: The spin-current model of electric polarization of spin origin is developed for a magnetic structure with anisotropic tensor gyromagnetic ratio (g-factor). Three mechanisms of the magnetoelectric effect are proposed, caused by the symmetric Heisenberg exchange interaction, the Dzyaloshinsky-Moriya interaction, and the spin-spin interaction related to the odd anisotropy of the symmetric exchange interaction of magnetic ions via nonmagnetic ion. The dependence of electric polarization on the spin density and tensor g-factor in the generalized spin-current model is derived. New solutions for macroscopic electric polarization, that arise in the cycloidal and helicoidal spin orders and are caused by the non-diagonal components of the gyromagnetic ratio, are predicted. The extended of the spin-current model to including a tensor g-factor can be important for the magnetic ferroelectrics with heavy ions which take part in the formation of magnetoelectric effect.

</details>

### [151] [Effect of kinetic energy operator on double heterostructures spectra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23011)
*R. Valencia-Torres,J. García-Ravelo,E. Choreño-Ortiz,J. Avendaño*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 该论文研究了势场中载流子质量随位置变化时，动能算符（kinetic energy operator）的歧义性对双异质结构（double heterostructure）能谱的影响。采用解析推导超越方程与反射系数极点两种方法计算能谱，并补充了另一种动能算符的谱结果，最后批判性地分析了关于某些动能算符在简单异质结构中适用性的已有论断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 当电荷载流子的有效质量在异质结构中随位置变化时，动能算符的构造存在固有歧义性。该研究旨在系统评估这种歧义性对双异质结构（double heterostructure, DH）能谱计算的影响，并澄清此前关于不同动能算符（kinetic energy operator, KEO）相对重要性的某些论断。

Method: 采用两种互补方法计算能谱。第一种方法通过解析过程得到满足超越方程（transcendental equation）的能谱，但该方法并非对所有体系都适用；第二种方法将能谱对应于异质结构反射系数（reflection coefficient）的极点，该方法几乎适用于任何双异质结构。两种方法结合使用，以计算另一种动能算符的谱结果。

Result: 所获得的能谱补充了先前文献中已报道的结果，新增了另一种动能算符（KEO）对应的谱。通过这两种方法的对比分析，批判性地检验了此前关于某些动能算符（kinetic energy operator）在较简单异质结构中具有何种相关性的若干论断。

Conclusion: 动能算符的歧义性对双异质结构（double heterostructure, DH）能谱有实质性影响；解析推导超越方程与反射系数极点这两种方法可以互为补充，用于系统评估不同动能算符（KEO）的效应，并对已有文献中的相关论断进行重新审视和批判性分析。

Abstract: We report on the effect of the kinetic energy operator ambiguity on the energy spectra of various double heterostructures when the mass of the charge carriers, subjected to a potential, depends on position. The spectra are calculated using two complementary techniques. In the first case, which is not always possible, the energy spectrum satisfies a transcendental equation, which is obtained through an analytical process. While in the second, which can be used practically in any double heterostructure (DH), the energy spectra correspond to the poles of the reflection coefficient of the heterostructure. The spectra thus obtained complement those already reported in a previous reference, since we now include the spectra of another kinetic energy operator (KEO). Finally, we show how these methods allow us to critically analyze some statements that have been made about the relevance of some kinetic energy operators in some simpler heterostructures.

</details>


### [152] [The large-mass limit of interacting quantum gases in the continuum](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23020)
*Spyros Garouniatis,Grega Saksida,Vedran Sohinger*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了热平衡下相互作用量子（玻色或费米）气体的大质量极限，证明在适当定义的大质量极限下，系统退化为经典相互作用粒子气体。研究在连续体系（continuum regime）中展开，通过调节化学势，以Ginibre环系综（Ginibre loop ensemble）为起点进行分析。在有限体积下，针对稳定且Hölder连续的相互作用势获得了显式收敛速率；对于非负且满足适当可积性条件的相互作用势，利用集团展开（cluster expansions）研究了无限体积问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 此前Fröhlich、Knowles、Schlein及第三作者已在格点（lattice）上研究了玻色子的大质量极限问题，本文旨在将该分析推广至连续体系（continuum regime），其中需要适当调节化学势（chemical potential）。

Method: 以Ginibre环系综（Ginibre loop ensemble）为起点，该系综允许将热平衡下的相互作用量子气体描述为相互作用布朗路径（Brownian paths）的系综。在有限体积下，对于稳定（stable）且Hölder连续的相互作用势进行分析；对于非负且满足适当可积性条件的相互作用势，采用集团展开（cluster expansions）处理无限体积问题。

Result: 在有限体积下，获得了大质量极限的显式收敛速率（explicit rates of convergence）。在无限体积下，对于非负且满足可积性条件的相互作用势，建立了相应的极限结果。

Conclusion: 在适当定义的大质量极限（large-mass limit）下，相互作用的量子（玻色或费米）气体退化为经典相互作用粒子气体（gas of classical interacting particles）。

Abstract: We study the large-mass limit of interacting quantum (Bose or Fermi) gases in thermal equilibrium. We show that in the suitably-defined large-mass limit, the system gives rise to a gas of classical interacting particles. The corresponding question for bosons on a lattice was previously addressed by Fröhlich, Knowles, Schlein, and the third author. In this work, we study the continuum regime which requires us to suitably tune the chemical potential. The starting point of our analysis is the Ginibre loop ensemble, which allows one to describe a system of interacting quantum gases in thermal equilibrium in terms of an ensemble of interacting Brownian paths. In a finite volume, our analysis is performed for stable and Hölder continuous interaction potentials and we are able to obtain explicit rates of convergence. When the interaction potential is nonnegative and satisfies suitable integrability conditions, we study the associated infinite-volume problem by means of cluster expansions.

</details>


### [153] [Matched asymptotics of Rayleigh-wave fields near cuspidal ridges and gorges](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23253)
*Oleg Kiselev*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过局部匹配渐近方法（local matched-asymptotic description）构建了尖点形自由表面附近瑞利波（Rayleigh waves）产生的时谐弹性场（time-harmonic elastic fields）描述。尖点状凹谷（cuspidal gorge）的主导场为Williams裂纹尖端场（Williams crack-tip field），应力行为为r^{-1/2}；尖点状脊（cuspidal ridge）则表现为弹性喇叭（elastic horn），其自由尖端场渐近刚性（bounded stress），而截断尖端则产生高能分支，应力增长为ρ^{-m}。有限元计算验证了这些预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究瑞利波在具有尖点形几何元素（cuspidal elements）的自由表面附近产生的时谐弹性场，此类几何包括尖点状凹谷和尖点状脊，其局部行为尚缺乏统一的渐近描述。

Method: 采用局部匹配渐近方法（local matched-asymptotic description）构建时谐弹性场的解析描述；自由表面由指数0<α<1的尖点图（cusp graph）或等效的消失宽度喇叭（vanishing-width horn）b(s)=B s^m表示，其中m=1/α>1；并结合有限元（finite-element）数值计算验证。

Result: 尖点状凹谷的主导场为Williams裂纹尖端场，应力行为为r^{-1/2}；尖点状脊的自由尖端场渐近刚性（应力有界），而截断尖端的高能分支中应力增长为σ∼ρ^{-m}。有限元计算结果支持这些预测：脊的自由尖端测试未出现裂纹式增长，截断脊恢复高能律，凹谷应力斜率接近-1/2。

Conclusion: 尖点形自由表面的弹性场行为由其几何类型决定：凹谷以裂纹型奇异性主导，脊则以刚性尖端为可容许解，截断尖端产生更强奇异性。该工作为瑞利波在尖锐几何附近的局部场行为提供了定量渐近框架。

Abstract: We construct a local matched-asymptotic description of time-harmonic elastic fields generated by Rayleigh waves near cuspidal elements of a traction-free surface. The free surface is represented locally by a cusp graph with exponent $0<α<1$, or equivalently by a vanishing-width horn $b(s)=B s^m$, $m=1/α>1$. A cuspidal gorge is a zero-opening re-entrant notch: its leading field is the Williams crack-tip field, and the stresses behave as $r^{-1/2}$. The cusp exponent affects the gorge through lower-order corrections and through the stress cut-off produced by rounding the bottom. In contrast, a cuspidal ridge behaves as an elastic horn with vanishing width. The leading admissible free-tip field is asymptotically rigid (bounded stress), distinct from the high-energy branch supported by a finite tip truncation, where stresses grow as $σ\sim ρ^{-m}$. Finite-element calculations for the local static Lamé problems support these predictions: the free-tip ridge test confirms the absence of crack-like growth, the truncated ridge recovers the high-energy law, and the gorge stress slope is found to be close to $-1/2$.

</details>


### [154] [Q-Manifolds and Sigma Models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23496)
*Noriaki Ikeda*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文综述了Batalin-Vilkovisky（BV）形式论的最新进展及其相关几何结构，将BV形式论的数学结构总结为Q-流形和QP-流形，并通过李代数、李代数胚等高阶代数胚实例加以阐释，最后利用李代数胚和Courant代数胚的几何结构构造了BV作用量泛函。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 系统梳理Batalin-Vilkovisky（BV）形式论在几何方面的最新发展，并阐明其与李代数、李代数胚等代数结构的深层联系。

Method: 采用Q-流形（Q-manifold）和QP-流形（QP-manifold）的数学框架来统一描述BV形式论的结构，并以李代数（Lie algebras）、李代数胚（Lie algebroids）及高阶代数胚作为典型实例加以说明。

Result: 阐释了BV形式论的数学结构可归结为Q-流形与QP-流形；展示了李代数、李代数胚及高阶代数胚是Q-和QP-流形的典型例子；并基于李代数胚和Courant代数胚（Courant algebroids）的几何结构构造了BV作用量泛函（BV action functionals）。

Conclusion: BV形式论的几何化描述——Q-流形与QP-流形框架——为理解李代数、李代数胚及高阶代数胚提供了统一的视角，并可通过这些几何结构直接构造BV作用量泛函。

Abstract: Recent developments of Batalin-Vilkovisky (BV) formalism and related geometry are reviewed. Mathematical structures of BV formalism are summarized as a Q-manifold and a QP-manifold. Lie algebras, Lie algebroids and other higher algebroids are explained as typical examples of Q- and QP-manifolds. Finally, the BV action functionals are constructed by geometric structures of Lie algebroids and Courant algebroids.

### [155] [A Note on the Resolvent Algebra and Functional Integral Approach to the van Hove Model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23497)
*Yoshitsugu Sekine*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文是一组关于van Hove模型的计算笔记，从算子代数（Weyl代数和预解代数）与泛函积分两种视角，讨论了点源情形下红外与紫外截断的移除、基态与β-KMS态的存在性，以及有限温度无穷大体系中的玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚（Bose–Einstein condensation）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 系统梳理van Hove模型在算子代数与泛函积分框架下的数学结构，澄清截断移除与热力学极限下态的存在性问题。

Method: 采用算子代数方法（Weyl代数与预解代数（resolvent algebra））以及泛函积分方法（functional integral approach），对点源耦合情形下的红外与紫外截断（infrared and ultraviolet cutoffs）进行移除分析。

Result: 点源情形下，红外与紫外截断的移除能够实现，基态（ground state）与β-KMS态存在；在无穷大体系有限温度下可出现玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚。

Conclusion: van Hove模型在算子代数与泛函积分双重视角下均支持截断移除与热力学极限的构建，且能描述玻色-爱因斯坦凝聚现象。

Abstract: This paper is a collection of the author's computational notes on the van Hove model and contains no essentially new results. We discuss, from both the operator-algebraic perspective via the Weyl algebra and the resolvent algebra and the functional integral approach, the removal of infrared and ultraviolet cutoffs and the existence of the ground state and $β$-KMS states in the case of a point source. In the infinite-volume system at finite temperature, Bose--Einstein condensation can arise.

</details>


### [156] [Regularization of Divergent Power Sums via Fractional Extension of Differential Generators](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23544)
*Eric A. Galapon*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文重新审视发散级数 $\sum_{n=1}^{\infty}n^\alpha$ 的正则化问题，提出一种两步正则化方案：先对整数 $m$ 正则化，再通过一致性条件推广到非整数 $\alpha$。该方法以微分生成元 $L$ 构造广义谱函数（GSF），发现正则化结果等于黎曼 zeta 正则化值加上由生成元 $L$ 决定的附加项。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 发散级数 $\sum_{n=1}^{\infty}n^\alpha$ 的正则化是量子场论（quantum field theory）和统计力学（statistical mechanics）中的基本问题，现有的黎曼 zeta 正则化（Riemann zeta regularization）虽被广泛使用，但其推广到非整数 $\alpha$ 的连续性与一致性缺乏系统性框架。本文旨在建立一种更具一般性的正则化处方，将黎曼 zeta 正则化作为特例纳入，并保证整数与非整数情形之间的连续过渡。

Method: 将正则化问题分解为两步：第一步，对每个非负整数 $m$ 定义发散和 $\sum_{n=1}^{\infty}n^m$ 的正则化；第二步，在一致性条件（整数 $m$ 的正则化值需从非整数 $\alpha$ 的情形连续地得到）下，将正则化推广到非整数 $\alpha$。该方法引入一个微分生成元 $L=L(\mathrm{d}/\mathrm{d}t)$，通过它构造广义谱函数（generalized spectral function, GSF）$K_L(t)$。要求 GSF 在复平面中具有以 $z=0$ 为极点的全纯延拓 $K_L(z)$，从而将正则化值表示为闭路积分。对于生成元 $L=h(t)\mathrm{d}/\mathrm{d}t$（其中 $1/h(z)$ 为整函数），推导出具体的正则化结果。

Result: 对于整数 $m$，正则化值为 $\sum_{n=1}^{\infty} n^m = (2πi)^{-1}\oint_C L^m K_L(z) z^{-1}\mathrm{d}z$，其中 $C$ 为仅包围原点处极点的闭合围道。对于非整数 $\alpha$，在一致性条件下正则化值为 $\sum_{n=1}^{\infty}n^\alpha=(2πi)^{-1}\int_{\tilde{C}} L^\alpha K_L(z) z^{-1}\mathrm{d}z$，其中 $L^\alpha$ 是 $L^m$ 的分数阶推广，$\tilde{C}$ 为 $C$ 的适当形变。该正则化结果等于黎曼 zeta 正则化值加上由生成元 $L$ 决定的附加项。

Conclusion: 本文提出的两步正则化方案为发散级数 $\sum_{n=1}^{\infty}n^\alpha$ 提供了统一且一致的正则化框架，其核心是通过微分生成元 $L$ 和广义谱函数 $K_L(t)$ 的构造实现整数与非整数情形的连续衔接。黎曼 zeta 正则化被证明是该方案的一个特例，而生成元的自由度引入了额外的修正项，为不同物理场景下的正则化选择提供了灵活性。

Abstract: We reconsider the problem of regularizing the divergent series $\sum_{n=1}^{\infty}n^α$ for $\operatorname{Re}α>-1$, and offer a regularization prescription that yields the Riemann zeta regularization as a special case. The development of the regularization is framed as a two-step problem. The first step is prescribing a regularization of the divergent sum $\sum_{n=1}^{\infty}n^m$ for every non-negative integer $m$; and the second step is the extension of the sum for non-integer $α$. The extension is obtained under the consistency condition that the regularized sum for integer $m$ emerges continuously from the sum for non-integer $α$. The scheme is specified by a differential generator $L=L(\mathrm{d}/\mathrm{d}t)$ through which a generalized spectral function (GSF), $K_L(t)$, is constructed. Under the condition that the GSF has a holomorphic complex extension $K_L(z)$ with $z=0$ as a pole, the case for integer $m$ takes the regularized value $\sum_{n=1}^{\infty} n^m = (2πi)^{-1}\oint_C L^m K_L(z) z^{-1}\mathrm{d}z$, where $C$ is a closed contour enclosing only the pole of $K_L(z)$ at the origin. On the other hand, under the consistency condition, the case for non-integer $α$ takes the value $\sum_{n=1}^{\infty}n^α=(2πi)^{-1}\int_{\tilde{C}} L^α K_L(z) z^{-1}\mathrm{d}z$, where $L^α$ is the fractional extension of $L^m$ and $\tilde{C}$ is an appropriate deformation of the contour $C$. Here, we obtain the regularization corresponding to the generator $L=h(t) \mathrm{d}/\mathrm{d}t$, where $h(t)$ has the analytic extension $h(z)$ such that $1/h(z)$ is an entire function. We find that the regularized sum is equal to the Riemann zeta regularized value plus terms determined by the generator $L$.

</details>


### [157] [Deformed and undeformed localized wave solutions for the two-component (2+1)-dimensional Fokas-Lenells equation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23684)
*Yanan Wang*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用广义达布变换（Darboux transformation, DT）方法，对(2+1)维双分量Fokas-Lenells方程进行了系统研究，构造了行列式形式的广义DT，并得到了变形孤子、变形positons以及变形呼吸子、变形Y形呼吸子等精确解，同时通过广义DT导出了高阶怪波解和呼吸子-怪波解，丰富了该方程的解族，并验证了DT在多维多分量系统中的有效性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 研究(2+1)维双分量Fokas-Lenells方程，该方程描述了非线性介质中具有多模相互作用和多维效应的超短光脉冲传播，旨在丰富该方程的解族并验证达布变换（Darboux transformation）方法在多维多分量系统中的适用性。

Method: 首先构造广义达布变换（generalized Darboux transformation）的行列式形式；随后利用DT方法在零背景和非零背景下分别获得变形孤子、变形positons以及变形呼吸子、变形Y形呼吸子；最后通过广义DT导出高阶怪波解和呼吸子-怪波解。

Result: 获得了变形孤子（deformed solitons）、变形positons（deformed positons，零背景下）以及变形呼吸子（deformed breathers）、变形Y形呼吸子（deformed Y-shaped breathers，非零背景下）；此外还得到了未变形的解，包括高阶怪波解（higher-order rogue wave solutions）和呼吸子-怪波解（breather-rogue wave solutions）。

Conclusion: 本研究不仅丰富了(2+1)维双分量Fokas-Lenells方程的解族，还验证了达布变换方法在多维和多分量系统中的有效性。

Abstract: In this paper, we focus on the two-component (2+1)-dimensional Fokas-Lenells equation, which models the propagation of ultrashort optical pulses in nonlinear media with multi-mode interactions and multi-dimensional effects. Firstly, we construct the determinant form of the generalized Darboux transformation (DT). Secondly, we obtain deformed solitons, deformed positons on the zero background and deformed breathers, deformed Y-shaped breathers on the nonzero backgrounds by DT method. Finally, the undeformed solutions including higher-order rogue wave solutions and breather-rogue wave solutions are derived by generalized DT. This work enriches the solution family associated with the equation, but also illustrates the efficiency of DT method in multi-dimensional and multi-component systems.

</details>


### [158] [Gradual eigenvector ergodization in coupled Ginibre matrices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23708)
*Margherita Disertori,Yan V. Fyorodov*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了由两个独立复Ginibre随机矩阵通过确定性耦合参数c相互作用构成的非厄米系统，揭示了特征向量随耦合强度从局域化到全系统扩展的渐近行为，并发现当耦合强度按N的平方根缩放时，原点处的平均特征值密度在临界值|\tilde{c}|=1处消失，表明谱支撑在复平面中分裂为两个不连通区域。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米随机矩阵（non-Hermitian random matrices）为理解具有损耗或增益的耗散量子混沌系统（dissipative quantum chaotic systems）的普适行为提供了重要框架。本文旨在定量刻画两个相互作用非厄米子系统的特征向量随耦合强度从局域化到全系统扩展的渐变过程。

Method: 模型由两个独立的N×N复Ginibre矩阵（complex Ginibre matrices）构成，通过确定性矩阵c 1_N耦合，其中c为复耦合参数，|c|控制相互作用强度。系统在N→∞极限下推导特征向量扩展的渐近公式，并在耦合按c=√N \tilde{c}缩放时计算原点z=0处的平均特征值密度（mean eigenvalue density）。

Result: 当|c|=0时，特征向量局域于单个子系统；随着|c|增大，特征向量逐渐扩展至整个系统，渐近公式完整刻画了特征向量在整个过渡区域的逐渐遍历化（gradual ergodization）过程。当耦合按c=√N \tilde{c}缩放时，原点处极限密度在|\tilde{c}|>1时消失，表明谱支撑（density support）在复平面中分裂为两个不相交的区域。

Conclusion: 该模型给出了耦合强度主导下特征向量从局域化到完全遍历化的完整定量图像，并揭示了在强耦合极限下谱支撑的分裂现象，为理解非厄米量子混沌系统的普适行为提供了新的解析结果。

Abstract: Non-Hermitian random matrices provide a useful framework for understanding universal characteristics of dissipative quantum chaotic systems with loss or gain. We consider a model of two such system represented by two independent $N\times N$ complex Ginibre matrices interacting via a deterministic matrix $c{\bf 1}_N$, where $c$ is the complex coupling parameter whose magnitude $|c|$ controls the interaction strength. We characterize quantitatively how the eigenvectors of the whole system, initially localized in one of the individual subsystems for $|c|=0$, eventually spread over the full system with growing interaction strength. The resulting asymptotic formula describing such spread in the limit $N\to \infty$ is very explicit and provides a full picture of the gradual ergodization of eigenvectors as a function of the coupling parameter $|c|$ in the whole transition regime. As a by-product of our method we also compute the mean eigenvalue density for our model at the origin of the spectral bulk $z=0$ in the fully ergodic regime, when the coupling is scaled with the matrix size as $c=\sqrt{N}\tilde{c}$. We find that as $N\to \infty$ the limiting density at the origin vanishes beyond the critical value $|\tilde{c}|=1$, signalling of a split of the density support in the complex plane into two disjoint domains.

</details>

### [160] [Liouville Quantum Duality and Random Planar Maps II](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24180)
*Bertrand Duplantier,Emmanuel Guitter*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文是块加权平面地图与刘维尔量子对偶项目的第二部分，聚焦对偶临界点的标度性质，推导了根块大小与总大小的条件分布，证明其与修改后的刘维尔量子引力（LQG）结果完全一致，并分析了块距离剖面、多分形谱等，通过三类具体模型予以验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在块加权平面地图（block-weighted planar map）与刘维尔量子对偶（Liouville quantum duality）的框架下，进一步验证对偶临界点（dual critical point）上的标度行为是否与刘维尔量子引力（Liouville quantum gravity, LQG）的理论预言一致，从而深化对地图组合结构与量子重力之间对偶关系的理解。

Method: 推导根块大小（root block size）在总大小给定下的条件分布，以及总大小在根块大小给定下的分布；将分区函数比值与LQG中带有原子贡献（atomic contributions）的修正刘维尔随机测度进行解析对比；通过双根地图（doubly rooted maps）的块距离剖面（block distance profile）与单块地图的距离剖面建立严格联系；分析常规与对偶刘维尔测度的多分形（multifractal）性质，预测对应的谱。

Result: 条件分布律与LQG结果完美匹配；对偶与直接带穿刺分区函数（partition functions with punctures）的比值具有普适性（universal），其LQG表达式精确对应组合模拟结果；双根地图的块距离剖面可归约为单块地图的距离剖面；给出了多分形谱的量子与欧几里得（Euclidean）两个视角的预测。

Conclusion: 三类具体模型（简单块分解的四角剖分、四角地图构成的树状结构、3-连通块分解的双立方地图）均验证了理论结果，每个模型仅有一个非普适常数唯一确定对应原子刘维尔测度的强度，进一步证实了组合地图与LQG之间的精确对偶关系。

Abstract: This is Part II of our project on block-weighted planar maps and Liouville quantum duality. Focusing on the scaling properties at the dual critical point, we derive the conditional distribution of the root block size given the total size, as well as, conversely, the distribution of the total size for a fixed root block size. We show that these laws are in perfect agreement with the results of Liouville quantum gravity (LQG), obtained by modifying the standard Liouville random measure with additional atomic contributions representing localized quantum areas. The ratio of dual and direct partition functions with punctures is shown to be universal, its explicit LQG expression exactly matching its combinatorial analogue. We also investigate the block distance profile for doubly rooted maps, which is here rigorously related to the distance profile of maps consisting of a single block. Finally, we analyze the multifractal properties of the usual and dual Liouville measures, predicting the associated spectra, from both quantum and Euclidean perpectives. We illustrate our results through specific realizations of block-weighted planar maps, i.e., quadrangulations decomposed into simple blocks, tree-like structures formed by attaching quartic maps, and bicubic maps decomposed into 3-connected blocks. For each model, we give the single non-universal constant which uniquely determines the strength of the corresponding atomic Liouville measure.

### [161] [Torus one-point functions in critical loop models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24491)
*Paul Roux,Sylvain Ribault,Jesper Lykke Jacobsen*

Main category: math-ph

TL;DR: 本文证明了临界环模型（critical loop models）中环面单点函数（torus 1-point functions）可以用不同中心荷（central charge）下的球面四点函数（sphere 4-point functions）表示。与Moore–Seiberg形式体系不同，球面上的交叉对称性（crossing symmetry）由此蕴含了环面上的模协变性（modular covariance）。作者利用数值自举方法（numerical bootstrap）系统计算了临界环模型中的环面单点函数，重点关注6个最简单首要场（primary fields）的单点函数，得到了10个满足模协变方程的解。这些单点函数是共形块（conformal blocks）的无限线性组合，其系数是双Gamma函数（double Gamma functions）的乘积乘以环权重（loop weights）的多项式函数。对每个解，作者确定了前6到12个多项式。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 理解环面单点函数与球面四点函数之间的内在联系，并在超越Moore–Seiberg形式体系的框架下，建立球面交叉对称性与环面模协变性之间的逻辑关系，从而推动共形场论（conformal field theory）中不同几何拓扑下关联函数之间统一描述的发展。

Method: 采用数值自举方法（numerical bootstrap），基于模协变方程系统计算临界环模型中环面单点函数的级数表达式。单点函数被展开为共形块的无限线性组合，系数由双Gamma函数乘积和环权重的多项式函数构成，并通过计算确定每个解的前6至12个多项式。

Result: 针对6个最简单的首要场，获得了10个满足模协变方程的环面单点函数解；每个解对应一组确定的系数多项式，作者给出了每个解的前6至12个多项式。

Conclusion: 临界环模型中环面单点函数可由球面四点函数在另一中心荷下的形式表达，这一发现在理论上简化了几何拓扑不同的关联函数之间的关系；数值自举方法能够有效求解环面单点函数，为后续共形场论的计算提供了可行路径。

Abstract: We show that in critical loop models, torus 1-point functions can be expressed in terms of sphere 4-point functions at a different central charge. Unlike in the Moore--Seiberg formalism, crossing symmetry on the sphere therefore implies modular covariance on the torus.
  We systematically compute torus 1-point functions in critical loop models, using a numerical bootstrap approach. We focus on the 1-point functions of the 6 simplest primary fields, which give rise to 10 solutions of modular covariance equations. Such 1-point functions are infinite linear combinations of conformal blocks. The coefficients are products of double Gamma functions, times polynomial functions of loop weights. For each solution, we determine the first 6 to 12 polynomials.

### [162] [Super-Chevalley Restriction and Relative Lie Algebra Cohomology over the 2|3 Algebra](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23549)

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 构造并分析自然 $3|2$ 超交换限制映射（super-commuting restriction map）作为 Chevalley 限制（Chevalley restriction）的超类似物，通过具体实例 $\mathfrak{so}_7$、$\mathfrak{sl}_2$ 等约化李代数检验该映射的同构性、稳定像预期（stable-image expectations）以及 Langlands 对偶（Langlands duality）下的上同调不变量。

Conclusion: 记录恢复对偶性所需的差分算子（differential）的猜想性量子形变（quantum deformation），并提供将 $\mathfrak{so}_7$ 的偶然类与非 Cartan 类配对的一阶证据（first-order evidence），暗示可能存在更深层的量子校正结构。

Abstract: Let $A:=\mathbb{C}[z_+,z_-]\otimes Λ(θ_1,θ_2,θ_3)$, with $z_\pm$ even and $θ_1,θ_2,θ_3$ odd. For a reductive Lie algebra $\mathfrak g$, let $\mathfrak g[A]:=\mathfrak g\otimes A$ be the corresponding current Lie superalgebra. Motivated by the Chang--Yin description of weak-coupling $1/16$-BPS cohomology in $\mathcal N=4$ super-Yang--Mills, we study the relative Lie algebra cohomology $H^\bullet(\mathfrak g[A],\mathfrak g;\mathbb{C})$. We isolate three finite-rank phenomena. First, the natural $3|2$ super-commuting restriction map, viewed as a super analogue of Chevalley restriction and its commuting-scheme variants, already fails to be an isomorphism for $\mathfrak g=\mathfrak{so}_7$; the obstruction is a non-Cartan class. Second, the same algebra produces explicit fortuitous classes for $\mathfrak{sl}_2$ and $\mathfrak{so}_7$, giving concrete counterexamples to naive stable-image expectations suggested by the type-A Loday--Quillen--Tsygan theorem and its current-algebra refinements. Third, the classical relative cohomologies for the Langlands-dual pair $(\mathfrak{so}_7,\mathfrak{sp}_6)$ are not isomorphic. We then record the conjectural quantum deformation of the differential expected to restore duality, together with first-order evidence pairing the fortuitous and non-Cartan $\mathfrak{so}_7$ classes.

### [163] [Quantitative Hölder Regularity, Concentration, and Spectral Applications for Lyapunov Exponents of Random $GL(2,\mathbb{R})$ Cocycles, with Extensions to $GL(d,\mathbb{R})$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24057)
*Abdoulaye Thiam*

Main category: math.DS

TL;DR: 本文为GL(2,ℝ)及高维随机矩阵乘积的Lyapunov指数建立了定量正则性理论，给出了显式闭式Hölder指数和模量连续性常数，并扩展至大偏差原理、浓度不等式、Markov链驱动乘积以及一维随机Schrödinger算子的态密度连续性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有随机矩阵乘积Lyapunov指数的连续性结果多为定性或仅知存在性，缺乏显式的定量Hölder指数和模量连续性常数，且在不同度量框架下的精确行为尚不明确。

Method: 采用谱隙方法（spectral-gap method），基于Wasserstein-plus-Hausdorff度量建立显式闭式Hölder指数β_*(ν,θ)，并利用同一框架推导大偏差原理、Hoeffding-Azuma浓度不等式、Markov链驱动乘积的显式连续性指数，以及随机Schrödinger算子态密度的定量对数Hölder模量。

Result: 给出了GL(2,ℝ)上具简单Lyapunov谱的紧支撑测度ν的显式Hölder指数与常数；识别了Tall-Viana对数Hölder指数在自然混合假设下为κ_*(ν,θ)=θ/(2+θ)，在永续（perpetuity）区域为θ/(8(1+θ))；将Hölder理论推广至GL(d,ℝ)的顶指数及各次顶指数（子指数）；方法最优性命题表明β_*是线性公理下的最优指数。

Conclusion: 谱隙方法能够系统性地导出多类随机动力系统对象（Lyapunov指数、大偏差率函数、浓度不等式、Schrödinger算子态密度）的定量正则性，但无法在整个紧支撑测度空间上实现一致Hölder连续性，存在本质性下界限制。

Abstract: This paper develops a quantitative regularity theory for the Lyapunov exponents of random products of matrices in $GL(2,\mathbb{R})$, with extensions to $GL(d,\mathbb{R})$ for all $d \geq 2$. At every compactly supported measure $ν$ with simple Lyapunov spectrum, we give an explicit closed-form Hölder exponent $β_*(ν, θ)$ and constant in the modulus of continuity of $λ_\pm$ in the Wasserstein-plus-Hausdorff metric, depending only on the eccentricity of $\mathrm{supp}\,ν$, the Lyapunov gap, and the Hölder index $θ$. The same spectral-gap method yields a large deviation principle with explicit rate function, Hoeffding-Azuma concentration inequalities, an extension to Markov-chain driven cocycles with closed-form exponent, and a quantitative log-Hölder modulus of continuity for the integrated density of states of one-dimensional random Schrödinger operators with absolutely continuous disorder. The Hölder theory extends to $GL(d,\mathbb{R})$ for the top exponent under spectral simplicity, and to the partial sums $Λ_k = λ_1 + \cdots + λ_k$ under strong $k$-irreducibility, yielding Hölder continuity of each individual sub-top exponent. A method-optimality proposition shows that $β_*$ is the best exponent obtainable from the linear balance of axioms (A1)-(A3) of the spectral-gap method; strict improvement requires either modifying these axioms or adopting a different proof strategy. A lower-bound proposition adapted from Duarte, Klein, and Santos rules out uniform Hölder continuity across $\mathcal{M}_c(GL(2,\mathbb{R}))$.
