### [164] [Fixed-phase Resonance Tracking for Fast Nonlinear Resonant Ultrasound Spectroscopy](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22889)
*Jan Kober,Radovan Zeman,Marco Scalerandi*

Main category: eess.IV

TL;DR: 本文提出一种模型辅助的离散时间共振追踪方法（model-assisted discrete-time resonance tracking method），通过线性化频率-相位模型（linearized frequency-phase model）和前馈校正（feedforward correction）实现无需全频段扫描的实时共振频率跟踪，在砂岩棒的非线性共振超声谱（NRUS）实验和调理-弛豫协议（conditioning-relaxation protocol）中验证了其有效性，并指出测量速度与模态稳定性显著影响非线性参数推断。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统NRUS实验依赖重复采集共振曲线，但由于快速和慢速动态效应（fast and slow dynamic effects）导致的材料参数演化，测量结果对测量协议（measurement protocol）高度敏感。因此，需要一种不依赖全频段扫频、能实时维持系统于瞬时共振状态的测量方法来减少协议敏感性和测量时间。

Method: 方法将共振定义为激励与响应之间的预设相位关系（prescribed phase relation），基于线性化的频率-相位模型迭代更新激励频率，以维持系统在瞬时共振条件；并可结合前馈校正（feedforward correction）对激励幅值等外部控制参数进行调整，以抑制瞬态波建立（transient wave buildup）。

Result: 在砂岩棒上进行NRUS实验和调理-弛豫协议实验，成功估计了共振频率和阻尼（damping）参数。与传统方法对比表明，测量速度（measurement speed）和模态稳定性（mode stability）对推断出的非线性指标（nonlinear indicators）有显著影响。

Conclusion: 该共振追踪框架不仅适用于非线性声学（nonlinear acoustics），还可推广至任意参数缓慢演化的共振系统（resonant systems with slowly evolving parameters），具有通用性。

Abstract: Nonlinear Resonant Ultrasound Spectroscopy (NRUS) experiments that rely on repeated sampling of resonance curves are inherently sensitive to measurement protocol due to evolution of material parameters caused by fast and slow dynamic effects. We introduce a model-assisted discrete-time resonance tracking method that maintains a system at its instantaneous resonance condition without the need to acquire full frequency sweeps. Resonance is defined through a prescribed phase relation between excitation and response, and the excitation frequency is iteratively updated using a linearized frequency--phase model. The procedure allows controlled suppression of transient wave buildup using optional feedforward correction with respect to external control parameter. The method is demonstrated on NRUS and on conditioning--relaxation protocol conducted on sandstone bar, providing estimates of resonance frequency and damping. Comparison with conventional approaches shows that measurement speed and mode stability significantly influence the inferred nonlinear indicators. The proposed framework is not limited to nonlinear acoustics and can be applied to arbitrary resonant systems with slowly evolving parameters.

### [165] [On the Cancellation of Nuclear Effects in the Valence Region](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23110)

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究深非弹性散射（deep-inelastic scattering, DIS）中原子核对束缚核子结构函数的修正程度，并检验在价夸克分布峰值运动学区域附近是否存在显著的核效应。

Method: 分析了从氘到铅靶的同标量截面比σ^A/σ^{²H}的世界实验数据，重点关注动量分数x在0.25至0.35区间内的行为，并结合核修正的微观模型（microscopic model）进行讨论。

Result: 在所有原子核中，该区域的截面比平均值达到0.9985±0.0022，表明核修正极小且存在显著的抵消效应。

Conclusion: 束缚核子的结构函数在价夸克分布峰值附近区域几乎不受原子核环境影响，核修正被有效抵消。该结果需要结合微观模型进一步解释。

Abstract: Deep-inelastic $e/μ$ scattering data off targets ranging from deuterium to lead indicate that the nuclear modifications to the structure functions of bound nucleons are minimal in the kinematic region around the peak of the valence quark distributions. An analysis of world measurements of the isoscalar cross-section ratios $σ^A/σ^{{}^2\text{H}}$ in the region of $0.25 \leq x \leq 0.35$ shows a remarkable cancellation across all nuclei, with an average value of $0.9985 \pm 0.0022$. We discuss these results and possible interpretations in the context of a microscopic model of nuclear modifications of the structure functions.

</details>

### [166] [Terahertz magneto-nanoscopy of encapsulated monolayer graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22940)
*Richard H. J. Kim,Sunwoong Yang,Taehoon Kim,Samuel J. Haeuser,Joong-Mok Park,Randall K. Chan,Thomas Koschny,Young-Mi Bahk,Sung Ju Hong,Jigang Wang*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本研究利用散射型扫描近场光学显微镜（s-SNOM）技术，在5 K低温、1 T磁场下探测了单层封装石墨烯在太赫兹波段的纳米尺度电导率。实验观察到石墨烯近乎完美的高波矢反射行为，并发现磁场能引起该行为的细微变化。测量结果与描述狄拉克费米子回旋共振的磁光导率及近场光谱对比度理论计算高度吻合，为理解二维量子材料中温度与磁场对纳米尺度太赫兹输运的影响奠定了基础。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索封装单层石墨烯在低温（5 K）和磁场（最高1 T）条件下的纳米尺度电导率行为，特别是太赫兹（terahertz）光谱区域中磁场依赖的响应，以填补对二维量子材料中温度与磁场效应在纳米尺度太赫兹输运中作用的认识空白。

Method: 采用散射型扫描近场光学显微镜（s-SNOM）技术，在5 K至更高温度范围及最高1 T磁场下探测石墨烯接近电荷中性点（charge neutrality）时的磁场依赖响应，并结合磁光导率（magneto-optical conductivity）与近场光谱对比度的理论计算进行对比分析。

Result: 观察到石墨烯在太赫兹波段表现出近乎完美的高波矢（high-$q$）反射体行为，但外加磁场会引发该行为的细微变化；实验测量结果与理论计算中描述狄拉克费米子（Dirac fermions）场可调回旋共振（field-tunable cyclotron resonance）的磁光导率及近场光谱对比度一致。

Conclusion: 该结果为理解温度与磁场对二维量子材料中纳米尺度太赫兹输运的影响提供了初步步骤，表明s-SNOM技术可有效探测石墨烯在极低温及磁场下的近场光学响应，为后续研究奠定了基础。

Abstract: This study investigates the nanoscale conductivity of encapsulated monolayer graphene at temperatures down to 5 K and magnetic fields of up to 1 T. We use the scattering-type scanning near-field optical microscopy (s-SNOM) technique to probe magnetic-field-dependent responses from graphene close to charge neutrality in the terahertz spectral region. We observe the near-perfect high-$q$ reflector behavior of graphene but with subtle changes by the presence of magnetic fields. Measurements align with calculations of the magneto-optical conductivity and the near-field spectroscopic contrast that describes the field-tunable cyclotron resonance of Dirac fermions. Our result provides an initial step toward understanding temperature and magnetic-field effects on nanoscale terahertz transport in two-dimensional quantum materials.

</details>


### [167] [Spin Seebeck Effect in Normal-Metal--Chiral-Insulator Heterostructure](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23111)
*Jiayan Zhang,Gaoyang Li,Gaomin Tang,Yanxia Xing*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文在非平衡格林函数框架下，理论分析了正常金属-手性绝缘体异质结构中的声子介导自旋塞贝克效应，发现了负微分自旋塞贝克效应和自旋流整流两种非线性现象，并提出利用手性声子实现热控自旋电子器件的可能路径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 声子（phonon）能够通过原子运动的圆极化携带角动量并呈现手性（chirality），从而可通过将声子角动量转换为电子自旋角动量实现声子介导的自旋塞贝克效应（spin Seebeck effect, SSE）。作者旨在建立这一效应的理论框架，并系统研究影响自旋输运的多种因素。

Method: 采用非平衡格林函数（nonequilibrium Green's function formalism）方法，构建正常金属（normal-metal, NM）-手性绝缘体（chiral-insulator, CI）异质结构的理论模型，计算其中的自旋流（spin current）。

Result: 发现了两种显著的非线性自旋输运现象：负微分自旋塞贝克效应（negative differential SSE）和自旋流整流（spin-current rectification）。前者源于热偏压与热激发电子密度之间的竞争；后者暗示了热控自旋二极管（thermally controlled spin diode）的可行性。

Conclusion: 自旋输运行为与一种有效的界面谱密度（effective interfacial spectral density）密切相关。该工作为利用手性声子（chiral phonons）实现热控自旋电子器件提供了新途径。

Abstract: Phonons can carry angular momentum and exhibit chirality through the circular polarization of atomic motion. This enables a phonon-mediated spin Seebeck effect (SSE) via the conversion of phonon angular momentum into electron spin angular momentum. In this Letter, we develop a theoretical framework for calculating the spin current in a normal-metal (NM)-chiral-insulator (CI) heterostructure within the nonequilibrium Green's function formalism. We discuss the influence of (i) the thermal bias across the NM-CI interface, (ii) the chemical potential of the NM, and (iii) the insertion of an additional interfacial layer, on the spin transport properties. We identify two remarkable nonlinear spin transport phenomena: negative differential SSE and spin-current rectification. The negative differential SSE arises from the competition between the thermal bias and the thermally excited electron density. The spin-current rectification suggests the possibility of realizing a thermally controlled spin diode. We also find that the spin transport behavior is closely associated with an effective interfacial spectral density. This work provides a novel route toward thermally controlled spintronic devices using chiral phonons.

</details>


### [168] [Analytical Treatment of Noise-Suppressed Klein Tunneling in Graphene with Possible Implications for Quantum-Dot Qubits](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23279)
*Kamal Azaidaoui,Ahmed Jellal,Hocine Bahlouli,A. Al Luhaibi,Michael Vogl*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文将随时间涨落的势垒（由高斯白噪声建模）映射为与时间无关的林德布拉德方程（Lindblad equation），系统分析了噪声对量子隧穿的影响。结果表明，噪声引入耗散，抑制了薛定谔粒子的法布里-珀罗振荡（Fabry-Pérot oscillations）并导致透射指数衰减；在石墨烯中，噪声诱导出势垒内的复纵波矢，显著抑制包括克莱因隧穿（Klein tunneling）在内的透射，为石墨烯量子点与自旋量子比特器件的设计提供了可控耗散途径。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索势垒高度随时间涨落（建模为高斯白噪声）对量子隧穿过程的影响，特别是对石墨烯中克莱因隧穿（Klein tunneling）的调控机制，以期实现更可控的电子输运。

Method: 将随机动力学映射到一个等效的时间无关的林德布拉德方程（Lindblad equation），从而获得密度矩阵的完全解析解。

Result: 对于薛定谔粒子，噪声引入耗散，抑制了法布里-珀罗振荡（Fabry-Pérot oscillations），透射呈指数衰减。对于石墨烯，噪声在势垒内诱导出复纵波矢，导致透射（包括正入射时的克莱因隧穿）被强烈抑制。

Conclusion: 含噪势垒可作为可调谐耗散元件，为增强石墨烯基器件中电子输运的控制提供了新途径；该结果还可用于指导石墨烯量子点的设计，以用于自旋量子比特器件。

Abstract: We study quantum tunneling through a potential barrier whose height fluctuates in time and is modeled by Gaussian white noise. We map the stochastic dynamics onto an equivalent time-independent Lindblad equation for the density matrix, allowing fully analytical solutions. For Schrödinger particles, noise introduces dissipation that suppresses Fabry-Pérot oscillations and yields an exponentially decaying transmission. Applying the same formalism to graphene, we demonstrate that noise induces a complex longitudinal wavevector within the barrier, leading to a strong suppression of transmission and Klein tunneling, even at normal incidence. Our approach promises improved control over Klein tunneling. These results demonstrate that noisy barriers can act as tunable dissipative elements, offering a pathway to enhanced control of electron transport in graphene-based devices. We also briefly discuss how our results could guide the design of graphene quantum dots for potential use in spin qubit devices.

</details>


### [169] [Noise spectroscopy of insulating and itinerant altermagnets](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23297)
*Lucas V. Pupim,Mathias S. Scheurer*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文基于理论计算，提出利用噪声磁力测定（noise magnetometry）技术区分交变磁体（altermagnet）与反铁磁体（antiferromagnet），并揭示其主导轨道特征（如d波或g波）。研究发现在巡游交变磁体中，电荷涨落噪声提供最显著的对称性敏感信号；在均匀块体、应变或畴壁附近，交变磁体特有的噪声贡献可作为唯一识别标志，且畴壁噪声的角依赖可揭示轨道特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 交变磁学（altermagnetism）领域的一个核心目标是在多种化合物中通过实验明确识别和表征交变磁序。这促使研究者探索能够基于对称性特征清晰区分交变磁体与反铁磁体，并揭示磁有序参量主导轨道特征（如d波或g波）的工具。

Method: 本文采用理论研究方法，探讨噪声磁力测定在不同体系和场景中的潜力，分别分析来自磁振子（magnons）和巡游电子（itinerant electrons）的贡献；同时讨论了与偶极张量（dipole tensor）相关的晶格效应。

Result: 交变磁体与反铁磁体在磁振子噪声谱上存在差异，但最显著的对称性敏感特征出现在巡游交变磁体的电荷涨落中。在均匀块体、存在应变或畴壁附近，仅交变磁体的对称性允许产生特定的噪声贡献，从而提供独特的识别信号。此外，畴壁附近噪声的角依赖（angular dependence）可用于获取交变磁体的轨道特征。

Conclusion: 本工作有望为在多种候选材料中通过实验明确识别交变磁性铺平道路。

Abstract: One of the central goals in the emergent field of altermagnetism is the unambiguous experimental identification and characterization of altermagnetic order across a variety of compounds. This motivates exploring tools that can clearly distinguish altermagnets from antiferromagnets, based on symmetry signatures, and offer access to the dominant orbital character (e.g., $d$-wave vs. $g$-wave) of the magnetic order parameter. In this work, we theoretically explore the potential of noise magnetometry for this task, studying contributions from both magnons and itinerant electrons in different regimes and scenarios. While altermagnetism and antiferromagnetism also lead to different noise spectra for magnons, we find the most striking and symmetry-sensitive signatures in the charge fluctuations of itinerant altermagnets. Both for the homogeneous bulk case and in the presence of strain and/or around domain walls, we identify noise contributions that are only permitted by symmetry in the altermagnet and, thus, provide a unique signature of altermagnetism. Furthermore, the angular dependence of noise around domain walls also offers access to the orbital character of the altermagnet. On a more technical note, we discuss the role and relevance of lattice effects related to the dipole tensor. We hope that our work will help pave the way towards the clear experimental identification of altermagnetism across a wide range of candidate materials.

</details>


### [170] [Boundary-Robust Transmission Asymmetry as a Topological Signature in Open Floquet Lattices](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23420)
*Ren Zhang,Xiao-Yu Ouyang,Xu-Dong Dai,Xi Dai*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文识别了开放弗洛凯晶格（open Floquet lattices）中一种边界鲁棒的拓扑签名：尽管非绝热边界会强烈重塑透射谱线，但累积的左-右透射不对称性（integrated left-right transmission asymmetry）会饱和到一个由体弗洛凯绕数（bulk Floquet winding number）决定的平台。该效应的根源是深体分支布居原理（deep-bulk branch-population principle），并可通过冷原子透射谱学或电子输运的接触模型依赖读出进行探测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 开放弗洛凯晶格中非绝热边界会强烈影响透射行为，但能否从中提取出不受边界效应干扰的体拓扑信息尚待阐明。

Method: 提出深体分支布居原理（deep-bulk branch-population principle）：在长样品极限下，每个传播的弗洛凯-布洛赫分支（Floquet-Bloch branch）均以单位权重被布居，因为真正的弗洛凯束缚态（Floquet bound states）是非普遍的。由此建立累积透射不平衡（cumulative transmission imbalance）与体弗洛凯绕数（bulk Floquet winding number）之间的定量联系。

Result: 左-右透射不对称性的积分值在长样品极限下饱和到一个由体弗洛凯绕数决定的平台，该平台对边界细节具有鲁棒性。在电子输运场景中，基于弗洛凯-朗道尔-比特克（Floquet-Landauer-Büttiker）图像得到近 2ef 的响应，而阻塞因子后处理（blocking-factor post-processing）则产生定性不同的信号。

Conclusion: 累积透射不平衡是开放弗洛凯晶格中一种边界鲁棒的拓扑可观测量，可通过冷原子透射谱学或特定接触模型的电子输运进行直接探测，为实验验证弗洛凯拓扑提供了一个新的可行方案。

Abstract: We identify a boundary-robust topological signature of open Floquet lattices: although nonadiabatic boundaries strongly reshape the transmission lineshape, the integrated left--right transmission asymmetry saturates to a plateau set by the bulk Floquet winding number. Its origin is a deep-bulk branch-population principle: in the long-sample limit, each propagating Floquet--Bloch branch is generically populated with unit weight, since true Floquet bound states are nongeneric. The robust observable is therefore the cumulative transmission imbalance rather than the boundary-sensitive transmission profile. We propose direct detection by cold-atom transmission spectroscopy. For electronic transport, the same asymmetry admits contact-model-dependent electrical readouts: a coherent Floquet--Landauer--Büttiker interpretation predicts a near-\(2ef\) response in weak SAW devices, whereas a blocking-factor post-processing yields a qualitatively different signal.

</details>


### [171] [Mesoscopic Josephson effect in graphene disk at magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23470)
*Adam Rycerz*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文研究了圆盘形Corbino几何结构中的超导体-石墨烯-超导体（S-g-S）结，发现当磁场调节至临界电流趋于零且正常态电阻趋于无穷时，电流-相位关系呈现非正弦特性，偏斜度S≈0.14，且IcRN≈1.85Δ0/e。结果基于Dirac-Bogoliubov-De-Gennes方程的量子力学模式匹配分析，并与相干散射简化模型进行了对比。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 介观约瑟夫森结（mesoscopic Josephson junction）的电流-相位关系（current-phase relation）比传统隧道结更为复杂，其偏斜度（skewness）S>0与正常态引线中接近1的透射概率（transmission probabilities）有关。本文旨在探索这种非正弦行为是否也会出现在圆盘形Corbino几何的超导体-石墨烯-超导体结中，尤其是在极端磁场条件下。

Method: 采用量子力学的模式匹配分析（mode-matching analysis）方法求解Dirac-Bogoliubov-De-Gennes方程，并与一个假设两个圆形界面之间非相干散射（incoherent scattering）的简化模型进行对比。

Result: 当磁场调节至Ic→0且RN→∞时，IcRN≈1.85Δ0/e，偏斜度S≈0.14。

Conclusion: 圆盘形Corbino几何的S-g-S结在特定磁场条件下会呈现出类似介观约瑟夫森结的复杂电流-相位关系，其IcRN乘积和偏斜度偏离传统隧道结的正弦关系预测值。

Abstract: Unlike for tunneling Josephson junctions, for which the current-phase relation is given by the sine function, with the critical current ($I_c$) and normal-state resistance ($R_N$) following the relation $I_cR_N=(π/2)\,Δ_0/e$ (where $Δ_0$ is the superconducting gap and electron charge is $-e$), mesoscopic Josephson junctions show more complex current-phase relations, with the skewness $S>0$, what is related to the presence -- in case the leads are in the normal state -- of transmission probabilities taking the values comparable to $1$. Here, we show that these features also appear for a superconductor-graphene-superconductor (S-g-S) junction in the disk-shaped (Corbino) geometry, when the magnetic field is adjusted such that $I_c\rightarrow{}0$ and $R_N\rightarrow{}\infty$. In such a case, the product $I_cR_N\approx{}1.85\,Δ_0/e$, and the skewness $S\approx{}0.14$. The results obtained from quantum-mechanical mode-matching analysis for the Dirac-Bogoliubov-De-Gennes equation are compared with simpler model assuming incoherent scattering between two circular interfaces separating the sample and the leads.

</details>


### [172] [A Symmetric Unified Transport and Charge Model for MOSFETs from Diffusive to Ballistic Regimes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23541)
*Chien-Ting Tung*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出一种对称统一输运（symmetric unified transport, UT）紧凑模型，桥接漂移-扩散（drift-diffusion, DD）与弹道输运（ballistic transport, BT）两种物理机制，自洽描述DD-BT过渡区域的电流与电荷行为，并通过理论分析与多沟道长度MOSFET实验数据验证了模型的准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有紧凑模型在准弹道（quasi ballistic）输运区域未能充分考虑电容减小效应，且缺乏能够统一描述从DD平方律行为到弹道极限（ballistic limit）的连续对称模型。

Method: 采用自洽的电流-电荷联合建模方法，在电荷密度公式中引入量子电容（quantum capacitance）与载流子输运；通过物理定义的高场散射长度（high field scattering length）统一描述漏端速度饱和与源端热速度极限；并开发了物理的沟道电荷与电容模型以捕捉准弹道区的电容减小。

Result: 模型在多个沟道长度的MOSFET实验数据上实现了准确拟合，仅使用物理输运参数；公式连续且对称，通过了直流（DC）与交流（AC）对称性测试。

Conclusion: 该统一输运紧凑模型能够连续、自洽地覆盖DD到BT的全部输运区域，为先进MOSFET的电路仿真提供了物理基础完备的建模方案。

Abstract: This paper presents a symmetric unified transport (UT) compact model for MOSFETs that bridges drift-diffusion (DD) and ballistic transport (BT) regimes. The proposed model self consistently accounts for both current and charge across the DD-BT transition. Quantum capacitance and carrier transport are incorporated into the charge density formulation. Drain side velocity saturation and the source side thermal velocity limit are unified within a single framework using a physically motivated high field scattering length, enabling accurate modeling from DD square law behavior to the ballistic limit. In addition, a physical channel charge and capacitance model is developed to capture capacitance reduction in the quasi ballistic regime, which is not considered in standard compact models. The model is verified using theoretical analysis and experimental data from MOSFETs with multiple channel lengths, achieving accurate fitting using only physical transport parameters. The formulation is continuous and symmetric, and it passes both DC and AC symmetry tests.

</details>


### [173] [Van Hove Singularity-Driven Topological Magnetism in Twisted MoTe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23587)
*Heonjoon Park,Julian Stewart,Xiao-Wei Zhang,Taige Wang,Canxun Zhang,Evgeny Redekop,Jiaqi Cai,Weijie Li,Eric Anderson,Takashi Taniguchi,Kenji Watanabe,Jiun-Haw Chu,David Cobden,Andrea Young,Liang Fu,Ting Cao,Di Xiao,Xiaodong Xu*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文报告了大角度扭曲双层二碲化钼（MoTe2）中由范霍夫奇点（van Hove singularities, vHSs）、强关联和谷拓扑（valley topology）共同作用导致的拓扑磁性（topological magnetism）迹象，并在4.8度器件中观测到自发反常霍尔效应热点及拓扑霍尔效应（topological Hall effect）等特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 范霍夫奇点能强烈放大电子相互作用并可在拓扑能带中稳定关联相，然而对其如何驱动拓扑磁性及相关相变的微观机制尚不清楚，亟需实验验证。

Method: 研究采用大角度（4.8度）扭曲双层MoTe2器件，通过静电栅压调控至范霍夫奇点，结合输运测量和反射磁圆二色性（reflective magnetic circular dichroism）技术，表征反常霍尔效应及磁光响应。

Result: 在填充数 nu ≈ -1 附近观测到自发反常霍尔效应热点；联合输运与磁光测量表明该区域并非由单纯磁化主导，而源于关联的谷间相干反铁磁态（intervalley-coherent antiferromagnetic state），并随掺杂演变为倾斜相（canted phase）；增加磁场后，霍尔响应出现与拓扑霍尔效应一致的额外有限场分量，最终转变为陈数为 C = -1 的陈绝缘体（Chern insulator）。

Conclusion: 研究表明，莫尔拓扑能带中可调控的范霍夫奇点是实现手性磁性（chiral magnetism）和工程化拓扑相变的有效途径。

Abstract: Van Hove singularities (vHSs) strongly amplify electron interactions and can stabilize correlated phases in topological bands. Here we report signatures of topological magnetism in large-angle twisted bilayer MoTe2 driven by the interplay of vHSs, strong correlations, and valley topology. In a 4.8 degree device, electrostatic tuning to a vHS produces a spontaneous anomalous Hall hot spot near nu = -1. Combined transport and reflective magnetic circular dichroism measurements indicate that this regime is not governed by magnetization alone, but instead emerges from a correlated intervalley-coherent antiferromagnetic state that evolves with doping into a canted phase. With increasing magnetic field, the Hall response develops an additional finite-field component consistent with a topological Hall effect from a noncoplanar spin texture, before transitioning into a C = -1 Chern insulator. Our results establish tunable vHSs in moire topological bands as a route to chiral magnetism and engineering topological phase transitions.

### [174] [Observation of Erratic Non-Hermitian Skin Effect in Phononic Crystals](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23713)

TL;DR: 本文通过声子晶体实验，观测了无序非厄米趋肤效应（erratic non-Hermitian skin effect, ENHSE）的动态现象，发现其无序依赖的局域化特征与随机行走极值统计一致，并实现了对卫星峰的选择性调控。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非厄米趋肤效应（non-Hermitian skin effect）在无序与局域非互易耦合共存下的行为尚不清楚，ENHSE挑战了传统的体-边对应关系（bulk-boundary correspondence），亟需实验验证与深入理解。

Method: 在具有无序虚规范场（imaginary gauge fields）的声子晶体（phononic crystals）中进行实验观测；采用二聚化链（dimerized chain）结构，通过调节交错无序强度（staggered disorder strengths）实现对卫星峰的选择性操控。

Result: ENHSE的局域化发生在体区（bulk）且与激发位置无关；主峰与卫星峰精确位于累积规范场（cumulative gauge field）的局部极大值处，符合随机行走极值统计（random-walk extreme-value statistics）；通过调节交错无序强度可选择性操控卫星峰。

Conclusion: 该研究加深了对非厄米物理（non-Hermitian physics）的理解，并为基于无序工程（disorder-engineered）的非厄米波控（non-Hermitian wave control）提供了新途径。

Abstract: The erratic non-Hermitian skin effect (ENHSE), emerging from the interplay between disorders and locally nonreciprocal yet globally reciprocal couplings, has reshaped the conventional bulk-boundary correspondence through its disorder-dependent localization properties. Here, we experimentally observe the dynamical phenomena of ENHSE in phononic crystals with disordered imaginary gauge fields. The erratic localization occurs in the bulk independent of the excitation position, with the main and satellite peaks precisely located at the local maxima of the cumulative gauge field in accordance with random-walk extreme-value statistics. Remarkably, the selective manipulation of satellite peaks can be realized by tuning the staggered disorder strengths in a dimerized chain. These findings can deepen the understanding of non-Hermitian physics and establish a new route for disorder-engineered non-Hermitian wave control.

Method: 首先建立理论框架，分析实现完美透射（即克莱因隧穿，Klein tunneling）与可控极化变换所需的条件。随后构建显式模型：由AA堆叠（AA-stacked）扶手椅边缘（armchair edges）双层石墨烯纳米带与局域层间相互作用（localized interlayer interaction）组成量子耦合器，并针对窄/宽两种耦合器尺寸考察理想极化通道的透射行为。

Result: 在窄耦合器和宽耦合器中均实现了通过所需极化通道的完美透射。极化态透射率可通过外部场进行精细调节，表明该系统具备可调谐的极化选择透射能力。

Conclusion: 基于狄拉克材料的量子耦合器能够同时满足高透射效率与极化调控两种需求，为设计新一代可调谐量子器件提供了理论依据。

Abstract: We develop a theoretical framework for designing quantum couplers based on Dirac materials that can modulate the polarization of transmitted quasiparticles without significantly perturbing their propagation. We analyze in detail the conditions required for perfect transmission (Klein tunneling) together with controlled polarization transformation of the incoming states. We then discuss an explicit model of a quantum coupler composed of AA-stacked bilayer graphene nanoribbons with armchair edges and a localized interlayer interaction. Perfect transmission through the desired polarization channels is examined for both narrow and wide couplers. We show that the transmission of polarized states can be finely tuned by external fields.

Abstract: Negative permittivity metamaterial is a scientifically rich avenue due to its tremendous application in several arena of materials research including novel superlens, band-gap materials, invisibility cloaks, antenna and filter design. Traditionally, epsilon negative (ENG) behaviour is achieved in multi-phase composites with the addition of conducting metal fillers. However, this study reports colossal ENG feature in a single phase Calcium Ferrite for a particular nano hollow spherical (NHS) morphology, without the use of any filler. On the contrary, the same material synthesized in a different morphology, namely, nano solid sphere (NSS) shows conventional dielectric behaviour. Occurrence of ENG is successfully interpreted with the phase inversion of dominant polarization within the hollow cavity of NHS. This report marks a significant step in realizing colossal ENG in a single phase material just by restructuring the nanoscale morphology.

Method: 建立了一套非布洛赫框架（non-Bloch framework），用于计算非线性系统的连续能带（continuum bands），该框架能够在开放边界条件下准确复现非线性系统的本征谱，并在此基础上对非线性陈绝缘体进行了扩展分析。

Abstract: Nonlinear eigenvalue problems arise in a wide range of physical systems, in which system parameters depend on the eigenvalue. Such systems have been proposed to exhibit an extreme sensitivity of their spectra to boundary conditions, which leads to the breakdown of conventional topological characterizations. In this work, we establish a non-Bloch framework for calculating continuum bands that reproduce the spectra of the nonlinear system with open boundary conditions. This non-Bloch band theory enables us not only to calculate the eigenvalues but also to reveal phenomena unique to the nonlinear system. ### [178] [Structural Colours with Transition Metal Dichalcogenide Nanostructures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24411)
*Ida Juliane Bundgaard,Catarina G. Ferreira,Yonas Lebsir,Christos Tserkezis*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 本文提出过渡金属二硫属化物（TMD）纳米结构作为实现结构色的理想平台。通过理论计算TMD纳米球阵列的反射光谱，展示了通过调节纳米球半径和间距即可获得丰富色彩，其主要源自尺寸依赖的米氏（Mie）模式。研究还表明，改变材料或晶格单元可进一步扩展色域，激子（excitonic）自杂化效应可增强可调性，而TMD各向异性（anisotropy）对结构色的影响在小结构典型视角下可忽略。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有结构色材料在光谱调控范围和颜色可调性方面仍有局限，亟需探索兼具强光-物质相互作用和可加工性的新型纳米平台。TMD纳米结构因其优异的激子效应和可调光学特性，有潜力填补这一空白。

Method: 采用半解析计算方法计算TMD纳米球阵列的反射光谱，分析纳米球半径、间距、材料种类、晶格单元类型及激子属性对结构色的影响，并结合色度学（colourimetry）视角对颜色空间进行系统评估。

Result: 仅通过调节纳米球半径和间距即可生成宽范围颜色，色彩主要源自尺寸依赖的米氏（Mie）模式；选用不同材料或晶格单元可进一步覆盖更大色域；激子自杂化（self-hybridisation）可实现额外的颜色可调性；TMD各向异性在典型视角下对结构色影响可忽略，但视角本身会影响颜色呈现。

Conclusion: TMD纳米结构（尤其是纳米球阵列）是极具前景的结构色平台，其色彩可通过几何参数、材料选择和激子工程灵活调控，为下一代结构色器件设计提供了通用理论指导。

Abstract: We introduce transition metal-dichalcogenide (TMD) nanostructures as a promising platform for the realisation of structural colours. Processing of semianalytically calculated reflectance spectra of TMD nanosphere arrays shows a wide range of colours, which are obtained simply through tailoring the radius and separation of spheres in the array, with the size-dependent Mie modes of the nanoparticles being the primary contributor to the spectra. Additionally, it is demonstrated that further coverage of the colour space can be obtained by employing different materials or different lattice unit cells. Theoretical examination of the impact of the excitonic attributes of TMDs on the resulting structural colours indicates that self-hybridisation between nanoparticle modes and excitonic transitions may be employed for further tuneability. Moreover, the impact of TMD anisotropy on the structural colours is shown to be negligible for small structures at typical viewing angles, while the viewing angle itself may impact the colour. This work sets out to be a general investigation of TMD nanoarchitectures, with a focus on nanosphere arrays, for structural colours, by examining both inherent material features through the lens of colourimetry, and the ability of such structures to sustain a broad range of hues.

### [179] [Electrical tunability of terahertz nonlinearity in graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24651)
*Sergey Kovalev,Hassan A. Abstract: Graphene is conceivably the most nonlinear optoelectronic material. Its nonlinear optical coefficients in the terahertz (THz) frequency range surpass those of other materials by many orders of magnitude. This, in particular, allows one to use graphene for extremely efficient up-conversion of sub-THz electronic input signals into the THz frequency range at room temperature and under ambient conditions, thus paving the way for practical graphene-based ultrahigh-frequency electronic technology. Here, we show that the THz nonlinearity of graphene can be efficiently controlled using electrical gating, with gating voltages as low as a few volts. For example, optimal electrical gating enhances the power conversion efficiency in THz third-harmonic generation in graphene by about two orders of magnitude. This essentially converts graphene from an almost perfectly linear, inert electronic material to a material with the highest possible THz nonlinearity. We demonstrate gating control of THz nonlinearity of graphene for both ultrashort single-cycle and quasi-monochromatic multi-cycle input signals. Our experimental results are in quantitative agreement with a physical model of graphene nonlinearity, describing the time-dependent thermodynamic balance maintained within the electronic population of graphene during interaction with ultrafast electric fields. Our results can serve as a basis for straightforward and accurate design of devices and applications for efficient electronic signal processing in graphene at ultra-high frequencies.

We present a theoretical description of the process of charge separation and singlet-triplet mixing, arriving at expressions for the singlet return probability that take into account experimentally observed finite probabilities of the creation of singlets with various patterns of valley occupations. In our analysis we focus on magnetic fields for which the electron spin Zeeman splitting is close to the valley splitting in one of the dots, when the spin-valley coupling causes a strong renormalization of the frequency of oscillations of singlet return probability. The latter effect has been recently used to perform valley splitting mapping by shuttling of one quantum dot to various locations with respect to the other. We give a detailed description of singlet-triplet dynamics near these spin-valley resonances and compare the results of calculations with measurements on double quantum dots in two distinct Si/SiGe heterostructures. Comparison of theory with experiments in which the presence of a few valley occupation patterns is visible, gives insight into the valley dependence of $g$-factors in these structures, providing support for a recently proposed theoretical model of this dependence. *Utkan Güngördü,Rusko Ruskov,Silas Hoffman,Kyle Serniak,Andrew J. Kerman,Charles Tahan*

Main category: cond-mat.mes-hall

TL;DR: 该论文基于多体理论推导了单通道量子点超导结（S-QD-S junction）中gatemon量子比特的量子相位动力学，预言了有效电容重整化（renormalization）和非对称隧穿结中与栅压及占据数相关的电荷偏移，并通过分析两个安德烈夫分支（Andreev branches）随栅压和隧穿透明度的演化，量化了这些效应对量子比特能谱和非谐性（anharmonicity）的影响，同时提出了一种实验检测预言电荷偏移的方案。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的transmon量子比特中超导结的量子相位动力学较为简单，而基于超导体-量子点-超导体（S-QD-S）结的gatemon由于存在两个亚能隙安德烈夫束缚态（Andreev bound states, ABSs），其相位动力学更加丰富。该研究旨在从多体理论出发，揭示此前被忽略的有效电容重整化和电荷偏移效应，并量化这些效应对gatemon量子比特性能的实际影响。

Method: 研究基于作者此前在Phys. Rev. B 111, 214503 (2025)中建立的多体理论方法，推导出依赖于栅压的有效哈密顿量（effective Hamiltonian），该哈密顿量自洽地（self-consistently）包含了相位量子化（phase quantization）。通过分析两个安德烈夫分支与点栅电压（dot-gate voltages）和结隧穿透明度（junction transparencies）的相互作用，定量计算了这些效应对量子比特能谱和非谐性的影响。

Result: 多体理论预言了两种主要效应：(i) 结的有效电容发生重整化（renormalization）；(ii) 在具有隧穿不对称性（tunneling asymmetry）的结中，存在依赖于栅压和占据数的电荷偏移（charge offsets）。进一步的量化分析展示了这些效应在量子比特能谱和非谐性上的可观测影响，并与简化的gatemon模型进行了关联对比。

Conclusion: 该工作揭示了单通道量子点gatemon中因多体效应导致的有效电容重整化和电荷偏移对量子比特性能的显著影响，并提出了一个可用于实验检测预言电荷偏移的具体方案，为深入理解gatemon量子比特的量子相位动力学提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Gatemon qubits are based on a superconductor-quantum dot-superconductor (S-QD-S) junction which enables in situ electrostatic tuning via a gate electrode. For a single-channel QD this structure gives rise to two subgap Andreev bound states (ABSs), and generally leads to a richer quantum phase dynamics as compared to conventional transmons. In a recent work [Phys. Rev. B 111, 214503 (2025)] we derived the quantum phase dynamics from a many-body treatment which leads to an effective gate voltage-dependent Hamiltonian that self-consistently incorporates the phase quantization. It predicts (i) a renormalization of the junction's effective capacitance and (ii) the presence of gate voltage and occupation-dependent charge offsets in junctions with tunneling asymmetry. Here, we quantify the observable impact of these effects on the qubit's energy spectrum and anharmonicity, by studying the interplay of the two Andreev branches as a function of dot-gate voltages and junction transparencies. We show the relation of these predictions to simplified gatemon models and propose a protocol to experimentally detect the predicted charge offsets.

</details>

### [182] [Quantum Dynamics and Collapse-and-Revival Phenomena in the Dunkl Anharmonic Oscillator](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22945)
*D. Ojeda-Guillén,R. D. Mota,M. Salazar-Ramírez*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文利用SU(1,1)群的代数方法，研究了Dunkl非谐振子（Kerr介质）哈密顿量，通过Dunkl产生湮灭算子得到宇称依赖的精确能谱，并分析了Dunkl参数对量子动力学中塌缩与复兴现象及压缩态生成的影响。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Kerr介质（Kerr medium）的量子动力学研究通常基于标准谐振子代数，而Dunkl变形（Dunkl deformation）引入的额外宇称依赖性尚未被系统解析处理。作者希望从SU(1,1)群的代数结构出发，精确求解Dunkl非谐振子模型，并揭示Dunkl参数对量子动力学特征的调控作用。

Method: 将Dunkl非谐振子哈密顿量用Dunkl产生算子（creation operator）和湮灭算子（annihilation operator）表示，这些算子闭合形成su(1,1)李代数（Lie algebra），从而精确对角化哈密顿量并获得宇称依赖的能谱。初始态取为偶宇称与奇宇称Dunkl相干态（coherent states）的叠加，计算场正交分量（field quadrature）和存活概率（survival probability），并通过正交分量方差（quadrature variance）分析压缩效应。

Result: Dunkl参数μ可调节分数复兴（fractional revivals）行为，并在特定变形值下于半周期处实现完美态重构（perfect state reconstructions）。正交分量方差分析表明，Dunkl变形在t≈π附近产生干涉诱导的压缩态（squeezed states）。当μ→0时，标准Kerr介质动力学完全恢复。

Conclusion: Dunkl变形为Kerr介质系统提供了一种额外的调控自由度，可精确控制量子态的复兴与压缩行为，在量子信息处理中具有潜在应用价值。

Abstract: We study the Dunkl anharmonic oscillator (Kerr medium) Hamiltonian from an algebraic approach of the $SU(1,1)$ group. In order to obtain the exact energy spectrum of this problem, we write its Hamiltonian in terms of the Dunkl creation and annihilation operators, which close the $su(1,1)$ Lie algebra. This allows us to exactly solve this Hamiltonian and obtain its parity-dependent energy spectrum. Then, we investigate the quantum dynamics of the system, particularly the collapse and revival phenomena, by using an initial state given by a superposition of even and odd Dunkl coherent states. We compute the field quadrature and the survival probability, showing that the Dunkl parameter $μ$ modulates the fractional revivals and produces perfect state reconstructions at half-periods for specific deformation values. We analyze the quadrature variance to show that the Dunkl deformation generates interference-induced squeezed states around $t \approx π$. The standard Kerr medium dynamics are exactly recovered in the limit $μ\rightarrow 0$.

</details>


### [183] [Accelerating quantum Gibbs sampling without quantum walks](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22996)
*Jiaqi Leng,Jiaqing Jiang,Lin Lin*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种无游走（walk-free）的量子算法，用于制备纯化吉布斯态（purified Gibbs states），在满足精确Kubo-Martin-Schwinger细致平衡的一类量子吉布斯采样器上实现谱间隙依赖的二次加速，并通过将母哈密顿量分解为非交换一阶算子，将问题转化为奇异值滤波（singular-value filtering）问题，进而利用量子奇异值变换（quantum singular value transformation）算法达到加速效果。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Szegedy量子游走能为可逆经典马尔可夫链提供通用的二次加速，但将其机制扩展到量子吉布斯采样（quantum Gibbs sampling）在非特殊情形下一直存在困难。本文旨在突破这一局限，为更广泛的量子吉布斯采样器设计具有二次谱间隙加速的吉布斯态制备算法。

Method: 核心方法包括：(1) 将满足精确Kubo-Martin-Schwinger细致平衡（Kubo-Martin-Schwinger detailed balance）的量子吉布斯采样器对应的母哈密顿量（parent Hamiltonian）显式分解为非交换一阶算子（noncommutative first-order operators）；(2) 利用该分解将纯化吉布斯态的制备转化为奇异值滤波问题；(3) 应用量子奇异值变换算法，在标准相干访问（coherent-access）假设下实现谱间隙依赖的二次改进。

Result: 该框架在谱间隙依赖上实现了二次加速，且适用于Davies设定（Davies setting）之外的多种可高效实现的吉布斯采样器。此外，基于相同的分解引入了一种辅助耗散动力学（auxiliary dissipative dynamics），可在双重希尔伯特空间（doubled Hilbert space）的亚稳态（metastable regime）中生成暖启动（warm starts）。

Conclusion: 本文提出的无游走量子算法系统性地扩展了量子吉布斯采样的加速方法，为更广泛的量子吉布斯采样器提供了制备纯化吉布斯态的有效途径，并借助辅助耗散动力学进一步支持亚稳态下的暖启动生成，具有潜在的实际应用价值。

Abstract: Szegedy's quantum walk gives a generic quadratic speedup for reversible classical Markov chains, but extending this mechanism to quantum Gibbs sampling has remained challenging beyond special cases. We present a walk-free quantum algorithm for preparing purified Gibbs states with a quadratic improvement in spectral-gap dependence for a broad class of quantum Gibbs samplers that satisfy exact Kubo-Martin-Schwinger detailed balance. Our main structural result is an explicit factorization of the corresponding parent Hamiltonian into noncommutative first-order operators. This turns purified Gibbs-state preparation into a singular-value filtering problem and enables a quantum singular value transformation algorithm with quadratically improved gap dependence under standard coherent-access assumptions. The framework applies to several efficiently implementable Gibbs samplers beyond the Davies setting. We also introduce an auxiliary dissipative dynamics based on the same factorization, which can be used to generate warm starts in the doubled Hilbert space in metastable regimes.

</details>


### [184] [Non-unitary extension of Grover's search algorithm](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23382)
*V. N. A. Lula-Rocha,M. A. S. Trindade*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种Grover搜索算法的非幺正扩展，通过改变扩散算子承载的希尔伯特空间隐藏几何来实现。该算法执行一次更大的旋转而非多项式次小旋转。在Kraus算子方法下复杂度为O(N)，但结合量子奇异值变换、块编码和切比雪夫多项式逼近后，复杂度达到O(√N)，与标准Grover算法相同，但额外消耗一个量子比特资源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索通过非幺正操作（non-unitary operation）扩展Grover搜索算法（Grover's search algorithm）的可能性，旨在改变希尔伯特空间（Hilbert space）的隐藏几何以更高效地找到搜索问题的解。

Method: 通过扩散算子（diffusion operator）改变希尔伯特空间的隐藏几何，实现非幺正扩展。分析了Kraus算子（Kraus operator）方法下的实现，并进一步采用量子奇异值变换（quantum singular value transform）、块编码（block encoding）和切比雪夫多项式逼近（Chebyshev polynomial approximation）进行优化。

Result: 在Kraus算子方法下，后选择（post-selection）中测量到解的概率需要O(N)次算法重复，不优于经典解。而采用量子奇异值变换结合块编码和切比雪夫多项式逼近后，复杂度降至O(√N)，达到Grover算法下界（Grover's bound），但额外多消耗一个量子比特。

Conclusion: 非幺正扩展的Grover算法通过引入额外量子比特资源，可以达到与标准Grover算法相同的O(√N)复杂度；单纯Kraus算子方法则无优势。

Abstract: We have developed a non-unitary extension of Grover's search algorithm by changing the hidden geometry of Hilbert space carried by diffusion operator. Our algorithm finds the solution for search problem by performing a unique bigger rotation rather than small rotations in order polynomial times in the size $N$ of search space. We analyze the complexity of implementing the non-unitary operation and we observed that the price paid by performing this rotation is due the normalization. In Kraus operator approach we need $O(N)$ repetition of the algorithm to have a chance of measuring a solution in a post-selection, this is no better than the classical solution. However, the quantum singular value transform in addition with block encoding and Chebyshev polynomial approximation, we got complexity $O(\sqrt{N})$ and reach the Grover's bound with an extra resource of one single qubit, compared with the standard Grover's algorithm.

</details>


### [185] [Witnessing entanglement between photon and matter due to graviton exchange](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24496)
*Arijit Dutta,Marko Toroš,Sougato Bose,Anupam Mazumdar*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于斯托克斯参数（Stokes parameters）的纠缠检测方案，用于检验引力量子性质所导致的物质自旋量子比特与光子之间的纠缠。通过构建正定部分转置（PPT）判据并分析纠缠相位，该方案在非最大纠缠态下达到最大负值 -0.052，并在光子重叠参数 |γ| ∈ [0.71, 1) 范围内有效检测量子关联。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 广义相对论的核心检验之一是引力导致的光线弯曲。近期有实验方案提出，自旋为2的无质量引力子会在物质与光子之间产生纠缠，从而在实验室中检验引力的量子性质。因此，需要发展有效的纠缠检测判据来捕捉这种仅由自旋-2诱导的纠缠信号。

Method: 提出一种正定部分转置（PPT）判据来见证该纠缠。通过扫描与纠缠相位成比例的末态重叠（|γ|），利用斯托克斯可观测量测量光子态，并耦合光子到本地振荡器（local oscillator），通过控制其相位探测激光束中宏观干涉的正交分量，从而构造引力量子性质的纠缠见证。

Result: 对于非最大纠缠态，该PPT判据的最大负值达到 -0.052。纠缠有效检测范围为光子相干态重叠参数 0.71 ≤ |γ| < 1，在此区间内可清晰观测到量子关联信号。

Conclusion: 该PPT判据能够在实验室环境中有效检测由引力量子性质介导的纠缠，为验证引力的量子本性提供了一种关键实验手段，且仅在重叠参数满足特定范围内才能获得清晰的量子关联信号。

Abstract: The paper presents a scheme to detect entanglement arising from the quantum nature of gravity between a spin qubit and photons, using Stokes parameters. One of the crucial tests of the general theory of relativity is the bending of light due to the curvature. Recently, a quantum counterpart of this experiment to test the quantum nature of the gravitational interaction has been proposed, in which the spin-2, massless graviton yields entanglement between matter and a photon sector. Hence, it provides one of the most crucial experimental signatures for testing the quantum nature of gravity in a lab, since only spin-2-induced entanglement can yield the correct deflection of light due to matter. Here, we propose a positive partial-transpose (PPT) witness criterion for witnessing such an entanglement. We scan the entangled states in this context by studying the overlap of the final state, which is proportional to the entanglement phase. We exploit the Stokes observables to measure the photon state and the spins in the matter sector, thereby constructing a witness for the quantum nature of gravity in this setup. To quantify this entanglement, we will couple the photon to a local oscillator, whose phase need to be controlled to probe the orthogonal components of the macroscopic interference in the laser beam. We have shown that for a non-maximally entangled state mediated by the quantum nature of gravity, the witness attains a maximal negativity of $-0.052$. Our findings indicate that this witness effectively detects entanglement within the range $0.71 \leq |γ| < 1$, where $γ$ is the overlap between the two coherent states of the photon, providing a clear signature of quantum correlations.

</details>


### [186] [Design Principles for Enhanced Quantum Transport with Site-Dependent Noise](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23005)
*Maggie Lawrence,Elise Wang,Dvira Segal*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了一维晶格中通过位点依赖（site-dependent）的退相干（dephasing）来优化环境噪声，从而增强稳态量子输运；相比均匀退相干，优化后的空间非均匀退相干能显著提高输运效率，并伴随稳态空间退局域化（delocalization）的增加。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 已有研究主要关注在空间均匀系统-环境耦合下优化系统参数，本文转而直接优化环境噪声本身——即允许位点依赖于退相干强度——以探索非均匀环境噪声对量子输运的调控潜力。

Method: 采用林德布拉德主方程（Lindblad master equation）框架，对一维晶格（包含倾斜势或无序势）中的局域退相干进行优化，以最大化稳态粒子流（steady-state population flux），并考虑短程与长程相干隧穿（coherent tunneling）。

Result: 在倾斜势下，短程隧穿偏好交替位点上的选择性退相干，而长程隧穿则受益于随注入位点距离增加的退相干分布；在无序系统中，强失谐位点需增强局域退相干以促进输运。所有情形下，位点优化的退相干均优于均匀退相干，并伴随稳态空间退局域化增强。

Conclusion: 退相干通过局部展宽能级帮助克服失谐（detuning）和相消干涉（destructive interference）；空间结构化的环境噪声可作为调控开放系统量子输运与态相干性的有效策略。

Abstract: Environmental noise can enhance transport, an effect known as environmental noise-assisted quantum transport. Most theoretical studies focus on optimizing system parameters under spatially uniform system-environment coupling. Here, instead, we optimize the environmental noise itself by allowing for site-dependent dephasing. We investigate steady-state transport in one-dimensional lattices with either ramped or disordered energy landscapes, considering both short- and long-range coherent tunneling. In the absence of environmental effects, in the thermodynamic limit these systems can exhibit localization, and thus suppressed transport, arising from destructive interference. Using a Lindblad master equation framework, we implement local dephasing optimized to maximize steady-state population flux. We find that for ramp potentials, short-range tunneling favors selective dephasing on alternating sites, whereas long-range tunneling benefits from a dephasing profile that increases with distance from the injection site. In energetically disordered systems, strongly detuned sites require enhanced local dephasing under short-range tunneling to facilitate transport. In all cases, we find that site-optimized dephasing allows higher transport efficiency than uniform dephasing, and it is accompanied by increased spatial delocalization of the steady state. Our results provide microscopic insight into the interplay between coherent dynamics and environmental noise. Dephasing broadens energy levels locally, helping to overcome detuning and destructive interference. More generally, we establish spatially-structured environmental noise as a strategy for controlling both quantum transport and state coherence in open systems.

</details>


### [187] [Qutrit Clifford+T gates by two-body angular momentum couplings, rotations and one-axis-twistings](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23007)
*F. E. S. Steinhoff*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了基于角动量表示的三比特（qutrit）Clifford+T门集合的实现方案，证明了该集合中的所有幺正门可通过旋转（rotations）和单轴扭曲（one-axis-twisting）操作实现，并利用Jordan-Schwinger映射和交叉Kerr相互作用（cross-Kerr interaction）给出了玻色子模（bosonic modes）下的等效实现。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为三能级量子系统（qutrit）提供一个物理上可实现且高效的Clifford+T门集合实现方案，该集合是容错量子计算（fault-tolerant quantum computing）的关键组成部分。

Method: 发展了三比特的角动量表示（angular momentum representation），利用旋转和单轴扭曲操作实现局域门，利用线性角动量耦合实现受控旋转门。通过Jordan-Schwinger映射将实现方案转化为玻色子模形式，并引入交叉Kerr相互作用实现任意三比特Clifford+T门。

Result: 完整的三比特Clifford+T集合可仅用双体角动量耦合、旋转和单轴扭曲操作表达。与先前方案相比，玻色子模实现优化了所需模式数，并展示了制备纠缠态（entangled states）的简单方案。

Conclusion: 所提出的角动量表示框架为三比特Clifford+T门集在多种量子系统中的实验实现提供了可行途径，尤其适用于具有角动量自由度或玻色子模式的物理平台。

Abstract: We develop an angular momentum representation and implementation of the Clifford+T set of unitaries for qutrits. We show that local gates from this set can be realized by the sole use of suitable rotations and one-axis-twisting operations, which are at most quadratic in the angular momentum operators and thus can be experimentally realized in many quantum systems. Controlled rotations are shown to only require linear angular momentum couplings and, as a consequence, the full qutrit Clifford+T set is shown to be expressed solely in terms of two-body angular momentum couplings, rotations and one-axis-twisting operations. By employing the Jordan-Schwinger map, we show an analogous implementation in terms of bosonic modes, improving on the number of modes with regard to a previous scheme. Moreover, we employ the cross-Kerr interaction in order to obtain any qutrit Clifford+T gate for bosonic modes. We illustrate our findings with simple schemes for preparing entangled states of interest.

</details>


### [188] [An Analysis of Commutation-Based Trotter Ordering Strategies on Heisenberg-Style Hamiltonians](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23138)
*Reuben Tate,Shamminuj Aktar,Stephan Eidenbenz*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究了在Trotter化（Trotterization）时间演化近似中，利用哈密顿量的对易结构（commutation structure）设计不同项排序策略（ordering strategies）对降低近似误差的影响，并通过图着色技术（graph coloring）构建对易图（commutation graph）来优化分组，在Heisenberg模型上进行了理论与实证分析。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有Trotter化误差界通常较为宽松，且已知误差大小会受到哈密顿量各项演化顺序的显著影响，因此需要系统性地研究不同排序策略对误差的影响。

Method: 作者考虑了几种基于哈密顿量对易结构的排序策略（commutation-based ordering strategies），即将相互对易的项划分到同一组中；分组通过在对易图（commutation graph）上应用图着色技术实现。此外还对比了若干基线排序策略，并在1D和2D Heisenberg模型系统上进行了经验误差计算。

Result: 针对特定类别的哈密顿量，论文证明了对易图的结构与性质；并在Heisenberg系统上的经验计算显示，不同的排序策略会导致真实Trotter误差（true Trotter error）的显著差异。

Conclusion: 基于对易结构的分组排序策略能够有效影响Trotter误差，图着色技术为系统化构建这些分组提供了可行途径。

Abstract: Trotterization is a technique that allows one to approximate a time evolution of a Hamiltonian by repeatedly evolving the individual terms of the Hamiltonian one-at-a-time for small time durations. Bounds on the error of this approximation exist; however, they are typically loose and moreover, it is known that the true error can be greatly influenced by the order in which the terms of the Hamiltonian are evolved. In this work, we consider various ordering strategies that exploit the commutation structure of the Hamiltonian, in addition to a few other baseline ordering strategies. These commutation-based strategies involve dividing the terms of the Hamiltonian into groups where all the terms within each group commute with one another. These groupings can be obtained by using graph coloring techniques on what we call the "commutation graph" of the Hamiltonian. We prove various results regarding the structure and properties of such commutation graphs for certain classes of Hamiltonians. We also empirically calculate the (true) Trotter error using these ordering strategies on various 1D and 2D Heisenberg-style systems.

</details>


### [189] [Coherence dynamics in quantum many-body systems with conservation laws](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23192)
*Sreemayee Aditya,Emanuele Tirrito,Piotr Sierant,Xhek Turkeshi*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文研究守恒律如何影响多体动力学中量子相干性（quantum coherence）的传播。通过U(1)对称随机电路、电荷与偶极矩守恒电路以及遍历哈密顿动力学，结合多种数值方法，发现守恒律将全局相干性的对数饱和替换为慢速流体力学弛豫，而局部相干性在对称约束电路中呈现明显的“上升-峰值-下降”结构，其峰值时间随子系统大小代数增长；遍历哈密顿则在较大子系统中将峰值扩展为平台，揭示出不同的机制。相干性因此成为敏感探测对称约束热化（symmetry-constrained thermalization）的工具。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 量子相干性在多体动力学中的传播规律尚不清晰，尤其守恒律（conservation laws）对其如何塑造是未充分理解的问题。本文旨在系统揭示不同守恒律下相干性全局与局部的演化行为，并为量子资源动力学与多体输运建立联系。

Method: 采用U(1)对称随机电路（U(1)-symmetric random circuits）、电荷与偶极矩守恒电路（charge-and-dipole conserving circuits）以及遍历哈密顿动力学（ergodic Hamiltonian dynamics）三类模型。研究方法包括精确矢量演化（exact vector evolution）、矩阵乘积态模拟（matrix product state simulations）和复制子张量网络方法（replica tensor networks methods），分别从全局（参与熵）和局部（相对熵）两个层面探测相干性。

Result: 全局相干性：守恒律将无约束电路中的对数饱和替换为慢速流体力学弛豫（slow hydrodynamic relaxation）。局部相干性：对称约束电路呈现清晰的“上升-峰值-下降”（rise-peak-fall）结构，峰值时间随子系统大小代数增长；遍历哈密顿在较大子系统中将峰值扩展为延伸的平台（extended plateau）。

Conclusion: 守恒律从根本上改变了量子相干性的传播行为，相干性可作为敏感探测对称约束热化的探针，将量子资源动力学与多体输运（many-body transport）联系起来。

Abstract: We study how conservation laws shape the spreading of quantum coherence in many-body dynamics. Focusing on $U(1)$-symmetric random circuits, charge-and-dipole conserving circuits, as well as ergodic Hamiltonian dynamics, we probe coherences both globally, via the participation entropy, and locally, via the relative entropy of coherence. Combining exact vector evolution, matrix product state simulations, and replica tensor networks methods, we find that conservation laws replace the logarithmic saturation of unconstrained circuits with slow hydrodynamic relaxation of the global coherence measures. Locally, symmetry-constrained circuits show a clean rise-peak-fall structure whose peak time grows algebraically with subsystem size. In contrast, ergodic Hamiltonians broaden the peak into an extended plateau at larger subsystems, highlighting a qualitatively distinct mechanism. Coherence thus emerges as a sensitive probe of symmetry-constrained thermalization, linking quantum resource dynamics to many-body transport.

### [190] [Principles of relativistic quantum statistical thermodynamics: a class of exactly solvable models](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23409)
*A. Yu. Zakharov*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该论文将相互作用原子系统表示为原子系统与一个辅助标量协变场（auxiliary scalar covariant field）的并集，证明该辅助场是Klein-Gordon场的叠加，并建立了相对论性哈密顿量的一般形式。研究表明，相对论配分函数的精确计算可归结为辅助场参数的重整化（renormalization），而场自由度会导致经典相对论系统中的紫外灾难（ultraviolet catastrophe）；辅助场的量子化可消除这一发散，并在相对论量子统计热力学框架内证明了相变的存在。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有相互作用多原子系统的相对论性统计热力学描述尚不完善，特别是如何处理场自由度导致的发散问题以及建立严格的一般性相对论哈密顿量形式。

Method: 将相互作用原子系统分解为原子子系统与一个辅助标量协变场，该场仅在非相对论近似下等价于给定的静态原子间势（static interatomic potential）。辅助场被构造为Klein-Gordon场的叠加，其参数由对应原子间势的傅里叶变换的奇点决定。

Result: 建立了相互作用原子系统的相对论性哈密顿量的一般形式；证明相对论配分函数的精确计算可化为辅助场参数的重整化；发现经典相对论系统中场自由度导致总能量发散（紫外灾难的类似物），而辅助场的量子化可消除此发散；在相对论量子统计热力学框架内证明了相变的存在性。

Conclusion: 该工作为相对论量子统计热力学（relativistic quantum statistical thermodynamics）提供了严格的数学基础，揭示了辅助场量子化在消除发散和描述相变中的关键作用。

Abstract: A system of interacting atoms is represented as an union of two subsystems, one of which is the system of atoms, and the other is an auxiliary scalar covariant field, which is equivalent to a given static interatomic potential of general form only in the non-relativistic approximation. It is shown that the auxiliary field is a superposition of Klein-Gordon fields, the parameters of which are related to singular points of the Fourier transform of the corresponding interatomic potential. The general form of the relativistic Hamiltonian system of interacting atoms is established. It is shown that the exact calculation of the relativistic partition function of a system of interacting atoms, taking into account the field degrees of freedom, reduces to renormalizing the parameters of the auxiliary field. It is established that the field degrees of freedom lead to a divergence in the total energy of a classical relativistic system - an analogue of the ultraviolet catastrophe. Quantization of the auxiliary field eliminates this divergence. The existence of a phase transition within the framework of relativistic quantum statistical thermodynamics has been proven.

### [191] [Peak-valley mechanism for Hilbert space fragmentation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23659)
*Jianlong Fu,Hoi Chun Po*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出“峰谷碎片化（peak-valley fragmentation）”机制，用于在一维整数自旋链中实现强Hilbert空间碎片化（HSF），为理解无序自由系统中的非热行为提供统一框架。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管已知许多表现出强Hilbert空间碎片化（HSF）的模型，但现有分析通常是模型依赖的，缺乏通用的组织原则。

Method: 引入“峰谷碎片化（PV fragmentation）”机制：通过在计算基下定义一组由几何表示中交替峰谷的高度和深度标记的涌现好量子数（emergent good quantum numbers），构造简单局域规则以实现强HSF。

Result: 该框架不仅能解释已知的强HSF模型及其破坏HSF性质的变体，还能系统构造高自旋系统中的新碎片化模型，并识别出高阶HSF模型。

Conclusion: 峰谷碎片化为强HSF提供了一种简单的统一机制，有望成为孤立系统中遍历性破缺（ergodicity breaking）研究的一般组织原则。

Abstract: Ergodicity breaking in isolated systems has emerged as an important frontier in the study of quantum many-body physics. While generic Hamiltonians are expected to obey the eigenstate thermalization hypothesis (ETH), recent studies on Hilbert space fragmentation (HSF) have revealed possible robust nonthermal behavior even in disorder-free systems. Although numerous models exhibiting strong HSF are already known, existing analyses are typically model dependent, and a general organizing principle remains elusive. In this work, we introduce a simple mechanism for achieving strong HSF in one-dimensional integer spin chains, which we term "peak-valley (PV) fragmentation". The key idea is to devise a simple local rule which ensures the spin states in the computational basis can be labeled by a set of emergent good quantum numbers corresponding to the heights and depths of alternating peaks and valleys in a geometrical representation. We demonstrate that some known examples of strong HSF models, as well as their variants which break the HSF property, can be understood within the framework of PV fragmentation. Our approach also enables systematic construction of new fragmented models in higher-spin systems, and allows us to identify higher-order HSF models.

### [192] [Entanglement (1+2) QED in a double layer of Dirac Materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23673)
*Facundo Arreyes,Federico Escudero,Arián Gorza,Sebastián Ardenghi*

TL;DR: 该论文通过动量空间纠缠分析，研究了双层蜂窝晶格中两个狄拉克准粒子在平面电磁腔耦合下的纠缠特性。使用戴森-施温格方程（Bethe-Salpeter equation）和阶梯近似（ladder approximation）建模，发现自能重整化（self-energy renormalization）驱动纠缠熵从微扰控制的低值到强增强的交叉，稳定纠缠要求准粒子相干时间超过层间光子传播时间，最大纠缠区域可用于实现贝尔态（Bell-like states）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究狄拉克材料（Dirac materials）中准粒子间动量空间纠缠（momentum-space entanglement）的形成机制，特别是自能重整化、虚粒子交换和旋量几何（spinor geometry）如何协同塑造纠缠景观。

Method: 将低能激发建模为$(1+2)$维有质量狄拉克费米子，采用阶梯近似推导贝特-萨尔皮特方程（Bethe-Salpeter equation）；围绕自由二体准粒子态使用玻恩级近似（Born-level approximation），由腔光子传播子（cavity photon propagator）介导相互作用；从约化子晶格密度矩阵（reduced sublattice density matrix）计算动量分辨的冯·诺依曼熵（von Neumann entropy）。

Result: 在微扰控制区域内纠缠熵较小；引入唯象自能修飾后，观察到纠缠熵从低值到强增强的交叉（crossover）；仅当准粒子相干时间（coherence time）超过层间光子传播时间时才能获得稳定纠缠；最大熵区域可用于实现贝尔态。

Conclusion: 自能重整化、虚粒子交换和旋量几何共同重塑狄拉克材料的纠缠景观，为在凝聚态系统中实现量子纠缠态提供了新途径。

Abstract: We investigate the momentum-space entanglement between two Dirac quasiparticles in a double-layer honeycomb lattice coupled via a planar electromagnetic cavity. We model the low-energy excitations as massive Dirac fermions in $(1+2)$ dimensions and derive the Bethe-Salpeter equation using the ladder approximation. We use a Born-level approximation around a free two-body quasiparticle state, where the interaction is mediated by the cavity photon propagator. From the reduced sublattice density matrix, we compute a momentum-resolved von Neumann entropy. Within the perturbatively controlled regime, the entropy remains small, while phenomenological self-energy dressing drives a crossover to strong enhancement of the entanglement entropy. Stationary entanglement is obtained only when the quasiparticle coherence time exceeds the photon propagation time between the layers. The maximum-entropy regime appears to be a viable method for achieving Bell-like states. These results demonstrate how self-energy renormalization, virtual particle exchange, and spinor geometry combine to reshape the entanglement landscape of Dirac materials.

### [193] [Minimal spin-rotor model for Barnett and Einstein--de Haas physics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23768)
*Saikat Banerjee*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文通过一个精确可解的自旋-转子（spin-rotor）模型，证明当机械自由度被量子化时，Barnett效应的有效场图像会发生质变，从经典的Zeeman问题转变为产生自旋-转子量子纠缠的算符值Barnett场（operator-valued Barnett field）问题。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统的Barnett效应（Barnett effect）通过机械旋转产生的有效磁场来理解，而其互易的Einstein-de Haas效应（Einstein–de Haas effect）描述自旋角动量向机械运动的转移。本文的动机在于探究当机械自由度本身被量子化时，这一有效场图像是否以及如何发生变化。

Method: 引入了一个精确可解的极小自旋-转子模型，其中自旋1/2与一个量子转子（quantum rotor）耦合。通过分析固定角动量扇区（fixed angular-momentum sector）与转子扇区叠加态（superposition of rotor sectors）两种情况下的动力学行为，计算约化自旋纯度（reduced spin purity）、转子相干性（rotor coherence）和纠缠熵（entanglement entropy）等量。

Result: 在固定角动量扇区中，模型复现了传统的Barnett分裂（Barnett splitting），形式上等价于一个Zeeman问题（Zeeman problem）。但对于转子扇区的叠加态，Barnett场变为算符值，所产生的动力学直接产生了相干的自旋-转子纠缠，表现为约化自旋纯度降低、转子相干性变化以及纠缠熵的产生。

Conclusion: 研究结果确定了一个极小量子系统，在该系统中Barnett有效场图像偏离其经典形式，并通过自旋依赖的转子相干性获得了互易的（reciprocal）表现，从而揭示了量子化机械自由度下Barnett效应与Einstein-de Haas效应之间的深层联系。

Abstract: The Barnett effect is usually understood through an effective magnetic field generated by mechanical rotation, while its reciprocal Einstein--de Haas effect describes the transfer of spin angular momentum to mechanical motion. We show that this effective-field picture changes qualitatively once the mechanical degree of freedom itself is quantized. To demonstrate this, we introduce an exactly solvable minimal spin-rotor model in which a spin-$1/2$ is coupled to a quantum rotor. In a fixed angular-momentum sector, the model reproduces the conventional Barnett splitting and remains formally equivalent to a Zeeman problem. For a superposition of rotor sectors, however, the Barnett field becomes operator-valued and the resulting dynamics generates coherent spin-rotor entanglement. This is directly visible in the reduced spin purity, rotor coherence, and entanglement entropy. Our results identify a minimal quantum setting in which the Barnett effective-field picture departs from its classical form and acquires a reciprocal manifestation through spin-dependent rotor coherence.

Conclusion: 低场EDMR可作为灵敏探测近表面施主体系中磁时钟跃迁的新工具，这一成果对硅基量子器件（silicon-based quantum devices）中自旋相干性的控制具有重要意义。

Abstract: Magnetic clock transitions (CTs), defined by vanishing first-order sensitivity of the transition frequency to magnetic field fluctuations, provide a powerful route to suppress decoherence in donor spin systems. Here, we present the observation of magnetic field CTs from an ensemble of near-surface $^{75}$As ($I = 3/2$) spins in silicon using low-field ($< 10$~mT) continuous-wave electrically detected magnetic resonance (EDMR). As the CT condition is approached, pronounced linewidth broadening is observed, consistent with a donor Hamiltonian informed linewidth model. These results establish low-field EDMR as a sensitive probe of CTs in near-surface donor systems relevant to silicon-based quantum devices.

Main category: quant-ph

  <summary>Details</summary>

Conclusion: 双曲（非欧几里得）NQS拟设在具有层级结构（hierarchical structures）的量子多体问题中普遍优于欧几里得NQS拟设；洛伦兹RNN因其优异的性能-效率权衡，被认为是最有前景的双曲NQS变体。

Abstract: In this work, we extend the class of previously introduced non-Euclidean neural quantum states (NQS) which consists only of Poincaré hyperbolic GRU, to new variants including Poincaré RNN as well as Lorentz RNN and Lorentz GRU. In addition to constructing and introducing the new non-Euclidean hyperbolic NQS ansatzes, we generalized the results of our earlier work regarding the definitive outperformances delivered by hyperbolic Poincaré GRU NQS ansatzes when benchmarked against their Euclidean counterparts in the Variational Monte Carlo (VMC) experiments involving the quantum many-body settings of the Heisenberg $J_1J_2$ and $J_1J_2J_3$ models, which exhibit hierarchical structures in the forms of the different degrees of nearest-neighbor interactions. Here, in particular, using larger systems consisting of 100 spins, we found that all four hyperbolic RNN/GRU NQS variants always outperformed their respective Euclidean counterparts. Specifically, for all $J_2$ and $(J_2,J_3)$ couplings considered, including $J_2=0.0$, Lorentz RNN NQS and Poincaré RNN NQS always outperformd Euclidean RNN NQS, while Lorentz/Poincaré GRU NQS always outperformed Euclidean GRU NQS, with a single exception when $J_2=0.0$ for Poincaré GRU NQS. Furthermore, among the four hyperbolic NQS ansatzes, depending on the specific $J_2$ or $(J_2, J_3)$ couplings, on four out of eight experiment settings, Lorentz GRU and Poincaré GRU took turns to be the top performing variant among all Euclidean and hyperbolic NQS ansatzes considered, while Lorentz RNN, with up to three times fewer parameters, was capable of not only surpassing the Euclidean GRU eight out of eight times but also outperforming both Lorentz GRU and Poincaré GRU four out of eight times, to emerge as the best overall hyperbolic NQS ansatz.

Method: 采用kicked-Ising模型作为可解析处理的平台，以横场Ising模型的吉布斯态（Gibbs state）为初始态，结合解析和数值方法，在演化过程中同时引入热效应（thermal effects）和退相干效应（decoherence effects）。

Result: 以ergotropy作为核心性能指标，表征了注入能量和可提取能量，识别出即便存在环境效应时充电性能仍保持鲁棒的特定参数区间。

Conclusion: 该工作为评估量子电池在热效应和耗散效应下的性能提供了一个系统性的理论框架。

Abstract: Quantum batteries (QBs) have emerged as a promising route for fast energy storage and on-chip power supply in quantum devices. Given the limited analytical understanding of open Floquet QBs, we employ the kicked-Ising model as a tractable platform to systematically study its performance under realistic conditions, including finite temperature effects and environmental dissipation. Starting from Gibbs states of the transverse-field Ising model, we incorporate thermal and decoherence effects along the evolution, using both analytical and numerical approaches. Taking ergotropy as a central figure of merit, we characterize the injected and extractable energy, and identify regimes where charging remains robust despite environmental effects. Our results provide a systematic framework for assessing QB performance under thermal and dissipative effects.

</details>


### [197] [Gauge-covariant projected entangled paired states for interacting systems in a magnetic field](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24574)
*Wei Tang,Gunnar Möller,Frank Verstraete,Laurens Vanderstraeten*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一种基于投影纠缠对态（PEPS）的波函数构造方法，通过在张量网络中引入虚拟磁通（virtual flux），在保持物理期望值平移不变性的前提下，实现对均匀磁场中二维格点系统的高效模拟，无需依赖规范选择（gauge choice）或扩展磁原胞（magnetic unit cell）。

  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 均匀磁场中二维格点系统的哈密顿量因矢势（vector potential）的规范选择而将平移对称性（translational symmetry）降阶为磁平移群（magnetic translation group），然而基态物理可观测量通常仍保持完全的平移不变性。现有模拟方法需要引入扩展的磁原胞，增加了计算复杂度。因此，需要一种不依赖规范选择、且能自然保持平移不变性的数值方法。

Method: 提出一种带有虚拟磁通张量（virtual flux tensor）模式的投影纠缠对态（projected entangled-pair state, PEPS）波函数。该波函数通过构造保证所有物理期望值在（可能放大的原胞内）具有平移不变性。模拟时，每个原胞（plaquette）的磁通仅作为连续参数（continuous parameter）进入张量网络收缩（tensor network contraction）过程，因此可直接沿用平移不变PEPS的常规收缩与优化方法。

Result: 该方法使得在均匀磁场中模拟相互作用多体系统时，可以完全独立于矢势的规范选择，并且无需考虑扩展的磁原胞。磁通仅作为一个连续参数参与张量网络收缩，从而实现了对规范无关（gauge-independent）的模拟。

Conclusion: 本文提出的方法为均匀磁场中相互作用多体系统的数值模拟提供了一种规范无关的通用框架，有效避免了传统方法中因规范选择或磁原胞扩展带来的额外复杂性。

Abstract: The Hamiltonian for a system of itinerant particles on a two-dimensional lattice in a uniform magnetic field reduces the translational symmetry to a magnetic translation group, because of the need to choose a particular gauge for the vector potential. Nonetheless, in many situations all physical observables of the ground state remain entirely translation invariant. In this work, we introduce a projected entangled-pair state (PEPS) wavefunction with a pattern of virtual flux tensors, for which all physical expectation values are translation invariant by construction, possibly within an enlarged unit cell reflecting any symmetry breaking in the target state. Moreover, we show that the usual contraction and optimization methods for translation-invariant PEPS can be used, with the magnetic flux per plaquette only entering as a continuous parameter in the tensor network contractions. Therefore, our approach provides a method for simulating an interacting many-body system in a uniform magnetic field independently of the gauge choice for the vector potential and bypassing the need to consider extended magnetic unit cells.

Time of flight secondary ion mass spectrometry (ToF-SIMS) was used to measure the relative concentration of W isotopes. $^{183}$W, the only W isotope that has a net nuclear spin and is the major cause of spin decoherence, was at a relative abundance of 1.2%, a factor of 10 lower than natural abundance. We also observed PL emission from single ions after integrating nano-photonic devices with the thin film. These results establish isotopically engineered CaWO$_{4}$ thin films as a promising platform for future studies of nuclear-spin-limited coherence and for scalable rare-earth-ion-based quantum nanophotonic devices.

### [199] [Operating a contextual Stern-Gerlach apparatus](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24727)
*Th. K. Mavrogordatos*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 采用两能级“原子”跃迁的赝自旋模拟自旋，共振驱动场模拟磁场，并结合相位敏感的连续腔场探测来实现对两个输出结果稳定性的调控。

Result: 在驱动强度降低时，系统的 dressed 态（ dressed states）被自发 dressed 态极化（ self-consistent spontaneous dressed-state polarization）取代；特定监测设置下持续产生相干态叠加（coherent-state superpositions），体现了高度上下文相关性；当双稳态缺失时，光电子“原子”发射统计可作为腔场涨落的诊断工具。

Conclusion: 该工作不仅提供了一个类比斯特恩-格拉赫实验的腔 QED 实现，还展示了上下文性在量子系统调控中的核心作用，并提供了一种基于发射统计的腔场涨落诊断方法。

Abstract: We propose a contextual cavity/circuit QED analogue and extension of the Stern-Gerlach experiment, where the pseudo-spin of a two-state `atomic' transition plays the role of the ``spin'', while the resonant field driving the transition stands for the ``magnetic field''. A phase-sensitive continuous detection of the cavity field coupled to the induced `atomic' dipole affects the stability of the two distinct outcomes. The dressed states comprising the latter give their place to a self-consistent spontaneous dressed-state polarization as the driving strength is lowered. The associated evolution proves anew highly contextual, underpinned by a persistent production of coherent-state superpositions for a particular setting of the monitoring device. Finally, when bistability is absent, we employ the photoelectron `atomic' emission statistics as a diagnostic tool of the cavity field fluctuations.

### [200] [Experimental high-dimensional multi-qubit Bell non-locality on a superconducting quantum processor](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24740)
*Yousef Mafi,Ali G. Moghaddam,Teemu Ojanen*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 该研究利用超导量子硬件，在12个量子比特（qubits）上编码了d=64维系统，首次同时观测到高维（high-dimensional）和多体贝尔非定域性（many-body Bell non-locality）。实验在d=32以上的系统中证实了非定域性强度超越二维量子界限，且这种违背具有集体性——所有量子比特共同贡献，而大部分二分跨区配对（pairwise correlations）仍表现为贝尔定域性（Bell-local）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探索此前不可达的量子关联（quantum correlations）区域，即同时实现高维（high-dimensional）和多体（many-body）贝尔非定域性（Bell non-locality），并利用量子处理器验证量子力学（quantum mechanics）的基础预言。

Method: 基于超导量子硬件（superconducting quantum hardware）的近期进展，在12个量子比特（qubits）上编码两个d=64维系统，通过观测量子比特间的关联来检验贝尔非定域性（Bell non-locality）。

Result: 在d=64维系统间观测到高置信度的贝尔违背（Bell violation）；当系统维度d≥32时，非定域关联（nonlocal correlations）强度超过d=2量子系统的上界。所有量子比特共同贡献非定域关联，而大部分二分跨区配对仍保持贝尔定域性（Bell-local）。

Conclusion: 当前量子处理器能够探索此前不可及的量子力学基础预言区域，同时基础量子效应可用来基准测试（benchmark）量子硬件的性能。

Abstract: Combining recent advances in superconducting quantum hardware, we explore quantum correlations in a previously inaccessible regime by observing \emph{simultaneously} high-dimensional and many-body Bell non-locality. We report a high-confidence Bell violation in the correlations between two $d=64$-dimensional systems encoded in twelve qubits. For system sizes up to $d=32$, the strength of the observed nonlocal correlations exceeds the quantum upper bound for $d=2$ systems, providing direct evidence of high-dimensional nonlocality. Furthermore, we demonstrate that the observed violation is genuinely collective: all qubits contribute to the nonlocal correlations, while most pairwise correlations across the bipartition remain Bell-local. Our work illustrates how present-day quantum processors enable the exploration of fundamental predictions of quantum mechanics in previously inaccessible regimes and, in turn, how fundamental quantum effects can be used to benchmark their performance.

### [201] [Contracting Tensor Networks with Generalized Belief Propagation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24760)
*Joseph Tindall,Grace M. Sommers,Hilbert Kappen*

Main category: quant-ph

TL;DR: 本文详细阐述了如何将广义信念传播（generalized belief propagation, GBP）——一种基于重叠区域层次传递消息的算法——用于近似但高效地收缩张量网络，并通过多种二维/三维、无限/有限张量网络的数值与解析求解，展示了该方法在统计物理与量子多体问题中的有效性与准确性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 原有的信念传播（belief propagation, BP）作为一种用于图模型（graphical models）统计推断的算法，近年来被用于近似张量网络收缩，但精度有限。本文旨在推广BP方法，通过引入广义信念传播（GBP）来提升张量网络近似的准确性。

Method: 本文提出将广义信念传播（GBP）应用于张量网络收缩，其核心是在张量网络的一组重叠区域（overlapping regions）的层级结构中传递消息。原始信念传播（BP）被作为GBP的一个特例（对应最简单的区域选择）处理。作者对二维和三维、无限和有限张量网络，针对多种区域选择方案实现了GBP算法，并采用数值方法以及在某些可解情形下的解析方法求解相应的不动点方程（fixed point equations）。

Result: 通过多种示例验证了方法的有效性：计算全反铁磁伊辛模型（fully frustrated Ising model）的配分函数（partition function）、三维冰模型（ice models）的基态简并度（ground state degeneracy）、变形AKLT量子态（deformed AKLT quantum state）上的可观测量，以及评估随机生成张量网络态（randomly generated tensor network states）的范数（norm）。

Conclusion: 广义信念传播（GBP）能够在不显著增加计算复杂度的前提下，显著提升张量网络近似收缩的精度。原始信念传播（BP）可视为该框架的一个特例，而合适的区域选择策略使得GBP在统计物理和量子多体系统的计算中具有广泛适用性。

Abstract: Recent years have seen a growing interest in the use of belief propagation - an algorithm originally introduced for performing statistical inference on graphical models - for approximate, but highly efficient, tensor network contraction. Here, we detail how to apply generalized belief propagation (GBP) - where messages are passed within a hierarchy of overlapping regions of the tensor network - to approximately contract tensor networks and obtain accurate results. The original belief propagation algorithm is a corner case of this approach, corresponding to a particularly simple choice of regions of the tensor network. We implement the GBP algorithm for a number of different region choices on a range of two- and three-dimensional, infinite and finite tensor networks, solving the corresponding fixed point equations both numerically and, in certain tractable cases, analytically. Our examples include calculating the partition function of the fully frustrated Ising model, computing the ground state degeneracy of three-dimensional ice models, measuring observables on the deformed AKLT quantum state and evaluating the norm of randomly generated tensor network states.

### [202] [Statistical Mechanics of Household Income and Wealth: Derivation from Firm Dynamics via Maximum Entropy and Mixture Aggregation](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22976)
*Robert T. Nachtrieb*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 该论文从第一性原理推导出发，揭示了发达经济体收入与财富的双层结构（约97%人口服从指数分布、约3%上层服从幂律分布），通过一个包含吉布拉定律、最大熵原理和加性噪声财富动力学的机制链，定量再现了帕累托尾部指数α_w≈1.30及员工与所有者财富温度比T_w/T_y≈1.7年，并在无自由参数条件下成功验证了企业退出率的时间标度律。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 解释发达经济体中收入与财富分布为何普遍呈现指数主体加幂律尾部的双层结构，并试图从第一性原理（first principles）出发，通过明确的机制链条给出定量推导与无参数检验。

Method: 构建包含三个核心环节的机制链：（1）企业增长满足吉布拉定律（Gibrat's law），推导出齐普夫企业规模分布（Zipf firm-size distribution）；（2）对企业内部工资应用最大熵原理（maximum entropy），并结合跨企业混合聚合（mixture aggregation），得到员工收入的玻尔兹曼-吉布斯分布（Boltzmann–Gibbs distribution）；（3）对员工财富采用带有零反射壁（reflecting wall at zero）的加性噪声财富动力学（additive-noise wealth dynamics），导出玻尔兹曼-吉布斯财富分布；对企业所有者则通过乘性资本回报（multiplicative capital returns）得出帕累托财富尾部（Pareto wealth tail），指数α_w=1/θ。经验参数来自已有文献（如企业价值标度V∝s^0.77），未引入可调参数。

Result: 无参数地复现了帕累托尾部指数α_w≈1.30；首次定量估计了人均回报规模指数ζ≈-0.23；在经验值ν≈0.3、c≈0.81、k≈0.15及长期储蓄率≈5%下，模型给出财富温度与收入温度之比T_w/T_y≈1.7年，即底层家庭财富约为年收入的1-2倍；企业退出率的时间标度律为~t^{-1/2}log t，表观指数b=0.295±0.03，与BDS企业年龄数据吻合且无自由参数。

Conclusion: 该模型从微观机制出发，统一解释了收入-财富分布的普适双组分结构，并能在无需调参的情况下再现多个关键实证数据（帕累托指数、财富收入比、企业退出率），具有较强的预测能力和跨国可检验性。

Abstract: The distribution of income and wealth in developed economies exhibits a robust two-class structure: an exponential (Boltzmann--Gibbs) bulk covering $\sim\!97\%$ of the population, and a power-law (Pareto) tail in the upper $\sim\!3\%$. We derive this structure from first principles via an explicit mechanistic chain: Gibrat's law for firm growth implies a Zipf firm-size distribution; maximum entropy applied to within-firm wages, combined with mixture aggregation across firms, yields a Boltzmann--Gibbs income distribution with temperature $T_y$ for employees; additive-noise wealth dynamics with a reflecting wall at zero produce a Boltzmann--Gibbs employee wealth distribution with temperature $T_w$. For firm owners, multiplicative capital returns produce a Pareto wealth tail with exponent $α_w = 1/θ$, where $θ$ encodes how total returns scale with firm size. The empirical value $α_w \approx 1.30$ \cite{Yakovenko2009} is reproduced with no tuned parameters from the observed firm value scaling $V = V_0(s/s_0)^{0.77}$~\cite{Axtell2001}, and simultaneously yields the first quantitative estimate of the returns-per-employee size exponent: $ζ= θ- 1 \approx -0.23$. For empirical values $ν\approx 0.3$, $c \approx 0.81$, $k \approx 0.15$ (BEA long-run savings rate $\approx 5\%$), the model gives $T_w/T_y \approx 1.7\,\text{yr}$, i.e.\ lower-class households hold roughly 1--2 years of income as wealth, with the precise ratio depending on savings and tax rates and testable cross-country. As a parameter-free empirical test, firms near zero profit have a cash martingale whose first-passage time gives establishment exit rate $\sim t^{-1/2}$; convolving with the Zipf firm-size distribution yields firm-level exit rate $\sim t^{-1/2}\!\log t$, with apparent exponent $b = 0.295 \pm 0.03$, confirmed against BDS firm-age data with no free parameters.

</details>


### [203] [Equations of Motion for an Economy: Capital Deepening, Technology, and Firm Survival](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22995)
*Robert T. Nachtrieb*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文直接从会计恒等式出发，推导了竞争性经济中资本深化（capital deepening）的运动方程，无需假设生产函数。提出了“利润命令”（profit imperative）作为可行资本生产率的下界，并建立了四个耦合的弛豫方程。基于BEA和BDS数据的校准显示，生产率通道（productivity channel）在过去75年中始终为零，而一个微小的正生产率步进即可在资本寿命期内使增长率翻倍，并给出了企业退出率的可证伪预测。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统经济增长理论通常依赖生产函数假设，但该前提在实证中难以完全成立。本文试图直接从会计恒等式出发，在不预设生产函数的情况下，推导资本深化的运动方程，以更基础的方式理解经济动态。

Method: 从会计恒等式出发推导资本生产率η、人均资本κ、前沿生产率η_new和劳动份额q的四个耦合弛豫方程，引入“利润命令”η^*作为约束。采用BEA 2-digit NAICS部门数据（1998–2023）和75年战后记录进行校准，并使用BDS数据验证退出率预测。

Result: 校准结果显示，所有可识别部门在过去25年及75年战后记录中，生产率通道φ=0。一个φ=0.01 yr⁻¹的微小步进——历史上未有的1%/年新资本生产率提升——可在单个资本寿命期内使总增长率几乎翻倍，并给出清晰的可观测特征：BEA部门数据中η(t)呈上弯曲线。零利润阈值附近的企业具有现金鞅（cash martingale），预测企业退出率∝t^{-1/2}，经Zipf企业规模分布卷积后得到退出率∝t^{-1/2}log t，表观指数b=0.295±0.03，与BDS数据一致且无自由参数。

Conclusion: 本文提供了一个不依赖生产函数的经济增长分析框架，揭示了两个物理上不同的通道——结构性廉价化通道（structural cheapening channel）始终活跃，而生产率通道在历史记录中未展现。模型得出的可证伪预测为检验其有效性提供了明确的实证路径。

Abstract: We derive equations of motion for capital deepening in a competitive economy directly from accounting identities, without assuming a production function. A profit imperative $η^* \equiv (w/κ+ 1/τ)/(1-f_p)$ sets the minimum viable capital productivity, where $η= Y/K$ [yr$^{-1}$] is capital productivity, $κ= K/L$ is capital per worker, $w$ is the wage rate, $τ$ is the capital lifetime, and $f_p$ is the production tax share. Four coupled relaxation equations govern $κ$, $η$, the frontier productivity $η_{\rm new}$ of new investment, and the labor share $q \equiv w/y$, with the sandwich constraint $η^* \leq η_{\rm new} \leq η$ maintained as an exact invariant. The frontier equation separates two physically distinct channels: a structural cheapening channel ($μ$, always active, drives $η_{\rm new}$ downward) and a productivity channel ($φ$, historically zero). Calibration against BEA 2-digit NAICS sector data (1998--2023) confirms $φ= 0$ for all identifiable sectors over 25 years; the 75-year postwar record extends this finding across four capital lifetimes. A step $φ= 0.01$\,yr$^{-1}$ -- a 1\%/yr improvement in new-capital productivity, modest but historically unprecedented -- nearly doubles the aggregate growth rate within one capital lifetime, a falsifiable prediction with a precise observable signature: upward-curving $η(t)$ in BEA sector data. Firms near the zero-profit threshold have a cash martingale, predicting establishment exit rate $\sim t^{-1/2}$; convolved with the Zipf firm-size distribution~\cite{WP}, this yields firm exit rate $\sim t^{-1/2}\!\log t$ with apparent exponent $b = 0.295 \pm 0.03$, confirmed against BDS data with no free parameters.

</details>


### [204] [Nesting Controls Phase Transitions in Higher-Order Contagion](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23337)
*Hugo P. Maia,Guilherme Ferraz de Arruda,Silvio C. Ferreira,Yamir Moreno*

Main category: physics.soc-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出一个量化超图中高阶与低阶交互嵌套程度的系数，并系统揭示了该嵌套系数对传染病动力学相变行为（如激活阈值与突变更替）的调控机制，确立了嵌套性作为高阶系统相变的关键结构决定因素。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 高阶交互（higher-order interactions）的组织方式对集体动力学（collective dynamics）具有核心影响，但目前尚缺乏一种通用结构原理来解释超图（hypergraph）上的传染过程如何受其底层结构支配。

Method: 引入嵌套系数（nesting coefficient），定量刻画低阶交互嵌入高阶交互的程度，从而在单纯复形（simplicial complex）与随机超图（random hypergraph）之间定义一个连续谱。在此基础上，采用高阶易感-感染-易感模型（higher-order susceptible-infected-susceptible model, SIS model）进行动力学分析。

Result: 增加嵌套会降低激活阈值（activation threshold）并抑制不连续相变（discontinuous transition），而弱嵌套则倾向于促进爆炸式行为（explosive behavior）；嵌套与交互阶数（interaction order）之间的相关性可调节活动起始点，但对相变的不连续性影响较小；在合成网络与实证网络中，嵌套性均为滞后效应（hysteresis）的强预测因子。

Conclusion: 嵌套性是决定高阶系统相变行为的关键结构因素，为理解超图上的集体动力学提供了一个统一的组织原理。

Abstract: The organization of higher-order interactions plays a central role in shaping collective dynamics, yet a general structural principle governing contagion on hypergraphs remains lacking. Here we introduce a nesting coefficient that quantifies how lower-order interactions are embedded within higher-order ones, defining a continuum between simplicial complexes and random hypergraphs. Using a higher-order susceptible-infected-susceptible model, we show that increasing nesting lowers the activation threshold and suppresses discontinuous transitions, while weak embedding favors explosive behavior. We further demonstrate that correlations between nesting and interaction order modulate the onset of activity while only weakly affecting transition discontinuity. Analysis of synthetic and empirical networks reveals that nesting strongly predicts hysteresis, establishing it as a key structural determinant of phase transitions in higher-order systems.

</details>
