### [205] [Visualizing Vortex Cluster Dynamics in the Weak Type-II Superconductor CaSb$_2$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23117)
*Yusuke Iguchi,Nabhanila Nandi,Mohamed Oudah*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 通过扫描SQUID成像技术，在CaSb₂中观测到密集涡旋团簇（vortex clusters），其特征（增强的边界磁化率、被抑制的内部涡旋运动）既不符合孤立涡旋（isolated vortex）行为也不符合磁通管（flux tube）行为。尽管超流密度（superfluid density）符合单能隙BCS模型且Ginzburg-Landau参数略超出type-II/1区间，但仍清晰观测到涡旋团簇与空间非均匀动力学，表明其物理机制超越了现有的单带超导体微观理论。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有单带超导体理论（type-II/1或type-1.5）无法解释CaSb₂中观测到的涡旋团簇行为，需要新的实验手段来直接可视化弱钉扎超导体（weakly pinned superconductor）中的磁动力学（magnetic dynamics），以探测可能存在的高阶、非单调的涡旋-涡旋相互作用（non-monotonic vortex-vortex interactions）。

Method: 采用扫描SQUID（scanning superconducting quantum interference device）成像技术，对弱钉扎超导体CaSb₂进行局部磁动力学（local magnetic dynamics）可视化测量。

Result: 在CaSb₂中观测到密集涡旋团簇，其边界磁化率（boundary susceptibility）增强而内部涡旋运动受到抑制；该行为与孤立涡旋和磁通管行为均不一致。超流密度拟合显示为单能隙（single-gap）BCS行为，Ginzburg-Landau参数略超出type-II/1区域。

Conclusion: CaSb₂中涡旋团簇与空间非均匀动力学的存在，表明弱钉扎超导体中存在超出单带超导体现有微观理论的物理机制，或与高阶非单调涡旋-涡旋相互作用有关。

Abstract: Scanning SQUID imaging of CaSb$_2$ reveals dense vortex clusters with enhanced boundary susceptibility and suppressed internal vortex motion, which features inconsistent with both isolated vortex and flux tube behaviors. These measurements provide the first local visualization of magnetic dynamics within vortex clusters in a weakly pinned superconductor, offering a new route to probe non-monotonic vortex-vortex interactions that are typically expected in single-band type-II/1 or multiband type-1.5 superconductors. Although the superfluid density follows a single-gap BCS model and the Ginzburg-Landau parameter of CaSb$_2$ lies slightly outside the type-II/1 regime, vortex clustering and spatially inhomogeneous dynamics are clearly observed, indicating physics beyond existing microscopic theories for single-band superconductors.

</details>


### [206] [Persistent Fermi Pockets and Robust Electron Pairing in Lightly Doped CuO$_2$ Planes of Cuprate Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23162)
*Hao Chen,Jumin Shi,Yinghao Li,Xiangyu Luo,Yiwen Chen,Chaohui Yin,Yingjie Shu,Jiuxiang Zhang,Taimin Miao,Bo Liang,Wenpei Zhu,Neng Cai,Xiaolin Ren,Chengtian Lin,Shenjin Zhang,Zhimin Wang,Fengfeng Zhang,Feng Yang,Qinjun Peng,Zuyan Xu,Guodong Liu,Hanqing Mao,Xintong Li,Tao Xiang,Lin Zhao,X. J. Zhou*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本研究利用高分辨率空间分辨激光角分辨光电子能谱（laser ARPES）探测多层铜氧化物超导体Bi₂Sr₂Ca_{n-1}Cu_nO_{2n+4+δ} (n=5~8)中CuO₂面的本征电子结构，发现内层CuO₂面在极低掺杂水平（空穴掺杂低至0.007）下即呈现定义良好的费米口袋，表明从母体莫特绝缘体（Mott insulator）到金属态的突变性转变，并观测到不同内层平面具有无间隙费米口袋与各向异性超导能隙（~33 meV）共存的复杂电子态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 铜氧化物高温超导电性通常被认为源于对莫特绝缘体的掺杂，但掺杂母体的基本性质以及电子配对的微观起源仍是理解超导电性出现的关键问题。本研究旨在通过探测高质量屏蔽无序的内层CuO₂面，揭示本征电子相图，从而厘清掺杂驱动的转变与配对机制。

Method: 采用高分辨率空间分辨激光角分辨光电子能谱（laser ARPES）技术，对多层铜氧化物Bi₂Sr₂Ca_{n-1}Cu_nO_{2n+4+δ} (n=5~8)中CuO₂面的本征电子结构进行探测。利用内层CuO₂面受到外层屏蔽从而免受无序干扰的特性，作为探测本征电子相图的理想平台。

Result: 观测到空穴掺杂水平低至0.007时即出现定义良好的费米口袋（Fermi pockets），证明从母体莫特绝缘体到金属态在极微量掺杂下存在突变性转变。最内层CuO₂面（IP₀）呈现无间隙费米口袋，而第二内层CuO₂面（IP₁）则表现出各向异性超导能隙（~33 meV），表明稳健的电子配对与强反铁磁序（antiferromagnetic order）共存。

Conclusion: 研究结果为理解铜氧化物超导体中掺杂驱动的相变和配对机制提供了修正后的框架，指出内层CuO₂面在极低掺杂下即发生莫特绝缘体到金属态的突变转变，且超导能隙与反铁磁序可在不同内层平面中共存。

Abstract: High temperature superconductivity in cuprate superconductors is generally considered to be generated from doping the Mott insulators. The fundamental nature of the doped parent compounds as well as the microscopic origin of electron pairing remain critical issues in understanding the emergence of superconductivity. Here, using high-resolution spatially-resolved laser angle-resolved photoemission spectroscopy, we investigate the intrinsic electronic structures of the CuO$_2$ planes in multilayer cuprates Bi$_2$Sr$_2$Ca$_{n-1}$Cu$_n$O$_{2n+4+δ}$ (n=5$\sim$8). The inner CuO$_2$ planes are well shielded from the disorders and provide a rare and ideal platform to probe the intrinsic electronic phase diagram. We observe well-defined Fermi pockets with hole doping levels as low as 0.007, demonstrating an abrupt transition from the parent Mott insulator to a metallic state upon the introduction of an infinitesimal amount of doping. The innermost CuO$_2$ planes (IP$_0$) display gapless Fermi pockets, while the second innermost planes (IP$_1$) exhibit anisotropic superconducting gaps up to $\sim$33$\,$meV, indicative of robust electron pairing coexisting with strong antiferromagnetic order. Our findings provide a revised framework for understanding the doping-driven transitions and pairing mechanisms in cuprate superconductors.

### [207] [Record magnetoresistance, enhanced superconductivity, and fermiology in WTe2](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23378)
*Gianluca Delgado,Elliott Runburg,Chaowei Hu,Yuzhou Zhao,Jonathan M. DeStefano,Keng Tou Chu,Florie Mesple,Ellis Thompson,Kenji Watanabe,Takashi Taniguchi,Jihui Yang,Matthew Yankowitz,Xiaodong Xu,Jiun-Haw Chu,David H. Cobden*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 通过一种名为水平通量输运（horizontal flux transport）的新型晶体生长技术，成功制备出高质量拓扑半金属（topological semimetal）WTe₂晶体，其无序度降低一个数量级，在低温下展现出迄今报道的最大磁电阻（magnetoresistance），并在静电掺杂的单层体系中首次观测到量子振荡（quantum oscillations）以及栅压调控的超导穹顶（superconducting dome），临界温度提升至约1.8 K。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 过渡金属硫族化物（transition metal chalcogenides）的电子性质对晶体缺陷极为敏感，而现有晶体质量限制了对其本征物性的研究和应用。因此，亟需发展新的晶体生长方法以降低无序度，从而揭示材料更深层次的物理性质。

Method: 采用并优化了一种名为水平通量输运（horizontal flux transport）的新型晶体生长技术，用于制备拓扑半金属（topological semimetal）WTe₂晶体。

Result: 所生长的WTe₂晶体无序度降低一个数量级；低温下实现了金属中迄今报道的最大磁电阻（magnetoresistance）；在静电掺杂的单层（monolayer）样品中首次观测到量子振荡（quantum oscillations），由此确定了能带简并度（band degeneracies）和电场诱导的谷劈裂（valley splitting）；同时观测到一个栅压调控的超导穹顶（superconducting dome），临界温度显著提升至约1.8 K。

Conclusion: 这一晶体生长技术的突破为利用WTe₂发展拓扑电子学（topological electronics）和栅控超导器件（gated superconducting devices）开辟了新途径，并有望在其他硫族化物中实现类似的性能突破。

Abstract: The diverse electronic properties of transition metal chalcogenides can be very sensitive to crystal imperfections. A new crystal growth technique, known as horizontal flux transport, offers a route to improved crystal quality. By refining this technique and applying it to the topological semimetal WTe2, we achieved crystals with an order of magnitude less disorder as determined by electrical transport and scanning tunneling microscopy measurements. At low temperatures these crystals exhibit the largest magnetoresistance reported in a metal. Exfoliated monolayers show quantum oscillations for the first time in the electrostatically doped metallic states, enabling determination of band degeneracies and the valley splitting induced by an electric field. Moreover, they exhibit a gated superconducting dome with a greatly enhanced critical temperature approaching 1.8 K. This advance opens up new avenues for employing WTe2 in topological electronics and gated superconducting devices, and promises comparable breakthroughs with other chalcogenides.

### [208] [Unconventional mixed state in the nematic superconductor LiFeAs](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23401)
*G. Lamura,T. Winyard,P. Gentile,M. Speight,F. Anger,B. Buchner,S. Wurmehl,T. Shiroka*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过横向μ子自旋谱学（transverse muon-spin spectroscopy）在LiFeAs单晶中发现了一种非常规涡旋晶格，并证明该新混合相由“无核”涡旋（coreless vortices）条纹构成，这些涡旋是两个空间分离的半量子涡旋（half-quantum vortices）的束缚态。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在第二类块体超导体（type-II bulk superconductors）的混合态中，传统上磁场以携带一个磁通量子（magnetic flux quantum）的涡旋形式穿透样品，形成阿布里科索夫涡旋晶格（Abrikosov vortex lattice）。本研究的动机是探索是否存在偏离这一常规图像的非常规涡旋结构。

Method: 采用横向μ子自旋谱学（transverse muon-spin spectroscopy）对LiFeAs单晶进行实验测量。

Result: 在LiFeAs单晶中观测到非常规涡旋晶格（unconventional vortex lattice）的存在。进一步证据表明，这种新的混合相由“无核”涡旋（coreless vortices）的条纹结构组成，每个“无核”涡旋是两个空间分离的半量子涡旋（half-quantum vortices）的束缚态。

Conclusion: LiFeAs中存在不同于传统Abrikosov涡旋晶格的非常规混合相，其基本单元为半量子涡旋束缚态所形成的无核涡旋条纹，这一发现拓展了对第二类超导体混合态物理的理解。

Abstract: In the mixed state of type-II bulk superconductors, the magnetic field penetrates in the form of vortices enclosing one magnetic flux quantum: this is the conventional Abrikosov vortex lattice. Here, by using transverse muon-spin spectroscopy, we demonstrate the presence of an unconventional vortex lattice in LiFeAs single crystals. We also show evidence that the new mixed phase consists of stripes of "coreless" vortices, which are bound states of two spatially separated half-quantum vortices.

### [209] [Campbell penetration depth in a single crystal of heavy fermion superconductor CeCoIn$_5$](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23657)
*Hyunsoo Kim,Makariy A. Tanatar,Cedomir Petrovic,Ruslan Prozorov*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 本文通过频率域隧道二极管谐振器测量了重费米子超导体CeCoIn₅单晶中随温度与磁场变化的磁穿透深度，发现Campbell穿透深度λ_C(H)显著偏离常规的√H行为，并在特征磁场处出现斜率突变，指示涡旋晶格对称性变化；同时λ_C(T)导出的临界电流密度J_c(T)在整个温区内近似线性温度依赖，与常规第二类超导体预期截然不同，为CeCoIn₅的非传统超导电性提供了新证据。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为探索重费米子超导体CeCoIn₅可能存在的非传统超导电性（unconventional superconductivity），利用尚未被应用的Campbell穿透深度测量手段，获取其涡旋钉扎及临界电流密度的微观信息。

Method: 采用频率域隧道二极管谐振器（frequency-domain tunnel diode resonator）测量CeCoIn₅单晶中温度与磁场依赖的磁穿透深度λ_m(T,H)；通过在有限直流磁场下测量得到Campbell穿透深度λ_C(T,H)，进而推导出未弛豫的真实临界电流密度J_c。

Result: CeCoIn₅的λ_C(H)显著偏离常规第二类超导体预期的√H行为，在特征磁场值处呈现斜率突变；由λ_C(T)计算得到的J_c(T)在整个温度范围内呈现近乎线性的温度依赖关系。

Conclusion: λ_C(H)偏离常规行为被视为涡旋晶格对称性改变（vortex lattice symmetry change）的特征信号；结合J_c(T)的线性温度依赖，表明CeCoIn₅表现出非传统超导电性，为理解重费米子超导机制提供了来自Campbell穿透深度的新实验证据。

Abstract: The temperature and magnetic field dependent magnetic penetration depth, $λ_m(T,H)$, was measured in a single crystal of a heavy fermion superconductor CeCoIn$_5$ using a frequency-domain tunnel diode resonator. In addition to the London penetration depth, which yields the superfluid density, measurements in a finite DC magnetic field provide Campbell penetration depth, $λ_C(T,H)$, which is directly linked to the true (unrelaxed) critical current density, $J_c$. The measured $λ_C(H)$ in CeCoIn$_5$ deviates significantly from the conventional $\sim \sqrt{H}$ behavior, and its slope changes abruptly at the characteristic magnetic field values. Considering that our sample is in the clean limit, we interpret this deviation as a fingerprint of the vortex lattice symmetry change. The temperature dependence $J_c(T)$ of CeCoIn$_5$ calculated from $λ_C(T)$ is nearly $T$-linear over the entire temperature range, also in stark contrast to expectations in a conventional type-II superconductor. Our results provide new evidence for unconventional superconductivity in CeCoIn$_5$ from the never-before-measured Campbell penetration depth.

</details>


### [210] [Cosine bands, flat bands and superconductivity in orthorhombic iron selenide](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24298)
*Ian D R Mackinnon,Jose A Alarco*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 通过第一性原理计算，系统分析了正交相β-FeSe1-x在16K以下、高达23 GPa压力下的电子能带结构，发现平带（flat bands）与余弦型能带（cosine-shaped bands）的相互作用随压力增强，维持并提升了超导特性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究β-FeSe1-x在高压下超导特性的电子起源，尤其是平带与余弦型能带对电荷分布、费米面拓扑及超导能隙的影响机制。

Method: 基于实验测定的晶胞参数，对正交相β-FeSe1-x在16 K以下、0–23 GPa压力范围内进行电子能带结构计算；采用源自Cmma对称性且带有2c超晶格的P1晶胞，以缓解能带交叉效应。

Result: 平行于c轴的所有压力下均存在余弦型能带；P1晶胞计算将能带交叉的影响缓解至9.0 GPa，并得到了与实验值一致的超导能隙（superconducting gap）。沿GZ方向的平带出现在费米能级附近，影响层间电荷分布与转移；平带还随压力增加改变费米面拓扑，尤其在c*方向（沿ky偏移）。在b*方向的费米面上，余弦能带分裂并形成利于电子-空穴配对（electron-hole pairing）的排列，节点拐点位于费米能级。当压力超过12.0 GPa时，平带与折叠余弦带相互作用，引发额外能带色散。

Conclusion: 计算表明，平带参与了β-FeSe1-x的超导过程，并随压力增大而增强和维持其超导特性，直至23 GPa。

Abstract: Electronic band structures (EBSs) for orthorhombic beta FeSe1-x at less than 16 K and up to 23 GPa using experimentally determined cell dimensions are evaluated for cosine-shaped bands near, or crossing, EF. Cosine shaped bands are present in reciprocal directions parallel to the c axis at all pressures. Calculations using a P1 cell derived from Cmma symmetry with a 2c superlattice moderates the effect of intersecting bands to 9.0 GPa. This approach enables determination of a superconducting gap consistent with experimentally determined values. Key influences on charge distribution and transfer in the interplanar region of beta FeSe1-x are lone pair electrons which feature as flat bands (FBs) near EF along GZ in an EBS. FBs also influence the topology of Fermi surfaces as pressure increases and in directions parallel to the c* direction (i.e. offset along ky) within the Brillouin zone. At the Fermi surface along b*, cosine bands split and align favorably for electron-hole pairing with nodal inflection points located at EF. For P greater than 12.0 GPa, FBs interact with folded cosine bands invoking additional band dispersions. These calculations suggest that FBs participate in, and with increased pressure, enhance and sustain the superconducting properties of beta FeSe1-x to 23 GPa.

</details>


### [211] [Nonintegral Flux Trapping in Frustrated Josephson Networks of Triplet Superconductors](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24734)
*Grayson R. Frazier,Colton Lelievre,Yi Li*

Main category: cond-mat.supr-con

TL;DR: 该论文表明，在约瑟夫森结网络（Josephson junction network）中，自旋三重态配对关联（spin triplet pairing correlations）之间的各向异性耦合会导致受挫的 d 矢量（d vector）织构，进而支持自发约瑟夫森电流和非整数磁通俘获。这一机制可在超导多晶和单晶超导体中实现，并区别于通常的半量子涡旋（half-quantum vortices）。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为了探索在超导体系中由几何阻挫（geometric frustration）和各向异性耦合产生非平凡拓扑织构的新物理机制，特别是自旋三重态超导中 d 矢量织构对磁通行为的调控作用。

Method: 通过类比经典自旋系统（classical spin systems）中的几何阻挫和各向异性超交换（anisotropic superexchange），分析约瑟夫森网络中各向异性耦合条件下 U(1) 超导相位差与 d 矢量相对取向之间的竞争关系，研究库珀对隧穿过程中 d 矢量织构作为涌现几何相位（emergent geometric phase）的行为。

Result: 发现对于幺正三重态配对序（unitary triplet pairing order），当反对称约瑟夫森耦合（antisymmetric Josephson coupling）超过某一临界值时，系统可支持 π 磁通俘获（π-flux trapping），该机制不同于标准的半量子涡旋。

Conclusion: 揭示了利用磁织构（magnetic textures）与自旋三重态超导配对序之间的相互作用来设计受挫约瑟夫森网络的新途径。

Abstract: In a Josephson junction network, anisotropic coupling between spin triplet pairing correlations can lead to frustrated $d$ vector textures that support spontaneous Josephson currents and nonintegral flux trapping. Such networks can appear in superconducting polycrystals, as well as single-crystal superconductors. In analogy to classical spin systems, in which the presence of geometric frustration and anisotropic superexchange can lead to nontrivial spin textures, Josephson networks with anisotropic Josephson couplings cannot simultaneously optimize their $\mathrm{U}(1)$ superconducting phase difference and relative $d$ vector orientations. The internal pairing structure of Cooper pairs twists as they tunnel across the Josephson junction, and the $d$ vector texture enters as an emergent geometric phase which can spontaneously trap fractional flux. For unitary triplet pairing order, this mechanism can support $π$-flux trapping above a critical value of antisymmetric Josephson coupling, and is distinct from usual half-quantum vortices. The results of this work reveal new routes to engineer frustrated Josephson networks from the interplay of magnetic textures and spin triplet superconducting pairing order.

### [212] [Hamiltonian Graph Inference Networks: Joint structure discovery and dynamics prediction for lattice Hamiltonian systems from trajectory data](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23606)
*Ru Geng,Panayotis Kevrekidis,Yixian Gao,Hong-Kun Zhang,Jian Zu*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出哈密顿图推断网络（HGIN），一种能从状态数据中同时恢复相互作用图并预测长时间轨迹的方法，适用于可分/不可分哈密顿量及异质节点动力学，在三个基准上将长时能量和轨迹预测误差降低六至十三个数量级。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 格点哈密顿系统（lattice Hamiltonian systems）在凝聚态、非线性光学和生物物理学中广泛存在，但从中学习动力学面临两个未知因素：相互作用拓扑（interaction topology）以及节点动力学（node dynamics）是否同质。现有图方法要么假设图已知，要么仅适用于节点动力学同质（homogeneous）的可分哈密顿量（separable Hamiltonian）。

Method: HGIN 包含两个模块：一个结构学习模块（structure-learning module），利用可学习的加权邻接矩阵（weighted adjacency matrix）在哈密顿方程损失（Hamilton's-equations loss）下训练；一个轨迹预测模块（trajectory-prediction module），通过 $k$-means 聚类将边划分为物理上不同的子图，每个子图分配独立的编码器，从而打破传统图神经网络（GNN）的参数共享瓶颈。

Result: 在三个基准（含长程相互作用的 Klein–Gordon 晶格、同质和异质的离散非线性薛定谔晶格）上，HGIN 相比基线方法将长时能量预测误差（long-time energy prediction error）和轨迹预测误差降低六至十三个数量级。对称性分析表明，学习到的权重编码了底层对势（pair potential）的宇称（parity）。

Conclusion: HGIN 能同时处理图拓扑未知、哈密顿量可分/不可分及节点动力学异质等复杂情形，显著提升长时间预测精度，并提供对系统相互作用结构的可解释读出（interpretable readout）。

Abstract: Lattice Hamiltonian systems underpin models across condensed matter, nonlinear optics, and biophysics, yet learning their dynamics from data is obstructed by two unknowns: the interaction topology and whether node dynamics are homogeneous. Existing graph-based approaches either assume the graph is given or, as in $α$-separable graph Hamiltonian network, infer it only for separable Hamiltonians with homogeneous node dynamics. We introduce the Hamiltonian Graph Inference Network (HGIN), which jointly recovers the interaction graph and predicts long-time trajectories from state data alone, for both separable and non-separable Hamiltonians and under heterogeneous node dynamics. HGIN couples a structure-learning module -- a learnable weighted adjacency matrix trained under a Hamilton's-equations loss -- with a trajectory-prediction module that partitions edges into physically distinct subgraphs via $k$-means clustering, assigning each subgraph its own encoder and thereby breaking the parameter-sharing bottleneck of conventional GNNs. On three benchmarks -- a Klein--Gordon lattice with long-range interactions and two discrete nonlinear Schrödinger lattices (homogeneous and heterogeneous) -- HGIN reduces long-time energy prediction error and trajectory prediction error by six to thirteen orders of magnitude relative to baselines. A symmetry argument on the Hamiltonian loss further shows that the learned weights encode the parity of the underlying pair potential, yielding an interpretable readout of the system's interaction structure.

</details>


### [213] [Agentic Fusion of Large Atomic and Language Models to Accelerate Materials Discovery](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23758)
*Mingze Li,Yu Rong,Songyou Li,Lihong Wang,Jiacheng Cen,Liming Wu,Anyi Li,Zongzhao Li,Qiuliang Liu,Rui Jiao,Tian Bian,Pengju Wang,Hao Sun,Jianfeng Zhang,Ji-Rong Wen,Deli Zhao,Shifeng Jin,Tingyang Xu,Wenbing Huang*

Main category: cs.LG

TL;DR: 本文提出 ElementsClaw，一个将大型原子模型（LAMs）与大型语言模型（LLMs）协同整合的智能体框架，用于自主执行从筛选到合成的完整材料发现流程，并在超导体领域成功指导合成了四种新材料，展示了高物理保真度的规模化发现能力。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 新材料的发现对全球能源和量子技术转型至关重要。现有预测或生成式深度学习模型通常孤立运行，缺乏自主编排能力来执行完整的发现流程，亟需一个能够整合多尺度计算与语义推理的自主化框架。

Method: ElementsClaw 是一个智能体框架（agentic framework），它协同了大型原子模型（Large Atomic Models, LAMs）与大型语言模型（Large Language Models, LLMs）。该框架根据多样化的人类需求，动态编排一套基于所提出的 Elements 模型微调而来的 LAM 工具用于原子尺度数值计算，同时利用 LLM 进行高层级语义推理，实现从孤立过程向集成化、人机交互式发现的转变。

Result: 在超导体领域，ElementsClaw 指导实验合成了四种新型超导体，包括转变温度为 6.8 K 的 Zr3ScRe8 和 6.7 K 的 HfZrRe4。在大规模筛选中，该系统仅用 28 GPU 小时便筛选了超过 240 万个稳定晶体，识别出 68,000 个高置信度的超导候选材料，极大扩展了已知超导空间。

Conclusion: ElementsClaw 证明了将 LAM 与 LLM 协同整合的智能体框架能够以高物理保真度加速材料发现，推动 AI 驱动的材料科学从孤立的预测过程向集成化、可交互的自主发现模式演进。

Abstract: The discovery of novel materials is critical for global energy and quantum technology transitions. While deep learning has fundamentally reshaped this landscape, existing predictive or generative models typically operate in isolation, lacking the autonomous orchestration required to execute the full discovery process. Here we present ElementsClaw, an agentic framework for materials discovery that synergizes Large Atomic Models (LAMs) with Large Language Models (LLMs). In response to varied human requirements, ElementsClaw dynamically orchestrates a suite of LAM tools finetuned from our proposed model Elements for atomic-scale numerical computation, while leveraging LLMs for high-level semantic reasoning. This shift moves AI-driven materials science from isolated processes toward integrated and human interactive discovery. In the demanding domain of superconductors, our agentic system guides the experimental synthesis of four new superconductors, including Zr3ScRe8 with a transition temperature of 6.8 K and HfZrRe4 at 6.7 K. At scale, ElementsClaw screens more than 2.4 million stable crystals within only 28 GPU hours, identifying 68,000 high-confidence superconducting candidates and vastly expanding the known superconducting space. These results demonstrate how our agent accelerates materials discovery with high physical fidelity.

### [214] [Pulsed Vertical Electric Dipole Over a Lossy Halfspace: On the Time-Domain Zenneck Wave](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23254)
*Giampiero Lovat*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文基于双变形技术（double-deformation technique），推导了有损半空间上方脉冲垂直电偶极子辐射瞬态电磁场的因果时域公式，将场分解为源极点、损耗极点、模态极点和最陡下降残差贡献，并识别出与频域Zenneck波对应的时域模态项，该模态项在有限晚时间区间内可主导场，而严格渐近尾保持t^{-5/2}代数衰减。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 在有损半空间（lossy half-space）的脉冲源问题中，频域Zenneck波是否存在清晰的时域对应物（time-domain manifestation）长期以来缺乏严格的理论分析。本文旨在通过因果时域方法，明确识别并解释与Zenneck波相关的时域信号特征。

Method: 从经典Sommerfeld表示出发，采用双变形技术，依次在横向波数平面和频率平面进行围道变形（contour deformation），将场显式分解为源极点、损耗极点、模态极点和最陡下降残差四个贡献项。通过标准双逆变换得到的参考解验证了所得表达式的因果性和正确性。

Result: 频率平面变形产生的模态贡献（与频域Zenneck极点相关）具有约化时间不变性（reduced-time invariance）和与表面波分量一致的空间衰减特性。在合适的源与观测条件下，该模态项可在宽泛且物理相关的有限晚时间区间内主导总场。然而，对于阻尼正弦激励，固定距离处的严格渐近尾仍保持t^{-5/2}的代数衰减阶次，贡献来自残差连续谱和模态极点族。

Conclusion: 本文给出了频域Zenneck波在脉冲半空间问题中严格的、可物理解释的时域表现形式，为理解有损介质中瞬态表面波的传播机制提供了理论基础。

Abstract: We investigate the transient electromagnetic field radiated by a pulsed vertical electric dipole above a lossy half-space and identify its time-domain signatures associated with the Zenneck wave. Starting from the classical Sommerfeld representation, we derive a causal time-domain formulation based on the double-deformation technique, with successive contour deformations in the transverse-wavenumber and frequency planes. This yields an explicit decomposition of the field into source-pole, loss-pole, modal-pole, and residual steepest-descent contributions. The resulting expressions exactly satisfy causality and are validated against a reference solution obtained through a standard double inverse transform. The analysis shows that one modal contribution, generated by the frequency-plane deformation and related to the frequency-domain Zenneck pole, exhibits reduced-time invariance and a spatial attenuation consistent with a surface-wave component. Under suitable source and observation conditions, this term can dominate the field over a broad and physically relevant finite late-time interval. At the same time, for the considered damped-sinusoidal excitation, the strict asymptotic tail at fixed distance remains algebraic of order $t^{-5/2}$, with contributions from both the residual continuous spectrum and the modal-pole family. These results provide a rigorous and physically interpretable time-domain manifestation of the frequency-domain Zenneck wave in the pulsed half-space problem.

</details>


### [215] [Crystalline metal flakes: Platforms for advanced plasmonics and hybrid 2D material architectures](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22988)
*Sergejs Boroviks,Siarhei Zavatski,Thorsten Feichtner,Jer-Shing Huang,Olivier J. F. Martin,Bert Hecht,N. Asger Mortensen*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文综述了晶体贵金属薄片（crystalline noble metal flakes）在纳米光子学（nanophotonics）中的关键作用，强调其原子级平坦表面、高结晶度和优异光学质量在等离激元学（plasmonics）、量子光产生和混合光子系统中带来的独特优势，并展望了未来发展前景。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统多晶金属膜因晶界、表面粗糙度和结构无序导致较高的光学损耗，限制了其光子学性能。晶体贵金属薄片凭借其单晶结构（monocrystalline structure）能够显著降低散射并提升性能，因此亟需对其在纳米光子学中的角色与进展进行系统综述。

Method: 本文采用综述（review）方法，系统梳理了晶体贵金属薄片在等离激元学、量子等离激元学（quantum plasmonics）、混合光子架构等领域的应用案例，涵盖聚焦离子束（focused-ion beam, FIB）铣削等精密纳米结构制备技术。

Result: 晶体薄片可作为近红外及更长波段的近乎理想金属镜，其表面粗糙度仅受限于原子台阶（atomic terrace steps）；其明确的{111}晶面可承载Tamm-Shockley表面态，支持二维等离激元（2D plasmons）与体模式共存。

Conclusion: 晶体贵金属薄片在解决纳米光子学中的基础和应用挑战方面具有独特优势，有望推动传感、光电子学以及非经典光产生等前沿领域的发展。

Abstract: Crystalline noble metal flakes are emerging as versatile platforms in nanophotonics, enabling a broad range of optical phenomena and applications. Their atomically flat surfaces, high crystallinity, and superior optical quality open new avenues in advanced plasmonics, quantum light generation, and hybrid photonic systems. In contrast to conventional polycrystalline metal films, which typically suffer from higher optical losses due to grain boundaries, surface roughness, and structural disorder, these monocrystalline flakes provide minimal scattering and enhanced performance. They serve as templates for precise nanostructuring through techniques like focused-ion beam (FIB) milling and are crucial for advanced applications in sensing and optoelectronics. Additionally, they facilitate frontier research in quantum plasmonics, enabling fundamental studies of nonlocal optical effects and the generation of nonclassical light. Furthermore, the well-defined $\{111\}$ facets of these flakes host Tamm--Shockley surface states that support 2D plasmons coexisting with bulk modes. At near-infrared wavelengths and beyond, crystalline flakes act as nearly ideal metallic mirrors, featuring surface roughness limited only to atomic terrace steps, making them highly suitable for integration with 2D materials in hybrid photonic architectures. This review surveys the key roles these flakes play, highlighting recent developments and discussing future prospects while emphasizing their unique benefits in addressing fundamental and applied challenges in modern nanophotonics.

</details>


### [216] [Deterministic Transferable Planar Dielectric Mirrors for Investigating Strong Light-Matter Coupling](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23062)
*Atanu Patra,Subhamoy Sahoo,Johannes Düreth,Simon Betzold,Sven Höfling*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出一种确定性干法转移（deterministic dry-transfer）技术，用于制备由SiO₂/TiO₂布拉格反射镜（Bragg mirror）构成的完整介质微腔，无需后生长剥离工艺，品质因子（Q factor）可达约4×10³。以WS₂单层为活性介质，在室温和低温下均观察到强激子-光子耦合（strong exciton-photon coupling）的明确特征。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统介质微腔中顶部反射镜的沉积工艺（如等离子体增强化学气相沉积或溅射）会损伤嵌入的发光体，尤其对范德华材料（van der Waals materials）中的原子级薄半导体影响严重；同时，常规沉积会覆盖或破坏预制的金属电极，需额外光刻和刻蚀步骤。因此，亟需一种不损伤发光材料且兼容电接触的微腔制备方法。

Method: 开发了一种确定性干法转移方法，利用上下两片SiO₂/TiO₂布拉格反射镜直接组装形成完整的介质微腔，无需任何后生长剥离（lift-off）工艺。以WS₂单层作为有源介质置于腔内。

Result: 所制备微腔的品质因子（Q factor）约为4×10³；在室温和低温下均观测到WS₂单层与腔模之间的强激子-光子耦合（strong exciton-photon coupling）特征。

Conclusion: 该干法转移方法是一种高效、无损的微腔制备途径，能保持层状材料发光体的结构完整性，为下一代集成光子器件（integrated photonic devices）提供了可行的技术方案。

Abstract: Optical cavities play a central role in photonic and quantum technologies by enhancing light-matter interactions. In semiconductor microcavities, achieving high quality (Q) factors typically relies on sophisticated epitaxial growth techniques, such as molecular beam epitaxy, which offer atomic-scale precision but are costly and limited in material compatibility. For dielectric microcavities, high Q factors can be achieved using dielectric Bragg mirrors. However, conventional deposition techniques for the top mirrors, such as plasma-enhanced chemical vapor deposition or sputtering, can damage embedded emitters. This limitation is particularly severe for van der Waals materials, especially atomically thin semiconductors. Moreover, the conventional top-mirror deposition can cover or degrade predefined metal contacts. Recovering electrical access typically requires additional lithography and etching steps. Here, a deterministic dry-transfer approach is developed to fabricate complete dielectric microcavities using both top and bottom SiO_2/TiO_2 Bragg mirrors without post-growth lift-off processes, reaching a Q factor ~ 4x10^3. Using a WS_2 monolayer as the active medium, clear signatures of strong exciton-photon coupling are observed at both room temperature and cryogenic temperatures. These results demonstrate an efficient cavity fabrication approach that preserves the integrity of the emitter of layered materials, enabling next generation integrated photonic devices.

</details>


### [217] [Emergence of dual axion response in condensed matter](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23186)
*Elina Kokurina,Dmitry Vagin,Eduardo Barredo-Alamilla,Maxim A. Gorlach*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文研究了反铁磁多层超构材料（antiferromagnetic multilayered metamaterials）中的非互易磁电效应（nonreciprocal magneto-electric effect），预测其中存在常规轴子响应（axion response）和由磁荷电动力学描述的双重轴子响应（dual axion response）。作者以自旋通过反铁磁交换耦合相互作用的凝聚态模型系统为对象，推导了有效电磁特性，预言了涌现的双重轴子场（emergent dual axion field），并通过数值模拟支持了结论，还提出了候选材料。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 近期理论预测反铁磁多层超构材料中存在两种不同类型的非互易磁电效应（nonreciprocal magneto-electric effect），其中一种可用磁荷电动力学描述的双重轴子响应（dual axion response）来解释。本文旨在通过具体的凝聚态模型系统验证和深化这一理论预言。

Method: 作者构建了一个自旋通过反铁磁交换相互作用（antiferromagnetic exchange interaction）耦合的凝聚态模型系统，并推导了其有效电磁性质（effective electromagnetic properties）。此外，通过数值模拟对理论预测进行验证。

Result: 该模型系统能够产生涌现的双重轴子场（emergent dual axion field）。数值模拟结果支持这一理论预测。

Conclusion: 作者确认了反铁磁系统中双重轴子响应的存在，并提出了可用于实验验证的候选材料（candidate materials），为研究非互易磁电效应提供了新的物理图像和材料平台。

Abstract: Recently, it was predicted that nonreciprocal magneto-electric effect in antiferromagnetic multilayered metamaterials occurs in two distinct versions. One is the conventional axion response, while another one is dual axion response captured by electrodynamics with magnetic charge. Here we investigate a model condensed matter system of spins coupled through antiferromagnetic exchange interaction and derive its effective electromagnetic properties. We predict that this system gives rise to the emergent dual axion field, support our conclusion by numerical simulations and put forward candidate materials.

</details>


### [218] [Non-Hermitian corner skin effect in a two-dimensional photonic crystal](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23209)
*Huyen Thanh Phan,Katsunori Wakabayashi*

  <summary>Details</summary>

Abstract: We numerically study topological effects of electromagnetic (EM) waves
  in a two-dimensional (2D) non-Hermitian photonic crystal (PhC) composed
  of lossy magneto-optical materials. In this system, not only the EM
  wavefunctions but also the complex eigenfrequencies exhibit nontrivial
  topological properties. We demonstrate that the non-Hermitian skin

  emerges at both the edges and corners of truncated structures. This
  phenomenon has no counterpart in Hermitian systems. In addition, we identify non-Hermitian topological edge states
  originating from the nontrivial topology of the bulk bands. While most
  previous studies of non-Hermitian topology have focused on
  tight-binding models, our work addresses a continuous photonic system,
  providing a more realistic platform and offering a concrete route

### [219] [Role of ultrafast electron-optical-phonon interactions in high harmonic generation from graphene](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23294)
*Adam Herling,Ofer Neufeld*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文通过包含静态极限下光学声子（optical phonons）的理论形式，研究石墨烯（graphene）中的高次谐波产生（HHG），发现光学声子通过耦合带间电流并引起谐波相位混乱（harmonic phase scrambling）强烈抑制HHG产额，导致约3 eV以上实验HHG缺失；同时光学声子导致退相位时间T2~5.7 fs、引入温度依赖并平滑椭偏率曲线，且这些效应与时间尺度无关，可推广至阿秒现象。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 固体高次谐波产生中，电子和光子被视为主要参与者，而普遍存在的声子（phonons）因其较长的时间尺度通常被认为可忽略。本文旨在从理论上揭示光学声子在石墨烯HHG中的实际作用，并解释实验中观察到的HHG缺失、退相位时间等未解问题。

Method: 采用包含静态极限下光学声子的理论形式，其中晶格在电子时间尺度上被视为冻结；通过采样热占据声子并进行系综平均（ensemble-averaging）来计算HHG。

Result: (i) 光学声子通过耦合带间电流并引起谐波相位混乱，强烈抑制HHG产额，解释了约3 eV以上缺乏实验HHG的现象；(ii) HHG产额呈现温度依赖性，但因声子能量尺度由零点运动（zero-point motion）主导，该依赖性较弱；(iii) 光学声子以约T2~5.7 fs的速率使带间相干性（interband coherences）退相位，显著快于电子-电子散射，表明热声子主导强场下的电子退相干；(iv) 声子使HHG椭偏率依赖曲线平滑化，与实验更吻合。

Conclusion: 所有效应均与时间尺度无关，源于电子-声子相互作用的静态图像，因此结果可推广至阿秒现象。本研究揭示了HHG中的退相位时间问题及声子在阿秒时间尺度上的作用，对石墨烯中的Floquet能隙、光电流等其他过程具有启示意义。

Abstract: High harmonic generation (HHG) is a widely explored process in solids, where intense lasers drive attosecond-to-femtosecond electron dynamics within bands, causing high-energy emission. While electrons and photons are considered the main players in HHG, solids also host ubiquitous phonons that are typically assumed negligible in HHG due to their longer timescales. We theoretically study HHG in graphene with a formalism including optical phonons in the static limit, where the lattice is frozen on the electronic timescale and HHG is computed by sampling thermally-occupied phonons and ensemble-averaging. We show that in graphene: (i) Optical phonons strongly suppress HHG yields by coupling to interband currents and causing harmonic phase scrambling (destructive interference), explaining the lack of experimental HHG above ~3 eV. (ii) HHG yields become temperature-dependent due to phonon occupations, though in graphene this dependence is weak since phonon energy scales are dominated by zero-point motion. (iii) Optical phonons dephase interband coherences at a rate equivalent to T2~5.7 fs, substantially faster than e-e scattering, suggesting thermal phonons dominate electronic decoherence in strong fields. (iv) Phonons smoothen HHG ellipticity-dependent curves, yielding better agreement with experiments. Remarkably, all effects are timescale-independent, arising in the static picture of electron-phonon interactions, making results transferable to attosecond phenomena. Our results shed light on the dephasing time problem in HHG and the role of phonons on attosecond timescales, with implications for other systems and processes such as Floquet gaps and photocurrents in graphene.

</details>


### [220] [Stark-tunable O-band single-photon sources based on deterministically fabricated quantum dot--circular Bragg gratings on silicon](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23422)
*Sarthak Tripathi,Kartik Gaur,Priyabrata Mudi,Peter Ludewig,Alexander Kosarev,Kerstin Volz,Imad Limame,Stephan Reitzenstein*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文展示了一种直接在硅上生长的InGaAs量子点（quantum dots）与电接触环形布拉格光栅（electrically contacted circular Bragg grating, eCBG）谐振器集成的器件，实现了电信O波段的高亮度单光子发射，兼具宽范围电调谐能力、高单光子纯度和液氮温度（77 K）下的稳健反聚束效应，为可扩展的硅基光子量子网络提供了实用化平台。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 半导体量子点具有优异的量子光学特性，但如何在单个平台上同时实现宽范围电可调谐、高效光子提取、高温运行、硅单片集成以及电信波长兼容性，仍是量子信息技术的重大挑战。本文旨在通过硅基集成方案解决上述多重约束。

Method: 采用直接在硅衬底上生长的InGaAs量子点，并结合电接触环形布拉格光栅（eCBG）谐振器结构。器件制造采用确定性电子束光刻（deterministic electron-beam lithography）和基于脊状结构的垂直p-i-n二极管架构，从而实现精确的器件集成和对单个发射体的电学控制。

Conclusion: 该工作建立了一种硅兼容、电寻址的电信O波段量子光源平台，兼具宽光谱调谐性、高单光子纯度和高温运行能力，为构建实用化的可扩展光子量子网络提供了可实现的规模化路径。

Abstract: Semiconductor quantum dots (QDs) offer outstanding quantum-optical properties, making them highly attractive for quantum information technologies. However, combining wide-range electrical tunability, efficient photon extraction, elevated-temperature operation, monolithic silicon integration, and telecom-wavelength compatibility remains a major challenge. Here, we demonstrate electrically contacted circular Bragg grating (eCBG) resonators incorporating InGaAs QDs directly grown on silicon, enabling bright single-photon emission in the telecom O-band. Deterministic electron-beam lithography and a ridge-based vertical p--i--n diode architecture enable precise device integration and electrical control of individual emitters. The QD--eCBGs exhibit a quantum-confined Stark shift of approximately 16 nm (11 meV) at 4 K, representing a record for QDs embedded in nanophotonic structures at telecom wavelengths. This is achieved alongside a photon extraction efficiency of $(21.7 \pm 3.0)\%$ into the first lens, while maintaining excellent radiative properties and high single-photon purity, with $g^{(2)}(0)=0.0078 \pm 0.0012$ below saturation and $g^{(2)}(0)=0.0183 \pm 0.0021$ at saturation under pulsed excitation. Robust antibunching persists up to 77 K, with $g^{(2)}(0)=0.0663 \pm 0.0056$, enabling operation with liquid-nitrogen or compact Stirling cryocoolers. Furthermore, spatially separated QD--eCBGs can be electrically tuned into spectral resonance without degrading photon statistics. These results establish a silicon-compatible, electrically addressable telecom O-band quantum light platform combining wide spectral tunability, high single-photon purity, and elevated-temperature operation, providing a scalable route toward practical photonic quantum networks.

### [221] [Ultrafast spectroscopy and role of interlayer coupling in high harmonic generation from layered solids](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23506)
*Eyal Uzner,Ofer Neufeld*

Main category: physics.optics

TL;DR: 本文提出了层状固体中层间耦合存在下的高次谐波产生（high harmonic generation, HHG）理论，分析了六方氮化硼、石墨和过渡金属二硫化物WS₂中的强场驱动过程。研究表明，即使驱动激光为面内偏振，足够强的层间耦合也会改变HHG发射特性（如角度或椭圆率依赖）。基于微扰理论推导出HHG产额遵循四阶多项式形式，并通过数值验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 层状固体中的高次谐波产生（HHG）研究通常仅考虑面内电子动力学，忽略了普遍存在的层间跃迁（interlayer hopping）效应。本文旨在填补这一空白，发展包含层间耦合的HHG理论，并探究其如何影响HHG发射特性。

Method: 采用解析微扰理论（perturbation theory），将激光驱动电流按层间耦合参数展开，推导HHG产额的解析形式；同时结合数值计算对六方氮化硼（hexagonal BN）、石墨（graphite）和过渡金属二硫化物WS₂进行验证。

Result: 足够强的层间耦合会改变HHG发射的典型特征，如角度或椭圆率依赖（ellipticity dependence），即便驱动激光偏振方向严格位于层内。HHG产额在微扰展开下呈现四阶多项式形式，这一解析结果得到数值验证。

Conclusion: 本研究为通过HHG光谱学（HHG spectroscopy）探测层间耦合提供了理论依据，并指出层间耦合的调制可作为控制超快动力学和阿秒脉冲产生（attopulse generation）的参数，结合激光驱动与机械应变实现调控。

Abstract: High harmonic generation (HHG) in solids has recently emerged as a powerful all-optical approach for probing material properties and ultrafast electron dynamics in quantum systems. It has been widely applied for studying two-dimensional and layered solids of various kinds. In these studies, the laser is usually polarized within the layered planes, where most electron dynamics occurs, while out-of-plane hopping is commonly neglected. This is despite of interlayer hopping being ubiquitous in nano-systems. Here we develop theory for HHG in layered solids in presence of interlayer coupling and employ it for studying strong-field driven hexagonal BN, graphite, and the transition metal dichalcogenide WS$_2$. We show that sufficiently intense couplings can alter typical HHG emission characteristics such as angular or ellipticity dependence even when the driving laser is polarized in-plane. We develop an analytic perturbation theory for the laser-driven current expanded in the interlayer coupling parameter and explicitly show that HHG yields follow a 4'th order polynomial form, which is validated numerically. Our work should motivate experiments for probing interlayer coupling via HHG spectroscopy, as well as exploring its modulation as a control parameter for ultrafast dynamics and attopulse generation via laser driving and mechanical strain.

### [222] [Comparative analysis of nonlinear elastic moduli of polystyrene, polycarbonate and PMMA](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23244)
*A. V. Belashov,A. A. Zhikhoreva,Y. M. Beltukov,I. V. Semenova*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文通过声弹性效应（acousto-elastic effect）测量方法，在0.45–3 MHz频率范围内系统比较了聚苯乙烯（PS）、聚甲基丙烯酸甲酯（PMMA）和聚碳酸酯（PC）三种聚合物的线性和非线性弹性模量的频率依赖性，发现线性模量随频率适度上升，非线性Murnaghan模量在低频段快速变化、高频段趋于稳定，并讨论了差异性来源。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有研究缺乏对聚合物材料在超声频段下线性（Lamé）与非线性（Murnaghan）弹性模量频率依赖性的系统实验对比，尤其是针对不同高分子材料的差异性分析。

Method: 基于声弹性效应（acousto-elastic effect）的测量方法，在0.45–3 MHz频率范围内，对聚苯乙烯、PMMA和聚碳酸酯的块状样品进行线性Lamé模量（λ, μ）和非线性Murnaghan模量（l, m, n）的频率依赖性测量。

Result: 三种聚合物的线性Lamé模量均随频率适度上升，其中PMMA的λ模量增幅最显著（约35%）。Murnaghan模量表现出显著的非线性频率依赖性：高于~1 MHz时模量变化不显著；低频段l和m的绝对值快速上升（l更显著），而n的绝对值下降并趋于正值。PMMA的线性和非线性模量均高于PC和PS，后两者数值接近。

Conclusion: 三种聚合物在线性与非线性弹性模量的频率依赖性上存在显著差异，PMMA表现出最高的模量数值和最大的频率敏感性，PC和PS的模量行为较为接近；研究对聚合物非线性弹性差异的潜在成因进行了讨论。

Abstract: We present the comparative experimental analysis of frequency dependencies of linear (Lamé) and nonlinear (Murnaghan) elastic moduli of polystyrene, PMMA and polycarbonate. The measurement methodology, based on the acousto-elastic effect, provided data on variations of these moduli in block samples of the polymers in the frequency range of 0.45-3 MHz. In all the three polymers the linear Lamé moduli demonstrated moderate rise with frequency, most pronounced rise was observed in modulus $λ$ of PMMA in about 35%. The frequency dependencies of Murnaghan moduli were considerably nonlinear. At higher frequencies above ~1 MHz no significant variations of the Murnaghan moduli occurred, while at lower frequencies the absolute values of the moduli $l$ and $m$ demonstrated rapid rise, more pronounced for the modulus $l$. At the same time the absolute values of the modulus $n$ decreased and demonstrated a tendency to become positive at lower frequencies. Both linear and nonlinear moduli of PMMA had higher values than those of PC and PS, with the latter two demonstrating close values of both types of moduli. The potential origins of the differences in nonlinear elastic properties of the three polymers are discussed.

### [223] [Cosolvency response in polymer brushes](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23521)
*Huaisong Yong,Binyu Zhao*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文提出了首个解析理论（analytic theory），以优雅的封闭形式解析解（closed-form analytical solutions）探索聚合物刷（polymer brushes）中的共溶剂效应（cosolvency effect）。该理论揭示了优先溶剂化（preferential solvation）诱导的有效排斥力，预测了不连续溶胀转变和再塌缩转变（re-collapse transition），并确定了共溶剂效应发生所需的优先溶剂化最小强度及排斥耦合条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 共溶剂效应是设计刺激响应性智能材料（stimulus-responsive smart materials）的关键，但此前缺乏针对聚合物刷的解析理论（analytic theory）研究。

Method: 采用最小自由能模型（minimal free-energy model），通过引入浓度依赖的χ函数（concentration-dependent χ-function）描述聚合物链的平衡溶剂化（equilibrium solvation），并推导出封闭形式解析解。

Result: 模型预测了随共溶剂浓度增加的不连续溶胀转变及后续的再塌缩转变（re-collapse transition）；对于低密度聚合物刷，推导出解析近似并绘制了发生不连续转变的参数空间相图（phase diagram）。

Conclusion: 共溶剂与溶剂在本体中的排斥相互作用并非必要条件；优先溶剂化（preferential solvation）及其诱导的排斥耦合需达到最小强度才能实现共溶剂效应。该工作为基于聚合物刷共溶剂效应的智能刺激响应材料提供了理性设计基础。

Abstract: We present the first analytic theory with elegant and closed-form analytical solutions to explore the cosolvency effect in polymer brushes, where polymer chains that are poorly soluble in two pure solvents become fully soluble in certain mixtures thereof. This effect is key to designing stimulus-responsive smart materials but has not previously been addressed by analytic theory for polymer brushes. Our theoretical framework reveals that preferential adsorption of cosolvent induces an effective repulsion between monomers solvated by cosolvent and those solvated by solvent. The equilibrium solvation of polymer chains by cosolvent gives rise to a concentration-dependent $χ$-function, which captures the effective interactions within the brush and reproduces the reentrant behavior characteristic of the cosolvency effect. The model predicts a discontinuous soluble transition followed by a re-collapse transition at higher cosolvent concentrations. Analytical treatment within a minimal free-energy model for the case of two symmetric poor solvents shows that the swelling and re-collapse transitions share the same thermodynamic origin. For low-density brushes, we derive an analytical approximation and delineate the phase diagram of parameter space in which discontinuous transitions occur. For cosolvency to take place, the theory specifies a minimum strength for preferential solvation and the associated repulsive coupling. Furthermore, it demonstrates that, contrary to previous models, repulsive interactions between cosolvent and solvent in the bulk are not required. This work lays the groundwork for the rational design of smart stimulus-responsive materials based on the cosolvency effect in polymer brushes, a capability which was not previously established.

</details>


### [224] [Constitutive relations for colloidal gel](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23642)
*Saikat Roy,Yezaz Ahmed Gadi Man*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文指出传统连续介质理论（continuum theories）在处理耗散凝胶（depletion gels）时基于无应力参考态和仿射变形（affine deformation）的假设不成立，并提出基于有应力参考态展开的简化本构关系（constitutive relations），通过大规模数值模拟验证了其鲁棒性。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 传统连续介质理论用于耗散凝胶时，依赖无应力参考态（stress-free reference state）和仿射变形这两个与无序凝胶材料（amorphous gel materials）实际情况不符的前提假设。凝胶从未真正到达势能面（potential energy landscape）的全局最小值，内部存在局部压应力、拉应力和零应力区交替分布，因此需要修正理论框架。

Method: 提出在存在应力的参考态（stressed reference state）附近展开自由能（free energy），引入谐波展开（harmonic expansion）中产生的标量项；通过大规模数值模拟（large-scale numerical simulations），在广泛的参数空间（parameter space）内分别对耗散凝胶和摩擦凝胶（frictional gels）进行验证。

Result: 传统连续介质理论在凝胶材料中具有局限性；所提出的简化本构关系能更好地捕捉凝胶材料的力学响应（mechanical response）；在涵盖耗散凝胶与摩擦凝胶的广泛参数空间下，该关系的鲁棒性（robustness）得到了数值模拟的充分支持。

Conclusion: 以有应力参考态为基础的本构关系更能反映凝胶材料实际的力学行为，为无序软物质体系的理论建模提供了更准确的方向。

Abstract: The theoretical treatment of depletion gels with central interactions often involves expanding the free energy around a stress-free reference state to derive a constitutive relation between global stress and strain. The premise upon which the previous continuum theories are based, i.e., the stress-free reference state and the affine deformation, both of which do not hold in the context of amorphous gel materials. Gels never reach a true global minimum in the potential energy landscape and contain local regions of significant compressive and tensile stress, interspersed with zero-stress regions. Hence, expansion of free energy around a stressed reference state will produce scalar terms in harmonic expansion, the effects of which are qualitatively different from the terms appearing in the expansion around an unstressed reference state. In this study, we demonstrate the limitations of traditional continuum theories and propose simple constitutive relations that better capture the mechanical response of gel materials. The robustness of the proposed relations is established through large-scale numerical simulations of depletion and frictional gels across a vast parameter space.

</details>


### [225] [Ostwald ripening controlled by diffusion of a sparingly soluble component](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23850)
*Alexey Kabalnov*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文在前期模型基础上，重新审视并拓展了关于难溶性添加剂抑制奥斯特瓦尔德熟化（Ostwald ripening）的模型。研究发现在准稳态下，熟化过程受难溶性组分扩散控制，可沿用经典LSW理论框架；当添加剂浓度较高时，粒径分布和熟化速率遵循经典LSW模式；当浓度较低时，粒径分布呈双峰分布，不再符合LSW规律。此外，本文推导了改进的熟化速率外推方程，并讨论了实际乳液稳定化策略。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 难溶性添加剂能够减缓或完全抑制分散体系中的奥斯特瓦尔德熟化，但其具体调控机制尚需深入建模与拓展。本文旨在重新审视和扩展作者前期的稳定化模型，以更全面地描述添加剂浓度、摩尔体积差异以及溶液非理想性对熟化行为的影响。

Method: 采用准稳态（quasi-steady-state）假设，通过难溶性组分的扩散控制机制，将经典LSW理论框架直接应用于该问题。通过推导改进的外推方程，考虑两组分的摩尔体积差异和溶液非理想性；并引入锁定参数（lock-in parameter）L1来刻画不同熟化模式之间的转变。

Result: 当添加剂（难溶性组分）浓度较高时，粒径分布与经典LSW理论的分布函数一致，熟化速率遵循经典立方定律（cubic law）。当添加剂浓度较低时，动力学不再遵循LSW模式，粒径分布呈现双峰分布（bimodal distribution）：细小颗粒富含难溶性组分，大颗粒则如同无添加剂时一样熟化。锁定参数L1可用于表征这两种模式之间的转变。

Conclusion: 本文所提出的扩展模型覆盖了全配方范围，能够解释不同添加剂浓度下的奥斯特瓦尔德熟化行为转变。改进的外推方程更具普适性。最后，论文探讨了针对乳液体系的实际稳定化方法。

Abstract: Additives of sparingly soluble components are known to slow down or completely inhibit Ostwald ripening in dispersed systems. In this paper, our earlier model of stabilization against Ostwald ripening is revisited and extended. In a quasi-steady-state mode, the process is shown to be controlled by the diffusion of the less soluble component, and the whole machinery of the classical Lifshits-Slezov-Wagner (LSW) theory can be leveraged almost without any change. The particle size distribution is predicted to follow the same distribution function pattern as in the classic LSW theory. The rate of ripening follows the classic cubic law. To extend our earlier result, an improved extrapolatory equation for the ripening rate is derived, that covers the whole formulation range, accounts for the difference in molar volumes of the components and for the solution non-ideality. The behavior described above is observed over the range of high concentrations of the poorly soluble component, with the cutoff determined by the lock-in number described in the previous paper of this series. When the concentration of the additive is low, the kinetics no longer follows the LSW pattern; instead, the particle size distribution becomes bimodal, with the fraction of 'fines' enriched by the poorly soluble component and the fraction of the large particles to ripen as if no additive were present. The lock-in parameter L1 can be used to characterize for the transition from one mode to another. In the end, some practical stabilization approaches for emulsions are discussed.

</details>


### [226] [Quenched Dipole Pairs in Viscous Fluid Membranes across the Saffman Crossover: Integrable Hamiltonian Dynamics](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23868)
*Satyagni Bhattacharya,Debdatta Dey,Samyak Jain,Yassir Khan,Tirthankar Mazumder,Aryaman Mihir Seth,Nikhil Mogalapalli,Divyansh Tiwari,Pravallika Vemparala,Rickmoy Samanta*

Main category: cond-mat.soft

TL;DR: 本文研究了黏性膜中力偶极子（force-dipole）流体动力学（hydrodynamics）在Saffman交叉（crossover）下的相空间重组，发现近场一维可积动力学到远场二维可积动力学的转变，并揭示拉拽型（pullers）偶极子具有普适的晚期塌缩标度律 \(R\sim (t_c-t)^{1/3}\)。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究黏性膜中取向固定的力偶极子（quenched dipoles）在Saffman交叉下的双偶极子相互作用重组机制，特别是在近场与远场之间动力学维度和可积性（integrability）的变化。

Method: 采用解析理论（analytic theory）分析耦合于无穷大流体的黏性膜中的力偶极子流体动力学，分别对近场和远场进行可积性分析和动力学方程的精确求解。

Result: 近场中两个固定取向偶极子的动力学是精确可解的且有效一维，具有固定的质心连线（line of centers）和分离平方的线性演化。远场保持可积但变为二维，具有耦合的径向-角向动力学和精确的第一积分（first integral）。对于拉拽型偶极子，角向动力学驱动系统趋向吸引流形（attracting manifold），导致晚期塌缩标度律 \(R\sim (t_c-t)^{1/3}\)，不同于近场的 \(R\sim (t_c-t)^{1/2}\)。

Conclusion: Saffman交叉重组了偶极相互作用的哈密顿相空间结构（Hamiltonian phase-space structure），产生从有效一维到完全耦合动力学的转变，为黏性流体膜中的聚集（aggregation）提供了最小理论框架。

Abstract: We investigate an analytic theory of force-dipole hydrodynamics in a viscous membrane coupled to an infinite surrounding fluid, focusing on quenched (orientation-fixed) dipoles. While the single-dipole flow exhibits the known Saffman crossover from a near-field \(v\sim r^{-1}\) to a screened far-field \(v\sim r^{-2}\), we show that this crossover induces a qualitatively new reorganization of dipole--dipole interactions. For two identical quenched dipoles, the near-field dynamics is exactly solvable and effectively one-dimensional, with a fixed line of centers and linear evolution of the squared separation. In the far field, the system remains integrable but becomes intrinsically two-dimensional, with coupled radial and angular dynamics and an exact first integral. For pullers, the angular dynamics drives alignment toward an attracting manifold, leading to universal late-time collapse \(R\sim (t_c-t)^{1/3}\), in contrast to the near-field scaling \(R\sim (t_c-t)^{1/2}\). The Saffman crossover thus reorganizes the Hamiltonian phase-space structure of dipolar interactions and produces a transition from effectively one-dimensional to fully coupled dynamics, providing a minimal framework for aggregation in viscous fluid membranes.

</details>

Our analysis reveals that these states emerge from a generic interplay between local nematic alignment and curvature-driven active currents. These results identify a robust route to boundary-induced structure formation in active matter and provide experimentally testable predictions.

Like human fingerprint, the trajectory is the identity of the motion containing fundamental dynamical information. Such irregular trajectories randomly inter-wind and twist to each other to produce a complicated turmoil configuration in which so far the unrealized mechanism of motion is hidden. Nowadays, the analytical method for this fingerprint trajectory is still missed. Here we develop a practicable method to decipher complicated trajectory configuration, which uncovers abundant dynamical information hiding in irregular trajectories, revealing the remarkable evolution of spatial-temporal micro-structure, thus leading to the novel systematic study of the dynamics of biological and soft matter.

### [229] [Shear-driven mixing of segregated granular materials](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24702)
*Hugo N. Ulloa,Tomás Trewhela*

<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 尽管颗粒流动与偏析建模已取得显著进展，但颗粒混合（granular mixing）——作为偏析（segregation）的自然对应过程——的物理机制尚未得到充分研究。本文旨在探究剪切驱动下初始偏析颗粒体系的混合动力学，明确控制颗粒在剪切流中偏析与混合程度及速率的因素。

Method: 采用理论分析（theoretical analysis）与数值实验（numerical experiments）相结合的方法，开发并验证了一个用于量化混合动力学的标度框架（scaling framework）。

Abstract: As granular materials flow and settle, interactions among particles of different sizes or properties drive mixing and segregation, producing rich dynamics that reshape systems ranging from industrial hoppers to planetary surfaces. A hallmark of such polydisperse flows is shear-driven size segregation, whereby particles rearrange so that larger grains migrate above smaller ones. Despite substantial progress in modelling granular flow and segregation, key questions concerning the underlying mechanisms remain unresolved. In particular, the physics of granular mixing -- the natural counterpart of segregation -- has received far less attention. Here, we investigate the dynamics of initially segregated granular materials driven out of equilibrium by external shear. We ask: what controls the extent and rate of segregation and mixing in a sheared granular flow? Answering this question is essential for understanding how external forcing disrupts stable and unstable particle configurations and for optimising processes that require controlled mixing. Using theoretical analysis and numerical experiments, we develop and validate a scaling framework that quantifies the mixing dynamics. Our results provide new insight into the physics of granular flows and lay the foundation for improved prediction and design in both natural and industrial settings.

### [230] [Electric potential of insulated conducting objects in presence of electric charges -- some exact and approximate results](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.22908)
*Karlo Filipan,Hrvoje Štefančić*

Main category: physics.class-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种新的 $J$ 形式主义（$J$ formalism），用于精确或近似求解绝缘导体的电势问题，无需计算表面电荷分布或周围空间的电势，并利用 Robin Hood 方法进行了数值验证。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 绝缘导体（insulated conducting object）的电势确定在理论和实践上都是一个重要问题，现有方法通常需要计算表面电荷分布或周围空间电势，过程复杂。

Method: 引入一种新的 $J$ 形式主义（$J$ formalism）重新表述电势确定问题；对于球形物体可精确计算，对于其他几何形状则利用绝缘导体的几何性质进行高效近似；数值性能通过 Robin Hood 方法（Robin Hood method）进行检验。

Result: $J$ 形式主义无需计算物体表面的表面电荷分布（surface charge distribution），也无需计算周围空间的电势；数值实验验证了该方法的性能。

Conclusion: 该方法可推广应用于导体电容（capacitance）的计算，具有潜在的实际应用价值。

Abstract: Determination of the electric potential of insulated conducting objects is an important problem both theoretically and practically. For an insulated conducting object in the presence of external charges or charges distributed on the object surface, the problem of potential determination is reformulated using a newly introduced $J$ formalism. Using the $J$ formalism, it is shown how the electric potential can be calculated exactly for spherical objects and efficiently approximated for other object geometries using geometrical properties of the insulated conducting object. This approach does not require calculation of the surface charge distribution at the object surface of the calculation of the electric potential in the surrounding space. Properties and the performance of the approach are investigated numerically using the Robin Hood method. Possible applications of the approach based on the $J$ formalism are outlined for calculation of capacitance of conducting objects.

### [231] [Universal tracer statistics in single-file transport](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24741)
*Soumyabrata Saha,Jitendra Kethepalli,Benjamin Guiselin,Jacopo De Nardis,Tridib Sadhu*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文揭示了一维硬棒气体（hard-rod gas）在随机（扩散型）和幺正（弹道型）两种截然不同的微观动力学下，其大尺度长时间统计行为中涌现的普适性：多个示踪粒子（tracer）的单时间联合分布呈现相同的非高斯涨落，仅差一个简单的动力学标度。该普适性在退火系综（annealed ensemble）和淬火系综（quenched ensemble）中都成立，差异仅体现在多时间统计中。结论基于精确微观解、涨落流体力学（fluctuating hydrodynamics）以及稀有事件模拟。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究一维硬棒气体在随机（扩散型）与幺正（弹道型）两种根本不同的微观动力学下，大尺度长时间统计行为中是否存在普适性，以及初始状态记忆如何影响涨落统计。

Method: 使用精确微观解法（exact microscopic solutions）分别求解两种动力学系统；针对弹道情形在退火系综中独立采用涨落流体力学分析；同时进行稀有事件模拟（rare-event simulations）来采样非典型涨落。

Result: 两种动力学下多个示踪粒子的单时间联合分布表现出相同的非高斯涨落，仅差一个简单的动力学标度；该普适性在退火和淬火系综中都成立，表明初始状态存在持久记忆；差异仅在多时间统计中于大尺度显现；类似现象也存在于电流涨落中。

Conclusion: 一维硬棒气体在随机和幺正两种微观动力学下，其大尺度统计行为存在显著的普适性，超出了传统动力学普适类的预期；初始状态的记忆效应在长时间统计中持续存在，而动力学差异仅通过多时间统计才能区分。

Abstract: We uncover an emergent universality in the large-scale, long-time statistics of a one-dimensional hard-rod gas evolving under two fundamentally different classes of microscopic dynamics: stochastic (diffusive) and unitary (ballistic). Remarkably, despite the difference of the two systems, the one-time joint distribution of the positions of multiple tracers exhibits identical non-Gaussian fluctuations, up to a simple dynamical scaling. This universality holds in both annealed and quenched ensembles, demonstrating a persistent memory of the initial state. Differences between the dynamics manifest at large scales only in multi-time statistics. Our conclusions are based on explicit large-deviation results for the one-time statistics of tracer pairs and the two-time statistics of a single tracer. Similar physics extends to current fluctuations, demonstrated explicitly in the quenched ensemble. We obtain these results from exact microscopic solutions for both dynamics and, independently, from fluctuating hydrodynamics in the ballistic case in the annealed ensemble. Our rare-event simulations further corroborate these findings and provide a novel demonstration of sampling atypical fluctuations in both types of hard-rod gas.

</details>


### [232] [Bayesian phase transition for the critical Ising model: Enlarged replica symmetry in the epsilon expansion and in 2D](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.23346)
*Kay Joerg Wiese,Alapan Das,Adam Nahum*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过复制场论（replica field theory）与数值模拟，研究临界伊辛模型（critical Ising model）中测量过程进入强测量相（strong-measurement phase）的相变，揭示了关联函数的多标度（multiscaling）行为以及复制描述中扩大的对称性（enlarged symmetry），该对称性可确定爱德华兹-安德森关联函数（Edwards-Anderson correlator）的精确指数。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 探究测量精度如何影响临界伊辛模型中测量过程的“测量相”（measurement phases），特别是进入强测量相的相变行为及其普适性质。

Method: 采用复制场论方法，在六维附近开展ε展开（epsilon expansion），并结合二维（two dimensions）下的数值模拟（numerical simulations）进行交叉验证；同时拓展了ε展开至具有幂律相互作用（power-law interactions）和/或长程测量（long-range measurement）的模型。

Result: 在临界点处观察到关联函数的多标度（multiscaling）行为，并发现复制描述中存在扩大的对称性（enlarged symmetry）；该对称性在微观层面上仅对特定测量协议成立，但在红外极限下可一般性地涌现；该对称性决定了爱德华兹-安德森关联函数（Edwards-Anderson correlator）的指数精确值，在二维和近上临界维度（upper critical dimension）均适用。

Conclusion: 该发现是伊辛自旋玻璃（Ising spin glass）中Nishimori现象（Nishimori phenomenon）在另一种复制极限下的类比，表明扩大的对称性在测量相变中具有关键且普适的作用。

Abstract: A process that images or measures bond energies in the critical Ising model can be in distinct measurement ``phases'', depending on the precision of measurement. We study the transition into the strong-measurement phase using replica field theory (an epsilon expansion around six dimensions) and numerical simulations in two dimensions. The results reveal multiscaling of correlation functions at the critical point, and a striking enlarged symmetry of the replica description. This is an analog of the Nishimori phenomenon in the Ising spin glass, in a distinct replica limit. The enlarged symmetry is present microscopically for certain measurement protocols, but more generally can emerge in the infrared, and it fixes the exact value of the exponent for the Edwards-Anderson correlator both in 2D and near the upper critical dimension. We also examine the epsilon expansion for models with power-law interactions and/or long-range measurement.

### [233] [Conformal Invariance of the large-$N$ limit of the $O(N)$ universality class](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24675)
*Santiago Cabrera,Gonzalo De Polsi,Adam Rançon,Nicolás Wschebor*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文在非微扰重整化群（non-perturbative renormalization group）框架下，对 O(N) 普适类（universality class）在大 N 极限下的共形对称性（conformal symmetry）给出了两种证明，揭示了理论结构如何实现共形对称性，并阐明了理论具有共形不变性（conformal invariance）的一般性条件。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 共形对称性被预期在临界点（criticality）处的平衡统计力学（equilibrium statistical mechanics）系统中实现，但在三维情形下证据稀少且仅存在于特定案例。本文旨在填补这一空白，为大 N 极限下的 O(N) 普适类提供严格证明。

Method: 在非微扰重整化群（non-perturbative renormalization group）框架内，给出了两种证明：一种为泛函（functional）证明，另一种为傅里叶空间（Fourier space）中逐顶点（vertex-by-vertex）的证明。

Result: 给出了 O(N) 普适类在大 N 极限下共形对称性的两种严格证明；揭示了理论为达成共形对称性所需的结构特征；从一般性角度阐明了理论具备共形不变性（conformal invariance）的预期条件。

Conclusion: 共形对称性在三维临界统计力学系统中虽然微妙，但通过非微扰重整化群方法可在 O(N) 普适类的大 N 极限下得到严格证明；该结论为进一步理解共形不变性的一般性条件提供了启示。

Abstract: Conformal symmetry is expected to be realized in many equilibrium statistical mechanical systems at criticality. Although this is certainly true in two-dimensional systems, the three-dimensional case is subtler, and only a few proofs exist, only so in very specific cases. In this work, we give two proofs for the large $N$ limit of the $O(N)$ universality class within the non-perturbative renormalization group framework: one functional, and one vertex-by-vertex in Fourier space. While doing so, we unveil how the theory is structured in order for conformal symmetry to be realized. As a consequence, we shed light on what to expect, on rather general grounds, for a theory to be conformally invariant.

</details>


### [234] [Beyond average: heterogeneous first-passage dynamics in many-particle systems with resetting](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24406)
*Juhee Lee,Seong-Gyu Yang,Ludvig Lizana*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文研究随机重置（stochastic resetting）如何影响多相互作用粒子体系中的首通过程（first-passage processes），发现集体重置会导致到达时间分布出现重尾和宽平台，平均到达时间随重置率增大而发散，且系统缺乏单一特征时间尺度。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 随机重置在单粒子动力学中已有较好理解，但其对多粒子集体行为的影响仍不明确。作者受人工选择（artificial selection）和回避（avoidance）问题的启发，旨在探究将幸存粒子重置到最极端粒子位置的协议如何改变多粒子系统的首通行为。

Method: 采用限制势（confining potential）中扩散粒子并带有吸收边界（absorbing boundary）的随机模拟（stochastic simulation），考察两种到达定义：第一个粒子到达边界的时间以及半数粒子到达边界的时间。协议为将所有幸存粒子重置到最极端粒子的位置。

Result: 重置导致到达时间分布出现重尾（heavy tails）和跨越多个数量级的宽平台（extended plateaus）。平均到达时间随重置率增大而增长，并在超过某个阈值后发散。轨迹层面分析显示强异质性（strong heterogeneity），表现为极短和极长的吸收时间并存。

Conclusion: 集体重置系统缺乏单一特征时间尺度，到达的定义（如首个粒子到达 vs 半数粒子到达）对理解和控制此类系统至关重要。

Abstract: We study how stochastic resetting affects first-passage processes in systems of many interacting particles. While resetting is well understood for single-particle dynamics, its consequences for collective behavior remain less clear. We consider a protocol in which all surviving particles are reset to the position of the most extreme one, motivated by problems in artificial selection and avoidance. Using stochastic simulations of particles diffusing in a confining potential with an absorbing boundary, we examine two notions of arrival: when the first particle reaches the boundary and the point at which half of the particles do. We find that resetting produces broad distributions of arrival times with heavy tails and extended plateaus that span several orders of magnitude. As the resetting rate increases, the mean arrival time grows and diverges beyond a threshold. Trajectory-level analysis also reveals strong heterogeneity, with very short and very long absorption times. These results show that collective resetting lacks a single characteristic time scale and that the definition of arrival is crucial for understanding and controlling such systems.

### [235] [Thermodynamic Parametrisation of the Vertebrate Lifetime Cycle Invariant: Biological Proper Time, Allometric Mass-Cancellation, and Clade-Specific Predictions](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24458)
*Mesfin Taye*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文提出生物时间等价原理（Principle of Biological Time Equivalence, PBTE），认为恒温脊椎动物一生约10^9次心跳周期的经验规律源自守恒的热力学熵预算，通过将熵产率与生理频率关联，在无自由参数条件下重现了该数值，并解释了不同类群间的系统偏差。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: Lindstedt与Calder发现恒温脊椎动物一生心跳周期总数约为10^9次，该经验规律缺乏物理解释。本文旨在为这一生物学时间尺度的普适性提供热力学（thermodynamics）基础。

Method: 提出生物时间等价原理（PBTE），以本构闭合关系$\dotΣ = σ_0 f$将熵产率（entropy production rate）与内在生理频率关联，积分得$Σ_{\mathrm{life}} = σ_0 \Nstar$。利用Kleiber标度律（$\propto M^{3/4}$）与Calder标度律进行代数指数约化，得到$\sigstar \propto M^{3/4+1/4-1}=M^0$，实现质量无关性。引入乘性修正因子$Φ_C$，纳入活动分配、体温、线粒体效率和外部风险等生理决定因素。

Result: 在无自由参数条件下再现了数值$N_0 \approx 1.52\times10^9$，与经验观测吻合。PBTE框架同时解释了为何不同类群存在系统偏差，修正因子$Φ_C$将长寿类群预测为每心跳周期有效熵产降低的区域。

Conclusion: 该工作为恒温脊椎动物一生心跳周期数不变性提供了热力学一致的解释，标志着生物时间度量可还原为热力学熵预算（thermodynamic entropy budget）约束，并为理解不同类群寿命差异提供了定量预测框架。

Abstract: Warm-blooded vertebrates accumulate approximately $\Nstar \approx 10^9$ cardiac cycles over a natural lifetime, a striking empirical regularity first quantified by Lindstedt and Calder yet lacking a physical interpretation. We propose that this invariance is consistent with a conserved thermodynamic budget, formulated here as the Principle of Biological Time Equivalence (PBTE). The framework rests on a constitutive closure $\dotΣ = σ_0 f$, which links the entropy production rate to the intrinsic physiological frequency; integration over the lifespan yields $Σ_{\mathrm{life}} = σ_0 \Nstar$, so that the observed constancy of $\Nstar$ corresponds to an approximately constant lifetime entropy budget. Algebraic exponent cancellation under Kleiber and Calder scaling laws, $\sigstar \propto M^{3/4+1/4-1}=M^0$, is consistent with mass-independence and reproduces the numerical value $N_0 \approx 1.52\times10^9$ without free parameters. The framework offers a thermodynamically consistent account of two outstanding problems: the origin of the numerical value of $\Nstar$ and the systematic deviations observed across clades. A multiplicative correction factor $Φ_C$, constructed from physiological determinants -- activity allocation, body temperature, mitochondrial efficiency, and extrinsic hazard -- predicts long-lived clades as regimes of reduced effective entropy production per cardiac cycle.

### [236] [Energetics of stochastic limit-cycle oscillators: when does coupling reduce dissipation?](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24553)
*Anton F. Burnet,Vansh Kharbanda,David Tobias,Benedikt Sabass*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文通过一个可解析求解的随机圆形极限环模型，研究了非线性振子（non-linear oscillator）在噪声环境下的稳态熵产生率（steady-state entropy production rate, EPR），分析了径向、相位（Kuramoto型）和笛卡尔耦合（Cartesian coupling）对能量耗散的影响，发现笛卡尔耦合在所有情况下均能降低系统的EPR。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 非线性振子在生物系统中（如内耳和神经网络）具有重要功能，其在噪声环境中维持振荡需要持续的能量耗散。理解不同耦合方式如何影响能量耗散，有助于揭示生物系统中能量利用与信号处理之间的基本关系。

Method: 构建了一个理想化的随机圆形极限环（stochastic circular limit cycle）模型，该模型可解析求解。分别研究了径向（radial）、相位（phase, Kuramoto-like）和笛卡尔（Cartesian）三种耦合方式，推导了单振子和耦合振子对的EPR解析表达式，并通过数值模拟进行验证。

Result: 单振子的EPR取决于三个关键因素：本征频率（intrinsic frequency）、切向速度涨落（tangential velocity fluctuations）和平均切向速度（mean tangential velocity）。系统动力学由一个无量纲有效温度（dimensionless effective temperature）——即本征弛豫时间尺度与扩散时间尺度之比——来刻画。有效温度和系统大小的变化会强烈影响EPR对耦合强度的依赖关系，在某些情况下导致定性不同的行为。不同耦合类型对切向速度分布的影响也不同。值得注意的是，在所有研究的情形中，笛卡尔耦合均能降低EPR，且这一结论不受有效温度和系统大小的影响。

Conclusion: 对理想化非线性振子的分析表明，不同类别的耦合相互作用以及振子内部相互竞争的弛豫与扩散时间尺度，对能量耗散具有不同的影响。笛卡尔耦合在所有条件下均能降低EPR，这为理解生物系统中耦合方式与能量效率之间的关系提供了理论依据。

Abstract: Non-linear oscillators serve important functions in many biological systems, including within the inner ear and neuronal networks. The sustainment of oscillations in noisy environments requires continuous energy dissipation, quantified by the steady-state entropy production rate (EPR). We study an idealized, analytically tractable model of a stochastic circular limit cycle and examine how mutual coupling in pairs and populations alters dissipation. For a single oscillator, the EPR depends on three key factors: intrinsic frequency, tangential velocity fluctuations, and mean tangential velocity. The dynamics are characterized by a dimensionless effective temperature given by the ratio of intrinsic relaxation and diffusion timescales. For radial (amplitude), phase (Kuramoto-like), and Cartesian couplings, we derive analytical expressions for the EPR and confirm them numerically. Varying the effective temperature and system size strongly influences how the EPR depends on coupling strength and, in some cases, results in qualitatively distinct behaviors. Moreover, the coupling types affect the tangential velocity distributions differently. Notably, in all cases studied, Cartesian coupling reduces the EPR relative to the uncoupled system, irrespective of effective temperature and system size. The analysis of idealized non-linear oscillators reveals that different classes of coupling interactions and competing timescales present in the oscillators have distinct effects on energy dissipation.

  <summary>Details</summary>

Method: 引入一族由整数$n$参数化的边界条件，对应边界处不同的速度分布，推广了标准通量加权麦克斯韦注入法（flux-weighted Maxwellian scheme）。结合刘维尔定理（Liouville's theorem）与边界注入规则，推导出稳态分布函数的显式解析表达式。

Conclusion: 该框架建立了微观边界动力学与宏观稳态分布之间的直接联系，表明边界注入规则的选取对系统稳态性质具有决定性影响，为无碰撞系统的非平衡稳态分析提供了精确解析工具。

Abstract: We present a technique to investigate the stationary states of a system of a collisionless system confined by an external potential and coupled to boundary reservoirs through prescribed reinjection rules. We consider a family of boundary conditions parametrized by an integer $n$, corresponding to different velocity distributions imposed at the boundaries, generalizing the standard flux-weighted Maxwellian scheme. By combining Liouville's theorem with the boundary injection rule, we derive an explicit analytical expression for the stationary distribution function. This framework provides a direct link between microscopic boundary dynamics and macroscopic stationary profiles. We show that thermal equilibrium is recovered only for the standard flux-weighted injection method, while for all other cases the system relaxes to manifestly non-thermal stationary states. The resulting density and temperature profiles exhibit non-trivial spatial structures, including non-monotonic behaviour and temperature gradients induced by the boundary conditions alone. Analytical predictions for stationary moments are obtained in closed form for representative cases and are nicely reproduced by particle-based numerical simulations.

Conclusion: 该精确动力学涨落-响应关系为非自治马尔可夫跳跃过程提供了统一的理论框架，能够恢复并深化经典的热力学和动力学涨落-响应结论，具有广泛的理论意义。

Abstract: We derive exact dynamical fluctuation-response relations (FRRs) for time-integrated observables of any nonautonomous Markov jump process. The finite-time covariance splits into an initial variability and an integral of response kernels along the driven dynamics. The identity sharpens the dynamical response thermodynamic and kinetic uncertainty relations and fluctuation-response inequalities (FRIs). It also recovers steady-state FRRs, fluctuation-dissipation theorem and Onsager reciprocity, identifies known autonomous FRIs as the zero-frequency mode.

### [239] [On the geometric algebras of the Ising model](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24688)
*N. Johnson,D. Marenduzzo,A. Morozov,E. Orlandini,G. M. Vasil*

Main category: cond-mat.stat-mech

TL;DR: 本文从克利福德几何代数（Clifford geometric algebra）与共形几何代数（conformal geometric algebra）的角度重新审视一维和二维伊辛模型（Ising model）的经典转移矩阵（transfer matrix）解法，展示了所有关键元素（转移矩阵、本征矢量、准粒子激发）可统一解释为共形克利福德代数中的元素，并揭示了伊辛模型与自由马约拉纳费米子（Majorana fermion）理论之间的内在联系。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 为经典的伊辛模型转移矩阵解法提供一种紧凑且物理上可解释的统一代数框架（unified algebraic framework），澄清标度变换（scale transformation）、费米子模式和对偶性（duality）在该模型中的作用，并为传统的费米子、格拉斯曼（Grassmann）或场论处理方法提供一种有益的教材性补充（pedagogical complement）。

Method: 以考夫曼（Kaufman）的自旋子表述（spinor formulation）为基础，将转移矩阵、本征矢量和准粒子激发均重新表述为适当的共形克利福德代数中的元素；将转移矩阵视为由共形双矢量（conformal bivector）生成的膨胀（dilation），本征矢量则对应于克利福德生成元的零组合（null combinations），从而类比马约拉纳费米子自由度的出现；在二维情形下将标准本征值方程重新解释为准粒子激发的色散关系（dispersion relation）。

Result: 所有显式精确结果均为已知结论，但该几何重构方法提供了一个统一的代数框架，揭示了伊辛模型中标度变换、费米子模式和对偶性的几何含义，并将转移矩阵的本征值问题与自由马约拉纳费米子的色散关系联系起来。

Conclusion: 该共形几何代数方法为理解伊辛模型提供了一种紧凑且物理直观的新视角，有望作为传统费米子、格拉斯曼或场论处理方法的教材性补充。

Abstract: We revisit the classical transfer matrix solution of the one- and two-dimensional Ising model from the perspective of Clifford and conformal geometric algebras. Building on Kaufman's spinor formulation, we show that all elements entering the solution, including the transfer matrix, its eigenvectors, and the quasiparticle excitations, admit a natural and unified interpretation as elements of an appropriate conformal Clifford algebra. In particular, the transfer matrix can be viewed as a dilation generated by a conformal bivector, while its eigenvectors correspond to null combinations of Clifford generators, closely paralleling the emergence of Majorana fermionic degrees of freedom. In the two-dimensional case, the standard eigenvalue equation for the row-to-row transfer matrix is reinterpreted as a dispersion relation for quasiparticle excitations, exposing the connection between the Ising model and a theory of free Majorana fermions. While all the explicit exact results recovered are well known, this geometric reformulation provides a unified algebraic framework which is compact and physically interpretable. Specifically, this clarifies the role of scale transformations, fermionic modes, and duality in the Ising model. We believe this approach offers a useful pedagogical complement to more conventional fermionic, Grassmann, or field theoretic treatments.

### [240] [Errors that matter: Uncertainty-aware universal machine-learning potentials calibrated on experiments](https://arxiv.org/abs/2604.24607)
*Matthias Kellner,Teitur Hansen,Thomas Bligaard,Karsten Wedel Jacobsen,Michele Ceriotti*

Main category: physics.chem-ph

TL;DR: 本文提出了一种将多个基于不同电子结构参考（electronic-structure references）训练的机器学习势（machine-learning potentials）集成并校准至实验数据的方法（PET-UAFD），从而将机器学习势从近似理论的精确插值器提升为以实验现实为锚定的真正预测性工具；同时引入 PET-EXP 协议，利用浅集成和统计重加权技术，以极低额外成本提供相对于实验测量的不确定度估计。


<details>
  <summary>Details</summary>
Motivation: 现有机器学习势模型（machine-learning potentials）虽能高效复现训练所依赖的量子力学计算精度，但其不确定度量化（uncertainty quantification）仅估计相对于参考计算的残差，而忽略了电子结构计算本身包含的近似所带来的不确定性贡献——后者往往是模型与实验观测之间偏差的主要来源。因此，需要一种方法将实验数据纳入校准，使模型能够对超出静态性质的预测也提供可靠的不确定度评估。

Method: 构建一个由多个基于不同电子结构参考（electronic-structure references）训练的机器学习势所组成的集成模型（ensemble），并借鉴不确定性感知泛函分布方法（uncertainty-aware functional distribution approach），将其校准至关于简单材料与分子的内聚能（cohesive energies）、原子化能（atomization energies）、晶格常数（lattice constants）和体积模量（bulk moduli）的实验数据上，得到名为 PET-UAFD 的集成模型。此外，引入 PET-EXP 协议，该协议利用浅集成（shallow ensembles）和统计重加权技术（statistical reweighting techniques），以几乎不增加计算成本的方式提供相对于实验测量的不确定度估计。

Result: 通过与液体密度和结构的实验测量结果对比表明，PET-UAFD 在超出其校准所用的静态性质之外，也能给出与现有最佳电子结构参考同样准确的预测，并且集成中的模型分布可用于评估预测的可靠性。PET-EXP 协议则能够以极低的额外成本提供准确的实验不确定性估计。

Conclusion: 该方法提供了一种实用且低成本的途径，将机器学习势从近似理论（如密度泛函理论）的忠实插值器（faithful interpolators）转变为以实验现实为锚定的真正预测性工具（genuinely predictive tools），有望广泛应用于多种组成和热力学条件下的物质模拟。

Abstract: Machine-learning models of atomic-scale interactions achieve the accuracy of the quantum mechanical calculations on which they are trained, but at a dramatically lower computational cost. Their predictions can be made trustworthy by uncertainty quantification techniques that estimate the residual error relative to their reference. These errors, however, do not include uncertainty contributions from the approximations inherent in the electronic structure calculations, which are often the main source of discrepancy with empirical observations. We construct an ensemble of ML potentials trained on multiple electronic-structure references and calibrate it against experimental data on cohesive energies, atomization energies, lattice constants and bulk moduli of simple materials and molecules, similar to the uncertainty-aware functional distribution approach. The resulting ensemble of models, which we call PET-UAFD, can be used to simulate matter across a wide range of compositions and thermodynamic conditions. By comparison with experimental measurements of the density and structure of liquids, we demonstrate that, even outside the static properties on which it was calibrated, PET-UAFD enables predictions that are as accurate against experiments as the best available electronic-structure reference and that the spread in the ensemble can be used to assess the reliability of such predictions. We also introduce the PET-EXP protocol that uses shallow ensembles and statistical reweighting techniques to provide accurate estimates of uncertainty relative to experimental measurements at virtually no additional cost over a simulation based on a single conventional ML potential. Ultimately, this approach provides a practical and inexpensive approach to elevate machine-learning potentials from faithful interpolators of approximate theories to genuinely predictive tools anchored in experimental reality.

</details>
